 nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam
 devīṃ sarasvatīṃ caiva tato jayam udīrayet
 dvaipāyanoṣṭhapuṭaniḥsṛtam aprameyaṃ
 puṇyaṃ pavitram atha pāpaharaṃ śivaṃ ca
 yo bhārataṃ samadhigacchati vācyamānaṃ
 kiṃ tasya puṣkarajalair abhiṣecanena
 śuklāmbaradharaṃ viṣṇuṃ śaśivarṇaṃ caturbhujam
 prasannavadanaṃ dhyāyet sarvavighnopaśāntaye
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a kṛtodakaṃ tu rājānaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c puraskṛtya mahābāhur uttatārākulendriyaḥ
a uttīrya ca mahīpālo bāṣpavyākulalocanaḥ
c papāta tīre gaṅgāyā vyādhaviddha iva dvipaḥ
a taṃ sīdamānaṃ jagrāha bhīmaḥ kṛṣṇena coditaḥ
c maivam ity abravīc cainaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ parabalārdanaḥ
a tam ārtaṃ patitaṃ bhūmau niśvasantaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
c dadṛśuḥ pāṇḍavā rājan dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā dīnamanasaṃ gatasattvaṃ janeśvaram
c bhūyaḥ śokasamāviṣṭāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ samupāviśan
a rājā ca dhṛtarāṣṭras tam upāsīno mahābhujaḥ
c vākyam āha mahāprājño mahāśokaprapīḍitam
a uttiṣṭha kuruśārdūla kuru kāryam anantaram
c kṣatradharmeṇa kauravya jiteyam avanis tvayā
a tāṃ bhuṅkṣva bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ suhṛdbhiś ca janeśvara
c na śocitavyaṃ paśyāmi tvayā dharmabhṛtāṃ vara
a śocitavyaṃ mayā caiva gāndhāryā ca viśāṃ pate
c putrair vihīno rājyena svapnalabdhadhano yathā
a aśrutvā hitakāmasya vidurasya mahātmanaḥ
c vākyāni sumahārthāni paritapyāmi durmatiḥ
a uktavān eṣa māṃ pūrvaṃ dharmātmā divyadarśanaḥ
c duryodhanāparādhena kulaṃ te vinaśiṣyati
a svasti ced icchase rājan kulasyātmana eva ca
c vadhyatām eṣa duṣṭātmā mando rājā suyodhanaḥ
a karṇaś ca śakuniś caiva mainaṃ paśyatu karhi cit
c dyūtasaṃpātam apy eṣām apramatto nivāraya
a abhiṣecaya rājānaṃ dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c sa pālayiṣyati vaśī dharmeṇa pṛthivīm imām
a atha necchasi rājānaṃ kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
b vināśam upayāsyanti tava putrā na saṃśayaḥ
c meḍhībhūtaḥ svayaṃ rājyaṃ pratigṛhṇīṣva pārthiva
a samaṃ sarveṣu bhūteṣu vartamānaṃ narādhipa
c anujīvantu sarve tvāṃ jñātayo jñātivardhana
a evaṃ bruvati kaunteya vidure dīrghadarśini
c duryodhanam ahaṃ pāpam anvavartaṃ vṛthāmatiḥ
a aśrutvā hy asya vīrasya vākyāni madhurāṇy aham
c phalaṃ prāpya mahad duḥkhaṃ nimagnaḥ śokasāgare
a vṛddhau hi te svaḥ pitarau paśyāvāṃ duḥkhitau nṛpa
c na śocitavyaṃ bhavatā paśyāmīha janādhipa
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktas tu rājñā sa dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa dhīmatā
c tūṣṇīṃ babhūva medhāvī tam uvācātha keśavaḥ
a atīva manasā śokaḥ kriyamāṇo janādhipa
c saṃtāpayati vaitasya pūrvapretān pitāmahān
a yajasva vividhair yajñair bahubhiḥ svāptadakṣiṇaiḥ
c devāṃs tarpaya somena svadhayā ca pitṝn api
d atithīn annapānena kāmair anyair akiṃcanān
a tvadvidhasya mahābuddhe naitad adyopapadyate
c viditaṃ veditavyaṃ te kartavyam api te kṛtam
a śrutāś ca rājadharmās te bhīṣmād bhāgīrathīsutāt
c kṛṣṇadvaipāyanāc caiva nāradād vidurāt tathā
a nemām arhasi mūḍhānāṃ vṛttiṃ tvam anuvartitum
c pitṛpaitāmahīṃ vṛttim āsthāya dhuram udvaha
a yuktaṃ hi yaśasā kṣatraṃ svargaṃ prāptum asaṃśayam
c na hi kaś cana śūrāṇāṃ nihato 'tra parāṅmukhaḥ
a tyaja śokaṃ mahārāja bhavitavyaṃ hi tat tathā
c na śakyās te punar draṣṭuṃ tvayā hy asmin raṇe hatāḥ
a etāvad uktvā govindo dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c virarāma mahātejās tam uvāca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a govinda mayi yā prītis tava sā viditā mama
c sauhṛdena tathā premṇā sadā mām anukampase
a priyaṃ tu me syāt sumahat kṛtaṃ cakragadādhara
c śrīman prītena manasā sarvaṃ yāvadanandana
a yadi mām anujānīyād bhavān gantuṃ tapovanam
b kṛtakṛtyo bhaviṣyāmi iti me niścitā matiḥ
c na hi śāntiṃ prapaśyāmi ghātayitvā pitāmaham
e karṇaṃ ca puruṣavyāghraṃ saṃgrāmeṣv apalāyinam
a karmaṇā yena mucyeyam asmāt krūrād ariṃdama
c karmaṇas tad vidhatsveha yena śudhyati me manaḥ
a tam evaṃvādinaṃ vyāsas tataḥ provāca dharmavit
c sāntvayan sumahātejāḥ śubhaṃ vacanam arthavat
a akṛtā te matis tāta punar bālyena muhyase
c kim ākāśe vayaṃ sarve pralapāma muhur muhuḥ
a viditāḥ kṣatradharmās te yeṣāṃ yuddhena jīvikā
c yathā pravṛtto nṛpatir nādhibandhena yujyate
a mokṣadharmāś ca nikhilā yāthātathyena te śrutāḥ
b yathā vai kāmajāṃ māyāṃ parityaktuṃ tvam arhasi
c asakṛc caiva saṃdehāś chinnās te kāmajā mayā
a aśraddadhāno durmedhā luptasmṛtir asi dhruvam
c maivaṃ bhava na te yuktam idam ajñānam īdṛśam
a prāyaścittāni sarvāṇi viditāni ca te 'nagha
c yuddhadharmāś ca te sarve dānadharmāś ca te śrutāḥ
a sa kathaṃ sarvadharmajñaḥ sarvāgamaviśāradaḥ
c parimuhyasi bhūyas tvam ajñānād iva bhārata
 vyāsa uvāca
a yudhiṣṭhira tava prajñā na samyag iti me matiḥ
c na hi kaś cit svayaṃ martyaḥ svavaśaḥ kurute kriyāḥ
a īśvareṇa niyukto 'yaṃ sādhv asādhu ca mānavaḥ
c karoti puruṣaḥ karma tatra kā paridevanā
a ātmānaṃ manyase cātha pāpakarmāṇam antataḥ
c śṛṇu tatra yathā pāpam apakṛṣyeta bhārata
a tapobhiḥ kratubhiś caiva dānena ca yudhiṣṭhira
b pūyante tu narā rājaṃs tasmād yajñāḥ parāyaṇam
c taranti nityaṃ puruṣā ye sma pāpāni kurvate
a yajñena tapasā caiva dānena ca narādhipa
c pūyante rājaśārdūla narā duṣkṛtakarmiṇaḥ
a asurāś ca surāś caiva puṇyahetor makhakriyām
c prayatante mahātmānas tasmād yajñāḥ parāyaṇam
a yajñair eva mahātmāno babhūvur adhikāḥ surāḥ
c tato devāḥ kriyāvanto dānavān abhyadharṣayan
a rājasūyāśvamedhau ca sarvamedhaṃ ca bhārata
c naramedhaṃ ca nṛpate tvam āhara yudhiṣṭhira
a yajasva vājimedhena vidhivad dakṣiṇāvatā
c bahukāmānnavittena rāmo dāśarathir yathā
a yathā ca bharato rājā dauḥṣantiḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ
c śākuntalo mahāvīryas tava pūrvapitāmahaḥ
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a asaṃśayaṃ vājimedhaḥ pāvayet pṛthivīm api
c abhiprāyas tu me kaś cit taṃ tvaṃ śrotum ihārhasi
a imaṃ jñātivadhaṃ kṛtvā sumahāntaṃ dvijottama
c dānam alpaṃ na śakyāmi dātuṃ vittaṃ ca nāsti me
a na ca bālān imān dīnān utsahe vasu yācitum
c tathaivārdravraṇān kṛcchre vartamānān nṛpātmajān
a svayaṃ vināśya pṛthivīṃ yajñārthe dvijasattama
c karam āhārayiṣyāmi kathaṃ śokaparāyaṇān
a duryodhanāparādhena vasudhā vasudhādhipāḥ
c pranaṣṭā yojayitvāsmān akīrtyā munisattama
a duryodhanena pṛthivī kṣayitā vittakāraṇāt
c kośaś cāpi viśīrṇo 'sau dhārtarāṣṭrasya durmateḥ
a pṛthivī dakṣiṇā cātra vidhiḥ prathamakalpikaḥ
c vidvadbhiḥ paridṛṣṭo 'yaṃ śiṣṭo vidhiviparyayaḥ
a na ca pratinidhiṃ kartuṃ cikīrṣāmi tapodhana
c atra me bhagavan samyak sācivyaṃ kartum arhasi
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktas tu pārthena kṛṣṇadvaipāyanas tadā
c muhūrtam anusaṃcintya dharmarājānam abravīt
d kośaś cāpi viśīrṇo 'yaṃ paripūrṇo bhaviṣyati
a vidyate draviṇaṃ pārtha girau himavati sthitam
c utsṛṣṭaṃ brāhmaṇair yajñe maruttasya mahīpateḥ
e tad ānayasva kaunteya paryāptaṃ tad bhaviṣyati
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a kathaṃ yajñe maruttasya draviṇaṃ tat samācitam
c kasmiṃś ca kāle sa nṛpo babhūva vadatāṃ vara
 vyāsa uvāca
a yadi śuśrūṣase pārtha śṛṇu kāraṃdhamaṃ nṛpam
c yasmin kāle mahāvīryaḥ sa rājāsīn mahādhanaḥ
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a śuśrūṣe tasya dharmajña rājarṣeḥ parikīrtanam
c dvaipāyana maruttasya kathāṃ prabrūhi me 'nagha
 vyāsa uvāca
a āsīt kṛtayuge pūrvaṃ manur daṇḍadharaḥ prabhuḥ
c tasya putro maheṣvāsaḥ prajātir iti viśrutaḥ
a prajāter abhavat putraḥ kṣupa ity abhiviśrutaḥ
c kṣupasya putras tv ikṣvākur mahīpālo 'bhavat prabhuḥ
a tasya putraśataṃ rājann āsīt paramadhārmikam
c tāṃs tu sarvān mahīpālān ikṣvākur akarot prabhuḥ
a teṣāṃ jyeṣṭhas tu viṃśo 'bhūt pratimānaṃ dhanuṣmatām
c viṃśasya putraḥ kalyāṇo viviṃśo nāma bhārata
a viviṃśasya sutā rājan babhūvur daśa pañca ca
c sarve dhanuṣi vikrāntā brahmaṇyāḥ satyavādinaḥ
a dānadharmaratāḥ santaḥ satataṃ priyavādinaḥ
c teṣāṃ jyeṣṭhaḥ khanīnetraḥ sa tān sarvān apīḍayat
a khanīnetras tu vikrānto jitvā rājyam akaṇṭakam
c nāśaknod rakṣituṃ rājyaṃ nānvarajyanta taṃ prajāḥ
a tam apāsya ca tad rāṣṭraṃ tasya putraṃ suvarcasam
c abhyaṣiñcata rājendra muditaṃ cābhavat tadā
a sa pitur vikriyāṃ dṛṣṭvā rājyān nirasanaṃ tathā
c niyato vartayām āsa prajāhitacikīrṣayā
a brahmaṇyaḥ satyavādī ca śuciḥ śamadamānvitaḥ
c prajās taṃ cānvarajyanta dharmanityaṃ manasvinam
a tasya dharmapravṛttasya vyaśīryat kośavāhanam
c taṃ kṣīṇakośaṃ sāmantāḥ samantāt paryapīḍayan
a sa pīḍyamāno bahubhiḥ kṣīṇakośas tv avāhanaḥ
c ārtim ārchat parāṃ rājā saha bhṛtyaiḥ pureṇa ca
a na cainaṃ parihartuṃ te 'śaknuvan parisaṃkṣaye
c samyagvṛtto hi rājā sa dharmanityo yudhiṣṭhira
a yadā tu paramām ārtiṃ gato 'sau sapuro nṛpaḥ
c tataḥ pradadhmau sa karaṃ prādurāsīt tato balam
a tatas tān ajayat sarvān prātisīmān narādhipān
c etasmāt kāraṇād rājan viśrutaḥ sa karaṃdhamaḥ
a tasya kāraṃdhamaḥ putras tretāyugamukhe 'bhavat
b putras tretāyugamukhe 'bhavad āvikṣasaṃjñakaḥ
b kāraṃdhama iti khyāto babhūva jagatīpatiḥ
c indrād anavaraḥ śrīmān devair api sudurjayaḥ
a tasya sarve mahīpālā vartante sma vaśe tadā
c sa hi samrāḍ abhūt teṣāṃ vṛttena ca balena ca
a avikṣin nāma dharmātmā śauryeṇendrasamo 'bhavat
c yajñaśīlaḥ karmaratir dhṛtimān saṃyatendriyaḥ
a tejasādityasadṛśaḥ kṣamayā pṛthivīsamaḥ
c bṛhaspatisamo buddhyā himavān iva susthiraḥ
a karmaṇā manasā vācā damena praśamena ca
c manāṃsy ārādhayām āsa prajānāṃ sa mahīpatiḥ
a ya īje hayamedhānāṃ śatena vidhivat prabhuḥ
c yājayām āsa yaṃ vidvān svayam evāṅgirāḥ prabhuḥ
a tasya putro 'ticakrāma pitaraṃ guṇavattayā
c marutto nāma dharmajñaś cakravartī mahāyaśāḥ
a nāgāyutasamaprāṇaḥ sākṣād viṣṇur ivāparaḥ
c sa yakṣyamāṇo dharmātmā śātakumbhamayāny uta
e kārayām āsa śubhrāṇi bhājanāni sahasraśaḥ
a meruṃ parvatam āsādya himavatpārśva uttare
c kāñcanaḥ sumahān pādas tatra karma cakāra saḥ
a tataḥ kuṇḍāni pātrīś ca piṭharāṇy āsanāni ca
c cakruḥ suvarṇakartāro yeṣāṃ saṃkhyā na vidyate
a tasyaiva ca samīpe sa yajñavāṭo babhūva ha
c īje tatra sa dharmātmā vidhivat pṛthivīpatiḥ
e maruttaḥ sahitaiḥ sarvaiḥ prajāpālair narādhipaḥ
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a kathaṃvīryaḥ samabhavat sa rājā vadatāṃ varaḥ
c kathaṃ ca jātarūpeṇa samayujyata sa dvija
a kva ca tat sāṃprataṃ dravyaṃ bhagavann avatiṣṭhate
c kathaṃ ca śakyam asmābhis tad avāptuṃ tapodhana
 vyāsa uvāca
a asurāś caiva devāś ca dakṣasyāsan prajāpateḥ
c apatyaṃ bahulaṃ tāta te 'spardhanta parasparam
a tathaivāṅgirasaḥ putrau vratatulyau babhūvatuḥ
c bṛhaspatir bṛhattejāḥ saṃvartaś ca tapodhanaḥ
a tāv api spardhinau rājan pṛthag āstāṃ parasparam
c bṛhaspatiś ca saṃvartaṃ bādhate sma punaḥ punaḥ
a sa bādhyamānaḥ satataṃ bhrātrā jyeṣṭhena bhārata
c arthān utsṛjya digvāsā vanavāsam arocayat
a vāsavo 'py asurān sarvān nirjitya ca nihatya ca
c indratvaṃ prāpya lokeṣu tato vavre purohitam
e putram aṅgiraso jyeṣṭhaṃ vipraśreṣṭhaṃ bṛhaspatim
a yājyas tv aṅgirasaḥ pūrvam āsīd rājā karaṃdhamaḥ
c vīryeṇāpratimo loke vṛttena ca balena ca
e śatakratur ivaujasvī dharmātmā saṃśitavrataḥ
a vāhanaṃ yasya yodhāś ca dravyāṇi vividhāni ca
b śayanāni ca mukhyāni mahārhāṇi ca sarvaśaḥ
c dhyānād evābhavad rājan mukhavātena sarvaśaḥ
a sa guṇaiḥ pārthivān sarvān vaśe cakre narādhipaḥ
c saṃjīvya kālam iṣṭaṃ ca saśarīro divaṃ gataḥ
a babhūva tasya putras tu yayātir iva dharmavit
c avikṣin nāma śatrukṣit sa vaśe kṛtavān mahīm
e vikrameṇa guṇaiś caiva pitevāsīt sa pārthivaḥ
a tasya vāsavatulyo 'bhūn marutto nāma vīryavān
c putras tam anuraktābhūt pṛthivī sāgarāmbarā
a spardhate satataṃ sa sma devarājena pārthivaḥ
c vāsavo 'pi maruttena spardhate pāṇḍunandana
a śuciḥ sa guṇavān āsīn maruttaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ
c yatamāno 'pi yaṃ śakro na viśeṣayati sma ha
a so 'śaknuvan viśeṣāya samāhūya bṛhaspatim
c uvācedaṃ vaco devaiḥ sahito harivāhanaḥ
a bṛhaspate maruttasya mā sma kārṣīḥ kathaṃ cana
c daivaṃ karmātha vā pitryaṃ kartāsi mama cet priyam
a ahaṃ hi triṣu lokeṣu surāṇāṃ ca bṛhaspate
c indratvaṃ prāptavān eko maruttas tu mahīpatiḥ
a kathaṃ hy amartyaṃ brahmaṃs tvaṃ yājayitvā surādhipam
c yājayer mṛtyusaṃyuktaṃ maruttam aviśaṅkayā
a māṃ vā vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te maruttaṃ vā mahīpatim
c parityajya maruttaṃ vā yathājoṣaṃ bhajasva mām
a evam uktaḥ sa kauravya devarājñā bṛhaspatiḥ
c muhūrtam iva saṃcintya devarājānam abravīt
a tvaṃ bhūtānām adhipatis tvayi lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ
c namucer viśvarūpasya nihantā tvaṃ balasya ca
a tvam ājahartha devānām eko vīra śriyaṃ parām
c tvaṃ bibharṣi bhuvaṃ dyāṃ ca sadaiva balasūdana
a paurohityaṃ kathaṃ kṛtvā tava devagaṇeśvara
c yājayeyam ahaṃ martyaṃ maruttaṃ pākaśāsana
a samāśvasihi deveśa nāhaṃ martyāya karhi cit
c grahīṣyāmi sruvaṃ yajñe śṛṇu cedaṃ vaco mama
a hiraṇyaretaso 'mbhaḥ syāt parivarteta medinī
c bhāsaṃ ca na raviḥ kuryān matsatyaṃ vicaled yadi
a bṛhaspativacaḥ śrutvā śakro vigatamatsaraḥ
c praśasyainaṃ viveśātha svam eva bhavanaṃ tadā
 vyāsa uvāca
a atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c bṛhaspateś ca saṃvādaṃ maruttasya ca bhārata
a devarājasya samayaṃ kṛtam āṅgirasena ha
c śrutvā marutto nṛpatir manyum āhārayat tadā
a saṃkalpya manasā yajñaṃ karaṃdhamasutātmajaḥ
c bṛhaspatim upāgamya vāgmī vacanam abravīt
a bhagavan yan mayā pūrvam abhigamya tapodhana
c kṛto 'bhisaṃdhir yajñāya bhavato vacanād guro
a tam ahaṃ yaṣṭum icchāmi saṃbhārāḥ saṃbhṛtāś ca me
c yājyo 'smi bhavataḥ sādho tat prāpnuhi vidhatsva ca
 bṛhaspatir uvāca
a na kāmaye yājayituṃ tvām ahaṃ pṛthivīpate
c vṛto 'smi devarājena pratijñātaṃ ca tasya me
 marutta uvāca
a pitryam asmi tava kṣetraṃ bahu manye ca te bhṛśam
c na cāsmy ayājyatāṃ prāpto bhajamānaṃ bhajasva mām
 bṛhaspatir uvāca
a amartyaṃ yājayitvāhaṃ yājayiṣye na mānuṣam
c marutta gaccha vā mā vā nivṛtto 'smy adya yājanāt
a na tvāṃ yājayitāsmy adya vṛṇu tvaṃ yam ihecchasi
c upādhyāyaṃ mahābāho yas te yajñaṃ kariṣyati
 vyāsa uvāca
a evam uktas tu nṛpatir marutto vrīḍito 'bhavat
c pratyāgacchac ca saṃvigno dadarśa pathi nāradam
a devarṣiṇā samāgamya nāradena sa pārthivaḥ
c vidhivat prāñjalis tasthāv athainaṃ nārado 'bravīt
a rājarṣe nātihṛṣṭo 'si kaccit kṣemaṃ tavānagha
c kva gato 'si kuto vedam aprītisthānam āgatam
a śrotavyaṃ cen mayā rājan brūhi me pārthivarṣabha
c vyapaneṣyāmi te manyuṃ sarvayatnair narādhipa
a evam ukto maruttas tu nāradena maharṣiṇā
c vipralambham upādhyāyāt sarvam eva nyavedayat
a gato 'smy aṅgirasaḥ putraṃ devācāryaṃ bṛhaspatim
c yajñārtham ṛtvijaṃ draṣṭuṃ sa ca māṃ nābhyanandata
a pratyākhyātaś ca tenāhaṃ jīvituṃ nādya kāmaye
c parityaktaś ca guruṇā dūṣitaś cāsmi nārada
a evam uktas tu rājñā sa nāradaḥ pratyuvāca ha
c āvikṣitaṃ mahārāja vācā saṃjīvayann iva
a rājann aṅgirasaḥ putraḥ saṃvarto nāma dhārmikaḥ
c caṅkramīti diśaḥ sarvā digvāsā mohayan prajāḥ
a taṃ gaccha yadi yājyaṃ tvāṃ na vāñchati bṛhaspatiḥ
c prasannas tvāṃ mahārāja saṃvarto yājayiṣyati
 marutta uvāca
a saṃjīvito 'haṃ bhavatā vākyenānena nārada
c paśyeyaṃ kva nu saṃvartaṃ śaṃsa me vadatāṃ vara
a kathaṃ ca tasmai varteyaṃ kathaṃ māṃ na parityajet
c pratyākhyātaś ca tenāpi nāhaṃ jīvitum utsahe
 nārada uvāca
a unmattaveṣaṃ bibhrat sa caṅkramīti yathāsukham
c vārāṇasīṃ tu nagarīm abhīkṣṇam upasevate
d yatra sākṣān mahādevo dehānte parameśvaraḥ
d vyācaṣṭe tārakajñānaṃ jantūnām apavargadam
a tasyā dvāraṃ samāsādya nyasethāḥ kuṇapaṃ kva cit
c taṃ dṛṣṭvā yo nivarteta sa saṃvarto mahīpate
a taṃ pṛṣṭhato 'nugacchethā yatra gacchet sa vīryavān
c tam ekānte samāsādya prāñjaliḥ śaraṇaṃ vrajeḥ
a pṛcchet tvāṃ yadi kenāhaṃ tavākhyāta iti sma ha
c brūyās tvaṃ nāradeneti saṃtapta iva śatruhan
a sa cet tvām anuyuñjīta mamābhigamanepsayā
c śaṃsethā vahnim ārūḍhaṃ mām api tvam aśaṅkayā
 vyāsa uvāca
a sa tatheti pratiśrutya pūjayitvā ca nāradam
c abhyanujñāya rājarṣir yayau vārāṇasīṃ purīm
a tatra gatvā yathoktaṃ sa puryā dvāre mahāyaśāḥ
c kuṇapaṃ sthāpayām āsa nāradasya vacaḥ smaran
a yaugapadyena vipraś ca sa purīdvāram āviśat
c tataḥ sa kuṇapaṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasā sa nyavartata
a sa taṃ nivṛttam ālakṣya prāñjaliḥ pṛṣṭhato 'nvagāt
c āvikṣito mahīpālaḥ saṃvartam upaśikṣitum
a sa enaṃ vijane dṛṣṭvā pāṃsubhiḥ kardamena ca
c śleṣmaṇā cāpi rājānaṃ ṣṭhīvanaiś ca samākirat
a sa tathā bādhyamāno 'pi saṃvartena mahīpatiḥ
c anvagād eva tam ṛṣiṃ prāñjaliḥ saṃprasādayan
a tato nivṛtya saṃvartaḥ pariśrānta upāviśat
c śītalacchāyam āsādya nyagrodhaṃ bahuśākhinam
 saṃvarta uvāca
a katham asmi tvayā jñātaḥ kena vā kathito 'smi te
c etad ācakṣva me tattvam icchase cet priyaṃ mama
a satyaṃ te bruvataḥ sarve saṃpatsyante manorathāḥ
c mithyā tu bruvato mūrdhā saptadhā te phaliṣyati
 marutta uvāca
a nāradena bhavān mahyam ākhyāto hy aṭatā pathi
c guruputro mameti tvaṃ tato me prītir uttamā
 saṃvarta uvāca
a satyam etad bhavān āha sa māṃ jānāti satriṇam
c kathayasvaitad ekaṃ me kva nu saṃprati nāradaḥ
 marutta uvāca
a bhavantaṃ kathayitvā tu mama devarṣisattamaḥ
c tato mām abhyanujñāya praviṣṭo havyavāhanam
d yojanīyo 'ham adhunā bhavatā munisattama
 vyāsa uvāca
a śrutvā tu pārthivasyaitat saṃvartaḥ parayā mudā
c etāvad aham apy enaṃ kuryām iti tadābravīt
a tato maruttam unmatto vācā nirbhartsayann iva
c rūkṣayā brāhmaṇo rājan punaḥ punar athābravīt
a vātapradhānena mayā svacittavaśavartinā
c evaṃ vikṛtarūpeṇa kathaṃ yājitum icchasi
a bhrātā mama samarthaś ca vāsavena ca satkṛtaḥ
c vartate yājane caiva tena karmāṇi kāraya
a gṛhaṃ svaṃ caiva yājyāś ca sarvā gṛhyāś ca devatāḥ
c pūrvajena mamākṣiptaṃ śarīraṃ varjitaṃ tv idam
a nāhaṃ tenānanujñātas tvām āvikṣita karhi cit
c yājayeyaṃ kathaṃ cid vai sa hi pūjyatamo mama
a sa tvaṃ bṛhaspatiṃ gaccha tam anujñāpya cāvraja
c tato 'haṃ yājayiṣye tvāṃ yadi yaṣṭum ihecchasi
 marutta uvāca
a bṛhaspatiṃ gataḥ pūrvam ahaṃ saṃvarta tac chṛṇu
c na māṃ kāmayate yājyam asau vāsavavāritaḥ
a amaraṃ yājyam āsādya mām ṛṣe mā sma mānuṣam
c yājayethā maruttaṃ tvaṃ martyadharmāṇam āturam
d śakreṇa pratiṣiddho 'haṃ maruttaṃ mā sma yājayeḥ
d na māṃ rocayate rājyam ayājyaṃ mām amānuṣam
a spardhate ca mayā vipra sadā vai sa hi pārthivaḥ
c evam astv iti cāpy ukto bhrātrā te balavṛtrahā
a sa mām abhigataṃ premṇā yājyavan na bubhūṣati
c devarājam upāśritya tad viddhi munipuṃgava
a so 'ham icchāmi bhavatā sarvasvenāpi yājitum
c kāmaye samatikrāntuṃ vāsavaṃ tvatkṛtair guṇaiḥ
a na hi me vartate buddhir gantuṃ brahman bṛhaspatim
c pratyākhyāto hi tenāsmi tathānapakṛte sati
 saṃvarta uvāca
a cikīrṣasi yathākāmaṃ sarvam etat tvayi dhruvam
c yadi sarvān abhiprāyān kartāsi mama pārthiva
a yājyamānaṃ mayā hi tvāṃ bṛhaspatipuraṃdarau
c dviṣetāṃ samabhikruddhāv etad ekaṃ samarthaya
a sthairyam atra kathaṃ te syāt sa tvaṃ niḥsaṃśayaṃ kuru
c kupitas tvāṃ na hīdānīṃ bhasma kuryāṃ sabāndhavam
 marutta uvāca
a yāvat tapet sahasrāṃśus tiṣṭheraṃś cāpi parvatāḥ
c tāval lokān na labheyaṃ tyajeyaṃ saṃgataṃ yadi
a mā cāpi śubhabuddhitvaṃ labheyam iha karhi cit
c samyag jñāne vaiṣaye vā tyajeyaṃ saṃgataṃ yadi
 saṃvarta uvāca
a āvikṣita śubhā buddhir dhīyatāṃ tava karmasu
c yājanaṃ hi mamāpy evaṃ vartate tvayi pārthiva
a saṃvidhāsye ca te rājann akṣayaṃ dravyam uttamam
c yena devān sagandharvāñ śakraṃ cābhibhaviṣyasi
a na tu me vartate buddhir dhane yājyeṣu vā punaḥ
c vipriyaṃ tu cikīrṣāmi bhrātuś cendrasya cobhayoḥ
a gamayiṣyāmi cendreṇa samatām api te dhruvam
c priyaṃ ca te kariṣyāmi satyam etad bravīmi te
 saṃvarta uvāca
a girer himavataḥ pṛṣṭhe muñjavān nāma parvataḥ
c tapyate yatra bhagavāṃs tapo nityam umāpatiḥ
a vanaspatīnāṃ mūleṣu ṭaṅkeṣu śikhareṣu ca
c guhāsu śailarājasya yathākāmaṃ yathāsukham
a umāsahāyo bhagavān yatra nityaṃ maheśvaraḥ
c āste śūlī mahātejā nānābhūtagaṇāvṛtaḥ
a tatra rudrāś ca sādhyāś ca viśve 'tha vasavas tathā
c yamaś ca varuṇaś caiva kuberaś ca sahānugaḥ
a bhūtāni ca piśācāś ca nāsatyāv aśvināv api
c gandharvāpsarasaś caiva yakṣā devarṣayas tathā
a ādityā marutaś caiva yātudhānāś ca sarvaśaḥ
b brahmādayaś ca maruto munayo 'dhyātmacintakāḥ
c upāsante mahātmānaṃ bahurūpam umāpatim
a ramate bhagavāṃs tatra kuberānucaraiḥ saha
c vikṛtair vikṛtākāraiḥ krīḍadbhiḥ pṛthivīpate
e śriyā jvalan dṛśyate vai bālādityasamadyutiḥ
a na rūpaṃ dṛśyate tasya saṃsthānaṃ vā kathaṃ cana
c nirdeṣṭuṃ prāṇibhiḥ kaiś cit prākṛtair māṃsalocanaiḥ
a noṣṇaṃ na śiśiraṃ tatra na vāyur na ca bhāskaraḥ
c na jarā kṣutpipāse vā na mṛtyur na bhayaṃ nṛpa
a tasya śailasya pārśveṣu sarveṣu jayatāṃ vara
c dhātavo jātarūpasya raśmayaḥ savitur yathā
a rakṣyante te kuberasya sahāyair udyatāyudhaiḥ
c cikīrṣadbhiḥ priyaṃ rājan kuberasya mahātmanaḥ
d tatra gatvā tvam anvāsya mahāyogeśvaraṃ śivam
d kuru praṇāmaṃ rājarṣe bhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ
a tasmai bhagavate kṛtvā namaḥ śarvāya vedhase
b ebhis tvaṃ nāmabhir devaṃ sarvavidyādhipaṃ stuhi
c rudrāya śitikaṇṭhāya surūpāya suvarcase
a kapardine karālāya haryakṣṇe varadāya ca
c tryakṣṇe pūṣṇo dantabhide vāmanāya śivāya ca
a yāmyāyāvyaktakeśāya sadvṛtte śaṃkarāya ca
c kṣemyāya harinetrāya sthāṇave puruṣāya ca
a harikeśāya muṇḍāya kṛśāyottāraṇāya ca
c bhāskarāya sutīrthāya devadevāya raṃhase
d bahurūpāya śarvāya priyāya priyavāsase
a uṣṇīṣiṇe suvaktrāya sahasrākṣāya mīḍhuṣe
c giriśāya praśāntāya yataye cīravāsase
a bilvadaṇḍāya siddhāya sarvadaṇḍadharāya ca
c mṛgavyādhāya mahate dhanvine 'tha bhavāya ca
a varāya saumyavaktrāya paśuhastāya varṣiṇe
c hiraṇyabāhave rājann ugrāya pataye diśām
d lelihānāya gotrāya siddhamantrāya vṛṣṇaye
a paśūnāṃ pataye caiva bhūtānāṃ pataye tathā
c vṛṣāya mātṛbhaktāya senānye madhyamāya ca
a sruvahastāya pataye dhanvine bhārgavāya ca
c ajāya kṛṣṇanetrāya virūpākṣāya caiva ha
a tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrāya tīkṣṇāya vaiśvānaramukhāya ca
c mahādyutaye 'naṅgāya sarvāṅgāya prajāvate
d vilohitāya dīptāya dīptākṣāya mahaujase
a tathā śukrādhipataye pṛthave kṛttivāsase
c kapālamāline nityaṃ suvarṇamukuṭāya ca
a mahādevāya kṛṣṇāya tryambakāyānaghāya ca
c krodhanāya nṛśaṃsāya mṛdave bāhuśāline
a daṇḍine taptatapase tathaiva krūrakarmaṇe
c sahasraśirase caiva sahasracaraṇāya ca
e namaḥ svadhāsvarūpāya bahurūpāya daṃṣṭriṇe
a pinākinaṃ mahādevaṃ mahāyoginam avyayam
c triśūlapāṇiṃ varadaṃ tryambakaṃ bhuvaneśvaram
a tripuraghnaṃ trinayanaṃ trilokeśaṃ mahaujasam
c prabhavaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ dhāraṇaṃ dharaṇīdharam
a īśānaṃ śaṃkaraṃ sarvaṃ śivaṃ viśveśvaraṃ bhavam
c umāpatiṃ paśupatiṃ viśvarūpaṃ maheśvaram
a virūpākṣaṃ daśabhujaṃ tiṣyagovṛṣabhadhvajam
b anantaṃ śāśvataṃ devaṃ triśṛṅgaṃ vṛṣabhekṣaṇam
c ugraṃ sthāṇuṃ śivaṃ ghoraṃ śarvaṃ gaurīśam īśvaram
a śitikaṇṭham ajaṃ śukraṃ pṛthuṃ pṛthuharaṃ haram
c viśvarūpaṃ virūpākṣaṃ bahurūpam umāpatim
a praṇamya śirasā devam anaṅgāṅgaharaṃ haram
c śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ yāhi mahādevaṃ caturmukham
d virocamānaṃ vapuṣā divyābharaṇabhūṣitam
d anādyantam ajaṃ śaṃbhuṃ sarvavyāpinam īśvaram
d nistraiguṇyaṃ nirudvegaṃ nirmalaṃ nidhim ojasām
d praṇamya prāñjaliḥ śarvaṃ prayāmi śaraṇaṃ haram
d sāmānyaṃ niścalaṃ nityam akāraṇam alepanam
d adhyātmavedam āsādya prayāmi śaraṇaṃ muhuḥ
d yasya nityaṃ viduḥ sthānaṃ mokṣam adhyātmacintakāḥ
d yoginas tattvamārgasthāḥ kaivalyaṃ padam akṣaram
d yaṃ viduḥ saṅganirmuktāḥ sāmānyaṃ samadarśinaḥ
d taṃ prapadye jagadyonim ayoniṃ nirguṇātmakam
d asṛjad yas tu bhūtādīn sapta lokān sanātanān
d sthitaḥ satyopari sthāṇus taṃ prapadye sanātanam
d bhaktānāṃ sulabhaṃ taṃ hi durlabhaṃ dūrapātinām
d adūrastham ajaṃ devaṃ prakṛteḥ parataḥ sthitam
d namāmi sarvalokasthaṃ vrajāmi śaraṇaṃ śivam
a evaṃ kṛtvā namas tasmai mahādevāya raṃhase
c mahātmane kṣitipate tat suvarṇam avāpsyasi
d labhante gāṇapatyaṃ ca tadekāgrā hi mānavāḥ
d kiṃ punaḥ svarṇabhāṇḍāni tasmāt tvaṃ gaccha mā ciram
d mahattaraṃ hi te lābhaṃ hastyaśvoṣṭrādibhiḥ saha
e suvarṇam āhariṣyantas tatra gacchantu te narāḥ
 vyāsa uvāca
a ity uktaḥ sa vacas tasya cakre kāraṃdhamātmajaḥ
b gaṅgādharaṃ namaskṛtya labdhavān dhanam uttamam
b kubera iva tat prāpya mahādevaprasādataḥ
c tato 'timānuṣaṃ sarvaṃ cakre yajñasya saṃvidhim
e sauvarṇāni ca bhāṇḍāni saṃcakrus tatra śilpinaḥ
f śālāś ca sarvasaṃbhārān kratoḥ saṃvartaśāsanāt
a bṛhaspatis tu tāṃ śrutvā maruttasya mahīpateḥ
c samṛddhim ati devebhyaḥ saṃtāpam akarod bhṛśam
a sa tapyamāno vaivarṇyaṃ kṛśatvaṃ cāgamat param
c bhaviṣyati hi me śatruḥ saṃvarto vasumān iti
a taṃ śrutvā bhṛśasaṃtaptaṃ devarājo bṛhaspatim
c abhigamyāmaravṛtaḥ provācedaṃ vacas tadā
 indra uvāca
a kaccit sukhaṃ svapiṣi tvaṃ bṛhaspate
kaccin manojñāḥ paricārakās te
c kaccid devānāṃ sukhakāmo 'si vipra
kaccid devās tvāṃ paripālayanti
 bṛhaspatir uvāca
a sukhaṃ śaye 'haṃ śayane mahendra
tathā manojñāḥ paricārakā me
c tathā devānāṃ sukhakāmo 'smi śakra
devāś ca māṃ subhṛśaṃ pālayanti
 indra uvāca
a kuto duḥkhaṃ mānasaṃ dehajaṃ vā
pāṇḍur vivarṇaś ca kutas tvam adya
c ācakṣva me tad dvija yāvad etān
nihanmi sarvāṃs tava duḥkhakartṝn
 bṛhaspatir uvāca
a maruttam āhur maghavan yakṣyamāṇaṃ
mahāyajñenottamadakṣiṇena
c taṃ saṃvarto yājayiteti me śrutaṃ
tad icchāmi na sa taṃ yājayeta
 indra uvāca
a sarvān kāmān anujāto 'si vipra
yas tvaṃ devānāṃ mantrayase purodhāḥ
c ubhau ca te janmamṛtyū vyatītau
kiṃ saṃvartas tava kartādya vipra
 bṛhaspatir uvāca
a devaiḥ saha tvam asurān saṃpraṇudya
jighāṃsase 'dyāpy uta sānubandhān
c yaṃ yaṃ samṛddhaṃ paśyasi tatra tatra
duḥkhaṃ sapatneṣu samṛddhabhāvaḥ
a ato 'smi devendra vivarṇarūpaḥ
sapatno me vardhate tan niśamya
c sarvopāyair maghavan saṃniyaccha
saṃvartaṃ vā pārthivaṃ vā maruttam
 indra uvāca
a ehi gaccha prahito jātavedo
bṛhaspatiṃ paridātuṃ marutte
c ayaṃ vai tvā yājayitā bṛhaspatis
tathāmaraṃ caiva kariṣyatīti
 agnir uvāca
a ayaṃ gacchāmi tava śakrādya dūto
bṛhaspatiṃ paridātuṃ marutte
c vācaṃ satyāṃ puruhūtasya kartuṃ
bṛhaspateś cāpacitiṃ cikīrṣuḥ
 vyāsa uvāca
a tataḥ prāyād dhūmaketur mahātmā
vanaspatīn vīrudhaś cāvamṛdnan
c kāmād dhimānte parivartamānaḥ
kāṣṭhātigo mātariśveva nardan
 marutta uvāca
a āścaryam adya paśyāmi rūpiṇaṃ vahnim āgatam
c āsanaṃ salilaṃ pādyaṃ gāṃ copānaya vai mune
 agnir uvāca
a āsanaṃ salilaṃ pādyaṃ pratinandāmi te 'nagha
c indreṇa tu samādiṣṭaṃ viddhi māṃ dūtam āgatam
 marutta uvāca
a kaccic chrīmān devarājaḥ sukhī ca
kaccic cāsmān prīyate dhūmaketo
c kaccid devāś cāsya vaśe yathāvat
tad brūhi tvaṃ mama kārtsnyena deva
 agnir uvāca
a śakro bhṛśaṃ susukhī pārthivendra
prītiṃ cecchaty ajarāṃ vai tvayā saḥ
c devāś ca sarve vaśagās tasya rājan
saṃdeśaṃ tvaṃ śṛṇu me devarājñaḥ
a yadarthaṃ māṃ prāhiṇot tvatsakāśaṃ
bṛhaspatiṃ paridātuṃ marutte
c ayaṃ gurur yājayitā nṛpa tvāṃ
martyaṃ santam amaraṃ tvāṃ karotu
 marutta uvāca
a saṃvarto 'yaṃ yājayitā dvijo me
bṛhaspater añjalir eṣa tasya
c nāsau devaṃ yājayitvā mahendraṃ
martyaṃ santaṃ yājayann adya śobhet
 agnir uvāca
a ye vai lokā devaloke mahāntaḥ
saṃprāpsyase tān devarājaprasādāt
c tvāṃ ced asau yājayed vai bṛhaspatir
nūnaṃ svargaṃ tvaṃ jayeḥ kīrtiyuktaḥ
a tathā lokā mānuṣā ye ca divyāḥ
prajāpateś cāpi ye vai mahāntaḥ
c te te jitā devarājyaṃ ca kṛtsnaṃ
bṛhaspatiś ced yājayet tvāṃ narendra
 saṃvarta uvāca
a māsmān evaṃ tvaṃ punar āgāḥ kathaṃ cid
bṛhaspatiṃ paridātuṃ marutte
c mā tvāṃ dhakṣye cakṣuṣā dāruṇena
saṃkruddho 'haṃ pāvaka tan nibodha
 vyāsa uvāca
a tato devān agamad dhūmaketur
dāhād bhīto vyathito 'śvatthaparṇavat
c taṃ vai dṛṣṭvā prāha śakro mahātmā
bṛhaspateḥ saṃnidhau havyavāham
a yat tvaṃ gataḥ prahito jātavedo
bṛhaspatiṃ paridātuṃ marutte
c tat kiṃ prāha sa nṛpo yakṣyamāṇaḥ
kaccid vacaḥ pratigṛhṇāti tac ca
 agnir uvāca
a na te vācaṃ rocayate marutto
bṛhaspater añjaliṃ prāhiṇot saḥ
c saṃvarto māṃ yājayitety abhīkṣṇaṃ
punaḥ punaḥ sa mayā procyamānaḥ
a uvācedaṃ mānuṣā ye ca divyāḥ
prajāpater ye ca lokā mahāntaḥ
c tāṃś cel labheyaṃ saṃvidaṃ tena kṛtvā
tathāpi neccheyam iti pratītaḥ
 indra uvāca
a punar bhavān pārthivaṃ taṃ sametya
vākyaṃ madīyaṃ prāpaya svārthayuktam
c punar yady ukto na kariṣyate vacas
tato vajraṃ saṃprahartāsmi tasmai
 agnir uvāca
a gandharvarāḍ yātv ayaṃ tatra dūto
bibhemy ahaṃ vāsava tatra gantum
c saṃrabdho mām abravīt tīkṣṇaroṣaḥ
saṃvarto vākyaṃ caritabrahmacaryaḥ
a yady āgaccheḥ punar evaṃ kathaṃ cid
bṛhaspatiṃ paridātuṃ marutte
c daheyaṃ tvāṃ cakṣuṣā dāruṇena
saṃkruddha ity etad avaihi śakra
 indra uvāca
a tvam evānyān dahase jātavedo
na hi tvad anyo vidyate bhasmakartā
c tvatsaṃsparśāt sarvaloko bibhety
aśraddheyaṃ vadase havyavāha
 agnir uvāca
a divaṃ devendra pṛthivīṃ caiva sarvāṃ
saṃveṣṭayes tvaṃ svabalenaiva śakra
c evaṃvidhasyeha satas tavāsau
kathaṃ vṛtras tridivaṃ prāg jahāra
 indra uvāca
a na caṇḍikā jaṅgamā no kareṇur
na vārisomaṃ prapibāmi vahne
c na durbale vai visṛjāmi vajraṃ
ko me 'sukhāya praharen manuṣyaḥ
a pravrājayeyaṃ kālakeyān pṛthivyām
apākarṣaṃ dānavān antarikṣāt
c divaḥ prahrādam avasānam ānayaṃ
ko me 'sukhāya prahareta martyaḥ
 agnir uvāca
a yatra śaryātiṃ cyavano yājayiṣyan
sahāśvibhyāṃ somam agṛhṇad ekaḥ
c taṃ tvaṃ kruddhaḥ pratyaṣedhīḥ purastāc
charyātiyajñaṃ smara taṃ mahendra
a vajraṃ gṛhītvā ca puraṃdara tvaṃ
saṃprāhārṣīś cyavanasyātighoram
c sa te vipraḥ saha vajreṇa bāhum
apāgṛhṇāt tapasā jātamanyuḥ
a tato roṣāt sarvato ghorarūpaṃ
sapatnaṃ te janayām āsa bhūyaḥ
c madaṃ nāmāsuraṃ viśvarūpaṃ
yaṃ tvaṃ dṛṣṭvā cakṣuṣī saṃnyamīlaḥ
a hanur ekā jagatīsthā tathaikā
divaṃ gatā mahato dānavasya
c sahasraṃ dantānāṃ śatayojanānāṃ
sutīkṣṇānāṃ ghorarūpaṃ babhūva
a vṛttāḥ sthūlā rajatastambhavarṇā
daṃṣṭrāś catasro dve śate yojanānām
c sa tvāṃ dantān vidaśann abhyadhāvaj
jighāṃsayā śūlam udyamya ghoram
a apaśyas tvaṃ taṃ tadā ghorarūpaṃ
sarve tv anye dadṛśur darśanīyam
c yasmād bhītaḥ prāñjalis tvaṃ maharṣim
āgacchethāḥ śaraṇaṃ dānavaghna
a kṣatrād evaṃ brahmabalaṃ garīyo
na brahmataḥ kiṃ cid anyad garīyaḥ
c so 'haṃ jānan brahmatejo yathāvan
na saṃvartaṃ gantum icchāmi śakra
 indra uvāca
a evam etad brahmabalaṃ garīyo
na brahmataḥ kiṃ cid anyad garīyaḥ
c āvikṣitasya tu balaṃ na mṛṣye
vajram asmai prahariṣyāmi ghoram
a dhṛtarāṣṭra prahito gaccha maruttaṃ
saṃvartena sahitaṃ taṃ vadasva
c bṛhaspatiṃ tvam upaśikṣasva rājan
vajraṃ vā te prahariṣyāmi ghoram
 vyāsa uvāca
a tato gatvā dhṛtarāṣṭro narendraṃ
provācedaṃ vacanaṃ vāsavasya
c gandharvaṃ māṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ nibodha
tvām āgataṃ vaktukāmaṃ narendra
a aindraṃ vākyaṃ śṛṇu me rājasiṃha
yat prāha lokādhipatir mahātmā
c bṛhaspatiṃ yājakaṃ tvaṃ vṛṇīṣva
vajraṃ vā te prahariṣyāmi ghoram
e vacaś ced etan na kariṣyase me
prāhaitad etāvad acintyakarmā
f bṛhaspatiṃ yājayituṃ na cecched
f vajraṃ tasmai prahariṣyāmi ghoram
 marutta uvāca
a tvaṃ caivaitad vettha puraṃdaraś ca
viśvedevā vasavaś cāśvinau ca
c mitradrohe niṣkṛtir vai yathaiva
nāstīti lokeṣu sadaiva vādaḥ
a bṛhaspatir yājayitā mahendraṃ
devaśreṣṭhaṃ vajrabhṛtāṃ variṣṭham
c saṃvarto māṃ yājayitādya rājan
na te vākyaṃ tasya vā rocayāmi
 gandharva uvāca
a ghoro nādaḥ śrūyate vāsavasya
nabhastale garjato rājasiṃha
c vyaktaṃ vajraṃ mokṣyate te mahendraḥ
kṣemaṃ rājaṃś cintyatām eṣa kālaḥ
 vyāsa uvāca
a ity evam ukto dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa rājā
śrutvā nādaṃ nadato vāsavasya
c taponityaṃ dharmavidāṃ variṣṭhaṃ
saṃvartaṃ taṃ jñāpayām āsa kāryam
 marutta uvāca
a imam aśmānaṃ plavamānam ārād
adhvā dūraṃ tena na dṛśyate 'dya
c prapadye 'haṃ śarma viprendra tvattaḥ
prayaccha tasmād abhayaṃ vipramukhya
a ayam āyāti vai vajrī diśo vidyotayan daśa
c amānuṣeṇa ghoreṇa sadasyās trāsitā hi naḥ
 saṃvarta uvāca
a bhayaṃ śakrād vyetu te rājasiṃha
praṇotsye 'haṃ bhayam etat sughoram
c saṃstambhinyā vidyayā kṣipram eva
mā bhais tvam asmād bhava cāpi pratītaḥ
a ahaṃ saṃstambhayiṣyāmi mā bhais tvaṃ śakrato nṛpa
c sarveṣām eva devānāṃ kṣapitāny āyudhāni me
a diśo vajraṃ vrajatāṃ vāyur etu
varṣaṃ bhūtvā nipatatu kānaneṣu
c āpaḥ plavantv antarikṣe vṛthā ca
saudāminī dṛśyatāṃ mā bibhas tvam
a atho vahnis trātu vā sarvatas te
kāmaṃ varṣaṃ varṣatu vāsavo vā
c vajraṃ tathā sthāpayatāṃ ca vāyur
mahāghoraṃ plavamānaṃ jalaughaiḥ
 marutta uvāca
a ghoraḥ śabdaḥ śrūyate vai mahāsvano
vajrasyaiṣa sahito mārutena
c ātmā hi me pravyathate muhur muhur
na me svāsthyaṃ jāyate cādya vipra
 saṃvarta uvāca
a vajrād ugrād vyetu bhayaṃ tavādya
vāto bhūtvā hanmi narendra vajram
c bhayaṃ tyaktvā varam anyaṃ vṛṇīṣva
kaṃ te kāmaṃ tapasā sādhayāmi
 marutta uvāca
a indraḥ sākṣāt sahasābhyetu vipra
havir yajñe pratigṛhṇātu caiva
c svaṃ svaṃ dhiṣṇyaṃ caiva juṣantu devāḥ
sutaṃ somaṃ pratigṛhṇantu caiva
 saṃvarta uvāca
a ayam indro haribhir āyāti rājan
devaiḥ sarvaiḥ sahitaḥ somapīthī
c mantrāhūto yajñam imaṃ mayādya
paśyasvainaṃ mantravisrastakāyam
 vyāsa uvāca
a tato devaiḥ sahito devarājo
rathe yuktvā tān harīn vājimukhyān
c āyād yajñam adhi rājñaḥ pipāsur
āvikṣitasyāprameyasya somam
a tam āyāntaṃ sahitaṃ devasaṃghaiḥ
pratyudyayau sapurodhā maruttaḥ
c cakre pūjāṃ devarājāya cāgryāṃ
yathāśāstraṃ vidhivat prīyamāṇaḥ
 saṃvarta uvāca
a svāgataṃ te puruhūteha vidvan
yajño 'dyāyaṃ saṃnihite tvayīndra
c śośubhyate balavṛtraghna bhūyaḥ
pibasva somaṃ sutam udyataṃ mayā
 marutta uvāca
a śivena māṃ paśya namaś ca te 'stu
prāpto yajñaḥ saphalaṃ jīvitaṃ me
c ayaṃ yajñaṃ kurute me surendra
bṛhaspater avaro janmanā yaḥ
 indra uvāca
a jānāmi te gurum enaṃ tapodhanaṃ
bṛhaspater anujaṃ tigmatejasam
c yasyāhvānād āgato 'haṃ narendra
prītir me 'dya tvayi manuḥ pranaṣṭaḥ
 saṃvarta uvāca
a yadi prītas tvam asi vai devarāja
tasmāt svayaṃ śādhi yajñe vidhānam
c svayaṃ sarvān kuru mārgān surendra
jānātv ayaṃ sarvalokaś ca deva
 vyāsa uvāca
a evam uktas tv āṅgirasena śakraḥ
samādideśa svayam eva devān
c sabhāḥ kriyantām āvasathāś ca mukhyāḥ
sahasraśaś citrabhaumāḥ samṛddhāḥ
a kḷptasthūṇāḥ kurutārohaṇāni
gandharvāṇām apsarasāṃ ca śīghram
c yeṣu nṛtyerann apsarasaḥ sahasraśaḥ
svargoddeśaḥ kriyatāṃ yajñavāṭaḥ
a ity uktās te cakrur āśu pratītā
divaukasaḥ śakravākyān narendra
c tato vākyaṃ prāha rājānam indraḥ
prīto rājan pūjayāno maruttam
a eṣa tvayāham iha rājan sametya
ye cāpy anye tava pūrve narendrāḥ
c sarvāś cānyā devatāḥ prīyamāṇā
havis tubhyaṃ pratigṛhṇantu rājan
a āgneyaṃ vai lohitam ālabhantāṃ
vaiśvadevaṃ bahurūpaṃ virājan
c nīlaṃ cokṣāṇaṃ medhyam abhyālabhantāṃ
calac chiśnaṃ matpradiṣṭaṃ dvijendrāḥ
a tato yajño vavṛdhe tasya rājño
yatra devāḥ svayam annāni jahruḥ
c yasmiñ śakro brāhmaṇaiḥ pūjyamānaḥ
sadasyo 'bhūd dharimān devarājaḥ
a tataḥ saṃvartaś cityagato mahātmā
yathā vahniḥ prajvalito dvitīyaḥ
c havīṃṣy uccair āhvayan devasaṃghāñ
juhāvāgnau mantravat supratītaḥ
a tataḥ pītvā balabhit somam agryaṃ
ye cāpy anye somapā vai divaukasaḥ
c sarve 'nujñātāḥ prayayuḥ pārthivena
yathājoṣaṃ tarpitāḥ prītimantaḥ
a tato rājā jātarūpasya rāśīn
pade pade kārayām āsa hṛṣṭaḥ
c dvijātibhyo visṛjan bhūri vittaṃ
rarāja vitteśa ivārihantā
a tato vittaṃ vividhaṃ saṃnidhāya
yathotsāhaṃ kārayitvā ca kośam
c anujñāto guruṇā saṃnivṛtya
śaśāsa gām akhilāṃ sāgarāntām
a evaṃguṇaḥ saṃbabhūveha rājā
yasya kratau tat suvarṇaṃ prabhūtam
c tat tvaṃ samādāya narendra vittaṃ
yajasva devāṃs tarpayāno vidhānaiḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tato rājā pāṇḍavo hṛṣṭarūpaḥ
śrutvā vākyaṃ satyavatyāḥ sutasya
c manaś cakre tena vittena yaṣṭuṃ
tato 'mātyair mantrayām āsa bhūyaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a ity ukte nṛpatau tasmin vyāsenādbhutakarmaṇā
c vāsudevo mahātejās tato vacanam ādade
a taṃ nṛpaṃ dīnamanasaṃ nihatajñātibāndhavam
c upaplutam ivādityaṃ sadhūmam iva pāvakam
a nirviṇṇamanasaṃ pārthaṃ jñātvā vṛṣṇikulodvahaḥ
c āśvāsayan dharmasutaṃ pravaktum upacakrame
 vāsudeva uvāca
a sarvaṃ jihmaṃ mṛtyupadam ārjavaṃ brahmaṇaḥ padam
c etāvāñ jñānaviṣayaḥ kiṃ pralāpaḥ kariṣyati
a naiva te niṣṭhitaṃ karma naiva te śatravo jitāḥ
c kathaṃ śatruṃ śarīrastham ātmānaṃ nāvabudhyase
a atra te vartayiṣyāmi yathādharmaṃ yathāśrutam
c indrasya saha vṛtreṇa yathā yuddham avartata
a vṛtreṇa pṛthivī vyāptā purā kila narādhipa
c dṛṣṭvā sa pṛthivīṃ vyāptāṃ gandhasya viṣaye hṛte
e dharāharaṇadurgandho viṣayaḥ samapadyata
a śatakratuś cukopātha gandhasya viṣaye hṛte
c vṛtrasya sa tataḥ kruddho vajraṃ ghoram avāsṛjat
a sa vadhyamāno vajreṇa pṛthivyāṃ bhūritejasā
c viveśa sahasaivāpo jagrāha viṣayaṃ tataḥ
a vyāptāsv athāpsu vṛtreṇa rase ca viṣaye hṛte
c śatakratur abhikruddhas tāsu vajram avāsṛjat
a sa vadhyamāno vajreṇa salile bhūritejasā
c viveśa sahasā jyotir jagrāha viṣayaṃ tataḥ
a vyāpte jyotiṣi vṛtreṇa rūpe 'tha viṣaye hṛte
c śatakratur abhikruddhas tatra vajram avāsṛjat
a sa vadhyamāno vajreṇa subhṛśaṃ bhūritejasā
c viveśa sahasā vāyuṃ jagrāha viṣayaṃ tataḥ
a vyāpte vāyau tu vṛtreṇa sparśe 'tha viṣaye hṛte
c śatakratur abhikruddhas tatra vajram avāsṛjat
a sa vadhyamāno vajreṇa tasminn amitatejasā
c ākāśam abhidudrāva jagrāha viṣayaṃ tataḥ
a ākāśe vṛtrabhūte ca śabde ca viṣaye hṛte
c śatakratur abhikruddhas tatra vajram avāsṛjat
a sa vadhyamāno vajreṇa tasminn amitatejasā
c viveśa sahasā śakraṃ jagrāha viṣayaṃ tataḥ
a tasya vṛtragṛhītasya mohaḥ samabhavan mahān
c rathaṃtareṇa taṃ tāta vasiṣṭhaḥ pratyabodhayat
a tato vṛtraṃ śarīrasthaṃ jaghāna bharatarṣabha
c śatakratur adṛśyena vajreṇetīha naḥ śrutam
a idaṃ dharmarahasyaṃ ca śakreṇoktaṃ maharṣiṣu
c ṛṣibhiś ca mama proktaṃ tan nibodha narādhipa
 vāsudeva uvāca
a dvividho jāyate vyādhiḥ śārīro mānasas tathā
c parasparaṃ tayor janma nirdvaṃdvaṃ nopalabhyate
a śarīre jāyate vyādhiḥ śārīro nātra saṃśayaḥ
c mānaso jāyate vyādhir manasy eveti niścayaḥ
a śītoṣṇe caiva vāyuś ca guṇā rājañ śarīrajāḥ
c teṣāṃ guṇānāṃ sāmyaṃ cet tad āhuḥ svasthalakṣaṇam
e uṣṇena bādhyate śītaṃ śītenoṣṇaṃ ca bādhyate
f ubhābhyāṃ badhyate vāyur vidhānam idam ucyate
a sattvaṃ rajas tamaś ceti trayas tv ātmaguṇāḥ smṛtāḥ
c teṣāṃ guṇānāṃ sāmyaṃ cet tad āhuḥ svasthalakṣaṇam
e teṣām anyatamotseke vidhānam upadiśyate
a harṣeṇa bādhyate śoko harṣaḥ śokena bādhyate
b ubhābhyāṃ vadhyate moho vidhānam idam ucyate
c kaś cid duḥkhe vartamānaḥ sukhasya smartum icchati
e kaś cit sukhe vartamāno duḥkhasya smartum icchati
a sa tvaṃ na duḥkhī duḥkhasya na sukhī susukhasya vā
c smartum icchasi kaunteya diṣṭaṃ hi balavattaram
a atha vā te svabhāvo 'yaṃ yena pārthāvakṛṣyase
c dṛṣṭvā sabhāgatāṃ kṛṣṇām ekavastrāṃ rajasvalām
e miṣatāṃ pāṇḍaveyānāṃ na tat saṃsmartum icchasi
a pravrājanaṃ ca nagarād ajinaiś ca vivāsanam
c mahāraṇyanivāsaś ca na tasya smartum icchasi
a jaṭāsurāt parikleśaś citrasenena cāhavaḥ
c saindhavāc ca parikleśo na tasya smartum icchasi
a punar ajñātacaryāyāṃ kīcakena padā vadhaḥ
c yājñasenyās tadā pārtha na tasya smartum icchasi
a yac ca te droṇabhīṣmābhyāṃ yuddham āsīd ariṃdama
c manasaikena yoddhavyaṃ tat te yuddham upasthitam
e tasmād abhyupagantavyaṃ yuddhāya bharatarṣabha
a param avyaktarūpasya paraṃ muktvā svakarmabhiḥ
c yatra naiva śaraiḥ kāryaṃ na bhṛtyair na ca bandhubhiḥ
e ātmanaikena yoddhavyaṃ tat te yuddham upasthitam
a tasminn anirjite yuddhe kām avasthāṃ gamiṣyasi
c etaj jñātvā tu kaunteya kṛtakṛtyo bhaviṣyasi
a etāṃ buddhiṃ viniścitya bhūtānām āgatiṃ gatim
c pitṛpaitāmahe vṛtte śādhi rājyaṃ yathocitam
 vāsudeva uvāca
a na bāhyaṃ dravyam utsṛjya siddhir bhavati bhārata
c śārīraṃ dravyam utsṛjya siddhir bhavati vā na vā
a bāhyadravyavimuktasya śārīreṣu ca gṛdhyataḥ
c yo dharmo yat sukhaṃ caiva dviṣatām astu tat tathā
a dvyakṣaras tu bhaven mṛtyus tryakṣaraṃ brahma śāśvatam
c mameti dvyakṣaro mṛtyur na mameti ca śāśvatam
a brahma mṛtyuś ca tau rājann ātmany eva vyavasthitau
c adṛśyamānau bhūtāni yodhayetām asaṃśayam
a avināśo 'sya sattvasya niyato yadi bhārata
c bhittvā śarīraṃ bhūtānām ahiṃsāṃ pratipadyate
a labdhvāpi pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ sahasthāvarajaṅgamām
c mamatvaṃ yasya naiva syāt kiṃ tayā sa kariṣyati
a atha vā vasataḥ pārtha vane vanyena jīvataḥ
c mamatā yasya dravyeṣu mṛtyor āsye sa vartate
a bāhyāntarāṇāṃ śatrūṇāṃ svabhāvaṃ paśya bhārata
c yan na paśyati tad bhūtaṃ mucyate sa mahābhayāt
a kāmātmānaṃ na praśaṃsanti loke
na cākāmāt kā cid asti pravṛttiḥ
b sarve kāmā manaso 'ṅgāt prasūtā
b yān paṇḍitaḥ saṃharate vicintya
b bhūyo bhūyo janmano 'bhyāsayogād
b yogī yogaṃ sāramārgaṃ vicintya
c dānaṃ hi vedādhyayanaṃ tapaś ca
kāmena karmāṇi ca vaidikāni
a vrataṃ yajñān niyamān dhyānayogān
kāmena yo nārabhate viditvā
c yad yad dhy ayaṃ kāmayate sa dharmo
na yo dharmo niyamas tasya mūlam
a atra gāthāḥ kāmagītāḥ kīrtayanti purāvidaḥ
c śṛṇu saṃkīrtyamānās tā nikhilena yudhiṣṭhira
a nāhaṃ śakyo 'nupāyena hantuṃ bhūtena kena cit
c yo māṃ prayatate hantuṃ jñātvā praharaṇe balam
e tasya tasmin praharaṇe punaḥ prādurbhavāmy aham
a yo māṃ prayatate hantuṃ yajñair vividhadakṣiṇaiḥ
c jaṅgameṣv iva karmātmā punaḥ prādurbhavāmy aham
a yo māṃ prayatate hantuṃ vedair vedāntasādhanaiḥ
c sthāvareṣv iva śāntātmā tasya prādurbhavāmy aham
a yo māṃ prayatate hantuṃ dhṛtyā satyaparākramaḥ
c bhāvo bhavāmi tasyāhaṃ sa ca māṃ nāvabudhyate
a yo māṃ prayatate hantuṃ tapasā saṃśitavrataḥ
c tatas tapasi tasyātha punaḥ prādurbhavāmy aham
a yo māṃ prayatate hantuṃ mokṣam āsthāya paṇḍitaḥ
c tasya mokṣaratisthasya nṛtyāmi ca hasāmi ca
e avadhyaḥ sarvabhūtānām aham ekaḥ sanātanaḥ
a tasmāt tvam api taṃ kāmaṃ yajñair vividhadakṣiṇaiḥ
c dharmaṃ kuru mahārāja tatra te sa bhaviṣyati
a yajasva vājimedhena vidhivad dakṣiṇāvatā
c anyaiś ca vividhair yajñaiḥ samṛddhair āptadakṣiṇaiḥ
a mā te vyathāstu nihatān bandhūn vīkṣya punaḥ punaḥ
c na śakyās te punar draṣṭuṃ ye hatāsmin raṇājire
a sa tvam iṣṭvā mahāyajñaiḥ samṛddhair āptadakṣiṇaiḥ
c loke kīrtiṃ parāṃ prāpya gatim agryāṃ gamiṣyasi
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evaṃ bahuvidhair vākyair munibhis tais tapodhanaiḥ
c samāśvasyata rājarṣir hatabandhur yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a so 'nunīto bhagavatā viṣṭaraśravasā svayam
c dvaipāyanena kṛṣṇena devasthānena cābhibhūḥ
a nāradenātha bhīmena nakulena ca pārthivaḥ
c kṛṣṇayā sahadevena vijayena ca dhīmatā
a anyaiś ca puruṣavyāghrair brāhmaṇaiḥ śāstradṛṣṭibhiḥ
c vyajahāc chokajaṃ duḥkhaṃ saṃtāpaṃ caiva mānasam
a arcayām āsa devāṃś ca brāhmaṇāṃś ca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c kṛtvātha pretakāryāṇi bandhūnāṃ sa punar nṛpaḥ
e anvaśāsata dharmātmā pṛthivīṃ sāgarāmbarām
a praśāntacetāḥ kauravyaḥ svarājyaṃ prāpya kevalam
c vyāsaṃ ca nāradaṃ caiva tāṃś cānyān abravīn nṛpaḥ
a āśvāsito 'haṃ prāg vṛddhair bhavadbhir munipuṃgavaiḥ
c na sūkṣmam api me kiṃ cid vyalīkam iha vidyate
a arthaś ca sumahān prāpto yena yakṣyāmi devatāḥ
c puraskṛtyeha bhavataḥ samāneṣyāmahe makham
a himavantaṃ tvayā guptā gamiṣyāmaḥ pitāmaha
b tathā vidhatsva viprarṣe tvayyāyattaḥ sa me kratuḥ
c bahvāścaryo hi deśaḥ sa śrūyate dvijasattama
a tathā bhagavatā citraṃ kalyāṇaṃ bahu bhāṣitam
c devarṣiṇā nāradena devasthānena caiva ha
a nābhāgadheyaḥ puruṣaḥ kaś cid evaṃvidhān gurūn
c labhate vyasanaṃ prāpya suhṛdaḥ sādhusaṃmatān
a evam uktās tu te rājñā sarva eva maharṣayaḥ
c abhyanujñāpya rājānaṃ tathobhau kṛṣṇaphalgunau
e paśyatām eva sarveṣāṃ tatraivādarśanaṃ yayuḥ
a tato dharmasuto rājā tatraivopāviśat prabhuḥ
c evaṃ nātimahān kālaḥ sa teṣām abhyavartata
a kurvatāṃ śaucakarmāṇi bhīṣmasya nidhane tadā
c mahādānāni viprebhyo dadatām aurdhvadaihikam
a bhīṣmakarṇapurogāṇāṃ kurūṇāṃ kurunandana
c sahito dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa pradadāv aurdhvadaihikam
a tato dattvā bahu dhanaṃ viprebhyaḥ pāṇḍavarṣabhaḥ
c dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ puraskṛtya viveśa gajasāhvayam
a sa samāśvāsya pitaraṃ prajñācakṣuṣam īśvaram
c anvaśād vai sa dharmātmā pṛthivīṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha
d yathā manur mahārāja rāmo dāśarathir yathā
d tathā bharatasiṃho 'pi pālayām āsa medinīm
d nādharmyam abhavat tatra sarvo dharmarucir janaḥ
d babhūva naraśārdūla yathā kṛtayugaṃ yugam
d kalim āsannam āviṣṭaṃ nivārya nṛpanandanaḥ
d bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito dhīmān babhau dharmabaloddhṛtaḥ
d vavarṣa bhagavān devaḥ kāle deśe yathepsitam
d nirāmayaṃ jagad abhūt kṣutpipāse na kiṃ cana
d ādhir nāsti manuṣyāṇāṃ vyasane nābhavan matiḥ
d brāhmaṇapramukhā varṇās te svadharmottarāḥ śivāḥ
d dharmaḥ satyapradhānaś ca satyaṃ sadviṣayānvitam
d dharmāsanasthaḥ sadbhiḥ sa strībālāturavṛddhakān
d varṇakramāt pūrvakṛtān nākālo rakṣaṇodyataḥ
d suvṛttivṛttidānādyair yajñārthair dāpitair api
d āmuṣmikaṃ bhayaṃ nāsti aihikaṃ kṛtam eva tu
d svargalokopamo lokas tadā tasmin praśāsati
d babhūva sukham evātra tad viśiṣṭataraṃ param
d nāryaḥ pativratāḥ sarvā rūpavatyaḥ svalaṃkṛtāḥ
d yathoktavṛttāḥ svaguṇair babhūvuḥ prītihetavaḥ
d pumāṃsaḥ puṇyaśīlāḍhyāḥ svaṃ svaṃ dharmam anuvratāḥ
d sukhinaḥ sūkṣmam apy eno nākurvanta kadā cana
d sarve narāś ca nāryaś ca satataṃ priyavādinaḥ
d ajihmamanasaḥ śuklā babhūvuḥ śramavarjitāḥ
d bhūṣitāḥ kuṇḍalair hāraiḥ kaṭakaiḥ kaṭisūtrakaiḥ
d suvāsasaḥ sugandhāḍhyāḥ prāyaśaḥ pṛthivītale
d sarve brahmavidaḥ śāntāḥ sarvatra pariniṣṭhitāḥ
d valīpalitahīnās tu sukhino dīrghadarśinaḥ
d icchā na jāyate 'nyatra varṇeṣu ca na saṃkaraḥ
d manuṣyāṇāṃ mahārāja maryādāsu vyavasthitāḥ
d tasmiñ śāsati rājendra mṛgavyālasarīsṛpāḥ
d anyonyam api cānyeṣu na bādhante vayāṃsi ca
d gāvaś ca guṇabhūyiṣṭhāḥ suvāladhimukhodarāḥ
d apīḍitāḥ karṣaṇādyair hṛtavyādhitavatsarāḥ
d avadhyakālā manujāḥ puruṣārtheṣu ca kramāt
d viṣayeṣv aniṣiddheṣu vedaśāstreṣu codyatāḥ
d suvṛttā vṛṣabhāḥ puṣṭā bhārasāhāḥ sukhodayāḥ
d atīva madhuraḥ śabdaḥ sparśaś cātisukho rasaḥ
d rūpaṃ dṛṣṭikṣamaṃ ramyaṃ manojñaṃ gandham udbabhau
d dharmārthakāmasaṃyuktaṃ mokṣābhyudayasādhanam
d prahlādajananaṃ puṇyaṃ saṃbabhūvātha mānasam
d sthāvarā bahupuṣpāḍhyāḥ phalacchāyāvahās tathā
d susparśā viṣahīnāś ca supatratvakprarohiṇaḥ
d manonukūlāḥ sarveṣāṃ ceṣṭā bhūtvāpavarjitāḥ
d tathāvidho 'pi rājarṣis tad vṛttam abhavad bhuvi
d sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannāḥ pāṇḍavā dharmacāriṇaḥ
d jyeṣṭhānuvartinaḥ sarve babhūvuḥ priyadarśanāḥ
d siṃhoraskā jitakrodhās tejobalasamanvitāḥ
d ājānubāhavaḥ sarve dānaśīlā jitendriyāḥ
d teṣu śāsatsu pṛthivīm ṛtavaḥ svaguṇair babhuḥ
d sukhodayāya vartante grahās tārāgaṇaiḥ saha
d mahī sasyaprabahulā sarvaratnaguṇodayā
d kāmadhug dhenuvad bhogān phalati sma sahasradhā
d manvādibhiḥ kṛtāḥ pūrvaṃ maryādā mānaveṣu yāḥ
d anatikramya tāḥ sarvāḥ kuleṣu samayāni ca
d anvaśāsanta te nityaṃ dharmaputrapriyaṃkarāḥ
d mahākulāni dharmiṣṭhā vardhayanto viśeṣataḥ
d manupraṇītayā vṛttyā te 'nvaśāsan vasuṃdharām
d rājavṛttir hi sā śaśvad dharmiṣṭhābhūn mahītale
d prāyo lokamatis tāta rājavṛttānugāminī
d evaṃ bhāratavarṣaṃ svaṃ rājā svargaṃ surendravat
d śaśāsa viṣṇunā sārdhaṃ gupto gāṇḍīvadhanvanā
 janamejaya uvāca
a vijite pāṇḍaveyais tu praśānte ca dvijottama
c rāṣṭre kiṃ cakratur vīrau vāsudevadhanaṃjayau
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a vijite pāṇḍaveyais tu praśānte ca viśāṃ pate
c rāṣṭre babhūvatur hṛṣṭau vāsudevadhanaṃjayau
a vijahrāte mudā yuktau divi deveśvarāv iva
c tau vaneṣu vicitreṣu parvatānāṃ ca sānuṣu
a śaileṣu ramaṇīyeṣu palvaleṣu nadīṣu ca
c caṅkramyamāṇau saṃhṛṣṭāv aśvināv iva nandane
a indraprasthe mahātmānau remāte kṛṣṇapāṇḍavau
c praviśya tāṃ sabhāṃ ramyāṃ vijahrāte ca bhārata
a tatra yuddhakathāś citrāḥ parikleśāṃś ca pārthiva
c kathāyoge kathāyoge kathayām āsatus tadā
d kathayām āsa yogena kathayām anupūrvaśaḥ sic
a ṛṣīṇāṃ devatānāṃ ca vaṃśāṃs tāv āhatus tadā
c prīyamāṇau mahātmānau purāṇāv ṛṣisattamau
a madhurās tu kathāś citrāś citrārthapadaniścayāḥ
c niścayajñaḥ sa pārthāya kathayām āsa keśavaḥ
a putraśokābhisaṃtaptaṃ jñātīnāṃ ca sahasraśaḥ
c kathābhiḥ śamayām āsa pārthaṃ śaurir janārdanaḥ
a sa tam āśvāsya vidhivad vidhānajño mahātapāḥ
c apahṛtyātmano bhāraṃ viśaśrāmeva sātvataḥ
a tataḥ kathānte govindo guḍākeśam uvāca ha
c sāntvayañ ślakṣṇayā vācā hetuyuktam idaṃ vacaḥ
a vijiteyaṃ dharā kṛtsnā savyasācin paraṃtapa
c tvadbāhubalam āśritya rājñā dharmasutena ha
a asapatnāṃ mahīṃ bhuṅkte dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c bhīmasenaprabhāvena yamayoś ca narottama
a dharmeṇa rājñā dharmajña prāptaṃ rājyam akaṇṭakam
c dharmeṇa nihataḥ saṃkhye sa ca rājā suyodhanaḥ
a adharmarucayo lubdhāḥ sadā cāpriyavādinaḥ
c dhārtarāṣṭrā durātmānaḥ sānubandhā nipātitāḥ
a praśāntām akhilāṃ pārtha pṛthivīṃ pṛthivīpatiḥ
c bhuṅkte dharmasuto rājā tvayā guptaḥ kurūdvaha
a rame cāhaṃ tvayā sārdham araṇyeṣv api pāṇḍava
c kim u yatra jano 'yaṃ vai pṛthā cāmitrakarśana
a yatra dharmasuto rājā yatra bhīmo mahābalaḥ
c yatra mādravatīputrau ratis tatra parā mama
a tathaiva svargakalpeṣu sabhoddeśeṣu bhārata
c ramaṇīyeṣu puṇyeṣu sahitasya tvayānagha
a kālo mahāṃs tv atīto me śūraputram apaśyataḥ
c baladevaṃ ca kauravya tathānyān vṛṣṇipuṃgavān
a so 'haṃ gantum abhīpsāmi purīṃ dvāravatīṃ prati
c rocatāṃ gamanaṃ mahyaṃ tavāpi puruṣarṣabha
a ukto bahuvidhaṃ rājā tatra tatra yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c sa ha bhīṣmeṇa yady uktam asmābhiḥ śokakārite
a śiṣṭo yudhiṣṭhiro 'smābhiḥ śāstā sann api pāṇḍavaḥ
c tena tac ca vacaḥ samyag gṛhītaṃ sumahātmanā
a dharmaputre hi dharmajñe kṛtajñe satyavādini
c satyaṃ dharmo matiś cāgryā sthitiś ca satataṃ sthirā
a tad gatvā taṃ mahātmānaṃ yadi te rocate 'rjuna
c asmadgamanasaṃyuktaṃ vaco brūhi janādhipam
a na hi tasyāpriyaṃ kuryāṃ prāṇatyāge 'py upasthite
c kuto gantuṃ mahābāho purīṃ dvāravatīṃ prati
a sarvaṃ tv idam ahaṃ pārtha tvatprītihitakāmyayā
c bravīmi satyaṃ kauravya na mithyaitat kathaṃ cana
a prayojanaṃ ca nirvṛttam iha vāse mamārjuna
c dhārtarāṣṭro hato rājā sabalaḥ sapadānugaḥ
a pṛthivī ca vaśe tāta dharmaputrasya dhīmataḥ
c sthitā samudravasanā saśailavanakānanā
e citā ratnair bahuvidhaiḥ kururājasya pāṇḍava
a dharmeṇa rājā dharmajñaḥ pātu sarvāṃ vasuṃdharām
c upāsyamāno bahubhiḥ siddhaiś cāpi mahātmabhiḥ
e stūyamānaś ca satataṃ bandibhir bharatarṣabha
a tan mayā saha gatvādya rājānaṃ kuruvardhanam
c āpṛccha kuruśārdūla gamanaṃ dvārakāṃ prati
a idaṃ śarīraṃ vasu yac ca me gṛhe
niveditaṃ pārtha sadā yudhiṣṭhire
c priyaś ca mānyaś ca hi me yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
sadā kurūṇām adhipo mahāmatiḥ
a prayojanaṃ cāpi nivāsakāraṇe
na vidyate me tvad ṛte mahābhuja
c sthitā hi pṛthvī tava pārtha śāsane
guroḥ suvṛttasya yudhiṣṭhirasya ha
a itīdam uktaṃ sa tadā mahātmanā
janārdanenāmitavikramo 'rjunaḥ
c tatheti kṛcchrād iva vācam īrayaj
janārdanaṃ saṃpratipūjya pārthiva
 janamejaya uvāca
a sabhāyāṃ vasatos tasyāṃ nihatyārīn mahātmanoḥ
c keśavārjunayoḥ kā nu kathā samabhavad dvija
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a kṛṣṇena sahitaḥ pārthaḥ svarājyaṃ prāpya kevalam
c tasyāṃ sabhāyāṃ ramyāyāṃ vijahāra mudā yutaḥ
a tataḥ kaṃ cit sabhoddeśaṃ svargoddeśasamaṃ nṛpa
c yadṛcchayā tau muditau jagmatuḥ svajanāvṛtau
a tataḥ pratītaḥ kṛṣṇena sahitaḥ pāṇḍavo 'rjunaḥ
c nirīkṣya tāṃ sabhāṃ ramyām idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a viditaṃ te mahābāho saṃgrāme samupasthite
c māhātmyaṃ devakīmātas tac ca te rūpam aiśvaram
a yat tu tad bhavatā proktaṃ tadā keśava sauhṛdāt
c tat sarvaṃ puruṣavyāghra naṣṭaṃ me naṣṭacetasaḥ
a mama kautūhalaṃ tv asti teṣv artheṣu punaḥ prabho
c bhavāṃś ca dvārakāṃ gantā nacirād iva mādhava
a evam uktas tataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ phalgunaṃ pratyabhāṣata
c pariṣvajya mahātejā vacanaṃ vadatāṃ varaḥ
a śrāvitas tvaṃ mayā guhyaṃ jñāpitaś ca sanātanam
c dharmaṃ svarūpiṇaṃ pārtha sarvalokāṃś ca śāśvatān
a abuddhvā yan na gṛhṇīthās tan me sumahad apriyam
b na ca sādya punar bhūyaḥ smṛtir me saṃbhaviṣyati
c nūnam aśraddadhāno 'si durmedhāś cāsi pāṇḍava
d na ca śakyaḥ punar vaktum aśeṣeṇa dhanaṃjaya
a sa hi dharmaḥ suparyāpto brahmaṇaḥ padavedane
c na śakyaṃ tan mayā bhūyas tathā vaktum aśeṣataḥ
a paraṃ hi brahma kathitaṃ yogayuktena tan mayā
c itihāsaṃ tu vakṣyāmi tasminn arthe purātanam
a yathā tāṃ buddhim āsthāya gatim agryāṃ gamiṣyasi
c śṛṇu dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭha gadataḥ sarvam eva me
a āgacchad brāhmaṇaḥ kaś cit svargalokād ariṃdama
c brahmalokāc ca durdharṣaḥ so 'smābhiḥ pūjito 'bhavat
d paripṛṣṭaś ca sa tadā yad āha dvijasattamaḥ
a asmābhiḥ paripṛṣṭaś ca yad āha bharatarṣabha
c divyena vidhinā pārtha tac chṛṇuṣvāvicārayan
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a mokṣadharmaṃ samāśritya kṛṣṇa yan mānupṛcchasi
c bhūtānām anukampārthaṃ yan mohacchedanaṃ prabho
a tat te 'haṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi yathāvan madhusūdana
c śṛṇuṣvāvahito bhūtvā gadato mama mādhava
a kaś cid vipras tapoyuktaḥ kāśyapo dharmavittamaḥ
c āsasāda dvijaṃ kaṃ cid dharmāṇām āgatāgamam
a gatāgate subahuśo jñānavijñānapāragam
c lokatattvārthakuśalaṃ jñātāraṃ sukhaduḥkhayoḥ
a jātīmaraṇatattvajñaṃ kovidaṃ puṇyapāpayoḥ
c draṣṭāram uccanīcānāṃ karmabhir dehināṃ gatim
a carantaṃ muktavat siddhaṃ praśāntaṃ saṃyatendriyam
c dīpyamānaṃ śriyā brāhmyā kramamāṇaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
a antardhānagatijñaṃ ca śrutvā tattvena kāśyapaḥ
c tathaivāntarhitaiḥ siddhair yāntaṃ cakradharaiḥ saha
a saṃbhāṣamāṇam ekānte samāsīnaṃ ca taiḥ saha
c yadṛcchayā ca gacchantam asaktaṃ pavanaṃ yathā
a taṃ samāsādya medhāvī sa tadā dvijasattamaḥ
c caraṇau dharmakāmo vai tapasvī susamāhitaḥ
e pratipede yathānyāyaṃ bhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ
a vismitaś cādbhutaṃ dṛṣṭvā kāśyapas taṃ dvijottamam
c paricāreṇa mahatā guruṃ vaidyam atoṣayat
a prītātmā copapannaś ca śrutacāritrasaṃyutaḥ
c bhāvena toṣayac cainaṃ guruvṛttyā paraṃtapaḥ
a tasmai tuṣṭaḥ sa śiṣyāya prasanno 'thābravīd guruḥ
c siddhiṃ parām abhiprekṣya śṛṇu tan me janārdana
a vividhaiḥ karmabhis tāta puṇyayogaiś ca kevalaiḥ
c gacchantīha gatiṃ martyā devaloke 'pi ca sthitim
a na kva cit sukham atyantaṃ na kva cic chāśvatī sthitiḥ
c sthānāc ca mahato bhraṃśo duḥkhalabdhāt punaḥ punaḥ
a aśubhā gatayaḥ prāptāḥ kaṣṭā me pāpasevanāt
c kāmamanyuparītena tṛṣṇayā mohitena ca
a punaḥ punaś ca maraṇaṃ janma caiva punaḥ punaḥ
c āhārā vividhā bhuktāḥ pītā nānāvidhāḥ stanāḥ
a mātaro vividhā dṛṣṭāḥ pitaraś ca pṛthagvidhāḥ
c sukhāni ca vicitrāṇi duḥkhāni ca mayānagha
a priyair vivāso bahuśaḥ saṃvāsaś cāpriyaiḥ saha
c dhananāśaś ca saṃprāpto labdhvā duḥkhena tad dhanam
a avamānāḥ sukaṣṭāś ca parataḥ svajanāt tathā
c śārīrā mānasāś cāpi vedanā bhṛśadāruṇāḥ
a prāptā vimānanāś cogrā vadhabandhāś ca dāruṇāḥ
c patanaṃ niraye caiva yātanāś ca yamakṣaye
a jarā rogāś ca satataṃ vāsanāni ca bhūriśaḥ
c loke 'sminn anubhūtāni dvaṃdvajāni bhṛśaṃ mayā
a tataḥ kadā cin nirvedān nikārān nikṛtena ca
c lokatantraṃ parityaktaṃ duḥkhārtena bhṛśaṃ mayā
d loke 'sminn anubhūyāham imaṃ mārgam anuṣṭhitaḥ
e tataḥ siddhir iyaṃ prāptā prasādād ātmano mayā
a nāhaṃ punar ihāgantā lokān ālokayāmy aham
c ā siddher ā prajāsargād ātmano me gatiḥ śubhā
a upalabdhā dvijaśreṣṭha tatheyaṃ siddhir uttamā
c itaḥ paraṃ gamiṣyāmi tataḥ parataraṃ punaḥ
e brahmaṇaḥ padam avyagraṃ mā te bhūd atra saṃśayaḥ
a nāhaṃ punar ihāgantā martyalokaṃ paraṃtapa
c prīto 'smi te mahāprājña brūhi kiṃ karavāṇi te
a yadīpsur upapannas tvaṃ tasya kālo 'yam āgataḥ
c abhijāne ca tad ahaṃ yadarthaṃ mā tvam āgataḥ
e acirāt tu gamiṣyāmi yenāhaṃ tvām acūcudam
a bhṛśaṃ prīto 'smi bhavataś cāritreṇa vicakṣaṇa
c paripṛccha yāvad bhavate bhāṣeyaṃ yat tavepsitam
a bahu manye ca te buddhiṃ bhṛśaṃ saṃpūjayāmi ca
c yenāhaṃ bhavatā buddho medhāvī hy asi kāśyapa
 vāsudeva uvāca
a tatas tasyopasaṃgṛhya pādau praśnān sudurvacān
c papraccha tāṃś ca sarvān sa prāha dharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
 kāśyapa uvāca
a kathaṃ śarīraṃ cyavate kathaṃ caivopapadyate
c kathaṃ kaṣṭāc ca saṃsārāt saṃsaran parimucyate
a ātmānaṃ vā kathaṃ yuktvā tac charīraṃ vimuñcati
c śarīrataś ca nirmuktaḥ katham anyat prapadyate
a kathaṃ śubhāśubhe cāyaṃ karmaṇī svakṛte naraḥ
c upabhuṅkte kva vā karma videhasyopatiṣṭhati
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a evaṃ saṃcoditaḥ siddhaḥ praśnāṃs tān pratyabhāṣata
c ānupūrvyeṇa vārṣṇeya yathā tan me vacaḥ śṛṇu
d siddhaḥ
d asminn evāśubhaphalā āyuṣyās tu kriyāḥ smṛtāḥ
 siddha uvāca
a āyuḥkīrtikarāṇīha yāni karmāṇi sevate
c śarīragrahaṇe 'nyasmiṃs teṣu kṣīṇeṣu sarvaśaḥ
a āyuḥkṣayaparītātmā viparītāni sevate
c buddhir vyāvartate cāsya vināśe pratyupasthite
a sattvaṃ balaṃ ca kālaṃ cāpy aviditvātmanas tathā
c ativelam upāśnāti tair viruddhāny anātmavān
a yadāyam atikaṣṭāni sarvāṇy upaniṣevate
c atyartham api vā bhuṅkte na vā bhuṅkte kadā cana
a duṣṭānnaṃ viṣamānnaṃ ca so 'nyonyena virodhi ca
c guru vāpi samaṃ bhuṅkte nātijīrṇe 'pi vā punaḥ
a vyāyāmam atimātraṃ vā vyavāyaṃ copasevate
c satataṃ karmalobhād vā prāptaṃ vegavidhāraṇam
a rasātiyuktam annaṃ vā divāsvapnaṃ niṣevate
c apakvānāgate kāle svayaṃ doṣān prakopayan
a svadoṣakopanād rogaṃ labhate maraṇāntikam
c atha codbandhanādīni parītāni vyavasyati
a tasya taiḥ kāraṇair jantoḥ śarīrāc cyavate yathā
c jīvitaṃ procyamānaṃ tad yathāvad upadhāraya
a ūṣmā prakupitaḥ kāye tīvravāyusamīritaḥ
c śarīram anuparyeti sarvān prāṇān ruṇaddhi vai
a atyarthaṃ balavān ūṣmā śarīre parikopitaḥ
c bhinatti jīvasthānāni tāni marmāṇi viddhi ca
a tataḥ savedanaḥ sadyo jīvaḥ pracyavate kṣaran
c śarīraṃ tyajate jantuś chidyamāneṣu marmasu
e vedanābhiḥ parītātmā tad viddhi dvijasattama
a jātīmaraṇasaṃvignāḥ satataṃ sarvajantavaḥ
c dṛśyante saṃtyajantaś ca śarīrāṇi dvijarṣabha
a garbhasaṃkramaṇe cāpi marmaṇām atisarpaṇe
c tādṛśīm eva labhate vedanāṃ mānavaḥ punaḥ
a bhinnasaṃdhir atha kledam adbhiḥ sa labhate naraḥ
c yathā pañcasu bhūteṣu saṃśritatvaṃ nigacchati
e śaityāt prakupitaḥ kāye tīvravāyusamīritaḥ
a yaḥ sa pañcasu bhūteṣu prāṇāpāne vyavasthitaḥ
c sa gacchaty ūrdhvago vāyuḥ kṛcchrān muktvā śarīriṇam
a śarīraṃ ca jahāty eva nirucchvāsaś ca dṛśyate
c nirūṣmā sa nirucchvāso niḥśrīko gatacetanaḥ
a brahmaṇā saṃparityakto mṛta ity ucyate naraḥ
c srotobhir yair vijānāti indriyārthāñ śarīrabhṛt
e tair eva na vijānāti prāṇam āhārasaṃbhavam
a tatraiva kurute kāye yaḥ sa jīvaḥ sanātanaḥ
c teṣāṃ yad yad bhaved yuktaṃ saṃnipāte kva cit kva cit
e tat tan marma vijānīhi śāstradṛṣṭaṃ hi tat tathā
a teṣu marmasu bhinneṣu tataḥ sa samudīrayan
c āviśya hṛdayaṃ jantoḥ sattvaṃ cāśu ruṇaddhi vai
e tataḥ sa cetano jantur nābhijānāti kiṃ cana
a tamasā saṃvṛtajñānaḥ saṃvṛteṣv atha marmasu
c sa jīvo niradhiṣṭhānaś cāvyate mātariśvanā
a tataḥ sa taṃ mahocchvāsaṃ bhṛśam ucchvasya dāruṇam
c niṣkrāman kampayaty āśu tac charīram acetanam
a sa jīvaḥ pracyutaḥ kāyāt karmabhiḥ svaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ
c aṅkitaḥ svaiḥ śubhaiḥ puṇyaiḥ pāpair vāpy upapadyate
a brāhmaṇā jñānasaṃpannā yathāvac chrutaniścayāḥ
c itaraṃ kṛtapuṇyaṃ vā taṃ vijānanti lakṣaṇaiḥ
a yathāndhakāre khadyotaṃ līyamānaṃ tatas tataḥ
c cakṣuṣmantaḥ prapaśyanti tathā taṃ jñānacakṣuṣaḥ
a paśyanty evaṃvidhāḥ siddhā jīvaṃ divyena cakṣuṣā
c cyavantaṃ jāyamānaṃ ca yoniṃ cānupraveśitam
a tasya sthānāni dṛṣṭāni trividhānīha śāstrataḥ
c karmabhūmir iyaṃ bhūmir yatra tiṣṭhanti jantavaḥ
a tataḥ śubhāśubhaṃ kṛtvā labhante sarvadehinaḥ
c ihaivoccāvacān bhogān prāpnuvanti svakarmabhiḥ
a ihaivāśubhakarmā tu karmabhir nirayaṃ gataḥ
c avāk sa niraye pāpo mānavaḥ pacyate bhṛśam
d arvāg gatir iyaṃ kaṣṭā yatra pacyanti mānavāḥ
e tasmāt sudurlabho mokṣa ātmā rakṣyo bhṛśaṃ tataḥ
a ūrdhvaṃ tu jantavo gatvā yeṣu sthāneṣv avasthitāḥ
c kīrtyamānāni tānīha tattvataḥ saṃnibodha me
e tac chrutvā naiṣṭhikīṃ buddhiṃ budhyethāḥ karmaniścayāt
a tārārūpāṇi sarvāṇi yac caitac candramaṇḍalam
c yac ca vibhrājate loke svabhāsā sūryamaṇḍalam
e sthānāny etāni jānīhi narāṇāṃ puṇyakarmaṇām
a karmakṣayāc ca te sarve cyavante vai punaḥ punaḥ
c tatrāpi ca viśeṣo 'sti divi nīcoccamadhyamaḥ
a na tatrāpy asti saṃtoṣo dṛṣṭvā dīptatarāṃ śriyam
c ity etā gatayaḥ sarvāḥ pṛthaktve samudīritāḥ
a upapattiṃ tu garbhasya vakṣyāmy aham ataḥ param
c yathāvat tāṃ nigadataḥ śṛṇuṣvāvahito dvija
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a śubhānām aśubhānāṃ ca neha nāśo 'sti karmaṇām
c prāpya prāpya tu pacyante kṣetraṃ kṣetraṃ tathā tathā
a yathā prasūyamānas tu phalī dadyāt phalaṃ bahu
c tathā syād vipulaṃ puṇyaṃ śuddhena manasā kṛtam
a pāpaṃ cāpi tathaiva syāt pāpena manasā kṛtam
c purodhāya mano hīha karmaṇy ātmā pravartate
a yathā karmasamādiṣṭaṃ kāmamanyusamāvṛtaḥ
c naro garbhaṃ praviśati tac cāpi śṛṇu cottaram
a śukraṃ śoṇitasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ striyā garbhāśayaṃ gatam
c kṣetraṃ karmajam āpnoti śubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham
a saukṣmyād avyaktabhāvāc ca na sa kva cana sajjate
c saṃprāpya brahmaṇaḥ kāyaṃ tasmāt tad brahma śāśvatam
e tad bījaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ tena jīvanti jantavaḥ
a sa jīvaḥ sarvagātrāṇi garbhasyāviśya bhāgaśaḥ
c dadhāti cetasā sadyaḥ prāṇasthāneṣv avasthitaḥ
e tataḥ spandayate 'ṅgāni sa garbhaś cetanānvitaḥ
a yathā hi lohaniṣyando niṣikto bimbavigraham
c upaiti tadvaj jānīhi garbhe jīvapraveśanam
a lohapiṇḍaṃ yathā vahniḥ praviśaty abhitāpayan
c tathā tvam api jānīhi garbhe jīvopapādanam
a yathā ca dīpaḥ śaraṇaṃ dīpyamānaḥ prakāśayet
c evam eva śarīrāṇi prakāśayati cetanā
a yad yac ca kurute karma śubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham
c pūrvadehakṛtaṃ sarvam avaśyam upabhujyate
a tatas tat kṣīyate caiva punaś cānyat pracīyate
c yāvat tan mokṣayogasthaṃ dharmaṃ naivāvabudhyate
a tatra dharmaṃ pravakṣyāmi sukhī bhavati yena vai
c āvartamāno jātīṣu tathānyonyāsu sattama
d śubhapradāni yāny āhus tāni kuryāc ca buddhimān
a dānaṃ vrataṃ brahmacaryaṃ yathoktavratadhāraṇam
c damaḥ praśāntatā caiva bhūtānāṃ cānukampanam
a saṃyamaś cānṛśaṃsyaṃ ca parasvādānavarjanam
c vyalīkānām akaraṇaṃ bhūtānāṃ yatra sā bhuvi
a mātāpitroś ca śuśrūṣā devatātithipūjanam
c gurupūjā ghṛṇā śaucaṃ nityam indriyasaṃyamaḥ
a pravartanaṃ śubhānāṃ ca tat satāṃ vṛttam ucyate
b sadbhir ācarito dharmaḥ sadācāre pratiṣṭhitaḥ
b ubhayārtho bhavaty eva svargārtho mokṣadas tathā
c tato dharmaḥ prabhavati yaḥ prajāḥ pāti śāśvatīḥ
a evaṃ satsu sadā paśyet tatra hy eṣā dhruvā sthitiḥ
c ācāro dharmam ācaṣṭe yasmin santo vyavasthitāḥ
a teṣu tad dharmanikṣiptaṃ yaḥ sa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ
c yas taṃ samabhipadyeta na sa durgatim āpnuyāt
a ato niyamyate lokaḥ pramuhya dharmavartmasu
c yas tu yogī ca muktaś ca sa etebhyo viśiṣyate
a vartamānasya dharmeṇa puruṣasya yathā tathā
c saṃsāratāraṇaṃ hy asya kālena mahatā bhavet
a evaṃ pūrvakṛtaṃ karma sarvo jantur niṣevate
c sarvaṃ tat kāraṇaṃ yena nikṛto 'yam ihāgataḥ
a śarīragrahaṇaṃ cāsya kena pūrvaṃ prakalpitam
c ity evaṃ saṃśayo loke tac ca vakṣyāmy ataḥ param
a śarīram ātmanaḥ kṛtvā sarvabhūtapitāmahaḥ
c trailokyam asṛjad brahmā kṛtsnaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamam
a tataḥ pradhānam asṛjac cetanā sā śarīriṇām
c yayā sarvam idaṃ vyāptaṃ yāṃ loke paramāṃ viduḥ
a iha tat kṣaram ity uktaṃ paraṃ tv amṛtam akṣaram
c trayāṇāṃ mithunaṃ sarvam ekaikasya pṛthak pṛthak
a asṛjat sarvabhūtāni pūrvasṛṣṭaḥ prajāpatiḥ
c sthāvarāṇi ca bhūtāni ity eṣā paurvikī śrutiḥ
a tasya kālaparīmāṇam akarot sa pitāmahaḥ
c bhūteṣu parivṛttiṃ ca punarāvṛttim eva ca
a yathātra kaś cin medhāvī dṛṣṭātmā pūrvajanmani
c yat pravakṣyāmi tat sarvaṃ yathāvad upapadyate
a sukhaduḥkhe sadā samyag anitye yaḥ prapaśyati
c kāyaṃ cāmedhyasaṃghātaṃ vināśaṃ karmasaṃhitam
a yac ca kiṃ cit sukhaṃ tac ca sarvaṃ duḥkham iti smaran
c saṃsārasāgaraṃ ghoraṃ tariṣyati sudustaram
a jātīmaraṇarogaiś ca samāviṣṭaḥ pradhānavit
c cetanāvatsu caitanyaṃ samaṃ bhūteṣu paśyati
a nirvidyate tataḥ kṛtsnaṃ mārgamāṇaḥ paraṃ padam
c tasyopadeśaṃ vakṣyāmi yāthātathyena sattama
a śāśvatasyāvyayasyātha padasya jñānam uttamam
c procyamānaṃ mayā vipra nibodhedam aśeṣataḥ
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a yaḥ syād ekāyane līnas tūṣṇīṃ kiṃ cid acintayan
c pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ parityajya sa nirārambhako bhavet
a sarvamitraḥ sarvasahaḥ samarakto jitendriyaḥ
c vyapetabhayamanyuś ca kāmahā mucyate naraḥ
a ātmavat sarvabhūteṣu yaś caren niyataḥ śuciḥ
b nityam eva yathānyāyaṃ yaś caren niyatendriyaḥ
c amānī nirabhīmānaḥ sarvato mukta eva saḥ
a jīvitaṃ maraṇaṃ cobhe sukhaduḥkhe tathaiva ca
c lābhālābhe priyadveṣye yaḥ samaḥ sa ca mucyate
a na kasya cit spṛhayate nāvajānāti kiṃ cana
c nirdvaṃdvo vītarāgātmā sarvato mukta eva saḥ
a anamitro 'tha nirbandhur anapatyaś ca yaḥ kva cit
c tyaktadharmārthakāmaś ca nirākāṅkṣī sa mucyate
a naiva dharmī na cādharmī pūrvopacitahā ca yaḥ
c dhātukṣayapraśāntātmā nirdvaṃdvaḥ sa vimucyate
a akarmā cāvikāṅkṣaś ca paśyañ jagad aśāśvatam
c asvastham avaśaṃ nityaṃ janmasaṃsāramohitam
a vairāgyabuddhiḥ satataṃ tāpadoṣavyapekṣakaḥ
c ātmabandhavinirmokṣaṃ sa karoty acirād iva
a agandharasam asparśam aśabdam aparigraham
c arūpam anabhijñeyaṃ dṛṣṭvātmānaṃ vimucyate
a pañcabhūtaguṇair hīnam amūrtimad alepakam
c aguṇaṃ guṇabhoktāraṃ yaḥ paśyati sa mucyate
a vihāya sarvasaṃkalpān buddhyā śārīramānasān
c śanair nirvāṇam āpnoti nirindhana ivānalaḥ
d sarvasaṃsthānanirmukto nirmamo niṣparigrahaḥ
d upaśāmyendriyagrāmaṃ yaś caren mukta eva saḥ
a vimuktaḥ sarvasaṃskārais tato brahma sanātanam
c param āpnoti saṃśāntam acalaṃ divyam akṣaram
a ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi yogaśāstram anuttamam
c yaj jñātvā siddham ātmānaṃ loke paśyanti yoginaḥ
a tasyopadeśaṃ paśyāmi yathāvat tan nibodha me
c yair dvāraiś cārayan nityaṃ paśyaty ātmānam ātmani
a indriyāṇi tu saṃhṛtya mana ātmani dhārayet
c tīvraṃ taptvā tapaḥ pūrvaṃ tato yoktum upakramet
a tapasvī tyaktasaṃkalpo dambhāhaṃkāravarjitaḥ
c manīṣī manasā vipraḥ paśyaty ātmānam ātmani
a sa cec chaknoty ayaṃ sādhur yoktum ātmānam ātmani
c tata ekāntaśīlaḥ sa paśyaty ātmānam ātmani
a saṃyataḥ satataṃ yukta ātmavān vijitendriyaḥ
c tathāyam ātmanātmānaṃ sādhu yuktaḥ prapaśyati
a yathā hi puruṣaḥ svapne dṛṣṭvā paśyaty asāv iti
c tathārūpam ivātmānaṃ sādhu yuktaḥ prapaśyati
a iṣīkāṃ vā yathā muñjāt kaś cin nirhṛtya darśayet
c yogī niṣkṛṣṭam ātmānaṃ tathā saṃpaśyate tanau
a muñjaṃ śarīraṃ tasyāhur iṣīkām ātmani śritām
c etan nidarśanaṃ proktaṃ yogavidbhir anuttamam
a yadā hi yuktam ātmānaṃ samyak paśyati dehabhṛt
c tadāsya neśate kaś cit trailokyasyāpi yaḥ prabhuḥ
a anyonyāś caiva tanavo yatheṣṭaṃ pratipadyate
b samyag yuktvā sa ātmānam ātmany evāvatiṣṭhate
c vinivṛtya jarāmṛtyū na hṛṣyati na śocati
a devānām api devatvaṃ yuktaḥ kārayate vaśī
c brahma cāvyayam āpnoti hitvā deham aśāśvatam
a vinaśyatsv api lokeṣu na bhayaṃ tasya jāyate
c kliśyamāneṣu bhūteṣu na sa kliśyati kena cit
a duḥkhaśokamayair ghoraiḥ saṅgasnehasamudbhavaiḥ
c na vicālyeta yuktātmā niḥspṛhaḥ śāntamānasaḥ
a nainaṃ śastrāṇi vidhyante na mṛtyuś cāsya vidyate
c nātaḥ sukhataraṃ kiṃ cil loke kva cana vidyate
d sadaiva muktasaṃsāro bhavaty ātmani yogataḥ
a samyag yuktvā yadātmānam ātmany eva prapaśyati
b vinivṛttajarāduḥkhaḥ sukhaṃ svapiti cāpi saḥ
b dehān yatheṣṭam abhyeti hitvemāṃ mānuṣīṃ tanum
c tadaiva na spṛhayate sākṣād api śatakratoḥ
a nirvedas tu na gantavyo yuñjānena kathaṃ cana
c yogam ekāntaśīlas tu yathā yuñjīta tac chṛṇu
a dṛṣṭapūrvāṃ diśaṃ cintya yasmin saṃnivaset pure
c purasyābhyantare tasya manaś cāryaṃ na bāhyataḥ
a purasyābhyantare tiṣṭhan yasminn āvasathe vaset
c tasminn āvasathe dhāryaṃ sabāhyābhyantaraṃ manaḥ
a pracintyāvasathaṃ kṛtsnaṃ yasmin kāye 'vatiṣṭhate
c tasmin kāye manaś cāryaṃ na kathaṃ cana bāhyataḥ
a saṃniyamyendriyagrāmaṃ nirghoṣe nirjane vane
c kāyam abhyantaraṃ kṛtsnam ekāgraḥ paricintayet
a dantāṃs tālu ca jihvāṃ ca galaṃ grīvāṃ tathaiva ca
c hṛdayaṃ cintayec cāpi tathā hṛdayabandhanam
a ity uktaḥ sa mayā śiṣyo medhāvī madhusūdana
c papraccha punar evemaṃ mokṣadharmaṃ sudurvacam
a bhuktaṃ bhuktaṃ katham idam annaṃ koṣṭhe vipacyate
c kathaṃ rasatvaṃ vrajati śoṇitaṃ jāyate katham
e tathā māṃsaṃ ca medaś ca snāyvasthīni ca poṣati
a katham etāni sarvāṇi śarīrāṇi śarīriṇām
c vardhante vardhamānasya vardhate ca kathaṃ balam
e nirojasāṃ niṣkramaṇaṃ malānāṃ ca pṛthak pṛthak
a kuto vāyaṃ praśvasiti ucchvasity api vā punaḥ
c kaṃ ca deśam adhiṣṭhāya tiṣṭhaty ātmāyam ātmani
a jīvaḥ kāyaṃ vahati cec ceṣṭayānaḥ kalevaram
c kiṃvarṇaṃ kīdṛśaṃ caiva niveśayati vai manaḥ
e yāthātathyena bhagavan vaktum arhasi me 'nagha
a iti saṃparipṛṣṭo 'haṃ tena vipreṇa mādhava
c pratyabruvaṃ mahābāho yathāśrutam ariṃdama
a yathā svakoṣṭhe prakṣipya koṣṭhaṃ bhāṇḍamanā bhavet
c tathā svakāye prakṣipya mano dvārair aniścalaiḥ
e ātmānaṃ tatra mārgeta pramādaṃ parivarjayet
a evaṃ satatam udyuktaḥ prītātmā nacirād iva
c āsādayati tad brahma yad dṛṣṭvā syāt pradhānavit
a na tv asau cakṣuṣā grāhyo na ca sarvair apīndriyaiḥ
c manasaiva pradīpena mahān ātmani dṛśyate
a sarvataḥpāṇipādaṃ taṃ sarvatokṣiśiromukham
b sarvataḥśrutimaṃl loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati
c jīvo niṣkrāntam ātmānaṃ śarīrāt saṃprapaśyati
a sa tad utsṛjya dehaṃ svaṃ dhārayan brahma kevalam
c ātmānam ālokayati manasā prahasann iva
d tad evam āśrayaṃ kṛtvā mokṣaṃ yāti tato mayi
a idaṃ sarvarahasyaṃ te mayoktaṃ dvijasattama
c āpṛcche sādhayiṣyāmi gaccha śiṣya yathāsukham
a ity uktaḥ sa tadā kṛṣṇa mayā śiṣyo mahātapāḥ
c agacchata yathākāmaṃ brāhmaṇaś chinnasaṃśayaḥ
 vāsudeva uvāca
a ity uktvā sa tadā vākyaṃ māṃ pārtha dvijapuṃgavaḥ
c mokṣadharmāśritaḥ samyak tatraivāntaradhīyata
a kaccid etat tvayā pārtha śrutam ekāgracetasā
c tadāpi hi rathasthas tvaṃ śrutavān etad eva hi
a naitat pārtha suvijñeyaṃ vyāmiśreṇeti me matiḥ
c nareṇākṛtasaṃjñena vidagdhenākṛtātmanā
a surahasyam idaṃ proktaṃ devānāṃ bharatarṣabha
c kaccin nedaṃ śrutaṃ pārtha martyenānyena kena cit
a na hy etac chrotum arho 'nyo manuṣyas tvām ṛte 'nagha
c naitad adya suvijñeyaṃ vyāmiśreṇāntarātmanā
a kriyāvadbhir hi kaunteya devalokaḥ samāvṛtaḥ
c na caitad iṣṭaṃ devānāṃ martyai rūpanivartanam
a parā hi sā gatiḥ pārtha yat tad brahma sanātanam
c yatrāmṛtatvaṃ prāpnoti tyaktvā duḥkhaṃ sadā sukhī
a evaṃ hi dharmam āsthāya ye 'pi syuḥ pāpayonayaḥ
c striyo vaiśyās tathā śūdrās te 'pi yānti parāṃ gatim
a kiṃ punar brāhmaṇāḥ pārtha kṣatriyā vā bahuśrutāḥ
c svadharmaratayo nityaṃ brahmalokaparāyaṇāḥ
a hetumac caitad uddiṣṭam upāyāś cāsya sādhane
c siddheḥ phalaṃ ca mokṣaś ca duḥkhasya ca vinirṇayaḥ
e ataḥ paraṃ sukhaṃ tv anyat kiṃ nu syād bharatarṣabha
a śrutavāñ śraddadhānaś ca parākrāntaś ca pāṇḍava
c yaḥ parityajate martyo lokatantram asāravat
e etair upāyaiḥ sa kṣipraṃ parāṃ gatim avāpnuyāt
a etāvad eva vaktavyaṃ nāto bhūyo 'sti kiṃ cana
c ṣaṇmāsān nityayuktasya yogaḥ pārtha pravartate
 vāsudeva uvāca
a atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c daṃpatyoḥ pārtha saṃvādam abhayaṃ nāma nāmataḥ
a brāhmaṇī brāhmaṇaṃ kaṃ cij jñānavijñānapāragam
c dṛṣṭvā vivikta āsīnaṃ bhāryā bhartāram abravīt
a kaṃ nu lokaṃ gamiṣyāmi tvām ahaṃ patim āśritā
c nyastakarmāṇam āsīnaṃ kīnāśam avicakṣaṇam
a bhāryāḥ patikṛtāṃl lokān āpnuvantīti naḥ śrutam
c tvām ahaṃ patim āsādya kāṃ gamiṣyāmi vai gatim
a evam uktaḥ sa śāntātmā tām uvāca hasann iva
c subhage nābhyasūyāmi vākyasyāsya tavānaghe
a grāhyaṃ dṛśyaṃ ca śrāvyaṃ ca yad idaṃ karma vidyate
c etad eva vyavasyanti karma karmeti karmiṇaḥ
a moham eva niyacchanti karmaṇā jñānavarjitāḥ
c naiṣkarmyaṃ na ca loke 'smin maurtam ity upalabhyate
a karmaṇā manasā vācā śubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham
c janmādimūrtibhedānāṃ karma bhūteṣu vartate
a rakṣobhir vadhyamāneṣu dṛśyadravyeṣu karmasu
c ātmastham ātmanā tena dṛṣṭam āyatanaṃ mayā
a yatra tad brahma nirdvaṃdvaṃ yatra somaḥ sahāgninā
c vyavāyaṃ kurute nityaṃ dhīro bhūtāni dhārayan
a yatra brahmādayo yuktās tad akṣaram upāsate
c vidvāṃsaḥ suvratā yatra śāntātmāno jitendriyāḥ
a ghrāṇena na tad āghreyaṃ na tad ādyaṃ ca jihvayā
c sparśena ca na tat spṛśyaṃ manasā tv eva gamyate
a cakṣuṣā na viṣahyaṃ ca yat kiṃ cic chravaṇāt param
c agandham arasasparśam arūpāśabdam avyayam
a yataḥ pravartate tantraṃ yatra ca pratitiṣṭhati
c prāṇo 'pānaḥ samānaś ca vyānaś codāna eva ca
a tata eva pravartante tam eva praviśanti ca
c samānavyānayor madhye prāṇāpānau viceratuḥ
a tasmin supte pralīyete samāno vyāna eva ca
c apānaprāṇayor madhye udāno vyāpya tiṣṭhati
e tasmāc chayānaṃ puruṣaṃ prāṇāpānau na muñcataḥ
a prāṇān āyamyate yena tam udānaṃ pracakṣate
c tasmāt tapo vyavasyanti tadbhavaṃ brahmavādinaḥ
a teṣām anyonyabhakṣāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ dehacāriṇām
c agnir vaiśvānaro madhye saptadhā vihito 'ntarā
a ghrāṇaṃ jihvā ca cakṣuś ca tvak ca śrotraṃ ca pañcamam
c mano buddhiś ca saptaitā jihvā vaiśvānarārciṣaḥ
a ghreyaṃ peyaṃ ca dṛśyaṃ ca spṛśyaṃ śravyaṃ tathaiva ca
c mantavyam atha boddhavyaṃ tāḥ sapta samidho mama
a ghrātā bhakṣayitā draṣṭā spraṣṭā śrotā ca pañcamaḥ
c mantā boddhā ca saptaite bhavanti paramartvijaḥ
a ghreye peye ca dṛśye ca spṛśye śravye tathaiva ca
b mantavye 'py atha boddhavye subhage paśya sarvadā
c havīṃṣy agniṣu hotāraḥ saptadhā sapta saptasu
e samyak prakṣipya vidvāṃso janayanti svayoniṣu
f karaṇaṃ karma kartā ca mokṣam ity eva vādinaḥ
a pṛthivī vāyur ākāśam āpo jyotiś ca pañcamam
c mano buddhiś ca saptaite yonir ity eva śabditāḥ
a havirbhūtā guṇāḥ sarve praviśanty agnijaṃ mukham
c antarvāsam uṣitvā ca jāyante svāsu yoniṣu
e tatraiva ca nirudhyante pralaye bhūtabhāvane
a tataḥ saṃjāyate gandhas tataḥ saṃjāyate rasaḥ
c tataḥ saṃjāyate rūpaṃ tataḥ sparśo 'bhijāyate
a tataḥ saṃjāyate śabdaḥ saṃśayas tatra jāyate
c tataḥ saṃjāyate niṣṭhā janmaitat saptadhā viduḥ
a anenaiva prakāreṇa pragṛhītaṃ purātanaiḥ
c pūrṇāhutibhir āpūrṇās te 'bhipūryanti tejasā
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
b indriyāṇāṃ ca saṃvādaṃ manasaś caiva bhāmini
c nibodha daśahotṝṇāṃ vidhānam iha yādṛśam
d śrotraṃ tvak cakṣuṣī jihvā nāsikā caraṇau karau
d upasthaḥ pāyur etāni hotṝṇi daśa bhāmini
d śabdasparśau rūparasau gandho vākyaṃ kriyā gatiḥ
d retomūtrapurīṣāṇāṃ tyāgo daśa havīṃṣi ca
d diśo vāyū raviś candraḥ pṛthvyagnī viṣṇur eva ca
d indraḥ prajāpatir mitram agnayo daśa bhāmini
d daśendriyāṇi hotṝṇi havīṃṣi daśa bhāmini
d viṣayā nāma samidho hūyante tu daśāgniṣu
d cittaṃ sruvaṃ ca vittaṃ ca pavitraṃ jñānam uttamam
d suvibhaktam idaṃ sarvaṃ jagad āsīd iti śrutam
d tato viviktā cintāsīt sā cittaṃ paryavekṣate
d śrutvā cittaṃ srug ity eva manaś cittaṃ tad ucyate
d tayor viviktā nāgāsīd acalā śabdalakṣaṇā
d nagneva yoṣā savrīḍā sā vāsaḥ paryavekṣate
d tasmāt saṃjajñire varṇāḥ svarā mantrās tathaiva ca
d etac ca naḥ sarasvatyāḥ prajāpatir athābravīt
a sarvam evātra vijñeyaṃ cittaṃ jñānam avekṣate
c retaḥ śarīrabhṛtkāye vijñātā tu śarīrabhṛt
a śarīrabhṛd gārhapatyas tasmād anyaḥ praṇīyate
c tataś cāhavanīyas tu tasmin saṃkṣipyate haviḥ
a tato vācaspatir jajñe samānaḥ paryavekṣate
c rūpaṃ bhavati vai vyaktaṃ tad anudravate manaḥ
 brāhmaṇy uvāca
a kasmād vāg abhavat pūrvaṃ kasmāt paścān mano 'bhavat
c manasā cintitaṃ vākyaṃ yadā samabhipadyate
a kena vijñānayogena matiś cittaṃ samāsthitā
c samunnītā nādhyagacchat ko vaināṃ pratiṣedhati
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a tām apānaḥ patir bhūtvā tasmāt preṣyaty apānatām
c tāṃ matiṃ manasaḥ prāhur manas tasmād avekṣate
a praśnaṃ tu vāṅmanasor māṃ yasmāt tvam anupṛcchasi
c tasmāt te vartayiṣyāmi tayor eva samāhvayam
a ubhe vāṅmanasī gatvā bhūtātmānam apṛcchatām
c āvayoḥ śreṣṭham ācakṣva chindhi nau saṃśayaṃ vibho
a mana ity eva bhagavāṃs tadā prāha sarasvatīm
c ahaṃ vai kāmadhuk tubhyam iti taṃ prāha vāg atha
a sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ caiva viddhy ubhe manasī mama
c sthāvaraṃ matsakāśe vai jaṅgamaṃ viṣaye tava
a yas tu te viṣayaṃ gacchen mantro varṇaḥ svaro 'pi vā
c tan mano jaṅgamaṃ nāma tasmād asi garīyasī
a yasmād asi ca mā vocaḥ svayam abhyetya śobhane
c tasmād ucchvāsam āsādya na vakṣyasi sarasvati
a prāṇāpānāntare devī vāg vai nityaṃ sma tiṣṭhati
c preryamāṇā mahābhāge vinā prāṇam apānatī
e prajāpatim upādhāvat prasīda bhagavann iti
a tataḥ prāṇaḥ prādurabhūd vācam āpyāyayan punaḥ
c tasmād ucchvāsam āsādya na vāg vadati karhi cit
a ghoṣiṇī jātanirghoṣā nityam eva pravartate
c tayor api ca ghoṣiṇyor nirghoṣaiva garīyasī
a gaur iva prasravaty eṣā rasam uttamaśālinī
c satataṃ syandate hy eṣā śāśvataṃ brahmavādinī
a divyādivyaprabhāvena bhāratī gauḥ śucismite
c etayor antaraṃ paśya sūkṣmayoḥ syandamānayoḥ
a anutpanneṣu vākyeṣu codyamānā sisṛkṣayā
c kiṃ nu pūrvaṃ tato devī vyājahāra sarasvatī
a prāṇena yā saṃbhavate śarīre
prāṇād apānaṃ pratipadyate ca
c udānabhūtā ca visṛjya dehaṃ
vyānena sarvaṃ divam āvṛṇoti
a tataḥ samāne pratitiṣṭhatīha
ity eva pūrvaṃ prajajalpa cāpi
c tasmān manaḥ sthāvaratvād viśiṣṭaṃ
tathā devī jaṅgamatvād viśiṣṭā
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c subhage saptahotṝṇāṃ vidhānam iha yādṛśam
a ghrāṇaṃ cakṣuś ca jihvā ca tvak śrotraṃ caiva pañcamam
c mano buddhiś ca saptaite hotāraḥ pṛthag āśritāḥ
a sūkṣme 'vakāśe santas te na paśyantītaretaram
c etān vai saptahotṝṃs tvaṃ svabhāvād viddhi śobhane
 brāhmaṇy uvāca
a sūkṣme 'vakāśe santas te kathaṃ nānyonyadarśinaḥ
c kathaṃsvabhāvā bhagavann etad ācakṣva me vibho
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a guṇājñānam avijñānaṃ guṇijñānam abhijñatā
c parasparaguṇān ete na vijānanti karhi cit
a jihvā cakṣus tathā śrotraṃ tvaṅ mano buddhir eva ca
c na gandhān adhigacchanti ghrāṇas tān adhigacchati
a ghrāṇaṃ cakṣus tathā śrotraṃ tvaṅ mano buddhir eva ca
c na rasān adhigacchanti jihvā tān adhigacchati
a ghrāṇaṃ jihvā tathā śrotraṃ tvaṅ mano buddhir eva ca
c na rūpāṇy adhigacchanti cakṣus tāny adhigacchati
a ghrāṇaṃ jihvā ca cakṣuś ca śrotraṃ buddhir manas tathā
c na sparśān adhigacchanti tvak ca tān adhigacchati
a ghrāṇaṃ jihvā ca cakṣuś ca tvaṅ mano buddhir eva ca
c na śabdān adhigacchanti śrotraṃ tān adhigacchati
d ghrāṇaṃ cakṣuś ca śrotraṃ ca tvag jihvā buddhir eva ca
a ghrāṇaṃ jihvā ca cakṣuś ca tvak śrotraṃ buddhir eva ca
c saṃśayān nādhigacchanti manas tān adhigacchati
a ghrāṇaṃ jihvā ca cakṣuś ca tvak śrotraṃ mana eva ca
c na niṣṭhām adhigacchanti buddhis tām adhigacchati
a atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c indriyāṇāṃ ca saṃvādaṃ manasaś caiva bhāmini
 mana uvāca
a na ghrāti mām ṛte ghrāṇaṃ rasaṃ jihvā na budhyate
c rūpaṃ cakṣur na gṛhṇāti tvak sparśaṃ nāvabudhyate
a na śrotraṃ budhyate śabdaṃ mayā hīnaṃ kathaṃ cana
c pravaraṃ sarvabhūtānām aham asmi sanātanam
a agārāṇīva śūnyāni śāntārciṣa ivāgnayaḥ
c indriyāṇi na bhāsante mayā hīnāni nityaśaḥ
a kāṣṭhānīvārdraśuṣkāṇi yatamānair apīndriyaiḥ
c guṇārthān nādhigacchanti mām ṛte sarvajantavaḥ
 indriyāṇy ūcuḥ
a evam etad bhavet satyaṃ yathaitan manyate bhavān
c ṛte 'smān asmadarthāṃs tu bhogān bhuṅkte bhavān yadi
a yady asmāsu pralīneṣu tarpaṇaṃ prāṇadhāraṇam
c bhogān bhuṅkṣe rasān bhuṅkṣe yathaitan manyate tathā
a atha vāsmāsu līneṣu tiṣṭhatsu viṣayeṣu ca
c yadi saṃkalpamātreṇa bhuṅkte bhogān yathārthavat
a atha cen manyase siddhim asmadartheṣu nityadā
c ghrāṇena rūpam ādatsva rasam ādatsva cakṣuṣā
a śrotreṇa gandham ādatsva niṣṭhām ādatsva jihvayā
c tvacā ca śabdam ādatsva buddhyā sparśam athāpi ca
a balavanto hy aniyamā niyamā durbalīyasām
c bhogān apūrvān ādatsva nocchiṣṭaṃ bhoktum arhasi
a yathā hi śiṣyaḥ śāstāraṃ śrutyartham abhidhāvati
c tataḥ śrutam upādāya śrutārtham upatiṣṭhati
a viṣayān evam asmābhir darśitān abhimanyase
c anāgatān atītāṃś ca svapne jāgaraṇe tathā
a vaimanasyaṃ gatānāṃ ca jantūnām alpacetasām
c asmadarthe kṛte kārye dṛśyate prāṇadhāraṇam
a bahūn api hi saṃkalpān matvā svapnān upāsya ca
c bubhukṣayā pīḍyamāno viṣayān eva dhāvasi
a agāram advāram iva praviśya
saṃkalpabhogo viṣayān avindan
c prāṇakṣaye śāntim upaiti nityaṃ
dārukṣaye 'gnir jvalito yathaiva
a kāmaṃ tu naḥ sveṣu guṇeṣu saṅgaḥ
kāmaṃ ca nānyonyaguṇopalabdhiḥ
c asmān ṛte nāsti tavopalabdhis
tvām apy ṛte 'smān na bhajeta harṣaḥ
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c subhage pañcahotṝṇāṃ vidhānam iha yādṛśam
a prāṇāpānāv udānaś ca samāno vyāna eva ca
c pañcahotṝn athaitān vai paraṃ bhāvaṃ vidur budhāḥ
 brāhmaṇy uvāca
a svabhāvāt sapta hotāra iti te pūrvikā matiḥ
c yathā vai pañca hotāraḥ paro bhāvas tathocyatām
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a prāṇena saṃbhṛto vāyur apāno jāyate tataḥ
c apāne saṃbhṛto vāyus tato vyānaḥ pravartate
a vyānena saṃbhṛto vāyus tatodānaḥ pravartate
c udāne saṃbhṛto vāyuḥ samānaḥ saṃpravartate
a te 'pṛcchanta purā gatvā pūrvajātaṃ prajāpatim
c yo no jyeṣṭhas tam ācakṣva sa naḥ śreṣṭho bhaviṣyati
 brahmovāca
a yasmin pralīne pralayaṃ vrajanti
sarve prāṇāḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ śarīre
c yasmin pracīrṇe ca punaś caranti
sa vai śreṣṭho gacchata yatra kāmaḥ
 prāṇa uvāca
a mayi pralīne pralayaṃ vrajanti
sarve prāṇāḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ śarīre
c mayi pracīrṇe ca punaś caranti
śreṣṭho hy ahaṃ paśyata māṃ pralīnam
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a prāṇaḥ pralīyata tataḥ punaś ca pracacāra ha
c samānaś cāpy udānaś ca vaco 'brūtāṃ tataḥ śubhe
a na tvaṃ sarvam idaṃ vyāpya tiṣṭhasīha yathā vayam
c na tvaṃ śreṣṭho 'si naḥ prāṇa apāno hi vaśe tava
e pracacāra punaḥ prāṇas tam apāno 'bhyabhāṣata
a mayi pralīne pralayaṃ vrajanti
sarve prāṇāḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ śarīre
c mayi pracīrṇe ca punaś caranti
śreṣṭho hy ahaṃ paśyata māṃ pralīnam
d śreṣṭho 'ham asmi sarveṣāṃ śrūyatāṃ yena hetunā
a vyānaś ca tam udānaś ca bhāṣamāṇam athocatuḥ
c apāna na tvaṃ śreṣṭho 'si prāṇo hi vaśagas tava
a apānaḥ pracacārātha vyānas taṃ punar abravīt
c śreṣṭho 'ham asmi sarveṣāṃ śrūyatāṃ yena hetunā
a mayi pralīne pralayaṃ vrajanti
sarve prāṇāḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ śarīre
c mayi pracīrṇe ca punaś caranti
śreṣṭho hy ahaṃ paśyata māṃ pralīnam
a prālīyata tato vyānaḥ punaś ca pracacāra ha
c prāṇāpānāv udānaś ca samānaś ca tam abruvan
e na tvaṃ śreṣṭho 'si no vyāna samāno hi vaśe tava
a pracacāra punar vyānaḥ samānaḥ punar abravīt
c śreṣṭho 'ham asmi sarveṣāṃ śrūyatāṃ yena hetunā
a mayi pralīne pralayaṃ vrajanti
sarve prāṇāḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ śarīre
c mayi pracīrṇe ca punaś caranti
śreṣṭho hy ahaṃ paśyata māṃ pralīnam
a tataḥ samānaḥ prālilye punaś ca pracacāra ha
b tato vyānaḥ samānaṃ tu prāṇāpānau tathocatuḥ
c prāṇāpānāv udānaś ca vyānaś caiva tam abruvan
e samāna na tvaṃ śreṣṭho 'si vyāna eva vaśe tava
f śreṣṭho 'ham asmi sarveṣāṃ śrūyatāṃ kena hetunā
f tatodānaḥ pralīyāśu samānaḥ punar abravīt
a samānaḥ pracacārātha udānas tam uvāca ha
c śreṣṭho 'ham asmi sarveṣāṃ śrūyatāṃ yena hetunā
a mayi pralīne pralayaṃ vrajanti
sarve prāṇāḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ śarīre
c mayi pracīrṇe ca punaś caranti
śreṣṭho hy ahaṃ paśyata māṃ pralīnam
a tataḥ prālīyatodānaḥ punaś ca pracacāra ha
c prāṇāpānau samānaś ca vyānaś caiva tam abruvan
e udāna na tvaṃ śreṣṭho 'si vyāna eva vaśe tava
a tatas tān abravīd brahmā samavetān prajāpatiḥ
c sarve śreṣṭhā na vā śreṣṭhāḥ sarve cānyonyadharmiṇaḥ
e sarve svaviṣaye śreṣṭhāḥ sarve cānyonyarakṣiṇaḥ
a ekaḥ sthiraś cāsthiraś ca viśeṣāt pañca vāyavaḥ
c eka eva mamaivātmā bahudhāpy upacīyate
a parasparasya suhṛdo bhāvayantaḥ parasparam
c svasti vrajata bhadraṃ vo dhārayadhvaṃ parasparam
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c nāradasya ca saṃvādam ṛṣer devamatasya ca
 devamata uvāca
a jantoḥ saṃjāyamānasya kiṃ nu pūrvaṃ pravartate
c prāṇo 'pānaḥ samāno vā vyāno vodāna eva ca
 nārada uvāca
a yenāyaṃ sṛjyate jantus tato 'nyaḥ pūrvam eti tam
c prāṇadvaṃdvaṃ ca vijñeyaṃ tiryagaṃ cordhvagaṃ ca yat
 devamata uvāca
a kenāyaṃ sṛjyate jantuḥ kaś cānyaḥ pūrvam eti tam
c prāṇadvaṃdvaṃ ca me brūhi tiryag ūrdhvaṃ ca niścayāt
 nārada uvāca
a saṃkalpāj jāyate harṣaḥ śabdād api ca jāyate
c rasāt saṃjāyate cāpi rūpād api ca jāyate
a sparśāt saṃjāyate cāpi gandhād api ca jāyate
c etad rūpam udānasya harṣo mithunasaṃbhavaḥ
a kāmāt saṃjāyate śukraṃ kāmāt saṃjāyate rasaḥ
c samānavyānajanite sāmānye śukraśoṇite
a śukrāc choṇitasaṃsṛṣṭāt pūrvaṃ prāṇaḥ pravartate
c prāṇena vikṛte śukre tato 'pānaḥ pravartate
a prāṇāpānāv idaṃ dvaṃdvam avāk cordhvaṃ ca gacchataḥ
c vyānaḥ samānaś caivobhau tiryag dvaṃdvatvam ucyate
a agnir vai devatāḥ sarvā iti vedasya śāsanam
c saṃjāyate brāhmaṇeṣu jñānaṃ buddhisamanvitam
a tasya dhūmas tamorūpaṃ rajo bhasma suretasaḥ
c sattvaṃ saṃjāyate tasya yatra prakṣipyate haviḥ
a āghārau samāno vyānaś ca iti yajñavido viduḥ
c prāṇāpānāv ājyabhāgau tayor madhye hutāśanaḥ
