e etad rūpam udānasya paramaṃ brāhmaṇā viduḥ
a nirdvaṃdvam iti yat tv etat tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu
a ahorātram idaṃ dvaṃdvaṃ tayor madhye hutāśanaḥ
c etad rūpam udānasya paramaṃ brāhmaṇā viduḥ
a ubhe caivāyane dvaṃdvaṃ tayor madhye hutāśanaḥ
c etad rūpam udānasya paramaṃ brāhmaṇā viduḥ
a ubhe satyānṛte dvaṃdvaṃ tayor madhye hutāśanaḥ
c etad rūpam udānasya paramaṃ brāhmaṇā viduḥ
a ubhe śubhāśubhe dvaṃdvaṃ tayor madhye hutāśanaḥ
c etad rūpam udānasya paramaṃ brāhmaṇā viduḥ
a sac cāsac caiva tad dvaṃdvaṃ tayor madhye hutāśanaḥ
c etad rūpam udānasya paramaṃ brāhmaṇā viduḥ
a prathamaṃ samāno vyāno vyasyate karma tena tat
c tṛtīyaṃ tu samānena punar eva vyavasyate
a śāntyarthaṃ vāmadevaṃ ca śāntir brahma sanātanam
c etad rūpam udānasya paramaṃ brāhmaṇā viduḥ
d yāvad dravyaguṇas tāvat pradīpaḥ saṃprakāśayet
d kṣīṇe dravyaguṇe jyotir antardhānāya gacchati
d vyaktaḥ sattvaguṇe hy eṣa puruṣo vyaktir īśate
d etad vipra vijānīṣva hanta bhūyo bravīmi te
d sahasreṇāpi durmedhā buddhimān sukham edhate
d evaṃ dharmasya vijñeyaṃ saṃsādhanam upāyataḥ
d upāyajño hi medhāvī sukham atyantam aśnute
d yathādhvānam apātheyaḥ prapanno mānavaḥ kva cit
d kleśena yāti mahatā vinaśyaty antarāpi vā
d tathā karmasu vijñeyaṃ phalaṃ bhavati mānava
d puruṣasyātmaniḥśreyaḥ śubhāśubhanidarśanaḥ
d yathā ca dīrgham adhvānaṃ padbhyām eva prapadyate
d adṛṣṭapūrvaṃ sahasā tattvadarśanavakritaḥ
d prāpnuvanto yathādhvānaṃ rathenehāśugāminā
d yāyād aśvaprayuktena tathā buddhimatāṃ gatiḥ
d uccaparvatam āruhya nanv avekṣeta bhūgatam
d rathena rathinaṃ paśyec caitanyena ca cetanam
d yāvad rathapathas tāvad rathe samupagacchati
d kṣīṇe rathapathe prājño ratham utsṛjya gacchati
d evaṃ gacchati medhāvī tattvayogavidhānavit
d samājñāya mahābuddher uttarād uttarottaram
d yathā mahārṇavaṃ ghoram udbhavaḥ saṃpragāhate
d bāhubhyām eva saṃmohād vadhaṃ gacchaty asaṃśayam
d nāvayā ca yathā prājño vinā prajñātaritrayā
d akrāntasalilaṃ gāhe kḷptaṃ saṃtarati svayam
d tīrṇo gacchet paraṃ pāraṃ nāvam utsṛjya nirmamaḥ
d vyākhyātaṃ pūrvakalpena yathā rathapadātinām
d mohāt saṃmoham āpanno mā vināśaṃ yathā tathā
d mamatvenābhibhūtasya tatraiva paridevane
d nāvaṃ na śakyam āruhya sthale 'pi paribhāvitum
d tathaiva sthalam āruhya nāpsu yātuṃ vidhīyate
d evaṃ karma kṛtaṃ cittaṃ viṣamasthaṃ pṛthak pṛthak
d yathā karma kṛtaṃ loke tathā tad upapadyate
d yatraiva gandho na raso na rūpasparśaśabdavat
d manyate 'tha mano buddhyā tat pradhānaṃ pracakṣate
d yat tat pradhānam avyaktam avyaktasya guṇo mahān
d mahataḥ pradhānabhūtasya guṇāḥ     smṛtāḥ
d bījadharmi yathā vyaktaṃ tathaiva prasavātmakam
d bījadharmā mahān ātmā vasavaś ceti naḥ śrutam
d bījadharmāt tv ahaṃkāraḥ prasavatve punaḥ punaḥ
d bījaprasavadharmāṇi mahābhūtāni pañca vai
d bījadharmiṇam ity āhuḥ prasavaṃ naiva kurvate
d viśeṣāḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ teṣāṃ cittaṃ viśeṣaṇam
d etad rūpam udānasya paramaṃ brāhmaṇā viduḥ
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c cāturhotravidhānasya vidhānam iha yādṛśam
a tasya sarvasya vidhivad vidhānam upadekṣyate
c śṛṇu me gadato bhadre rahasyam idam uttamam
a karaṇaṃ karma kartā ca mokṣa ity eva bhāmini
c catvāra ete hotāro yair idaṃ jagad āvṛtam
a hotṝṇāṃ sādhanaṃ caiva śṛṇu sarvam aśeṣataḥ
c ghrāṇaṃ jihvā ca cakṣuś ca tvak ca śrotraṃ ca pañcamam
e mano buddhiś ca saptaite vijñeyā guṇahetavaḥ
a gandho rasaś ca rūpaṃ ca śabdaḥ sparśaś ca pañcamaḥ
c mantavyam atha boddhavyaṃ saptaite karmahetavaḥ
a ghrātā bhakṣayitā draṣṭā spraṣṭā śrotā ca pañcamaḥ
c mantā boddhā ca saptaite vijñeyāḥ kartṛhetavaḥ
a svaguṇaṃ bhakṣayanty ete guṇavantaḥ śubhāśubham
c ahaṃ ca nirguṇo 'treti saptaite mokṣahetavaḥ
a viduṣāṃ budhyamānānāṃ svaṃ svaṃ sthānaṃ yathāvidhi
c guṇās te devatābhūtāḥ satataṃ bhuñjate haviḥ
a adan hy avidvān annāni mamatvenopapadyate
c ātmārthaṃ pācayan nityaṃ mamatvenopahanyate
a abhakṣyabhakṣaṇaṃ caiva madyapānaṃ ca hanti tam
c sa cānnaṃ hanti tac cānnaṃ sa hatvā hanyate budhaḥ
a attā hy annam idaṃ vidvān punar janayatīśvaraḥ
c sa cānnāj jāyate tasmin sūkṣmo nāma vyatikramaḥ
a manasā gamyate yac ca yac ca vācā nirudyate
c śrotreṇa śrūyate yac ca cakṣuṣā yac ca dṛśyate
a sparśena spṛśyate yac ca ghrāṇena ghrāyate ca yat
c manaḥṣaṣṭhāni saṃyamya havīṃṣy etāni sarvaśaḥ
a guṇavatpāvako mahyaṃ dīpyate havyavāhanaḥ
c yogayajñaḥ pravṛtto me jñānabrahmamanodbhavaḥ
e prāṇastotro 'pānaśastraḥ sarvatyāgasudakṣiṇaḥ
a karmānumantā brahmā me kartādhvaryuḥ kṛtastutiḥ
c kṛtapraśāstā tac chāstram apavargo 'sya dakṣiṇā
a ṛcaś cāpy atra śaṃsanti nārāyaṇavido janāḥ
c nārāyaṇāya devāya yad abadhnan paśūn purā
a tatra sāmāni gāyanti tāni cāhur nidarśanam
c devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ bhīru sarvātmānaṃ nibodha me
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a ekaḥ śāstā na dvitīyo 'sti śāstā
yathā niyukto 'smi tathā carāmi
a yo hṛcchayas tam aham anubravīmi
c hṛdy eṣa tiṣṭhan puruṣaḥ śāsti śāstā
tenaiva yuktaḥ pravaṇād ivodakam
a eko gurur nāsti tato dvitīyo
yo hṛcchayas tam aham anubravīmi
c tenānuśiṣṭā guruṇā sadaiva
parābhūtā dānavāḥ sarva eva
a eko bandhur nāsti tato dvitīyo
yo hṛcchayas tam aham anubravīmi
c tenānuśiṣṭā bāndhavā bandhumantaḥ
saptarṣayaḥ sapta divi prabhānti
a ekaḥ śrotā nāsti tato dvitīyo
yo hṛcchayas tam aham anubravīmi
c tasmin gurau guruvāsaṃ niruṣya
śakro gataḥ sarvalokāmaratvam
a eko dveṣṭā nāsti tato dvitīyo
yo hṛcchayas tam aham anubravīmi
c tenānuśiṣṭā guruṇā sadaiva
lokadviṣṭāḥ pannagāḥ sarva eva
a atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c prajāpatau pannagānāṃ devarṣīṇāṃ ca saṃvidam
a devarṣayaś ca nāgāś ca asurāś ca prajāpatim
c paryapṛcchann upāsīnāḥ śreyo naḥ procyatām iti
a teṣāṃ provāca bhagavāñ śreyaḥ samanupṛcchatām
c om ity ekākṣaraṃ brahma te śrutvā prādravan diśaḥ
a teṣāṃ prādravamāṇānām upadeśārtham ātmanaḥ
c sarpāṇāṃ daśane bhāvaḥ pravṛttaḥ pūrvam eva tu
a asurāṇāṃ pravṛttas tu dambhabhāvaḥ svabhāvajaḥ
c dānaṃ devā vyavasitā damam eva maharṣayaḥ
a ekaṃ śāstāram āsādya śabdenaikena saṃskṛtāḥ
c nānā vyavasitāḥ sarve sarpadevarṣidānavāḥ
a śṛṇoty ayaṃ procyamānaṃ gṛhṇāti ca yathātatham
c pṛcchatas tāvato bhūyo gurur anyo 'numanyate
a tasya cānumate karma tataḥ paścāt pravartate
c gurur boddhā ca śatruś ca dveṣṭā ca hṛdi saṃśritaḥ
a pāpena vicaraṃl loke pāpacārī bhavaty ayam
c śubhena vicaraṃl loke śubhacārī bhavaty uta
a kāmacārī tu kāmena ya indriyasukhe rataḥ
c vratavārī sadaivaiṣa ya indriyajaye rataḥ
a apetavratakarmā tu kevalaṃ brahmaṇi śritaḥ
c brahmabhūtaś caraṃl loke brahmacārī bhavaty ayam
a brahmaiva samidhas tasya brahmāgnir brahmasaṃstaraḥ
c āpo brahma gurur brahma sa brahmaṇi samāhitaḥ
a etad etādṛśaṃ sūkṣmaṃ brahmacaryaṃ vidur budhāḥ
c viditvā cānvapadyanta kṣetrajñenānudarśinaḥ
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a saṃkalpadaṃśamaśakaṃ śokaharṣahimātapam
c mohāndhakāratimiraṃ lobhavyālasarīsṛpam
a viṣayaikātyayādhvānaṃ kāmakrodhavirodhakam
c tad atītya mahādurgaṃ praviṣṭo 'smi mahad vanam
 brāhmaṇy uvāca
a kva tad vanaṃ mahāprājña ke vṛkṣāḥ saritaś ca kāḥ
c girayaḥ parvatāś caiva kiyaty adhvani tad vanam
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a na tad asti pṛthagbhāve kiṃ cid anyat tataḥ samam
c na tad asty apṛthagbhāve kiṃ cid dūrataraṃ tataḥ
a tasmād dhrasvataraṃ nāsti na tato 'sti bṛhattaram
c nāsti tasmād duḥkhataraṃ nāsty anyat tatsamaṃ sukham
a na tat praviśya śocanti na prahṛṣyanti ca dvijāḥ
c na ca bibhyati keṣāṃ cit tebhyo bibhyati ke ca na
a tasmin vane sapta mahādrumāś ca
phalāni saptātithayaś ca sapta
c saptāśramāḥ sapta samādhayaś ca
dīkṣāś ca saptaitad araṇyarūpam
a pañcavarṇāni divyāni puṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca
c sṛjantaḥ pādapās tatra vyāpya tiṣṭhanti tad vanam
a suvarṇāni dvivarṇāni puṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca
c sṛjantaḥ pādapās tatra vyāpya tiṣṭhanti tad vanam
a caturvarṇāni divyāni puṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca
c sṛjantaḥ pādapās tatra vyāpya tiṣṭhanti tad vanam
a śaṃkarāṇi trivarṇāni puṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca
c sṛjantaḥ pādapās tatra vyāpya tiṣṭhanti tad vanam
a surabhīṇy ekavarṇāni puṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca
c sṛjantaḥ pādapās tatra vyāpya tiṣṭhanti tad vanam
a bahūny avyaktavarṇāni puṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca
c visṛjantau mahāvṛkṣau tad vanaṃ vyāpya tiṣṭhataḥ
d visṛjanto mahāvṛkṣā vyāpya tiṣṭhanti tad vanam
a eko hy agniḥ sumanā brāhmaṇo 'tra
pañcendriyāṇi samidhaś cātra santi
c tebhyo mokṣāḥ sapta bhavanti dīkṣā
guṇāḥ phalāny atithayaḥ phalāśāḥ
a ātithyaṃ pratigṛhṇanti tatra sapta maharṣayaḥ
c arciteṣu pralīneṣu teṣv anyad rocate vanam
a pratijñāvṛkṣam aphalaṃ śānticchāyāsamanvitam
c jñānāśrayaṃ tṛptitoyam antaḥkṣetrajñabhāskaram
a ye 'dhigacchanti tat santas teṣāṃ nāsti bhayaṃ punaḥ
c ūrdhvaṃ cāvāk ca tiryak ca tasya nānto 'dhigamyate
a sapta striyas tatra vasanti sadyo
avāṅmukhā bhānumatyo janitryaḥ
c ūrdhvaṃ rasānāṃ dadate prajābhyaḥ
sarvān yathā sarvam anityatāṃ ca
a tatraiva pratitiṣṭhanti punas tatrodayanti ca
c sapta saptarṣayaḥ siddhā vasiṣṭhapramukhāḥ saha
a yaśo varco bhagaś caiva vijayaḥ siddhitejasī
c evam evānuvartante sapta jyotīṃṣi bhāskaram
a girayaḥ parvatāś caiva santi tatra samāsataḥ
c nadyaś ca sarito vāri vahantyo brahmasaṃbhavam
a nadīnāṃ saṃgamas tatra vaitānaḥ samupahvare
c svātmatṛptā yato yānti sākṣād dāntāḥ pitāmaham
a kṛśāśāḥ suvratāśāś ca tapasā dagdhakilbiṣāḥ
c ātmany ātmānam āveśya brahmāṇaṃ samupāsate
a ṛcam apy atra śaṃsanti vidyāraṇyavido janāḥ
c tad araṇyam abhipretya yathādhīram ajāyata
a etad etādṛśaṃ divyam araṇyaṃ brāhmaṇā viduḥ
c viditvā cānvatiṣṭhanta kṣetrajñenānudarśitam
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a gandhān na jighrāmi rasān na vedmi
rūpaṃ na paśyāmi na ca spṛśāmi
c na cāpi śabdān vividhāñ śṛṇomi
na cāpi saṃkalpam upaimi kiṃ cit
a arthān iṣṭān kāmayate svabhāvaḥ
sarvān dveṣyān pradviṣate svabhāvaḥ
c kāmadveṣāv udbhavataḥ svabhāvāt
prāṇāpānau jantudehān niveśya
a tebhyaś cānyāṃs teṣv anityāṃś ca bhāvān
bhūtātmānaṃ lakṣayeyaṃ śarīre
c tasmiṃs tiṣṭhan nāsmi śakyaḥ kathaṃ cit
kāmakrodhābhyāṃ jarayā mṛtyunā ca
a akāmayānasya ca sarvakāmān
avidviṣāṇasya ca sarvadoṣān
c na me svabhāveṣu bhavanti lepās
toyasya bindor iva puṣkareṣu
c naujaṃ tu dehāni tathā sametya sic
a nityasya caitasya bhavanti nityā
nirīkṣamāṇasya bahūn svabhāvān
c na sajjate karmasu bhogajālaṃ
divīva sūryasya mayūkhajālam
a atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c adhvaryuyatisaṃvādaṃ taṃ nibodha yaśasvini
a prokṣyamāṇaṃ paśuṃ dṛṣṭvā yajñakarmaṇy athābravīt
c yatir adhvaryum āsīno hiṃseyam iti kutsayan
a tam adhvaryuḥ pratyuvāca nāyaṃ chāgo vinaśyati
c śreyasā yokṣyate jantur yadi śrutir iyaṃ tathā
a yo hy asya pārthivo bhāgaḥ pṛthivīṃ sa gamiṣyati
c yad asya vārijaṃ kiṃ cid apas tat pratipadyate
a sūryaṃ cakṣur diśaḥ śrotre prāṇo 'sya divam eva ca
c āgame vartamānasya na me doṣo 'sti kaś cana
 yatir uvāca
a prāṇair viyoge chāgasya yadi śreyaḥ prapaśyasi
c chāgārthe vartate yajño bhavataḥ kiṃ prayojanam
a anu tvā manyatāṃ mātā pitā bhrātā sakhāpi ca
c mantrayasvainam unnīya paravantaṃ viśeṣataḥ
a ya evam anumanyeraṃs tān bhavān praṣṭum arhati
c teṣām anumataṃ śrutvā śakyā kartuṃ vicāraṇā
a prāṇā apy asya chāgasya prāpitās te svayoniṣu
c śarīraṃ kevalaṃ śiṣṭaṃ niśceṣṭam iti me matiḥ
a indhanasya tu tulyena śarīreṇa vicetasā
c hiṃsā nirveṣṭukāmānām indhanaṃ paśusaṃjñitam
a ahiṃsā sarvadharmāṇām iti vṛddhānuśāsanam
c yad ahiṃsraṃ bhavet karma tat kāryam iti vidmahe
a ahiṃseti pratijñeyaṃ yadi vakṣyāmy ataḥ param
c śakyaṃ bahuvidhaṃ vaktuṃ bhavataḥ kāryadūṣaṇam
a ahiṃsā sarvabhūtānāṃ nityam asmāsu rocate
c pratyakṣataḥ sādhayāmo na parokṣam upāsmahe
 adhvaryur uvāca
a bhūmer gandhaguṇān bhuṅkṣe pibasy āpomayān rasān
c jyotiṣāṃ paśyase rūpaṃ spṛśasy anilajān guṇān
a śṛṇoṣy ākāśajaṃ śabdaṃ manasā manyase matim
c sarvāṇy etāni bhūtāni prāṇā iti ca manyase
a prāṇādāne ca nityo 'si hiṃsāyāṃ vartate bhavān
c nāsti ceṣṭā vinā hiṃsāṃ kiṃ vā tvaṃ manyase dvija
 yatir uvāca
a akṣaraṃ ca kṣaraṃ caiva dvaidhībhāvo 'yam ātmanaḥ
c akṣaraṃ tatra sadbhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ kṣara ucyate
a prāṇo jihvā manaḥ sattvaṃ svabhāvo rajasā saha
c bhāvair etair vimuktasya nirdvaṃdvasya nirāśiṣaḥ
a samasya sarvabhūteṣu nirmamasya jitātmanaḥ
c samantāt parimuktasya na bhayaṃ vidyate kva cit
 adhvaryur uvāca
a sadbhir eveha saṃvāsaḥ kāryo matimatāṃ vara
c bhavato hi mataṃ śrutvā pratibhāti matir mama
a bhagavan bhagavadbuddhyā pratibuddho bravīmy aham
c mataṃ mantuṃ kratuṃ kartuṃ nāparādho 'sti me dvija
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a upapattyā yatis tūṣṇīṃ vartamānas tataḥ param
c adhvaryur api nirmohaḥ pracacāra mahāmakhe
a evam etādṛśaṃ mokṣaṃ susūkṣmaṃ brāhmaṇā viduḥ
c viditvā cānutiṣṭhanti kṣetrajñenānudarśinā
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c kārtavīryasya saṃvādaṃ samudrasya ca bhāmini
a kārtavīryārjuno nāma rājā bāhusahasravān
c yena sāgaraparyantā dhanuṣā nirjitā mahī
a sa kadā cit samudrānte vicaran baladarpitaḥ
c avākirac charaśataiḥ samudram iti naḥ śrutam
a taṃ samudro namaskṛtya kṛtāñjalir uvāca ha
c mā muñca vīra nārācān brūhi kiṃ karavāṇi te
a madāśrayāṇi bhūtāni tvadvisṛṣṭair maheṣubhiḥ
c vadhyante rājaśārdūla tebhyo dehy abhayaṃ vibho
 arjuna uvāca
a matsamo yadi saṃgrāme śarāsanadharaḥ kva cit
c vidyate taṃ mamācakṣva yaḥ samāsīta māṃ mṛdhe
 samudra uvāca
a maharṣir jamadagnis te yadi rājan pariśrutaḥ
c tasya putras tavātithyaṃ yathāvat kartum arhati
a tataḥ sa rājā prayayau krodhena mahatā vṛtaḥ
c sa tam āśramam āgamya rāmam evānvapadyata
a sa rāmapratikūlāni cakāra saha bandhubhiḥ
c āyāsaṃ janayām āsa rāmasya ca mahātmanaḥ
a tatas tejaḥ prajajvāla rāmasyāmitatejasaḥ
c pradahad ripusainyāni tadā kamalalocane
a tataḥ paraśum ādāya sa taṃ bāhusahasriṇam
c ciccheda sahasā rāmo bāhuśākham iva drumam
a taṃ hataṃ patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sametāḥ sarvabāndhavāḥ
c asīn ādāya śaktīś ca bhārgavaṃ paryavārayan
a rāmo 'pi dhanur ādāya ratham āruhya satvaraḥ
c visṛjañ śaravarṣāṇi vyadhamat pārthivaṃ balam
a tatas tu kṣatriyāḥ ke cij jamadagniṃ nihatya ca
c viviśur giridurgāṇi mṛgāḥ siṃhārditā iva
a teṣāṃ svavihitaṃ karma tadbhayān nānutiṣṭhatām
c prajā vṛṣalatāṃ prāptā brāhmaṇānām adarśanāt
a ta ete dramiḍāḥ kāśāḥ puṇḍrāś ca śabaraiḥ saha
c vṛṣalatvaṃ parigatā vyutthānāt kṣatradharmataḥ
a tatas tu hatavīrāsu kṣatriyāsu punaḥ punaḥ
c dvijair utpāditaṃ kṣatraṃ jāmadagnyo nyakṛntata
a ekaviṃśatimedhānte rāmaṃ vāg aśarīriṇī
c divyā provāca madhurā sarvalokapariśrutā
a rāma rāma nivartasva kaṃ guṇaṃ tāta paśyasi
c kṣatrabandhūn imān prāṇair viprayojya punaḥ punaḥ
a tathaiva taṃ mahātmānam ṛcīkapramukhās tadā
c pitāmahā mahābhāga nivartasvety athābruvan
a pitur vadham amṛṣyaṃs tu rāmaḥ provāca tān ṛṣīn
c nārhantīha bhavanto māṃ nivārayitum ity uta
 pitara ūcuḥ
a nārhase kṣatrabandhūṃs tvaṃ nihantuṃ jayatāṃ vara
c na hi yuktaṃ tvayā hantuṃ brāhmaṇena satā nṛpān
 pitara ūcuḥ
a atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c śrutvā ca tat tathā kāryaṃ bhavatā dvijasattama
a alarko nāma rājarṣir abhavat sumahātapāḥ
c dharmajñaḥ satyasaṃdhaś ca mahātmā sumahāvrataḥ
a sa sāgarāntāṃ dhanuṣā vinirjitya mahīm imām
c kṛtvā suduṣkaraṃ karma manaḥ sūkṣme samādadhe
a sthitasya vṛkṣamūle 'tha tasya cintā babhūva ha
c utsṛjya sumahad rājyaṃ sūkṣmaṃ prati mahāmate
 alarka uvāca
a manaso me balaṃ jātaṃ mano jitvā dhruvo jayaḥ
c anyatra bāṇān asyāmi śatrubhiḥ parivāritaḥ
a yad idaṃ cāpalān mūrteḥ sarvam etac cikīrṣati
c manaḥ prati sutīkṣṇāgrān ahaṃ mokṣyāmi sāyakān
 mana uvāca
a neme bāṇās tariṣyanti mām alarka kathaṃ cana
c tavaiva marma bhetsyanti bhinnamarmā mariṣyasi
a anyān bāṇān samīkṣasva yais tvaṃ māṃ sūdayiṣyasi
c tac chrutvā sa vicintyātha tato vacanam abravīt
d indriyārtheṣu sarveṣu buddhis teṣv iha gṛdhyati
d tasmād buddhiṃ prati śarān atimokṣyāmy ahaṃ śitān
 alarka uvāca
a āghrāya subahūn gandhāṃs tān eva pratigṛdhyati
c tasmād ghrāṇaṃ prati śarān pratimokṣyāmy ahaṃ śitān
 ghrāṇa uvāca
a neme bāṇās tariṣyanti mām alarka kathaṃ cana
c tavaiva marma bhetsyanti bhinnamarmā mariṣyasi
a anyān bāṇān samīkṣasva yais tvaṃ māṃ sūdayiṣyasi
c tac chrutvā sa vicintyātha tato vacanam abravīt
 alarka uvāca
a iyaṃ svādūn rasān bhuktvā tān eva pratigṛdhyati
c tasmāj jihvāṃ prati śarān pratimokṣyāmy ahaṃ śitān
 jihvovāca
a neme bāṇās tariṣyanti mām alarka kathaṃ cana
c tavaiva marma bhetsyanti bhinnamarmā mariṣyasi
a anyān bāṇān samīkṣasva yais tvaṃ māṃ sūdayiṣyasi
c tac chrutvā sa vicintyātha tato vacanam abravīt
 alarka uvāca
a spṛṣṭvā tvag vividhān sparśāṃs tān eva pratigṛdhyati
c tasmāt tvacaṃ pāṭayiṣye vividhaiḥ kaṅkapatribhiḥ
 tvag uvāca
a neme bāṇās tariṣyanti mām alarka kathaṃ cana
c tavaiva marma bhetsyanti bhinnamarmā mariṣyasi
a anyān bāṇān samīkṣasva yais tvaṃ māṃ sūdayiṣyasi
c tac chrutvā sa vicintyātha tato vacanam abravīt
 alarka uvāca
a śrutvā vai vividhāñ śabdāṃs tān eva pratigṛdhyati
c tasmāc chrotraṃ prati śarān pratimokṣyāmy ahaṃ śitān
 śrotra uvāca
a neme bāṇās tariṣyanti mām alarka kathaṃ cana
c tavaiva marma bhetsyanti tato hāsyasi jīvitam
a anyān bāṇān samīkṣasva yais tvaṃ māṃ sūdayiṣyasi
c tac chrutvā sa vicintyātha tato vacanam abravīt
 alarka uvāca
a dṛṣṭvā vai vividhān bhāvāṃs tān eva pratigṛdhyati
c tasmāc cakṣuḥ prati śarān pratimokṣyāmy ahaṃ śitān
 cakṣur uvāca
a neme bāṇās tariṣyanti mām alarka kathaṃ cana
c tavaiva marma bhetsyanti bhinnamarmā mariṣyasi
a anyān bāṇān samīkṣasva yais tvaṃ māṃ sūdayiṣyasi
c tac chrutvā sa vicintyātha tato vacanam abravīt
 alarka uvāca
a iyaṃ niṣṭhā bahuvidhā prajñayā tv adhyavasyati
c tasmād buddhiṃ prati śarān pratimokṣyāmy ahaṃ śitān
 buddhir uvāca
a neme bāṇās tariṣyanti mām alarka kathaṃ cana
c tavaiva marma bhetsyanti bhinnamarmā mariṣyasi
d anyān bāṇān samīkṣasva yais tvaṃ māṃ sūdayiṣyasi
 pitara ūcuḥ
a tato 'larkas tapo ghoram āsthāyātha suduṣkaram
c nādhyagacchat paraṃ śaktyā bāṇam eteṣu saptasu
e susamāhitacetās tu tato 'cintayata prabhuḥ
a sa vicintya ciraṃ kālam alarko dvijasattama
c nādhyagacchat paraṃ śreyo yogān matimatāṃ varaḥ
a sa ekāgraṃ manaḥ kṛtvā niścalo yogam āsthitaḥ
c indriyāṇi jaghānāśu bāṇenaikena vīryavān
e yogenātmānam āviśya saṃsiddhiṃ paramāṃ yayau
a vismitaś cāpi rājarṣir imāṃ gāthāṃ jagāda ha
c aho kaṣṭaṃ yad asmābhiḥ pūrvaṃ rājyam anuṣṭhitam
d bhogatṛṣṇāsamāyuktaiḥ pūrvaṃ rājyam upāsitam
e iti paścān mayā jñātaṃ yogān nāsti paraṃ sukham
a iti tvam api jānīhi rāma mā kṣatriyāñ jahi
c tapo ghoram upātiṣṭha tataḥ śreyo 'bhipatsyase
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a ity uktaḥ sa tapo ghoraṃ jāmadagnyaḥ pitāmahaiḥ
c āsthitaḥ sumahābhāgo yayau siddhiṃ ca durgamām
d ity uktaḥ pitṛbhiḥ so 'tha tapo ghoraṃ samāsthitaḥ
d jāmadagnyo mahābhāgaḥ siddhiṃ ca paramāṃ gataḥ
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a trayo vai ripavo loke nava vai guṇataḥ smṛtāḥ
c harṣaḥ stambho 'bhimānaś ca trayas te sāttvikā guṇāḥ
a śokaḥ krodho 'tisaṃrambho rājasās te guṇāḥ smṛtāḥ
c svapnas tandrī ca mohaś ca trayas te tāmasā guṇāḥ
a etān nikṛtya dhṛtimān bāṇasaṃghair atandritaḥ
c jetuṃ parān utsahate praśāntātmā jitendriyaḥ
a atra gāthāḥ kīrtayanti purākalpavido janāḥ
c ambarīṣeṇa yā gītā rājñā rājyaṃ praśāsatā
a samudīrṇeṣu doṣeṣu vadhyamāneṣu sādhuṣu
c jagrāha tarasā rājyam ambarīṣa iti śrutiḥ
a sa nigṛhya mahādoṣān sādhūn samabhipūjya ca
c jagāma mahatīṃ siddhiṃ gāthāṃ cemāṃ jagāda ha
a bhūyiṣṭhaṃ me jitā doṣā nihatāḥ sarvaśatravaḥ
c eko doṣo 'vaśiṣṭas tu vadhyaḥ sa na hato mayā
a yena yukto jantur ayaṃ vaitṛṣṇyaṃ nādhigacchati
c tṛṣṇārta iva nimnāni dhāvamāno na budhyate
a akāryam api yeneha prayuktaḥ sevate naraḥ
c taṃ lobham asibhis tīkṣṇair nikṛntantaṃ nikṛntata
a lobhād dhi jāyate tṛṣṇā tataś cintā prasajyate
c sa lipsamāno labhate bhūyiṣṭhaṃ rājasān guṇān
d tad avāptau tu labhate bhūyiṣṭhaṃ tāmasān guṇān
d etair doṣaiḥ punar dehī badhyamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ
d bhuktvā vai rājasān bhogāñ jāyate karma cehate
a sa tair guṇaiḥ saṃhatadehabandhanaḥ
punaḥ punar jāyati karma cehate
c janmakṣaye bhinnavikīrṇadehaḥ
punar mṛtyuṃ gacchati janmani sve
a tasmād enaṃ samyag avekṣya lobhaṃ
nigṛhya dhṛtyātmani rājyam icchet
c etad rājyaṃ nānyad astīti vidyād
yas tv atra rājā vijito mamaikaḥ
a iti rājñāmbarīṣeṇa gāthā gītā yaśasvinā
c ādhirājyaṃ puraskṛtya lobham ekaṃ nikṛntatā
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c brāhmaṇasya ca saṃvādaṃ janakasya ca bhāmini
a brāhmaṇaṃ janako rājā sannaṃ kasmiṃś cid āgame
c viṣaye me na vastavyam iti śiṣṭyartham abravīt
a ity uktaḥ pratyuvācātha brāhmaṇo rājasattamam
c ācakṣva viṣayaṃ rājan yāvāṃs tava vaśe sthitaḥ
a so 'nyasya viṣaye rājño vastum icchāmy ahaṃ vibho
c vacas te kartum icchāmi yathāśāstraṃ mahīpate
a ity uktaḥ sa tadā rājā brāhmaṇena yaśasvinā
c muhur uṣṇaṃ ca niḥśvasya na sa taṃ pratyabhāṣata
a tam āsīnaṃ dhyāyamānaṃ rājānam amitaujasam
c kaśmalaṃ sahasāgacchad bhānumantam iva grahaḥ
a samāśvāsya tato rājā vyapete kaśmale tadā
c tato muhūrtād iva taṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vākyam abravīt
a pitṛpaitāmahe rājye vaśye janapade sati
c viṣayaṃ nādhigacchāmi vicinvan pṛthivīm imām
a nādhyagacchaṃ yadā pṛthvyāṃ mithilā mārgitā mayā
c nādhyagacchaṃ yadā tasyāṃ svaprajā mārgitā mayā
a nādhyagacchaṃ yadā tāsu tadā me kaśmalo 'bhavat
c tato me kaśmalasyānte matiḥ punar upasthitā
a tayā na viṣayaṃ manye sarvo vā viṣayo mama
c ātmāpi cāyaṃ na mama sarvā vā pṛthivī mama
d yathā mama tathānyeṣām iti manye dvijottama
e uṣyatāṃ yāvad utsāho bhujyatāṃ yāvad iṣyate
a pitṛpaitāmahe rājye vaśye janapade sati
c brūhi kāṃ buddhim āsthāya mamatvaṃ varjitaṃ tvayā
a kāṃ vā buddhiṃ viniścitya sarvo vai viṣayas tava
c nāvaiṣi viṣayaṃ yena sarvo vā viṣayas tava
 janaka uvāca
a antavanta ihārambhā viditāḥ sarvakarmasu
c nādhyagaccham ahaṃ yasmān mamedam iti yad bhavet
a kasyedam iti kasya svam iti vedavacas tathā
c nādhyagaccham ahaṃ buddhyā mamedam iti yad bhavet
a etāṃ buddhiṃ viniścitya mamatvaṃ varjitaṃ mayā
c śṛṇu buddhiṃ tu yāṃ jñātvā sarvatra viṣayo mama
a nāham ātmārtham icchāmi gandhān ghrāṇagatān api
c tasmān me nirjitā bhūmir vaśe tiṣṭhati nityadā
a nāham ātmārtham icchāmi rasān āsye 'pi vartataḥ
c āpo me nirjitās tasmād vaśe tiṣṭhanti nityadā
a nāham ātmārtham icchāmi rūpaṃ jyotiś ca cakṣuṣā
c tasmān me nirjitaṃ jyotir vaśe tiṣṭhati nityadā
a nāham ātmārtham icchāmi sparśāṃs tvaci gatāś ca ye
c tasmān me nirjito vāyur vaśe tiṣṭhati nityadā
a nāham ātmārtham icchāmi śabdāñ śrotragatān api
c tasmān me nirjitāḥ śabdā vaśe tiṣṭhanti nityadā
a nāham ātmārtham icchāmi mano nityaṃ manontare
c mano me nirjitaṃ tasmād vaśe tiṣṭhati nityadā
a devebhyaś ca pitṛbhyaś ca bhūtebhyo 'tithibhiḥ saha
c ityarthaṃ sarva eveme samārambhā bhavanti vai
a tataḥ prahasya janakaṃ brāhmaṇaḥ punar abravīt
c tvajjijñāsārtham adyeha viddhi māṃ dharmam āgatam
a tvam asya brahmanābhasya buddhyārasyānivartinaḥ
c sattvaneminiruddhasya cakrasyaikaḥ pravartakaḥ
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a nāhaṃ tathā bhīru carāmi loke
tathā tvaṃ māṃ tarkayase svabuddhyā
c vipro 'smi mukto 'smi vanecaro 'smi
gṛhasthadharmā brahmacārī tathāsmi
a nāham asmi yathā māṃ tvaṃ paśyase cakṣuṣā śubhe
c mayā vyāptam idaṃ sarvaṃ yat kiṃ cij jagatīgatam
a ye ke cij jantavo loke jaṅgamāḥ sthāvarāś ca ha
c teṣāṃ mām antakaṃ viddhi dārūṇām iva pāvakam
a rājyaṃ pṛthivyāṃ sarvasyām atha vāpi triviṣṭape
c tathā buddhir iyaṃ vetti buddhir eva dhanaṃ mama
a ekaḥ panthā brāhmaṇānāṃ yena gacchanti tadvidaḥ
c gṛheṣu vanavāseṣu guruvāseṣu bhikṣuṣu
e liṅgair bahubhir avyagrair ekā buddhir upāsyate
a nānāliṅgāśramasthānāṃ yeṣāṃ buddhiḥ śamātmikā
c te bhāvam ekam āyānti saritaḥ sāgaraṃ yathā
a buddhyāyaṃ gamyate mārgaḥ śarīreṇa na gamyate
c ādyantavanti karmāṇi śarīraṃ karmabandhanam
a tasmāt te subhage nāsti paralokakṛtaṃ bhayam
c madbhāvabhāvaniratā mamaivātmānam eṣyasi
 brāhmaṇy uvāca
a nedam alpātmanā śakyaṃ vedituṃ nākṛtātmanā
c bahu cālpaṃ ca saṃkṣiptaṃ viplutaṃ ca mataṃ mama
a upāyaṃ tu mama brūhi yenaiṣā labhyate matiḥ
c tan manye kāraṇatamaṃ yata eṣā pravartate
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a araṇīṃ brāhmaṇīṃ viddhi gurur asyottarāraṇiḥ
c tapaḥśrute 'bhimathnīto jñānāgnir jāyate tataḥ
 brāhmaṇy uvāca
a yad idaṃ brahmaṇo liṅgaṃ kṣetrajñam iti saṃjñitam
c grahītuṃ yena tac chakyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ tasya tat kva nu
 brāhmaṇa uvāca
a aliṅgo nirguṇaś caiva kāraṇaṃ nāsya vidyate
c upāyam eva vakṣyāmi yena gṛhyeta vā na vā
a samyag apy upadiṣṭaś ca bhramarair iva lakṣyate
c karmabuddhir abuddhitvāj jñānaliṅgair ivāśritam
a idaṃ kāryam idaṃ neti na mokṣeṣūpadiśyate
c paśyataḥ śṛṇvato buddhir ātmano yeṣu jāyate
a yāvanta iha śakyeraṃs tāvato 'ṃśān prakalpayet
c vyaktān avyaktarūpāṃś ca śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a sarvān nānātvayuktāṃś ca sarvān pratyakṣahetukān
c yataḥ paraṃ na vidyeta tato 'bhyāse bhaviṣyati
 vāsudeva uvāca
a tatas tu tasyā brāhmaṇyā matiḥ kṣetrajñasaṃkṣaye
c kṣetrajñād eva parataḥ kṣetrajño 'nyaḥ pravartate
 arjuna uvāca
a kva nu sā brāhmaṇī kṛṣṇa kva cāsau brāhmaṇarṣabhaḥ
c yābhyāṃ siddhir iyaṃ prāptā tāv ubhau vada me 'cyuta
 vāsudeva uvāca
a mano me brāhmaṇaṃ viddhi buddhiṃ me viddhi brāhmaṇīm
c kṣetrajña iti yaś coktaḥ so 'ham eva dhanaṃjaya
 arjuna uvāca
a brahma yat paramaṃ vedyaṃ tan me vyākhyātum arhasi
c bhavato hi prasādena sūkṣme me ramate matiḥ
 vāsudeva uvāca
a atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c saṃvādaṃ mokṣasaṃyuktaṃ śiṣyasya guruṇā saha
a kaś cid brāhmaṇam āsīnam ācāryaṃ saṃśitavratam
c śiṣyaḥ papraccha medhāvī kiṃ svic chreyaḥ paraṃtapa
a bhagavantaṃ prapanno 'haṃ niḥśreyasaparāyaṇaḥ
c yāce tvāṃ śirasā vipra yad brūyāṃ tad vicakṣva me
a tam evaṃvādinaṃ pārtha śiṣyaṃ gurur uvāca ha
c kathayasva pravakṣyāmi yatra te saṃśayo dvija
a ity uktaḥ sa kuruśreṣṭha guruṇā guruvatsalaḥ
c prāñjaliḥ paripapraccha yat tac chṛṇu mahāmate
 śiṣya uvāca
a kutaś cāhaṃ kutaś ca tvaṃ tat satyaṃ brūhi yat param
c kuto jātāni bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca
a kena jīvanti bhūtāni teṣām āyuḥ kim ātmakam
c kiṃ satyaṃ kiṃ tapo vipra ke guṇāḥ sadbhir īritāḥ
e ke panthānaḥ śivāḥ santi kiṃ sukhaṃ kiṃ ca duṣkṛtam
a etān me bhagavan praśnān yāthātathyena sattama
c vaktum arhasi viprarṣe yathāvad iha tattvataḥ
d tvad anyaḥ kaś ca na praśnān etān vaktum ihārhati
d brūhi dharmavidāṃ śreṣṭha paraṃ kautūhalaṃ mama
d mokṣadharmārthakuśalo bhavāṃl lokeṣu gīyate
d sarvasaṃśayasaṃchettā tvad anyo na ca vidyate
d saṃsārabhīravaś caiva mokṣakāmās tathā vayam
 vāsudeva uvāca
a tasmai saṃpratipannāya yathāvat paripṛcchate
c śiṣyāya guṇayuktāya śāntāya guruvartine
e chāyābhūtāya dāntāya yataye brahmacāriṇe
e kulīnāya suśīlāya bhaktāya brahmavādine
a tān praśnān abravīt pārtha medhāvī sa dhṛtavrataḥ
c guruḥ kurukulaśreṣṭha samyak sarvān ariṃdama
a brahmaproktam idaṃ dharmam ṛṣipravarasevitam
c vedavidyāsamāvāpyaṃ tattvabhūtārthabhāvanam
d jñānaṃ tv eva paraṃ vidmaḥ saṃnyāsaṃ tapa uttamam
d yas tu veda nirābādhaṃ jñānatattvaṃ viniścayāt
d sarvabhūtastham ātmānaṃ sa sarvagatir iṣyate
d yo vidvān sahavāsaṃ ca vivāsaṃ caiva paśyati
d tathaivaikatvanānātve sa duḥkhāt parimucyate
d yo na kāmayate kiṃ cin na kiṃ cid abhimanyate
d ihalokastha evaiṣa brahmabhūyāya kalpate
d pradhānaguṇatattvajñaḥ sarvabhūtavidhānavit
d nirmamo nirahaṃkāro mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
d avyaktabījaprabhavo buddhiskandhamayo mahān
d mahāhaṃkāraviṭapa indriyāṅkurakoṭaraḥ
d mahābhūtaviśeṣaś ca viśeṣapratiśākhavān
d sadāparṇaḥ sadāpuṣpaḥ sadāśubhaphalodayaḥ
d ājīvaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ brahmabījaḥ sanātanaḥ
d etaj jñātvā ca tattvena jñānena parāmāsinā
d chittvā cāmaratāṃ prāpya jahāti mṛtyujanmanī
a bhūtabhavyabhaviṣyādidharmakāmārthaniścayam
c siddhasaṃghaparijñātaṃ purākalpaṃ sanātanam
a pravakṣye 'haṃ mahāprājña padam uttamam adya te
c buddhvā yad iha saṃsiddhā bhavantīha manīṣiṇaḥ
a upagamyarṣayaḥ pūrvaṃ jijñāsantaḥ parasparam
c bṛhaspatibharadvājau gautamo bhārgavas tathā
a vasiṣṭhaḥ kāśyapaś caiva viśvāmitro 'trir eva ca
c mārgān sarvān parikramya pariśrāntāḥ svakarmabhiḥ
a ṛṣim āṅgirasaṃ vṛddhaṃ puraskṛtya tu te dvijāḥ
c dadṛśur brahmabhavane brahmāṇaṃ vītakalmaṣam
a taṃ praṇamya mahātmānaṃ sukhāsīnaṃ maharṣayaḥ
c papracchur vinayopetā niḥśreyasam idaṃ param
a kathaṃ karma kriyāt sādhu kathaṃ mucyeta kilbiṣāt
c ke no mārgāḥ śivāś ca syuḥ kiṃ satyaṃ kiṃ ca duṣkṛtam
a kenobhau karmapanthānau mahattvaṃ kena vindati
c pralayaṃ cāpavargaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ prabhavāpyayau
a ity uktaḥ sa muniśreṣṭhair yad āha prapitāmahaḥ
c tat te 'haṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi śṛṇu śiṣya yathāgamam
 brahmovāca
a satyād bhūtāni jātāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca
c tapasā tāni jīvanti iti tad vitta suvratāḥ
a svāṃ yoniṃ punar āgamya vartante svena karmaṇā
c satyaṃ hi guṇasaṃyuktaṃ niyataṃ pañcalakṣaṇam
a brahma satyaṃ tapaḥ satyaṃ satyaṃ caiva prajāpatiḥ
c satyād bhūtāni jātāni bhūtaṃ satyamayaṃ mahat
a tasmāt satyāśrayā viprā nityaṃ yogaparāyaṇāḥ
c atītakrodhasaṃtāpā niyatā dharmasetavaḥ
a anyonyaniyatān vaidyān dharmasetupravartakān
c tān ahaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi śāśvatān lokabhāvanān
a cāturvidyaṃ tathā varṇāṃś caturaś cāśramān pṛthak
c dharmam ekaṃ catuṣpādaṃ nityam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ
a panthānaṃ vaḥ pravakṣyāmi śivaṃ kṣemakaraṃ dvijāḥ
c niyataṃ brahmabhāvāya yātaṃ pūrvaṃ manīṣibhiḥ
a gadatas taṃ mamādyeha panthānaṃ durvidaṃ param
c nibodhata mahābhāgā nikhilena paraṃ padam
a brahmacārikam evāhur āśramaṃ prathamaṃ padam
c gārhasthyaṃ tu dvitīyaṃ syād vānaprastham ataḥ param
e tataḥ paraṃ tu vijñeyam adhyātmaṃ paramaṃ padam
a jyotir ākāśam ādityo vāyur indraḥ prajāpatiḥ
c nopaiti yāvad adhyātmaṃ tāvad etān na paśyati
e tasyopāyaṃ pravakṣyāmi purastāt taṃ nibodhata
a phalamūlānilabhujāṃ munīnāṃ vasatāṃ vane
c vānaprasthaṃ dvijātīnāṃ trayāṇām upadiśyate
a sarveṣām eva varṇānāṃ gārhasthyaṃ tad vidhīyate
c śraddhālakṣaṇam ity evaṃ dharmaṃ dhīrāḥ pracakṣate
d naiṣṭhiko 'tha yatir vāpi vibhakto brahmacāriṇaḥ
a ity ete devayānā vaḥ panthānaḥ parikīrtitāḥ
c sadbhir adhyāsitā dhīraiḥ karmabhir dharmasetavaḥ
a eteṣāṃ pṛthag adhyāste yo dharmaṃ saṃśitavrataḥ
c kālāt paśyati bhūtānāṃ sadaiva prabhavāpyayau
a atas tattvāni vakṣyāmi yāthātathyena hetunā
c viṣayasthāni sarvāṇi vartamānāni bhāgaśaḥ
a mahān ātmā tathāvyaktam ahaṃkāras tathaiva ca
c indriyāṇi daśaikaṃ ca mahābhūtāni pañca ca
a viśeṣāḥ pañcabhūtānām ity eṣā vaidikī śrutiḥ
c caturviṃśatir eṣā vas tattvānāṃ saṃprakīrtitā
a tattvānām atha yo veda sarveṣāṃ prabhavāpyayau
c sa dhīraḥ sarvabhūteṣu na moham adhigacchati
a tattvāni yo vedayate yathātathaṃ
guṇāṃś ca sarvān akhilāś ca devatāḥ
c vidhūtapāpmā pravimucya bandhanaṃ
sa sarvalokān amalān samaśnute
 brahmovāca
a tad avyaktam anudriktaṃ sarvavyāpi dhruvaṃ sthiram
c navadvāraṃ puraṃ vidyāt triguṇaṃ pañcadhātukam
a ekādaśaparikṣepaṃ mano vyākaraṇātmakam
c buddhisvāmikam ity etat param ekādaśaṃ bhavet
a trīṇi srotāṃsi yāny asminn āpyāyante punaḥ punaḥ
c praṇāḍyas tisra evaitāḥ pravartante guṇātmikāḥ
a tamo rajas tathā sattvaṃ guṇān etān pracakṣate
c anyonyamithunāḥ sarve tathānyonyānujīvinaḥ
a anyonyāpāśrayāś caiva tathānyonyānuvartinaḥ
c anyonyavyatiṣaktāś ca triguṇāḥ pañca dhātavaḥ
a tamaso mithunaṃ sattvaṃ sattvasya mithunaṃ rajaḥ
c rajasaś cāpi sattvaṃ syāt sattvasya mithunaṃ tamaḥ
a niyamyate tamo yatra rajas tatra pravartate
c niyamyate rajo yatra sattvaṃ tatra pravartate
a naiśātmakaṃ tamo vidyāt triguṇaṃ mohasaṃjñitam
c adharmalakṣaṇaṃ caiva niyataṃ pāpakarmasu
d tāmasaṃ rūpam etat tu dṛśyate cāpi saṃgatam
a pravṛttyātmakam evāhū rajaḥ paryāyakārakam
c pravṛttaṃ sarvabhūteṣu dṛśyatotpattilakṣaṇam
a prakāśaṃ sarvabhūteṣu lāghavaṃ śraddadhānatā
c sāttvikaṃ rūpam evaṃ tu lāghavaṃ sādhusaṃmitam
a eteṣāṃ guṇatattvaṃ hi vakṣyate hetvahetubhiḥ
c samāsavyāsayuktāni tattvatas tāni vitta me
a saṃmoho 'jñānam atyāgaḥ karmaṇām avinirṇayaḥ
c svapnaḥ stambho bhayaṃ lobhaḥ śokaḥ sukṛtadūṣaṇam
a asmṛtiś cāvipākaś ca nāstikyaṃ bhinnavṛttitā
c nirviśeṣatvam andhatvaṃ jaghanyaguṇavṛttitā
a akṛte kṛtamānitvam ajñāne jñānamānitā
c amaitrī vikṛto bhāvo aśraddhā mūḍhabhāvanā
a anārjavam asaṃjñatvaṃ karma pāpam acetanā
c gurutvaṃ sannabhāvatvam asitatvam avāg gatiḥ
a sarva ete guṇā viprās tāmasāḥ saṃprakīrtitāḥ
c ye cānye niyatā bhāvā loke 'smin mohasaṃjñitāḥ
a tatra tatra niyamyante sarve te tāmasā guṇāḥ
c parivādakathā nityaṃ devabrāhmaṇavaidikāḥ
a atyāgaś cābhimānaś ca moho manyus tathākṣamā
c matsaraś caiva bhūteṣu tāmasaṃ vṛttam iṣyate
a vṛthārambhāś ca ye ke cid vṛthādānāni yāni ca
c vṛthābhakṣaṇam ity etat tāmasaṃ vṛttam iṣyate
a ativādo 'titikṣā ca mātsaryam atimānitā
c aśraddadhānatā caiva tāmasaṃ vṛttam iṣyate
a evaṃvidhās tu ye ke cil loke 'smin pāpakarmiṇaḥ
c manuṣyā bhinnamaryādāḥ sarve te tāmasā janāḥ
a teṣāṃ yoniṃ pravakṣyāmi niyatāṃ pāpakarmaṇām
c avāṅnirayabhāvāya tiryaṅnirayagāminaḥ
a sthāvarāṇi ca bhūtāni paśavo vāhanāni ca
c kravyādā dandaśūkāś ca kṛmikīṭavihaṃgamāḥ
a aṇḍajā jantavo ye ca sarve cāpi catuṣpadāḥ
c unmattā badhirā mūkā ye cānye pāparogiṇaḥ
a magnās tamasi durvṛttāḥ svakarmakṛtalakṣaṇāḥ
c avāksrotasa ity ete magnās tamasi tāmasāḥ
a teṣām utkarṣam udrekaṃ vakṣyāmy aham ataḥ param
c yathā te sukṛtāṃl lokāṃl labhante puṇyakarmiṇaḥ
a anyathā pratipannās tu vivṛddhā ye ca karmasu
c svakarmaniratānāṃ ca brāhmaṇānāṃ śubhaiṣiṇām
a saṃskāreṇordhvam āyānti yatamānāḥ salokatām
c svargaṃ gacchanti devānām ity eṣā vaidikī śrutiḥ
a anyathā pratipannās tu vivṛddhāḥ sveṣu karmasu
c punarāvṛttidharmāṇas te bhavantīha mānuṣāḥ
a pāpayoniṃ samāpannāś caṇḍālā mūkacūcukāḥ
c varṇān paryāyaśaś cāpi prāpnuvanty uttarottaram
a śūdrayonim atikramya ye cānye tāmasā guṇāḥ
c srotomadhye samāgamya vartante tāmase guṇe
a abhiṣaṅgas tu kāmeṣu mahāmoha iti smṛtaḥ
c ṛṣayo munayo devā muhyanty atra sukhepsavaḥ
a tamo moho mahāmohas tāmisraḥ krodhasaṃjñitaḥ
c maraṇaṃ tv andhatāmisraṃ tāmisraṃ krodha ucyate
a bhāvato guṇataś caiva yonitaś caiva tattvataḥ
c sarvam etat tamo viprāḥ kīrtitaṃ vo yathāvidhi
a ko nv etad budhyate sādhu ko nv etat sādhu paśyati
c atattve tattvadarśī yas tamasas tattvalakṣaṇam
a tamoguṇā vo bahudhā prakīrtitā
yathāvad uktaṃ ca tamaḥ parāvaram
c naro hi yo veda guṇān imān sadā
sa tāmasaiḥ sarvaguṇaiḥ pramucyate
 brahmovāca
a rajo 'haṃ vaḥ pravakṣyāmi yāthātathyena sattamāḥ
c nibodhata mahābhāgā guṇavṛttaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
a saṃghāto rūpam āyāsaḥ sukhaduḥkhe himātapau
c aiśvaryaṃ vigrahaḥ saṃdhir hetuvādo 'ratiḥ kṣamā
a balaṃ śauryaṃ mado roṣo vyāyāmakalahāv api
c īrṣyepsā paiśunaṃ yuddhaṃ mamatvaṃ paripālanam
a vadhabandhaparikleśāḥ krayo vikraya eva ca
c nikṛnta chindhi bhindhīti paramarmāvakartanam
a ugraṃ dāruṇam ākrośaḥ paravittānuśāsanam
c lokacintā vicintā ca matsaraḥ paribhāṣaṇam
a mṛṣāvādo mṛṣādānaṃ vikalpaḥ paribhāṣaṇam
c nindā stutiḥ praśaṃsā ca pratāpaḥ paritarpaṇam
a paricaryā ca śuśrūṣā sevā tṛṣṇā vyapāśrayaḥ
c vyūho 'nayaḥ pramādaś ca paritāpaḥ parigrahaḥ
a saṃskārā ye ca loke 'smin pravartante pṛthak pṛthak
c nṛṣu nārīṣu bhūteṣu dravyeṣu śaraṇeṣu ca
a saṃtāpo 'pratyayaś caiva vratāni niyamāś ca ye
c pradānam āśīryuktaṃ ca satataṃ me bhavatv iti
d āśīryuktāni karmāṇi paurtāni vividhāni ca
a svadhākāro namaskāraḥ svāhākāro vaṣaṭkriyā
c yājanādhyāpane cobhe tathaivāhuḥ parigraham
d dānaṃ pratigrahaś caiva prāyaścittāni maṅgalam
a idaṃ me syād idaṃ me syāt sneho guṇasamudbhavaḥ
c abhidrohas tathā māyā nikṛtir māna eva ca
a stainyaṃ hiṃsā parīvādaḥ paritāpaḥ prajāgaraḥ
c stambho dambho 'tha rāgaś ca bhaktiḥ prītiḥ pramodanam
a dyūtaṃ ca janavādaś ca saṃbandhāḥ strīkṛtāś ca ye
c nṛttavāditragītāni prasaṅgā ye ca ke cana
e sarva ete guṇā viprā rājasāḥ saṃprakīrtitāḥ
a bhūtabhavyabhaviṣyāṇāṃ bhāvānāṃ bhuvi bhāvanāḥ
c trivarganiratā nityaṃ dharmo 'rthaḥ kāma ity api
a kāmavṛttāḥ pramodante sarvakāmasamṛddhibhiḥ
c arvāksrotasa ity ete taijasā rajasāvṛtāḥ
a asmiṃl loke pramodante jāyamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ
c pretyabhāvikam īhanta iha laukikam eva ca
d pretyabhāvakarīṃ siddhim īhante rājasā janāḥ
e dadati pratigṛhṇanti japanty atha ca juhvati
a rajoguṇā vo bahudhānukīrtitā
yathāvad uktaṃ guṇavṛttam eva ca
c naro hi yo veda guṇān imān sadā
sa rājasaiḥ sarvaguṇair vimucyate
 brahmovāca
a ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi tṛtīyaṃ guṇam uttamam
c sarvabhūtahitaṃ loke satāṃ dharmam aninditam
a ānandaḥ prītir udrekaḥ prākāśyaṃ sukham eva ca
c akārpaṇyam asaṃrambhaḥ saṃtoṣaḥ śraddadhānatā
a kṣamā dhṛtir ahiṃsā ca samatā satyam ārjavam
c akrodhaś cānasūyā ca śaucaṃ dākṣyaṃ parākramaḥ
a mudhā jñānaṃ mudhā vṛttaṃ mudhā sevā mudhā śramaḥ
c evaṃ yo yuktadharmaḥ syāt so 'mutrānantyam aśnute
a nirmamo nirahaṃkāro nirāśīḥ sarvataḥ samaḥ
c akāmahata ity eṣa satāṃ dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ
a viśrambho hrīs titikṣā ca tyāgaḥ śaucam atandritā
c ānṛśaṃsyam asaṃmoho dayā bhūteṣv apaiśunam
a harṣas tuṣṭir vismayaś ca vinayaḥ sādhuvṛttatā
c śāntikarma viśuddhiś ca śubhā buddhir vimocanam
a upekṣā brahmacaryaṃ ca parityāgaś ca sarvaśaḥ
c nirmamatvam anāśīstvam aparikrītadharmatā
a mudhā dānaṃ mudhā yajño mudhādhītaṃ mudhā vratam
c mudhā pratigrahaś caiva mudhā dharmo mudhā tapaḥ
a evaṃvṛttās tu ye ke cil loke 'smin sattvasaṃśrayāḥ
c brāhmaṇā brahmayonisthās te dhīrāḥ sādhudarśinaḥ
a hitvā sarvāṇi pāpāni niḥśokā hy ajarāmarāḥ
c divaṃ prāpya tu te dhīrāḥ kurvate vai tatas tataḥ
a īśitvaṃ ca vaśitvaṃ ca laghutvaṃ manasaś ca te
c vikurvate mahātmāno devās tridivagā iva
a ūrdhvasrotasa ity ete devā vaikārikāḥ smṛtāḥ
c vikurvate prakṛtyā vai divaṃ prāptās tatas tataḥ
e yad yad icchanti tat sarvaṃ bhajante vibhajanti ca
a ity etat sāttvikaṃ vṛttaṃ kathitaṃ vo dvijarṣabhāḥ
c etad vijñāya vidhival labhate yad yad icchati
a prakīrtitāḥ sattvaguṇā viśeṣato
yathāvad uktaṃ guṇavṛttam eva ca
c naras tu yo veda guṇān imān sadā
guṇān sa bhuṅkte na guṇaiḥ sa bhujyate
 brahmovāca
a naiva śakyā guṇā vaktuṃ pṛthaktveneha sarvaśaḥ
c avicchinnāni dṛśyante rajaḥ sattvaṃ tamas tathā
a anyonyam anuṣajjante anyonyaṃ cānujīvinaḥ
c anyonyāpāśrayāḥ sarve tathānyonyānuvartinaḥ
a yāvat sattvaṃ tamas tāvad vartate nātra saṃśayaḥ
c yāvat tamaś ca sattvaṃ ca rajas tāvad ihocyate
a saṃhatya kurvate yātrāṃ sahitāḥ saṃghacāriṇaḥ
c saṃghātavṛttayo hy ete vartante hetvahetubhiḥ
a udrekavyatirekāṇāṃ teṣām anyonyavartinām
c vartate tad yathānyūnaṃ vyatiriktaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
a vyatiriktaṃ tamo yatra tiryagbhāvagataṃ bhavet
c alpaṃ tatra rajo jñeyaṃ sattvaṃ cālpataraṃ tataḥ
a udriktaṃ ca rajo yatra madhyasrotogataṃ bhavet
c alpaṃ tatra tamo jñeyaṃ sattvaṃ cālpataraṃ tataḥ
a udriktaṃ ca yadā sattvam ūrdhvasrotogataṃ bhavet
c alpaṃ tatra rajo jñeyaṃ tamaś cālpataraṃ tataḥ
a sattvaṃ vaikārikaṃ yonir indriyāṇāṃ prakāśikā
c na hi sattvāt paro bhāvaḥ kaś cid anyo vidhīyate
a ūrdhvaṃ gacchanti sattvasthā madhye tiṣṭhanti rājasāḥ
c jaghanyaguṇasaṃyuktā yānty adhas tāmasā janāḥ
a tamaḥ śūdre rajaḥ kṣatre brāhmaṇe sattvam uttamam
c ity evaṃ triṣu varṇeṣu vivartante guṇās trayaḥ
a dūrād api hi dṛśyante sahitāḥ saṃghacāriṇaḥ
c tamaḥ sattvaṃ rajaś caiva pṛthaktvaṃ nānuśuśruma
a dṛṣṭvā cādityam udyantaṃ kucorāṇāṃ bhayaṃ bhavet
c adhvagāḥ paritapyeraṃs tṛṣṇārtā duḥkhabhāginaḥ
a ādityaḥ sattvam uddiṣṭaṃ kucorās tu yathā tamaḥ
c paritāpo 'dhvagānāṃ ca rājaso guṇa ucyate
a prākāśyaṃ sattvam āditye saṃtāpo rājaso guṇaḥ
c upaplavas tu vijñeyas tāmasas tasya parvasu
a evaṃ jyotiḥṣu sarveṣu vivartante guṇās trayaḥ
c paryāyeṇa ca vartante tatra tatra tathā tathā
a sthāvareṣu ca bhūteṣu tiryagbhāvagataṃ tamaḥ
c rājasās tu vivartante snehabhāvas tu sāttvikaḥ
a ahas tridhā tu vijñeyaṃ tridhā rātrir vidhīyate
c māsārdhamāsavarṣāṇi ṛtavaḥ saṃdhayas tathā
a tridhā dānāni dīyante tridhā yajñaḥ pravartate
c tridhā lokās tridhā vedās tridhā vidyās tridhā gatiḥ
a bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyac ca dharmo 'rthaḥ kāma ity api
c prāṇāpānāv udānaś cāpy eta eva trayo guṇāḥ
a yat kiṃ cid iha vai loke sarvam eṣv eva tat triṣu
c trayo guṇāḥ pravartante avyaktā nityam eva tu
e sattvaṃ rajas tamaś caiva guṇasargaḥ sanātanaḥ
a tamo 'vyaktaṃ śivaṃ nityam ajaṃ yoniḥ sanātanaḥ
c prakṛtir vikāraḥ pralayaḥ pradhānaṃ prabhavāpyayau
a anudriktam anūnaṃ ca hy akampam acalaṃ dhruvam
c sad asac caiva tat sarvam avyaktaṃ triguṇaṃ smṛtam
e jñeyāni nāmadheyāni narair adhyātmacintakaiḥ
a avyaktanāmāni guṇāṃś ca tattvato
yo veda sarvāṇi gatīś ca kevalāḥ
c vimuktadehaḥ pravibhāgatattvavit
sa mucyate sarvaguṇair nirāmayaḥ
 brahmovāca
a avyaktāt pūrvam utpanno mahān ātmā mahāmatiḥ
c ādir guṇānāṃ sarveṣāṃ prathamaḥ sarga ucyate
a mahān ātmā matir viṣṇur viśvaḥ śaṃbhuś ca vīryavān
c buddhiḥ prajñopalabdhiś ca tathā khyātir dhṛtiḥ smṛtiḥ
a paryāyavācakaiḥ śabdair mahān ātmā vibhāvyate
c taṃ jānan brāhmaṇo vidvān na pramohaṃ nigacchati
a sarvataḥpāṇipādaś ca sarvatokṣiśiromukhaḥ
c sarvataḥśrutimāṃl loke sarvaṃ vyāpya sa tiṣṭhati
a mahāprabhārciḥ puruṣaḥ sarvasya hṛdi niśritaḥ
c aṇimā laghimā prāptir īśāno jyotir avyayaḥ
a tatra buddhimatāṃ lokāḥ saṃnyāsaniratāś ca ye
c dhyānino nityayogāś ca satyasaṃdhā jitendriyāḥ
a jñānavantaś ca ye ke cid alubdhā jitamanyavaḥ
c prasannamanaso dhīrā nirmamā nirahaṃkṛtāḥ
e vimuktāḥ sarva evaite mahattvam upayānti vai
a ātmano mahato veda yaḥ puṇyāṃ gatim uttamām
c sa dhīraḥ sarvalokeṣu na moham adhigacchati
e viṣṇur evādisargeṣu svayaṃbhūr bhavati prabhuḥ
a evaṃ hi yo veda guhāśayaṃ prabhuṃ
naraḥ purāṇaṃ puruṣaṃ viśvarūpam
c hiraṇmayaṃ buddhimatāṃ parāṃ gatiṃ
sa buddhimān buddhim atītya tiṣṭhati
 brahmovāca
a ya utpanno mahān pūrvam ahaṃkāraḥ sa ucyate
c aham ity eva saṃbhūto dvitīyaḥ sarga ucyate
a ahaṃkāraś ca bhūtādir vaikārika iti smṛtaḥ
c tejasaś cetanā dhātuḥ prajāsargaḥ prajāpatiḥ
a devānāṃ prabhavo devo manasaś ca trilokakṛt
c aham ity eva tat sarvam abhimantā sa ucyate
a adhyātmajñānanityānāṃ munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanām
c svādhyāyakratusiddhānām eṣa lokaḥ sanātanaḥ
a ahaṃkāreṇāharato guṇān imān
bhūtādir evaṃ sṛjate sa bhūtakṛt
c vaikārikaḥ sarvam idaṃ viceṣṭate
svatejasā rañjayate jagat tathā
 brahmovāca
a ahaṃkārāt prasūtāni mahābhūtāni pañca vai
c pṛthivī vāyur ākāśam āpo jyotiś ca pañcamam
a teṣu bhūtāni muhyante mahābhūteṣu pañcasu
c śabdasparśanarūpeṣu rasagandhakriyāsu ca
a mahābhūtavināśānte pralaye pratyupasthite
c sarvaprāṇabhṛtāṃ dhīrā mahad utpadyate bhayam
a yady asmāj jāyate bhūtaṃ tatra tat pravilīyate
c līyante pratilomāni jāyante cottarottaram
a tataḥ pralīne sarvasmin bhūte sthāvarajaṅgame
c smṛtimantas tadā dhīrā na līyante kadā cana
a śabdaḥ sparśas tathā rūpaṃ raso gandhaś ca pañcamaḥ
c kriyākāraṇayuktāḥ syur anityā mohasaṃjñitāḥ
a lobhaprajanasaṃyuktā nirviśeṣā hy akiṃcanāḥ
c māṃsaśoṇitasaṃghātā anyonyasyopajīvinaḥ
a bahir ātmāna ity ete dīnāḥ kṛpaṇavṛttayaḥ
c prāṇāpānāv udānaś ca samāno vyāna eva ca
a antarātmeti cāpy ete niyatāḥ pañca vāyavaḥ
c vāṅmanobuddhir ity ebhiḥ sārdham aṣṭātmakaṃ jagat
a tvagghrāṇaśrotracakṣūṃṣi rasanaṃ vāk ca saṃyatā
c viśuddhaṃ ca mano yasya buddhiś cāvyabhicāriṇī
a aṣṭau yasyāgnayo hy ete na dahante manaḥ sadā
c sa tad brahma śubhaṃ yāti yasmād bhūyo na vidyate
a ekādaśa ca yāny āhur indriyāṇi viśeṣataḥ
c ahaṃkāraprasūtāni tāni vakṣyāmy ahaṃ dvijāḥ
a śrotraṃ tvak cakṣuṣī jihvā nāsikā caiva pañcamī
c pādau pāyur upasthaṃ ca hastau vāg daśamī bhavet
a indriyagrāma ity eṣa mana ekādaśaṃ bhavet
c etaṃ grāmaṃ jayet pūrvaṃ tato brahma prakāśate
a buddhīndriyāṇi pañcāhuḥ pañca karmendriyāṇi ca
c śrotrādīny api pañcāhur buddhiyuktāni tattvataḥ
a aviśeṣāṇi cānyāni karmayuktāni tāni tu
c ubhayatra mano jñeyaṃ buddhir dvādaśamī bhavet
a ity uktānīndriyāṇīmāny ekādaśa mayā kramāt
c manyante kṛtam ity eva viditvaitāni paṇḍitāḥ
d ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvaṃ vividham indriyam
a trīṇi sthānāni bhūtānāṃ caturthaṃ nopapadyate
c sthalam āpas tathākāśaṃ janma cāpi caturvidham
a aṇḍajodbhijjasaṃsvedajarāyujam athāpi ca
c caturdhā janma ity etad bhūtagrāmasya lakṣyate
a acarāṇy api bhūtāni khecarāṇi tathaiva ca
c aṇḍajāni vijānīyāt sarvāṃś caiva sarīsṛpān
a saṃsvedāḥ kṛmayaḥ proktā jantavaś ca tathāvidhāḥ
c janma dvitīyam ity etaj jaghanyataram ucyate
a bhittvā tu pṛthivīṃ yāni jāyante kālaparyayāt
c udbhijjānīti tāny āhur bhūtāni dvijasattamāḥ
a dvipādabahupādāni tiryaggatimatīni ca
c jarāyujāni bhūtāni vitta tāny api sattamāḥ
a dvividhāpīha vijñeyā brahmayoniḥ sanātanā
c tapaḥ karma ca yat puṇyam ity eṣa viduṣāṃ nayaḥ
a dvividhaṃ karma vijñeyam ijyā dānaṃ ca yan makhe
c jātasyādhyayanaṃ puṇyam iti vṛddhānuśāsanam
a etad yo veda vidhivat sa muktaḥ syād dvijarṣabhāḥ
c vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhya iti caiva nibodhata
a ākāśaṃ prathamaṃ bhūtaṃ śrotram adhyātmam ucyate
c adhibhūtaṃ tathā śabdo diśas tatrādhidaivatam
a dvitīyaṃ māruto bhūtaṃ tvag adhyātmaṃ ca viśrutam
c spraṣṭavyam adhibhūtaṃ ca vidyut tatrādhidaivatam
a tṛtīyaṃ jyotir ity āhuś cakṣur adhyātmam ucyate
c adhibhūtaṃ tato rūpaṃ sūryas tatrādhidaivatam
a caturtham āpo vijñeyaṃ jihvā cādhyātmam iṣyate
b raso 'dhibhūtaṃ vijñeyam āpas tatrādhidaivatam
c adhibhūtaṃ rasaś cātra somas tatrādhidaivatam
a pṛthivī pañcamaṃ bhūtaṃ ghrāṇaś cādhyātmam iṣyate
c adhibhūtaṃ tathā gandho vāyus tatrādhidaivatam
a eṣa pañcasu bhūteṣu catuṣṭayavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ
c ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvaṃ trividham indriyam
a pādāv adhyātmam ity āhur brāhmaṇās tattvadarśinaḥ
c adhibhūtaṃ tu gantavyaṃ viṣṇus tatrādhidaivatam
a avāggatir apānaś ca pāyur adhyātmam iṣyate
c adhibhūtaṃ visargaś ca mitras tatrādhidaivatam
a prajanaḥ sarvabhūtānām upastho 'dhyātmam ucyate
c adhibhūtaṃ tathā śukraṃ daivataṃ ca prajāpatiḥ
a hastāv adhyātmam ity āhur adhyātmaviduṣo janāḥ
c adhibhūtaṃ tu karmāṇi śakras tatrādhidaivatam
a vaiśvadevī manaḥpūrvā vāg adhyātmam ihocyate
c vaktavyam adhibhūtaṃ ca vahnis tatrādhidaivatam
a adhyātmaṃ mana ity āhuḥ pañcabhūtānucārakam
c adhibhūtaṃ ca mantavyaṃ candramāś cādhidaivatam
d ahaṃkāras tathādhyātmaṃ sarvasaṃsārakārakam
d abhimāno 'dhibhūtaṃ ca rudras tatrādhidaivatam
a adhyātmaṃ buddhir ity āhuḥ ṣaḍindriyavicāriṇī
c adhibhūtaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ brahmā tatrādhidaivatam
a yathāvad adhyātmavidhir eṣa vaḥ kīrtito mayā
c jñānam asya hi dharmajñāḥ prāptaṃ buddhimatām iha
a indriyāṇīndriyārthāś ca mahābhūtāni pañca ca
c sarvāṇy etāni saṃdhāya manasā saṃpradhārayet
a kṣīṇe manasi sarvasmin na janmasukham iṣyate
c jñānasaṃpannasattvānāṃ tat sukhaṃ viduṣāṃ matam
a ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi sūkṣmabhāvakarīṃ śivām
c nivṛttiṃ sarvabhūteṣu mṛdunā dāruṇena vā
a guṇāguṇam anāsaṅgam ekacaryam anantaram
c etad brāhmaṇato vṛttam āhur ekapadaṃ sukham
a vidvān kūrma ivāṅgāni kāmān saṃhṛtya sarvaśaḥ
c virajāḥ sarvato mukto yo naraḥ sa sukhī sadā
a kāmān ātmani saṃyamya kṣīṇatṛṣṇaḥ samāhitaḥ
c sarvabhūtasuhṛn maitro brahmabhūyaṃ sa gacchati
a indriyāṇāṃ nirodhena sarveṣāṃ viṣayaiṣiṇām
c muner janapadatyāgād adhyātmāgniḥ samidhyate
a yathāgnir indhanair iddho mahājyotiḥ prakāśate
c tathendriyanirodhena mahān ātmā prakāśate
a yadā paśyati bhūtāni prasannātmātmano hṛdi
b etad eva hi loke 'smin mano hṛdi samāśritam
c svayaṃyonis tadā sūkṣmāt sūkṣmam āpnoty anuttamam
a agnī rūpaṃ payaḥ sroto vāyuḥ sparśanam eva ca
c mahī paṅkadharaṃ ghoram ākāśaṃ śravaṇaṃ tathā
d dṛśyam ādityam evāhur adhyātmaviduṣo janāḥ
a rāgaśokasamāviṣṭaṃ pañcasrotaḥsamāvṛtam
c pañcabhūtasamāyuktaṃ navadvāraṃ dvidaivatam
a rajasvalam athādṛśyaṃ triguṇaṃ ca tridhātukam
c saṃsargābhirataṃ mūḍhaṃ śarīram iti dhāraṇā
a duścaraṃ jīvaloke 'smin sattvaṃ prati samāśritam
c etad eva hi loke 'smin kālacakraṃ pravartate
a etan mahārṇavaṃ ghoram agādhaṃ mohasaṃjñitam
c visṛjet saṃkṣipec caiva bodhayet sāmaraṃ jagat
a kāmakrodhau bhayaṃ moham abhidroham athānṛtam
c indriyāṇāṃ nirodhena sa tāṃs tyajati dustyajān
a yasyaite nirjitā loke triguṇāḥ pañca dhātavaḥ
c vyomni tasya paraṃ sthānam anantam atha lakṣyate
a kāmakūlām apārāntāṃ manaḥsrotobhayāvahām
b pañcendriyamahākūlāṃ manovegamahodakām
c nadīṃ durgahradāṃ tīrṇaḥ kāmakrodhāv ubhau jayet
a sa sarvadoṣanirmuktas tataḥ paśyati yat param
c mano manasi saṃdhāya paśyaty ātmānam ātmani
a sarvavit sarvabhūteṣu vīkṣaty ātmānam ātmani
c ekadhā bahudhā caiva vikurvāṇas tatas tataḥ
a dhruvaṃ paśyati rūpāṇi dīpād dīpaśataṃ yathā
c sa vai viṣṇuś ca mitraś ca varuṇo 'gniḥ prajāpatiḥ
a sa hi dhātā vidhātā ca sa prabhuḥ sarvatomukhaḥ
c hṛdayaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ mahān ātmā prakāśate
a taṃ viprasaṃghāś ca surāsurāś ca
yakṣāḥ piśācāḥ pitaro vayāṃsi
c rakṣogaṇā bhūtagaṇāś ca sarve
maharṣayaś caiva sadā stuvanti
 brahmovāca
a manuṣyāṇāṃ tu rājanyaḥ kṣatriyo madhyamo guṇaḥ
c kuñjaro vāhanānāṃ ca siṃhaś cāraṇyavāsinām
a aviḥ paśūnāṃ sarveṣām ākhuś ca bilavāsinām
c gavāṃ govṛṣabhaś caiva strīṇāṃ puruṣa eva ca
a nyagrodho jambuvṛkṣaś ca pippalaḥ śālmalis tathā
c śiṃśapā meṣaśṛṅgaś ca tathā kīcakaveṇavaḥ
e ete drumāṇāṃ rājāno loke 'smin nātra saṃśayaḥ
a himavān pāriyātraś ca sahyo vindhyas trikūṭavān
c śveto nīlaś ca bhāsaś ca kāṣṭhavāṃś caiva parvataḥ
a śubhaskandho mahendraś ca mālyavān parvatas tathā
c ete parvatarājāno gaṇānāṃ marutas tathā
a sūryo grahāṇām adhipo nakṣatrāṇāṃ ca candramāḥ
c yamaḥ pitṝṇām adhipaḥ saritām atha sāgaraḥ
a ambhasāṃ varuṇo rājā sattvānāṃ mitra ucyate
c arko 'dhipatir uṣṇānāṃ jyotiṣām indur ucyate
a agnir bhūtapatir nityaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ bṛhaspatiḥ
c oṣadhīnāṃ patiḥ somo viṣṇur balavatāṃ varaḥ
a tvaṣṭādhirājo rūpāṇāṃ paśūnām īśvaraḥ śivaḥ
c dakṣiṇānāṃ tathā yajño vedānām ṛṣayas tathā
a diśām udīcī viprāṇāṃ somo rājā pratāpavān
c kuberaḥ sarvayakṣāṇāṃ devatānāṃ puraṃdaraḥ
e eṣa bhūtādikaḥ sargaḥ prajānāṃ ca prajāpatiḥ
a sarveṣām eva bhūtānām ahaṃ brahmamayo mahān
c bhūtaṃ parataraṃ matto viṣṇor vāpi na vidyate
a rājādhirājaḥ sarvāsāṃ viṣṇur brahmamayo mahān
c īśvaraṃ taṃ vijānīmaḥ sa vibhuḥ sa prajāpatiḥ
a narakiṃnarayakṣāṇāṃ gandharvoragarakṣasām
c devadānavanāgānāṃ sarveṣām īśvaro hi saḥ
a bhagadevānuyātānāṃ sarvāsāṃ vāmalocanā
c māheśvarī mahādevī procyate pārvatīti yā
a umāṃ devīṃ vijānīta nārīṇām uttamāṃ śubhām
c ratīnāṃ vasumatyas tu strīṇām apsarasas tathā
a dharmakāmāś ca rājāno brāhmaṇā dharmalakṣaṇāḥ
c tasmād rājā dvijātīnāṃ prayateteha rakṣaṇe
a rājñāṃ hi viṣaye yeṣām avasīdanti sādhavaḥ
c hīnās te svaguṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ pretyāvāṅmārgagāminaḥ
a rājñāṃ tu viṣaye yeṣāṃ sādhavaḥ parirakṣitāḥ
c te 'smiṃl loke pramodante pretya cānantyam eva ca
e prāpnuvanti mahātmāna iti vitta dvijarṣabhāḥ
a ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi niyataṃ dharmalakṣaṇam
c ahiṃsālakṣaṇo dharmo hiṃsā cādharmalakṣaṇā
a prakāśalakṣaṇā devā manuṣyāḥ karmalakṣaṇāḥ
c śabdalakṣaṇam ākāśaṃ vāyus tu sparśalakṣaṇaḥ
a jyotiṣāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ rūpam āpaś ca rasalakṣaṇāḥ
c dharaṇī sarvabhūtānāṃ pṛthivī gandhalakṣaṇā
a svaravyañjanasaṃskārā bhāratī satyalakṣaṇā
c manaso lakṣaṇaṃ cintā tathoktā buddhir anvayāt
a manasā cintayāno 'rthān buddhyā caiva vyavasyati
c buddhir hi vyavasāyena lakṣyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
a lakṣaṇaṃ mahato dhyānam avyaktaṃ sādhulakṣaṇam
c pravṛttilakṣaṇo yogo jñānaṃ saṃnyāsalakṣaṇam
a tasmāj jñānaṃ puraskṛtya saṃnyased iha buddhimān
c saṃnyāsī jñānasaṃyuktaḥ prāpnoti paramāṃ gatim
e atīto 'dvaṃdvam abhyeti tamomṛtyujarātigam
a dharmalakṣaṇasaṃyuktam uktaṃ vo vidhivan mayā
c guṇānāṃ grahaṇaṃ samyag vakṣyāmy aham ataḥ param
a pārthivo yas tu gandho vai ghrāṇeneha sa gṛhyate
c ghrāṇasthaś ca tathā vāyur gandhajñāne vidhīyate
a apāṃ dhāturaso nityaṃ jihvayā sa tu gṛhyate
c jihvāsthaś ca tathā somo rasajñāne vidhīyate
a jyotiṣaś ca guṇo rūpaṃ cakṣuṣā tac ca gṛhyate
c cakṣuḥsthaś ca tathādityo rūpajñāne vidhīyate
a vāyavyas tu tathā sparśas tvacā prajñāyate ca saḥ
c tvaksthaś caiva tathā vāyuḥ sparśajñāne vidhīyate
a ākāśasya guṇo ghoṣaḥ śrotreṇa sa tu gṛhyate
c śrotrasthāś ca diśaḥ sarvāḥ śabdajñāne prakīrtitāḥ
a manasas tu guṇaś cintā prajñayā sa tu gṛhyate
c hṛdisthacetanādhātur manojñāne vidhīyate
a buddhir adhyavasāyena dhyānena ca mahāṃs tathā
c niścitya grahaṇaṃ nityam avyaktaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ
a aliṅgagrahaṇo nityaḥ kṣetrajño nirguṇātmakaḥ
c tasmād aliṅgaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ kevalaṃ jñānalakṣaṇaḥ
a avyaktaṃ kṣetram uddiṣṭaṃ guṇānāṃ prabhavāpyayam
c sadā paśyāmy ahaṃ līnaṃ vijānāmi śṛṇomi ca
a puruṣas tad vijānīte tasmāt kṣetrajña ucyate
c guṇavṛttaṃ tathā kṛtsnaṃ kṣetrajñaḥ paripaśyati
a ādimadhyāvasānāntaṃ sṛjyamānam acetanam
c na guṇā vidur ātmānaṃ sṛjyamānaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
a na satyaṃ veda vai kaś cit kṣetrajñas tv eva vindati
c guṇānāṃ guṇabhūtānāṃ yat paraṃ parato mahat
a tasmād guṇāṃś ca tattvaṃ ca parityajyeha tattvavit
c kṣīṇadoṣo guṇān hitvā kṣetrajñaṃ praviśaty atha
a nirdvaṃdvo nirnamaskāro niḥsvadhākāra eva ca
c acalaś cāniketaś ca kṣetrajñaḥ sa paro vibhuḥ
 brahmovāca
a yad ādimadhyaparyantaṃ grahaṇopāyam eva ca
c nāmalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ sarvaṃ vakṣyāmi tattvataḥ
a ahaḥ pūrvaṃ tato rātrir māsāḥ śuklādayaḥ smṛtāḥ
c śraviṣṭhādīni ṛkṣāṇi ṛtavaḥ śiśirādayaḥ
a bhūmir ādis tu gandhānāṃ rasānām āpa eva ca
c rūpāṇāṃ jyotir ādis tu sparśādir vāyur ucyate
e śabdasyādis tathākāśam eṣa bhūtakṛto guṇaḥ
a ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi bhūtānām ādim uttamam
c ādityo jyotiṣām ādir agnir bhūtādir iṣyate
a sāvitrī sarvavidyānāṃ devatānāṃ prajāpatiḥ
c oṃkāraḥ sarvavedānāṃ vacasāṃ prāṇa eva ca
e yady asmin niyataṃ loke sarvaṃ sāvitram ucyate
a gāyatrī chandasām ādiḥ paśūnām aja ucyate
c gāvaś catuṣpadām ādir manuṣyāṇāṃ dvijātayaḥ
a śyenaḥ patatriṇām ādir yajñānāṃ hutam uttamam
c parisarpiṇāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ jyeṣṭhaḥ sarpo dvijottamāḥ
a kṛtam ādir yugānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ
c hiraṇyaṃ sarvaratnānām oṣadhīnāṃ yavās tathā
a sarveṣāṃ bhakṣyabhojyānām annaṃ paramam ucyate
c dravāṇāṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ peyānām āpa uttamāḥ
a sthāvarāṇāṃ ca bhūtānāṃ sarveṣām aviśeṣataḥ
c brahmakṣetraṃ sadā puṇyaṃ plakṣaḥ prathamajaḥ smṛtaḥ
a ahaṃ prajāpatīnāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ
c mama viṣṇur acintyātmā svayaṃbhūr iti sa smṛtaḥ
a parvatānāṃ mahāmeruḥ sarveṣām agrajaḥ smṛtaḥ
c diśāṃ ca pradiśāṃ cordhvā digjātā prathamaṃ tathā
a tathā tripathagā gaṅgā nadīnām agrajā smṛtā
c tathā sarodapānānāṃ sarveṣāṃ sāgaro 'grajaḥ
a devadānavabhūtānāṃ piśācoragarakṣasām
c narakiṃnarayakṣāṇāṃ sarveṣām īśvaraḥ prabhuḥ
a ādir viśvasya jagato viṣṇur brahmamayo mahān
c bhūtaṃ parataraṃ tasmāt trailokye neha vidyate
a āśramāṇāṃ ca gārhasthyaṃ sarveṣāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ
c lokānām ādir avyaktaṃ sarvasyāntas tad eva ca
a ahāny astamayāntāni udayāntā ca śarvarī
c sukhasyāntaḥ sadā duḥkhaṃ duḥkhasyāntaḥ sadā sukham
a sarve kṣayāntā nicayāḥ patanāntāḥ samucchrayāḥ
c saṃyogā viprayogāntā maraṇāntaṃ hi jīvitam
a sarvaṃ kṛtaṃ vināśāntaṃ jātasya maraṇaṃ dhruvam
c aśāśvataṃ hi loke 'smin sarvaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamam
a iṣṭaṃ dattaṃ tapo 'dhītaṃ vratāni niyamāś ca ye
c sarvam etad vināśāntaṃ jñānasyānto na vidyate
a tasmāj jñānena śuddhena prasannātmā samāhitaḥ
c nirmamo nirahaṃkāro mucyate sarvapāpmabhiḥ
 brahmovāca
a buddhisāraṃ manastambham indriyagrāmabandhanam
c mahābhūtāraviṣkambhaṃ nimeṣapariveṣṭanam
a jarāśokasamāviṣṭaṃ vyādhivyasanasaṃcaram
c deśakālavicārīdaṃ śramavyāyāmanisvanam
a ahorātraparikṣepaṃ śītoṣṇaparimaṇḍalam
c sukhaduḥkhāntasaṃkleśaṃ kṣutpipāsāvakīlanam
a chāyātapavilekhaṃ ca nimeṣonmeṣavihvalam
c ghoramohajanākīrṇaṃ vartamānam acetanam
a māsārdhamāsagaṇitaṃ viṣamaṃ lokasaṃcaram
c tamonicayapaṅkaṃ ca rajovegapravartakam
a sattvālaṃkāradīptaṃ ca guṇasaṃghātamaṇḍalam
c svaravigrahanābhīkaṃ śokasaṃghātavartanam
a kriyākāraṇasaṃyuktaṃ rāgavistāram āyatam
c lobhepsāparisaṃkhyātaṃ viviktajñānasaṃbhavam
a bhayamohaparīvāraṃ bhūtasaṃmohakārakam
c ānandaprītidhāraṃ ca kāmakrodhaparigraham
a mahadādiviśeṣāntam asaktaprabhavāvyayam
c manojavanam aśrāntaṃ kālacakraṃ pravartate
a etad dvaṃdvasamāyuktaṃ kālacakram acetanam
c visṛjet saṃkṣipec cāpi bodhayet sāmaraṃ jagat
a kālacakrapravṛttiṃ ca nivṛttiṃ caiva tattvataḥ
c yas tu veda naro nityaṃ na sa bhūteṣu muhyati
a vimuktaḥ sarvasaṃkleśaiḥ sarvadvaṃdvātigo muniḥ
c vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyaḥ prāpnoti paramāṃ gatim
a gṛhastho brahmacārī ca vānaprastho 'tha bhikṣukaḥ
c catvāra āśramāḥ proktāḥ sarve gārhasthyamūlakāḥ
a yaḥ kaś cid iha loke ca hy āgamaḥ saṃprakīrtitaḥ
c tasyāntagamanaṃ śreyaḥ kīrtir eṣā sanātanī
a saṃskāraiḥ saṃskṛtaḥ pūrvaṃ yathāvac caritavrataḥ
c jātau guṇaviśiṣṭāyāṃ samāvarteta vedavit
a svadāranirato dāntaḥ śiṣṭācāro jitendriyaḥ
c pañcabhiś ca mahāyajñaiḥ śraddadhāno yajeta ha
a devatātithiśiṣṭāśī nirato vedakarmasu
c ijyāpradānayuktaś ca yathāśakti yathāvidhi
a na pāṇipādacapalo na netracapalo muniḥ
c na ca vāgaṅgacapala iti śiṣṭasya gocaraḥ
a nityayajñopavītī syāc chuklavāsāḥ śucivrataḥ
c niyato damadānābhyāṃ sadā śiṣṭaiś ca saṃviśet
a jitaśiśnodaro maitraḥ śiṣṭācārasamāhitaḥ
c vaiṇavīṃ dhārayed yaṣṭiṃ sodakaṃ ca kamaṇḍalum
d trīṇi dhārayate nityaṃ kamaṇḍalum atandritaḥ
d ekam ācamanārthāya ekaṃ vai pādadhāvanam
d ekaṃ śaucavidhānārtham ity etat tritayaṃ tathā
a adhītyādhyāpanaṃ kuryāt tathā yajanayājane
c dānaṃ pratigrahaṃ caiva ṣaḍguṇāṃ vṛttim ācaret
a trīṇi karmāṇi yānīha brāhmaṇānāṃ tu jīvikā
c yājanādhyāpane cobhe śuddhāc cāpi pratigrahaḥ
a avaśeṣāṇi cānyāni trīṇi karmāṇi yāni tu
c dānam adhyayanaṃ yajño dharmayuktāni tāni tu
a teṣv apramādaṃ kurvīta triṣu karmasu dharmavit
c dānto maitraḥ kṣamāyuktaḥ sarvabhūtasamo muniḥ
a sarvam etad yathāśakti vipro nirvartayañ śuciḥ
c evaṃ yukto jayet svargaṃ gṛhasthaḥ saṃśitavrataḥ
 brahmovāca
a evam etena mārgeṇa pūrvoktena yathāvidhi
c adhītavān yathāśakti tathaiva brahmacaryavān
a svadharmanirato vidvān sarvendriyayato muniḥ
c guroḥ priyahite yuktaḥ satyadharmaparaḥ śuciḥ
a guruṇā samanujñāto bhuñjītānnam akutsayan
c haviṣyabhaikṣyabhuk cāpi sthānāsanavihāravān
a dvikālam agniṃ juhvānaḥ śucir bhūtvā samāhitaḥ
c dhārayīta sadā daṇḍaṃ bailvaṃ pālāśam eva vā
a kṣaumaṃ kārpāsikaṃ vāpi mṛgājinam athāpi vā
c sarvaṃ kāṣāyaraktaṃ syād vāso vāpi dvijasya ha
a mekhalā ca bhaven mauñjī jaṭī nityodakas tathā
c yajñopavītī svādhyāyī aluptaniyatavrataḥ
a pūtābhiś ca tathaivādbhiḥ sadā daivatatarpaṇam
c bhāvena niyataḥ kurvan brahmacārī praśasyate
a evaṃ yukto jayet svargam ūrdhvaretāḥ samāhitaḥ
c na saṃsarati jātīṣu paramaṃ sthānam āśritaḥ
a saṃskṛtaḥ sarvasaṃskārais tathaiva brahmacaryavān
c grāmān niṣkramya cāraṇyaṃ muniḥ pravrajito vaset
a carmavalkalasaṃvītaḥ svayaṃ prātar upaspṛśet
c araṇyagocaro nityaṃ na grāmaṃ praviśet punaḥ
a arcayann atithīn kāle dadyāc cāpi pratiśrayam
c phalapatrāvarair mūlaiḥ śyāmākena ca vartayan
a pravṛttam udakaṃ vāyuṃ sarvaṃ vāneyam ā tṛṇāt
c prāśnīyād ānupūrvyeṇa yathādīkṣam atandritaḥ
a āmūlaphalabhikṣābhir arced atithim āgatam
c yadbhakṣaḥ syāt tato dadyād bhikṣāṃ nityam atandritaḥ
a devatātithipūrvaṃ ca sadā bhuñjīta vāgyataḥ
c askanditamanāś caiva laghvāśī devatāśrayaḥ
a dānto maitraḥ kṣamāyuktaḥ keśaśmaśru ca dhārayan
c juhvan svādhyāyaśīlaś ca satyadharmaparāyaṇaḥ
a tyaktadehaḥ sadā dakṣo vananityaḥ samāhitaḥ
c evaṃ yukto jayet svargaṃ vānaprastho jitendriyaḥ
a gṛhastho brahmacārī ca vānaprastho 'tha vā punaḥ
c ya icchen mokṣam āsthātum uttamāṃ vṛttim āśrayet
a abhayaṃ sarvabhūtebhyo dattvā naiṣkarmyam ācaret
c sarvabhūtahito maitraḥ sarvendriyayato muniḥ
a ayācitam asaṃkḷptam upapannaṃ yadṛcchayā
c joṣayeta sadā bhojyaṃ grāsam āgatam aspṛhaḥ
a yātrāmātraṃ ca bhuñjīta kevalaṃ prāṇayātrikam
c dharmalabdhaṃ tathāśnīyān na kāmam anuvartayet
a grāsād ācchādanāc cānyan na gṛhṇīyāt kathaṃ cana
c yāvad āhārayet tāvat pratigṛhṇīta nānyathā
a parebhyo na pratigrāhyaṃ na ca deyaṃ kadā cana
c dainyabhāvāc ca bhūtānāṃ saṃvibhajya sadā budhaḥ
a nādadīta parasvāni na gṛhṇīyād ayācitam
c na kiṃ cid viṣayaṃ bhuktvā spṛhayet tasya vai punaḥ
a mṛdam āpas tathāśmānaṃ patrapuṣpaphalāni ca
c asaṃvṛtāni gṛhṇīyāt pravṛttānīha kāryavān
a na śilpajīvikāṃ jīved dvirannaṃ nota kāmayet
c na dveṣṭā nopadeṣṭā ca bhaveta nirupaskṛtaḥ
e śraddhāpūtāni bhuñjīta nimittāni vivarjayet
a mudhāvṛttir asaktaś ca sarvabhūtair asaṃvidam
c kṛtvā vahniṃ cared bhaikṣyaṃ vidhūme bhuktavajjane
a vṛtte śarāvasaṃpāte bhaikṣyaṃ lipseta mokṣavit
c lābhe na ca prahṛṣyeta nālābhe vimanā bhavet
d na cātibhikṣāṃ bhikṣeta kevalaṃ prāṇayātrikaḥ
a mātrāśī kālam ākāṅkṣaṃś cared bhaikṣyaṃ samāhitaḥ
c lābhaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ necchen na bhuñjītābhipūjitaḥ
e abhipūjitalābhād dhi vijugupseta bhikṣukaḥ
a śuktāny amlāni tiktāni kaṣāyakaṭukāni ca
c nāsvādayīta bhuñjāno rasāṃś ca madhurāṃs tathā
e yātrāmātraṃ ca bhuñjīta kevalaṃ prāṇayātrikam
a asaṃrodhena bhūtānāṃ vṛttiṃ lipseta mokṣavit
c na cānyam anubhikṣeta bhikṣamāṇaḥ kathaṃ cana
a na saṃnikāśayed dharmaṃ vivikte virajāś caret
c śūnyāgāram araṇyaṃ vā vṛkṣamūlaṃ nadīṃ tathā
e pratiśrayārthaṃ seveta pārvatīṃ vā punar guhām
a grāmaikarātriko grīṣme varṣāsv ekatra vā vaset
c adhvā sūryeṇa nirdiṣṭaḥ kīṭavac ca caren mahīm
a dayārthaṃ caiva bhūtānāṃ samīkṣya pṛthivīṃ caret
c saṃcayāṃś ca na kurvīta snehavāsaṃ ca varjayet
a pūtena cāmbhasā nityaṃ kāryaṃ kurvīta mokṣavit
c upaspṛśed uddhṛtābhir adbhiś ca puruṣaḥ sadā
a ahiṃsā brahmacaryaṃ ca satyam ārjavam eva ca
c akrodhaś cānasūyā ca damo nityam apaiśunam
a aṣṭāsv eteṣu yuktaḥ syād vrateṣu niyatendriyaḥ
c apāpam aśaṭhaṃ vṛttam ajihmaṃ nityam ācaret
a āśīryuktāni karmāṇi hiṃsāyuktāni yāni ca
c lokasaṃgrahadharmaṃ ca naiva kuryān na kārayet
a sarvabhāvān atikramya laghumātraḥ parivrajet
c samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu sthāvareṣu careṣu ca
a paraṃ nodvejayet kaṃ cin na ca kasya cid udvijet
c viśvāsyaḥ sarvabhūtānām agryo mokṣavid ucyate
a anāgataṃ ca na dhyāyen nātītam anucintayet
c vartamānam upekṣeta kālākāṅkṣī samāhitaḥ
a na cakṣuṣā na manasā na vācā dūṣayet kva cit
c na pratyakṣaṃ parokṣaṃ vā kiṃ cid duṣṭaṃ samācaret
a indriyāṇy upasaṃhṛtya kūrmo 'ṅgānīva sarvaśaḥ
c kṣīṇendriyamanobuddhir nirīkṣeta nirindriyaḥ
a nirdvaṃdvo nirnamaskāro niḥsvāhākāra eva ca
c nirmamo nirahaṃkāro niryogakṣema eva ca
a nirāśīḥ sarvabhūteṣu nirāsaṅgo nirāśrayaḥ
c sarvajñaḥ sarvato mukto mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
a apāṇipādapṛṣṭhaṃ tam aśiraskam anūdaram
c prahīṇaguṇakarmāṇaṃ kevalaṃ vimalaṃ sthiram
a agandharasam asparśam arūpāśabdam eva ca
c atvagasthy atha vāmajjam amāṃsam api caiva ha
a niścintam avyayaṃ nityaṃ hṛdistham api nityadā
c sarvabhūtastham ātmānaṃ ye paśyanti na te mṛtāḥ
a na tatra kramate buddhir nendriyāṇi na devatāḥ
c vedā yajñāś ca lokāś ca na tapo na parākramaḥ
e yatra jñānavatāṃ prāptir aliṅgagrahaṇā smṛtā
a tasmād aliṅgo dharmajño dharmavratam anuvrataḥ
c gūḍhadharmāśrito vidvān ajñātacaritaṃ caret
a amūḍho mūḍharūpeṇa cared dharmam adūṣayan
c yathainam avamanyeran pare satatam eva hi
a tathāvṛttaś cared dharmaṃ satāṃ vartmāvidūṣayan
c yo hy evaṃ vṛttasaṃpannaḥ sa muniḥ śreṣṭha ucyate
a indriyāṇīndriyārthāṃś ca mahābhūtāni pañca ca
c manobuddhir athātmānam avyaktaṃ puruṣaṃ tathā
a sarvam etat prasaṃkhyāya samyak saṃtyajya nirmalaḥ
c tataḥ svargam avāpnoti vimuktaḥ sarvabandhanaiḥ
a etad evāntavelāyāṃ parisaṃkhyāya tattvavit
c dhyāyed ekāntam āsthāya mucyate 'tha nirāśrayaḥ
a nirmuktaḥ sarvasaṅgebhyo vāyur ākāśago yathā
c kṣīṇakośo nirātaṅkaḥ prāpnoti paramaṃ padam
 brahmovāca
a saṃnyāsaṃ tapa ity āhur vṛddhā niścitadarśinaḥ
c brāhmaṇā brahmayonisthā jñānaṃ brahma paraṃ viduḥ
a avidūrāt paraṃ brahma vedavidyāvyapāśrayam
c nirdvaṃdvaṃ nirguṇaṃ nityam acintyaṃ guhyam uttamam
a jñānena tapasā caiva dhīrāḥ paśyanti tat padam
c nirṇiktatamasaḥ pūtā vyutkrāntarajaso 'malāḥ
a tapasā kṣemam adhvānaṃ gacchanti paramaiṣiṇaḥ
c saṃnyāsaniratā nityaṃ ye brahmaviduṣo janāḥ
a tapaḥ pradīpa ity āhur ācāro dharmasādhakaḥ
c jñānaṃ tv eva paraṃ vidma saṃnyāsas tapa uttamam
a yas tu veda nirābādhaṃ jñānaṃ tattvaviniścayāt
c sarvabhūtastham ātmānaṃ sa sarvagatir iṣyate
a yo vidvān sahavāsaṃ ca vivāsaṃ caiva paśyati
c tathaivaikatvanānātve sa duḥkhāt parimucyate
a yo na kāmayate kiṃ cin na kiṃ cid avamanyate
c ihalokastha evaiṣa brahmabhūyāya kalpate
a pradhānaguṇatattvajñaḥ sarvabhūtavidhānavit
c nirmamo nirahaṃkāro mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
a nirdvaṃdvo nirnamaskāro niḥsvadhākāra eva ca
c nirguṇaṃ nityam advaṃdvaṃ praśamenaiva gacchati
a hitvā guṇamayaṃ sarvaṃ karma jantuḥ śubhāśubham
c ubhe satyānṛte hitvā mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
a avyaktabījaprabhavo buddhiskandhamayo mahān
c mahāhaṃkāraviṭapa indriyāntarakoṭaraḥ
a mahābhūtaviśākhaś ca viśeṣapratiśākhavān
c sadāparṇaḥ sadāpuṣpaḥ śubhāśubhaphalodayaḥ
e ājīvaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ brahmavṛkṣaḥ sanātanaḥ
a etac chittvā ca bhittvā ca jñānena paramāsinā
c hitvā cāmaratāṃ prāpya jahyād vai mṛtyujanmanī
d   tattvajñānāsinā budhaḥ
d hitvā saṅgamayān pāśān mṛtyujanmajarodayān
e nirmamo nirahaṃkāro mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
a dvāv etau pakṣiṇau nityau sakhāyau cāpy acetanau
c etābhyāṃ tu paro yasya cetanāvān iti smṛtaḥ
a acetanaḥ sattvasaṃghātayuktaḥ
sattvāt paraṃ cetayate 'ntarātmā
c sa kṣetrajñaḥ sattvasaṃghātabuddhir
guṇātigo mucyate mṛtyupāśāt
 brahmovāca
a ke cid brahmamayaṃ vṛkṣaṃ ke cid brahmamayaṃ mahat
c ke cit puruṣam avyaktaṃ ke cit param anāmayam
e manyante sarvam apy etad avyaktaprabhavāvyayam
a ucchvāsamātram api ced yo 'ntakāle samo bhavet
c ātmānam upasaṃgamya so 'mṛtatvāya kalpate
a nimeṣamātram api cet saṃyamyātmānam ātmani
c gacchaty ātmaprasādena viduṣāṃ prāptim avyayām
a prāṇāyāmair atha prāṇān saṃyamya sa punaḥ punaḥ
c daśadvādaśabhir vāpi caturviṃśāt paraṃ tataḥ
a evaṃ pūrvaṃ prasannātmā labhate yad yad icchati
c avyaktāt sattvam udriktam amṛtatvāya kalpate
a sattvāt parataraṃ nānyat praśaṃsantīha tadvidaḥ
c anumānād vijānīmaḥ puruṣaṃ sattvasaṃśrayam
e na śakyam anyathā gantuṃ puruṣaṃ tam atho dvijāḥ
a kṣamā dhṛtir ahiṃsā ca samatā satyam ārjavam
c jñānaṃ tyāgo 'tha saṃnyāsaḥ sāttvikaṃ vṛttam iṣyate
a etenaivānumānena manyante 'tha manīṣiṇaḥ
c sattvaṃ ca puruṣaś caikas tatra nāsti vicāraṇā
a āhur eke ca vidvāṃso ye jñāne supratiṣṭhitāḥ
c kṣetrajñasattvayor aikyam ity etan nopapadyate
a pṛthagbhūtas tato nityam ity etad avicāritam
c pṛthagbhāvaś ca vijñeyaḥ sahajaś cāpi tattvataḥ
a tathaivaikatvanānātvam iṣyate viduṣāṃ nayaḥ
c maśakodumbare tv aikyaṃ pṛthaktvam api dṛśyate
a matsyo yathānyaḥ syād apsu saṃprayogas tathānayoḥ
c saṃbandhas toyabindūnāṃ parṇe kokanadasya ca
 gurur uvāca
a ity uktavantaṃ te viprās tadā lokapitāmaham
c punaḥ saṃśayam āpannāḥ papracchur dvijasattamāḥ
 ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
a kiṃ svid eveha dharmāṇām anuṣṭheyatamaṃ smṛtam
c vyāhatām iva paśyāmo dharmasya vividhāṃ gatim
a ūrdhvaṃ dehād vadanty eke naitad astīti cāpare
c ke cit saṃśayitaṃ sarvaṃ niḥsaṃśayam athāpare
a anityaṃ nityam ity eke nāsty astīty api cāpare
c ekarūpaṃ dvidhety eke vyāmiśram iti cāpare
e ekam eke pṛthak cānye bahutvam iti cāpare
a manyante brāhmaṇā evaṃ prājñās tattvārthadarśinaḥ
c jaṭājinadharāś cānye muṇḍāḥ ke cid asaṃvṛtāḥ
a asnānaṃ ke cid icchanti snānam ity api cāpare
c āhāraṃ ke cid icchanti ke cic cānaśane ratāḥ
a karma ke cit praśaṃsanti praśāntim api cāpare
c deśakālāv ubhau ke cin naitad astīti cāpare
e ke cin mokṣaṃ praśaṃsanti ke cid bhogān pṛthagvidhān
a dhanāni ke cid icchanti nirdhanatvaṃ tathāpare
c upāsyasādhanaṃ tv eke naitad astīti cāpare
a ahiṃsāniratāś cānye ke cid dhiṃsāparāyaṇāḥ
c puṇyena yaśasety eke naitad astīti cāpare
a sadbhāvaniratāś cānye ke cit saṃśayite sthitāḥ
c duḥkhād anye sukhād anye dhyānam ity apare sthitāḥ
a yajñam ity apare dhīrāḥ pradānam iti cāpare
c sarvam eke praśaṃsanti na sarvam iti cāpare
a tapas tv anye praśaṃsanti svādhyāyam apare janāḥ
c jñānaṃ saṃnyāsam ity eke svabhāvaṃ bhūtacintakāḥ
a evaṃ vyutthāpite dharme bahudhā vipradhāvati
c niścayaṃ nādhigacchāmaḥ saṃmūḍhāḥ surasattama
a idaṃ śreya idaṃ śreya ity evaṃ prasthito janaḥ
c yo hi yasmin rato dharme sa taṃ pūjayate sadā
a tatra no vihatā prajñā manaś ca bahulīkṛtam
c etad ākhyātum icchāmaḥ śreyaḥ kim iti sattama
a ataḥ paraṃ ca yad guhyaṃ tad bhavān vaktum arhati
c sattvakṣetrajñayoś caiva saṃbandhaḥ kena hetunā
a evam uktaḥ sa tair viprair bhagavāṃl lokabhāvanaḥ
c tebhyaḥ śaśaṃsa dharmātmā yāthātathyena buddhimān
 brahmovāca
a hanta vaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi yan māṃ pṛcchatha sattamāḥ
b guruṇā śiṣyam āsādya yad uktaṃ tan nibodhata
c samastam iha tac chrutvā samyag evāvadhāryatām
a ahiṃsā sarvabhūtānām etat kṛtyatamaṃ matam
c etat padam anudvignaṃ variṣṭhaṃ dharmalakṣaṇam
a jñānaṃ niḥśreya ity āhur vṛddhā niścayadarśinaḥ
c tasmāj jñānena śuddhena mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ
a hiṃsāparāś ca ye loke ye ca nāstikavṛttayaḥ
c lobhamohasamāyuktās te vai nirayagāminaḥ
a āśīryuktāni karmāṇi kurvate ye tv atandritāḥ
c te 'smiṃl loke pramodante jāyamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ
a kurvate ye tu karmāṇi śraddadhānā vipaścitaḥ
c anāśīryogasaṃyuktās te dhīrāḥ sādhudarśinaḥ
a ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi sattvakṣetrajñayor yathā
c saṃyogo viprayogaś ca tan nibodhata sattamāḥ
a viṣayo viṣayitvaṃ ca saṃbandho 'yam ihocyate
c viṣayī puruṣo nityaṃ sattvaṃ ca viṣayaḥ smṛtaḥ
a vyākhyātaṃ pūrvakalpena maśakodumbaraṃ yathā
c bhujyamānaṃ na jānīte nityaṃ sattvam acetanam
e yas tv eva tu vijānīte yo bhuṅkte yaś ca bhujyate
a anityaṃ dvaṃdvasaṃyuktaṃ sattvam āhur guṇātmakam
c nirdvaṃdvo niṣkalo nityaḥ kṣetrajño nirguṇātmakaḥ
a samaḥ saṃjñāgatas tv evaṃ yadā sarvatra dṛśyate
c upabhuṅkte sadā sattvam āpaḥ puṣkaraparṇavat
a sarvair api guṇair vidvān vyatiṣakto na lipyate
c jalabindur yathā lolaḥ padminīpatrasaṃsthitaḥ
e evam evāpy asaṃsaktaḥ puruṣaḥ syān na saṃśayaḥ
a dravyamātram abhūt sattvaṃ puruṣasyeti niścayaḥ
c yathā dravyaṃ ca kartā ca saṃyogo 'py anayos tathā
a yathā pradīpam ādāya kaś cit tamasi gacchati
c tathā sattvapradīpena gacchanti paramaiṣiṇaḥ
a yāvad dravyaguṇas tāvat pradīpaḥ saṃprakāśate
c kṣīṇadravyaguṇaṃ jyotir antardhānāya gacchati
a vyaktaḥ sattvaguṇas tv evaṃ puruṣo 'vyakta iṣyate
c etad viprā vijānīta hanta bhūyo bravīmi vaḥ
a sahasreṇāpi durmedhā na vṛddhim adhigacchati
b tat padaṃ samanuprāptaṃ yatra gatvā na śocati
b tvam apy etan mahābhāga yathoktaṃ brahmavarcasā
b vyaktaḥ sattvaguṇas tv evaṃ buddhimān sukham edhate
c caturthenāpy athāṃśena buddhimān sukham edhate
a evaṃ dharmasya vijñeyaṃ saṃsādhanam upāyataḥ
c upāyajño hi medhāvī sukham atyantam aśnute
a yathādhvānam apātheyaḥ prapanno mānavaḥ kva cit
c kleśena yāti mahatā vinaśyaty antarāpi vā
a tathā karmasu vijñeyaṃ phalaṃ bhavati vā na vā
c puruṣasyātmaniḥśreyaḥ śubhāśubhanidarśanam
a yathā ca dīrgham adhvānaṃ padbhyām eva prapadyate
c adṛṣṭapūrvaṃ sahasā tattvadarśanavarjitaḥ
a tam eva ca yathādhvānaṃ rathenehāśugāminā
c yāyād aśvaprayuktena tathā buddhimatāṃ gatiḥ
a uccaṃ parvatam āruhya nānvavekṣeta bhūgatam
c rathena rathinaṃ paśyet kliśyamānam acetanam
a yāvad rathapathas tāvad rathena sa tu gacchati
c kṣīṇe rathapathe prājño ratham utsṛjya gacchati
a evaṃ gacchati medhāvī tattvayogavidhānavit
c samājñāya mahābuddhir uttarād uttarottaram
a yathā mahārṇavaṃ ghoram aplavaḥ saṃpragāhate
c bāhubhyām eva saṃmohād vadhaṃ carcchaty asaṃśayam
a nāvā cāpi yathā prājño vibhāgajñas taritrayā
c aklāntaḥ salilaṃ gāhet kṣipraṃ saṃtarati dhruvam
a tīrṇo gacchet paraṃ pāraṃ nāvam utsṛjya nirmamaḥ
c vyākhyātaṃ pūrvakalpena yathā rathipadātinau
a snehāt saṃmoham āpanno nāvi dāśo yathā tathā
c mamatvenābhibhūtaḥ sa tatraiva parivartate
a nāvaṃ na śakyam āruhya sthale viparivartitum
c tathaiva ratham āruhya nāpsu caryā vidhīyate
a evaṃ karma kṛtaṃ citraṃ viṣayasthaṃ pṛthak pṛthak
c yathā karma kṛtaṃ loke tathā tad upapadyate
a yan naiva gandhino rasyaṃ na rūpasparśaśabdavat
c manyante munayo buddhyā tat pradhānaṃ pracakṣate
c rasanaṃ rūpasaṃsparśaṃ śabdavan manyate manaḥ
c yat paraś ca tato buddhyā
a tatra pradhānam avyaktam avyaktasya guṇo mahān
c mahataḥ pradhānabhūtasya guṇo 'haṃkāra eva ca
a ahaṃkārapradhānasya mahābhūtakṛto guṇaḥ
c pṛthaktvena hi bhūtānāṃ viṣayā vai guṇāḥ smṛtāḥ
a bījadharmaṃ yathāvyaktaṃ tathaiva prasavātmakam
c bījadharmā mahān ātmā prasavaś ceti naḥ śrutam
a bījadharmā tv ahaṃkāraḥ prasavaś ca punaḥ punaḥ
c bījaprasavadharmāṇi mahābhūtāni pañca vai
a bījadharmiṇa ity āhuḥ prasavaṃ ca na kurvate
c viśeṣāḥ pañcabhūtānāṃ teṣāṃ vittaṃ viśeṣaṇam
a tatraikaguṇam ākāśaṃ dviguṇo vāyur ucyate
c triguṇaṃ jyotir ity āhur āpaś cāpi caturguṇāḥ
a pṛthvī pañcaguṇā jñeyā trasasthāvarasaṃkulā
c sarvabhūtakarī devī śubhāśubhanidarśanā
a śabdaḥ sparśas tathā rūpaṃ raso gandhaś ca pañcamaḥ
c ete pañca guṇā bhūmer vijñeyā dvijasattamāḥ
a pārthivaś ca sadā gandho gandhaś ca bahudhā smṛtaḥ
c tasya gandhasya vakṣyāmi vistareṇa bahūn guṇān
a iṣṭaś cāniṣṭagandhaś ca madhuro 'mlaḥ kaṭus tathā
c nirhārī saṃhataḥ snigdho rūkṣo viśada eva ca
e evaṃ daśavidho jñeyaḥ pārthivo gandha ity uta
a śabdaḥ sparśas tathā rūpaṃ rasaś cāpāṃ guṇāḥ smṛtāḥ
c rasajñānaṃ tu vakṣyāmi rasas tu bahudhā smṛtaḥ
a madhuro 'mlaḥ kaṭus tiktaḥ kaṣāyo lavaṇas tathā
c evaṃ ṣaḍvidhavistāro raso vārimayaḥ smṛtaḥ
a śabdaḥ sparśas tathā rūpaṃ triguṇaṃ jyotir ucyate
c jyotiṣaś ca guṇo rūpaṃ rūpaṃ ca bahudhā smṛtam
a śuklaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ tathā raktaṃ nīlaṃ pītāruṇaṃ tathā
c hrasvaṃ dīrghaṃ tathā sthūlaṃ caturasrāṇu vṛttakam
a evaṃ dvādaśavistāraṃ tejaso rūpam ucyate
c vijñeyaṃ brāhmaṇair nityaṃ dharmajñaiḥ satyavādibhiḥ
a śabdasparśau ca vijñeyau dviguṇo vāyur ucyate
c vāyoś cāpi guṇaḥ sparśaḥ sparśaś ca bahudhā smṛtaḥ
a uṣṇaḥ śītaḥ sukho duḥkhaḥ snigdho viśada eva ca
c kaṭhinaś cikkaṇaḥ ślakṣṇaḥ picchilo dāruṇo mṛduḥ
a evaṃ dvādaśavistāro vāyavyo guṇa ucyate
c vidhivad brahmaṇaiḥ siddhair dharmajñais tattvadarśibhiḥ
a tatraikaguṇam ākāśaṃ śabda ity eva ca smṛtaḥ
c tasya śabdasya vakṣyāmi vistareṇa bahūn guṇān
a ṣaḍjarṣabhau ca gāndhāro madhyamaḥ pañcamas tathā
c ataḥ paraṃ tu vijñeyo niṣādo dhaivatas tathā
a iṣṭo 'niṣṭaś ca śabdas tu saṃhataḥ pravibhāgavān
c evaṃ bahuvidho jñeyaḥ śabda ākāśasaṃbhavaḥ
a ākāśam uttamaṃ bhūtam ahaṃkāras tataḥ param
c ahaṃkārāt parā buddhir buddher ātmā tataḥ paraḥ
a tasmāt tu param avyaktam avyaktāt puruṣaḥ paraḥ
c parāvarajño bhūtānāṃ yaṃ prāpyānantyam aśnute
d sarvabhūtātmabhūtātmā gacchaty ātmānam akṣaram
 brahmovāca
a bhūtānām atha pañcānāṃ yathaiṣām īśvaraṃ manaḥ
c niyame ca visarge ca bhūtātmā mana eva ca
a adhiṣṭhātā mano nityaṃ bhūtānāṃ mahatāṃ tathā
c buddhir aiśvaryam ācaṣṭe kṣetrajñaḥ sarva ucyate
a indriyāṇi mano yuṅkte sadaśvān iva sārathiḥ
c indriyāṇi mano buddhiṃ kṣetrajño yuñjate sadā
a mahābhūtasamāyuktaṃ buddhisaṃyamanaṃ ratham
c tam āruhya sa bhūtātmā samantāt paridhāvati
a indriyagrāmasaṃyukto manaḥsārathir eva ca
c buddhisaṃyamano nityaṃ mahān brahmamayo rathaḥ
a evaṃ yo vetti vidvān vai sadā brahmamayaṃ ratham
c sa dhīraḥ sarvalokeṣu na moham adhigacchati
a avyaktādi viśeṣāntaṃ trasasthāvarasaṃkulam
c candrasūryaprabhālokaṃ grahanakṣatramaṇḍitam
a nadīparvatajālaiś ca sarvataḥ paribhūṣitam
c vividhābhis tathādbhiś ca satataṃ samalaṃkṛtam
a ājīvaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ sarvaprāṇabhṛtāṃ gatiḥ
c etad brahmavanaṃ nityaṃ yasmiṃś carati kṣetravit
a loke 'smin yāni bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca
c tāny evāgre pralīyante paścād bhūtakṛtā guṇāḥ
e guṇebhyaḥ pañcabhūtāni eṣa bhūtasamucchrayaḥ
a devā manuṣyā gandharvāḥ piśācāsurarākṣasāḥ
c sarve svabhāvataḥ sṛṣṭā na kriyābhyo na kāraṇāt
a ete viśvakṛto viprā jāyante ha punaḥ punaḥ
c tebhyaḥ prasūtās teṣv eva mahābhūteṣu pañcasu
e pralīyante yathākālam ūrmayaḥ sāgare yathā
a viśvasṛgbhyas tu bhūtebhyo mahābhūtāni gacchati
c bhūtebhyaś cāpi pañcabhyo mukto gacchet prajāpatim
a prajāpatir idaṃ sarvaṃ tapasaivāsṛjat prabhuḥ
c tathaiva vedān ṛṣayas tapasā pratipedire
a tapasaś cānupūrvyeṇa phalamūlāśinas tathā
c trailokyaṃ tapasā siddhāḥ paśyantīha samāhitāḥ
a oṣadhāny agadādīnī nānāvidyāś ca sarvaśaḥ
c tapasaiva prasidhyanti tapomūlaṃ hi sādhanam
a yad durāpaṃ durāmnāyaṃ durādharṣaṃ duranvayam
c tat sarvaṃ tapasā sādhyaṃ tapo hi duratikramam
a surāpo brahmahā steyī bhrūṇahā gurutalpagaḥ
c tapasaiva sutaptena mucyante kilbiṣāt tataḥ
a manuṣyāḥ pitaro devāḥ paśavo mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ
c yāni cānyāni bhūtāni trasāni sthāvarāṇi ca
a tapaḥparāyaṇā nityaṃ sidhyante tapasā sadā
c tathaiva tapasā devā mahābhāgā divaṃ gatāḥ
a āśīryuktāni karmāṇi kurvate ye tv atandritāḥ
c ahaṃkārasamāyuktās te sakāśe prajāpateḥ
a dhyānayogena śuddhena nirmamā nirahaṃkṛtāḥ
c prāpnuvanti mahātmāno mahāntaṃ lokam uttamam
a dhyānayogād upāgamya prasannamatayaḥ sadā
c sukhopacayam avyaktaṃ praviśanty ātmavattayā
a dhyānayogād upāgamya nirmamā nirahaṃkṛtāḥ
c avyaktaṃ praviśantīha mahāntaṃ lokam uttamam
a avyaktād eva saṃbhūtaḥ samayajño gataḥ punaḥ
c tamorajobhyāṃ nirmuktaḥ sattvam āsthāya kevalam
a vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyaḥ sarvaṃ tyajati niṣkalaḥ
c kṣetrajña iti taṃ vidyād yas taṃ veda sa vedavit
a cittaṃ cittād upāgamya munir āsīta saṃyataḥ
c yaccittas tanmanā bhūtvā guhyam etat sanātanam
a avyaktādi viśeṣāntam avidyālakṣaṇaṃ smṛtam
c nibodhata yathā hīdaṃ guṇair lakṣaṇam ity uta
a dvyakṣaras tu bhaven mṛtyus tryakṣaraṃ brahma śāśvatam
c mameti ca bhaven mṛtyur na mameti ca śāśvatam
a karma ke cit praśaṃsanti mandabuddhitarā narāḥ
c ye tu buddhā mahātmāno na praśaṃsanti karma te
a karmaṇā jāyate jantur mūrtimān ṣoḍaśātmakaḥ
c puruṣaṃ sṛjate 'vidyā agrāhyam amṛtāśinam
a tasmāt karmasu niḥsnehā ye ke cit pāradarśinaḥ
c vidyāmayo 'yaṃ puruṣo na tu karmamayaḥ smṛtaḥ
d ya evam amṛtaṃ nityam agrāhyaṃ śaśvad akṣaram
d vaśyātmānam asaṃśliṣṭaṃ yo veda na mṛto bhavet
a apūrvam amṛtaṃ nityaṃ ya enam avicāriṇam
c ya enaṃ vindate ''tmānam agrāhyam amṛtāśinam
e agrāhyo 'mṛto bhavati ya ebhiḥ kāraṇair dhruvaḥ
a apohya sarvasaṃkalpān saṃyamyātmānam ātmani
c sa tad brahma śubhaṃ vetti yasmād bhūyo na vidyate
a prasādenaiva sattvasya prasādaṃ samavāpnuyāt
c lakṣaṇaṃ hi prasādasya yathā syāt svapnadarśanam
a gatir eṣā tu muktānāṃ ye jñānapariniṣṭhitāḥ
c pravṛttayaś ca yāḥ sarvāḥ paśyanti pariṇāmajāḥ
a eṣā gatir asaktānām eṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ
c eṣā jñānavatāṃ prāptir etad vṛttam aninditam
d niḥsaṅgenaiva tat sarvaṃ nirāśīpādalopanāt
a samena sarvabhūteṣu niḥspṛheṇa nirāśiṣā
c śakyā gatir iyaṃ gantuṃ sarvatra samadarśinā
a etad vaḥ sarvam ākhyātaṃ mayā viprarṣisattamāḥ
c evam ācarata kṣipraṃ tataḥ siddhim avāpsyatha
 gurur uvāca
a ity uktās te tu munayo brahmaṇā guruṇā tathā
c kṛtavanto mahātmānas tato lokān avāpnuvan
a tvam apy etan mahābhāga yathoktaṃ brahmaṇo vacaḥ
c samyag ācara śuddhātmaṃs tataḥ siddhim avāpsyasi
 vāsudeva uvāca
a ity uktaḥ sa tadā śiṣyo guruṇā dharmam uttamam
c cakāra sarvaṃ kaunteya tato mokṣam avāptavān
a kṛtakṛtyaś ca sa tadā śiṣyaḥ kurukulodvaha
c tat padaṃ samanuprāpto yatra gatvā na śocati
 arjuna uvāca
a ko nv asau brāhmaṇaḥ kṛṣṇa kaś ca śiṣyo janārdana
c śrotavyaṃ cen mayaitad vai tat tvam ācakṣva me vibho
 vāsudeva uvāca
a ahaṃ gurur mahābāho manaḥ śiṣyaṃ ca viddhi me
c tvatprītyā guhyam etac ca kathitaṃ me dhanaṃjaya
a mayi ced asti te prītir nityaṃ kurukulodvaha
c adhyātmam etac chrutvā tvaṃ samyag ācara suvrata
a tatas tvaṃ samyag ācīrṇe dharme 'smin kurunandana
c sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā mokṣaṃ prāpsyasi kevalam
a pūrvam apy etad evoktaṃ yuddhakāla upasthite
c mayā tava mahābāho tasmād atra manaḥ kuru
a mayā tu bharataśreṣṭha ciradṛṣṭaḥ pitā vibho
c tam ahaṃ draṣṭum icchāmi saṃmate tava phalguna
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a ity uktavacanaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ pratyuvāca dhanaṃjayaḥ
b yad iṣṭaṃ kuru sarvasyāpīśvaro 'smān prapālaya
b namas te sarvalokātman nārāyaṇa parātpara
b manomalāt tapo 'śakyaṃ karma cāvidyayā hatam
b dānam apy arthadoṣeṇa nāma tasmāt kalau smaret
b yadi gantuṃ kṛtā buddhir vāsudeva namo 'stu te
c gacchāvo nagaraṃ kṛṣṇa gajasāhvayam adya vai
a sametya tatra rājānaṃ dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c samanujñāpya durdharṣaṃ svāṃ purīṃ yātum arhasi
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tato 'bhyacodayat kṛṣṇo yujyatām iti dārukam
c muhūrtād iva cācaṣṭa yuktam ity eva dārukaḥ
a tathaiva cānuyātrāṇi codayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ
c sajjayadhvaṃ prayāsyāmo nagaraṃ gajasāhvayam
a ity uktāḥ sainikās te tu sajjībhūtā viśāṃ pate
c ācakhyuḥ sajjam ity eva pārthāyāmitatejase
a tatas tau ratham āsthāya prayātau kṛṣṇapāṇḍavau
c vikurvāṇau kathāś citrāḥ prīyamāṇau viśāṃ pate
a rathasthaṃ tu mahātejā vāsudevaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
c punar evābravīd vākyam idaṃ bharatasattama
a tvatprasādāj jayaḥ prāpto rājñā vṛṣṇikulodvaha
c nihatāḥ śatravaś cāpi prāptaṃ rājyam akaṇṭakam
a nāthavantaś ca bhavatā pāṇḍavā madhusūdana
c bhavantaṃ plavam āsādya tīrṇāḥ sma kurusāgaram
d bhaktāṃs tvam āśritān asmān pālayāmutra ceha ca
a viśvakarman namas te 'stu viśvātman viśvasaṃbhava
c yathāhaṃ tvā vijānāmi yathā cāhaṃ bhavanmanāḥ
d bhavāmi satataṃ kṛṣṇa tathā kuru mahāmate
a tvattejaḥsaṃbhavo nityaṃ hutāśo madhusūdana
c ratiḥ krīḍāmayī tubhyaṃ māyā te rodasī vibho
a tvayi sarvam idaṃ viśvaṃ yad idaṃ sthāṇujaṅgamam
c tvaṃ hi sarvaṃ vikuruṣe bhūtagrāmaṃ sanātanam
a pṛthivīṃ cāntarikṣaṃ ca tathā sthāvarajaṅgamam
c hasitaṃ te 'malā jyotsnā ṛtavaś cendriyānvayāḥ
a prāṇo vāyuḥ satatagaḥ krodho mṛtyuḥ sanātanaḥ
c prasāde cāpi padmā śrīr nityaṃ tvayi mahāmate
a ratis tuṣṭir dhṛtiḥ kṣāntis tvayi cedaṃ carācaram
c tvam eveha yugānteṣu nidhanaṃ procyase 'nagha
a sudīrgheṇāpi kālena na te śakyā guṇā mayā
c ātmā ca paramo vaktuṃ namas te nalinekṣaṇa
a vidito me 'si durdharṣa nāradād devalāt tathā
c kṛṣṇadvaipāyanāc caiva tathā kurupitāmahāt
a tvayi sarvaṃ samāsaktaṃ tvam evaiko janeśvaraḥ
c yac cānugrahasaṃyuktam etad uktaṃ tvayānagha
a etat sarvam ahaṃ samyag ācariṣye janārdana
c idaṃ cādbhutam atyarthaṃ kṛtam asmatpriyepsayā
a yat pāpo nihataḥ saṃkhye kauravyo dhṛtarāṣṭrajaḥ
c tvayā dagdhaṃ hi tat sainyaṃ mayā vijitam āhave
a bhavatā tat kṛtaṃ karma yenāvāpto jayo mayā
c duryodhanasya saṃgrāme tava buddhiparākramaiḥ
a karṇasya ca vadhopāyo yathāvat saṃpradarśitaḥ
c saindhavasya ca pāpasya bhūriśravasa eva ca
d tasmāt tvam eva saṃcintya hitaṃ kuru yathā tathā
a ahaṃ ca prīyamāṇena tvayā devakinandana
c yad uktas tat kariṣyāmi na hi me 'tra vicāraṇā
a rājānaṃ ca samāsādya dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c codayiṣyāmi dharmajña gamanārthaṃ tavānagha
a rucitaṃ hi mamaitat te dvārakāgamanaṃ prabho
c acirāc caiva dṛṣṭā tvaṃ mātulaṃ madhusūdana
e baladevaṃ ca durdharṣaṃ tathānyān vṛṣṇipuṃgavān
a evaṃ saṃbhāṣamāṇau tau prāptau vāraṇasāhvayam
c tathā viviśatuś cobhau saṃprahṛṣṭanarākulam
a tau gatvā dhṛtarāṣṭrasya gṛhaṃ śakragṛhopamam
c dadṛśāte mahārāja dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ janeśvaram
a viduraṃ ca mahābuddhiṃ rājānaṃ ca yudhiṣṭhiram
c bhīmasenaṃ ca durdharṣaṃ mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavau
e dhṛtarāṣṭram upāsīnaṃ yuyutsuṃ cāparājitam
a gāndhārīṃ ca mahāprājñāṃ pṛthāṃ kṛṣṇāṃ ca bhāminīm
c subhadrādyāś ca tāḥ sarvā bharatānāṃ striyas tathā
e dadṛśāte sthitāḥ sarvā gāndhārīṃ parivārya vai
a tataḥ sametya rājānaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭram ariṃdamau
c nivedya nāmadheye sve tasya pādāv agṛhṇatām
a gāndhāryāś ca pṛthāyāś ca dharmarājñas tathaiva ca
c bhīmasya ca mahātmānau tathā pādāv agṛhṇatām
d bhīmasya ca vavandāte tathā pādau mahātmanaḥ
d mahātmānau tathā pādau vavandatur ariṃdamau
d mahātmānau mahāvīryau tathā pādau vavandatuḥ
