a kṣattāraṃ cāpi saṃpūjya pṛṣṭvā kuśalam avyayam
b pariṣvajya mahātmānaṃ vaiśyāputraṃ mahāratham
c taiḥ sārdhaṃ nṛpatiṃ vṛddhaṃ tatas taṃ paryupāsatām
a tato niśi mahārāja dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ kurūdvahān
c janārdanaṃ ca medhāvī vyasarjayata vai gṛhān
a te 'nujñātā nṛpatinā yayuḥ svaṃ svaṃ niveśanam
c dhanaṃjayagṛhān eva yayau kṛṣṇas tu vīryavān
a tatrārcito yathānyāyaṃ sarvakāmair upasthitaḥ
c kṛṣṇaḥ suṣvāpa medhāvī dhanaṃjayasahāyavān
a prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāṃ kṛtapūrvāhṇikakriyau
c dharmarājasya bhavanaṃ jagmatuḥ paramārcitau
e yatrāste sa sahāmātyo dharmarājo mahāmanāḥ
a tatas tau tat praviśyātha dadṛśāte mahābalau
c dharmarājānam āsīnaṃ devarājam ivāśvinau
a tau samāsādya rājānaṃ vārṣṇeyakurupuṃgavau
c niṣīdatur anujñātau prīyamāṇena tena vai
a tataḥ sa rājā medhāvī vivakṣū prekṣya tāv ubhau
c provāca vadatāṃ śreṣṭho vacanaṃ rājasattamaḥ
a vivakṣū hi yuvāṃ manye vīrau yadukurūdvahau
c brūta kartāsmi sarvaṃ vāṃ na cirān mā vicāryatām
a ity ukte phalgunas tatra dharmarājānam abravīt
b ity ukte dharmarājena phalgunaḥ pratyabhāṣata
c vinītavad upāgamya vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradaḥ
a ayaṃ ciroṣito rājan vāsudevaḥ pratāpavān
c bhavantaṃ samanujñāpya pitaraṃ draṣṭum icchati
a sa gacched abhyanujñāto bhavatā yadi manyase
c ānartanagarīṃ vīras tad anujñātum arhasi
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a puṇḍarīkākṣa bhadraṃ te gaccha tvaṃ madhusūdana
c purīṃ dvāravatīm adya draṣṭuṃ śūrasutaṃ prabhum
a rocate me mahābāho gamanaṃ tava keśava
c mātulaś ciradṛṣṭo me tvayā devī ca devakī
a mātulaṃ vasudevaṃ tvaṃ baladevaṃ ca mādhava
c pūjayethā mahāprājña madvākyena yathārhataḥ
a smarethāś cāpi māṃ nityaṃ bhīmaṃ ca balināṃ varam
c phalgunaṃ nakulaṃ caiva sahadevaṃ ca mādhava
a ānartān avalokya tvaṃ pitaraṃ ca mahābhuja
c vṛṣṇīṃś ca punar āgaccher hayamedhe mamānagha
a sa gaccha ratnāny ādāya vividhāni vasūni ca
c yac cāpy anyan manojñaṃ te tad apy ādatsva sātvata
a iyaṃ hi vasudhā sarvā prasādāt tava mādhava
c asmān upagatā vīra nihatāś cāpi śatravaḥ
d svargāpavargaviṣayaṃ tvadbhaktānāṃ na durlabham
d saṃsāragahane tv adya pāpāgniṃ praśamāmbuda
a evaṃ bruvati kauravye dharmarāje yudhiṣṭhire
c vāsudevo varaḥ puṃsām idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a tavaiva ratnāni dhanaṃ ca kevalam
dharā ca kṛtsnā tu mahābhujādya vai
c yad asti cānyad draviṇaṃ gṛheṣu me
tvam eva tasyeśvara nityam īśvaraḥ
a tathety athoktaḥ pratipūjitas tadā
gadāgrajo dharmasutena vīryavān
c pitṛṣvasām abhyavadad yathāvidhi
saṃpūjitaś cāpy agamat pradakṣiṇam
a tayā sa samyak pratinanditas tadā
tathaiva sarvair vidurādibhis tataḥ
c viniryayau nāgapurād gadāgrajo
rathena divyena caturyujā hariḥ
a rathaṃ subhadrām adhiropya bhāminīṃ
yudhiṣṭhirasyānumate janārdanaḥ
c pitṛṣvasāyāś ca tathā mahābhujo
viniryayau paurajanābhisaṃvṛtaḥ
a tam anvagād vānaravaryaketanaḥ
sasātyakir mādravatīsutāv api
c agādhabuddhir viduraś ca mādhavaṃ
svayaṃ ca bhīmo gajarājavikramaḥ
a nivartayitvā kururāṣṭravardhanāṃs
tataḥ sa sarvān viduraṃ ca vīryavān
c janārdano dārukam āha satvaraḥ
pracodayāśvān iti sātyakis tadā
a tato yayau śatrugaṇapramardanaḥ
śinipravīrānugato janārdanaḥ
c yathā nihatyārigaṇāñ śatakratur
divaṃ tathānartapurīṃ pratāpavān
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tathā prayāntaṃ vārṣṇeyaṃ dvārakāṃ bharatarṣabhāḥ
c pariṣvajya nyavartanta sānuyātrāḥ paraṃtapāḥ
a punaḥ punaś ca vārṣṇeyaṃ paryaṣvajata phalgunaḥ
c ā cakṣurviṣayāc cainaṃ dadarśa ca punaḥ punaḥ
a kṛcchreṇaiva ca tāṃ pārtho govinde viniveśitām
c saṃjahāra tadā dṛṣṭiṃ kṛṣṇaś cāpy aparājitaḥ
a tasya prayāṇe yāny āsan nimittāni mahātmanaḥ
c bahūny adbhutarūpāṇi tāni me gadataḥ śṛṇu
a vāyur vegena mahatā rathasya purato vavau
c kurvan niḥśarkaraṃ mārgaṃ virajaskam akaṇṭakam
a vavarṣa vāsavaś cāpi toyaṃ śuci sugandhi ca
c divyāni caiva puṣpāṇi purataḥ śārṅgadhanvanaḥ
a sa prayāto mahābāhuḥ sameṣu marudhanvasu
c dadarśātha muniśreṣṭham uttaṅkam amitaujasam
d āgacchantam apaśyad vai udaṅkaṃ nāma nāmataḥ
d maharṣiṃ siddhatapasaṃ sarvalokāntaviśrutam
a sa taṃ saṃpūjya tejasvī muniṃ pṛthulalocanaḥ
c pūjitas tena ca tadā paryapṛcchad anāmayam
a sa pṛṣṭaḥ kuśalaṃ tena saṃpūjya madhusūdanam
c uttaṅko brāhmaṇaśreṣṭhas tataḥ papraccha mādhavam
a kaccic chaure tvayā gatvā kurupāṇḍavasadma tat
c kṛtaṃ saubhrātram acalaṃ tan me vyākhyātum arhasi
a abhisaṃdhāya tān vīrān upāvṛtto 'si keśava
c saṃbandhinaḥ sudayitān satataṃ vṛṣṇipuṃgava
a kaccit pāṇḍusutāḥ pañca dhṛtarāṣṭrasya cātmajāḥ
c lokeṣu vihariṣyanti tvayā saha paraṃtapa
a svarāṣṭreṣu ca rājānaḥ kaccit prāpsyanti vai sukham
c kauraveṣu praśānteṣu tvayā nāthena mādhava
a yā me saṃbhāvanā tāta tvayi nityam avartata
c api sā saphalā kṛṣṇa kṛtā te bharatān prati
 vāsudeva uvāca
a kṛto yatno mayā brahman saubhrātre kauravān prati
c na cāśakyanta saṃdhātuṃ te 'dharmarucayo mayā
d nāśakyanta yadā sāmye te sthāpayitum añjasā
a tatas te nidhanaṃ prāptāḥ sarve sasutabāndhavāḥ
c na diṣṭam abhyatikrāntuṃ śakyaṃ buddhyā balena vā
e maharṣe viditaṃ nūnaṃ sarvam etat tavānagha
a te 'tyakrāman matiṃ mahyaṃ bhīṣmasya vidurasya ca
b yathā tu militaṃ sarvaṃ mahyaṃ bhīṣmasya saṃgaram
c tato yamakṣayaṃ jagmuḥ samāsādyetaretaram
a pañca vai pāṇḍavāḥ śiṣṭā hatamitrā hatātmajāḥ
c dhārtarāṣṭrāś ca nihatāḥ sarve sasutabāndhavāḥ
a ity uktavacane kṛṣṇe bhṛśaṃ krodhasamanvitaḥ
c uttaṅkaḥ pratyuvācainaṃ roṣād utphālya locane
a yasmāc chaktena te kṛṣṇa na trātāḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥ
c saṃbandhinaḥ priyās tasmāc chapsye 'haṃ tvām asaṃśayam
a na ca te prasabhaṃ yasmāt te nigṛhya nivartitāḥ
c tasmān manyuparītas tvāṃ śapsyāmi madhusūdana
a tvayā hi śaktena satā mithyācāreṇa mādhava
c upacīrṇāḥ kuruśreṣṭhā yas tv etān samupekṣathāḥ
 vāsudeva uvāca
a śṛṇu me vistareṇedaṃ yad vakṣye bhṛgunandana
c gṛhāṇānunayaṃ cāpi tapasvī hy asi bhārgava
a śrutvā tvam etad adhyātmaṃ muñcethāḥ śāpam adya vai
c na ca māṃ tapasālpena śakto 'bhibhavituṃ pumān
a na ca te tapaso nāśam icchāmi japatāṃ vara
c tapas te sumahad dīptaṃ guravaś cāpi toṣitāḥ
a kaumāraṃ brahmacaryaṃ te jānāmi dvijasattama
c duḥkhārjitasya tapasas tasmān necchāmi te vyayam
 uttaṅka uvāca
a brūhi keśava tattvena tvam adhyātmam aninditam
c śrutvā śreyo 'bhidhāsyāmi śāpaṃ vā te janārdana
 vāsudeva uvāca
a tamo rajaś ca sattvaṃ ca viddhi bhāvān madāśrayān
b sthitisṛṣṭilayādhyakṣo viṣṇubrahmeśasaṃjñitaḥ
b kadā cit tamasā rudro viṣṇuḥ sattvaguṇe sthitaḥ
b rajasy api tathā brahmā guṇād anyaguṇānugau
b praṇavātmā ca śabdādīṃs triguṇātmā carācaram
c tathā rudrān vasūṃś cāpi viddhi matprabhavān dvija
a mayi sarvāṇi bhūtāni sarvabhūteṣu cāpy aham
c sthita ity abhijānīhi mā te 'bhūd atra saṃśayaḥ
a tathā daityagaṇān sarvān yakṣarākṣasapannagān
c gandharvāpsarasaś caiva viddhi matprabhavān dvija
c   yakṣagandharvarākṣasān
c nāgān apsarasaś caiva
a sad asac caiva yat prāhur avyaktaṃ vyaktam eva ca
c akṣaraṃ ca kṣaraṃ caiva sarvam etan madātmakam
a ye cāśrameṣu vai dharmāś caturṣu vihitā mune
c daivāni caiva karmāṇi viddhi sarvaṃ madātmakam
a asac ca sadasac caiva yad viśvaṃ sadasataḥ param
c tataḥ paraṃ nāsti caiva devadevāt sanātanāt
a oṃkāraprabhavān vedān viddhi māṃ tvaṃ bhṛgūdvaha
c yūpaṃ somaṃ tathaiveha tridaśāpyāyanaṃ makhe
a hotāram api havyaṃ ca viddhi māṃ bhṛgunandana
c adhvaryuḥ kalpakaś cāpi haviḥ paramasaṃskṛtam
a udgātā cāpi māṃ stauti gītaghoṣair mahādhvare
c prāyaścitteṣu māṃ brahmañ śāntimaṅgalavācakāḥ
e stuvanti viśvakarmāṇaṃ satataṃ dvijasattamāḥ
a viddhi mahyaṃ sutaṃ dharmam agrajaṃ dvijasattama
c mānasaṃ dayitaṃ vipra sarvabhūtadayātmakam
a tatrāhaṃ vartamānaiś ca nivṛttaiś caiva mānavaiḥ
c bahvīḥ saṃsaramāṇo vai yonīr hi dvijasattama
a dharmasaṃrakṣaṇārthāya dharmasaṃsthāpanāya ca
c tais tair veṣaiś ca rūpaiś ca triṣu lokeṣu bhārgava
a ahaṃ viṣṇur ahaṃ brahmā śakro 'tha prabhavāpyayaḥ
c bhūtagrāmasya sarvasya sraṣṭā saṃhāra eva ca
a adharme vartamānānāṃ sarveṣām aham apy uta
c dharmasya setuṃ badhnāmi calite calite yuge
e tās tā yonīḥ praviśyāhaṃ prajānāṃ hitakāmyayā
a yadā tv ahaṃ devayonau vartāmi bhṛgunandana
c tadāhaṃ devavat sarvam ācarāmi na saṃśayaḥ
a yadā gandharvayonau tu vartāmi bhṛgunandana
c tadā gandharvavac ceṣṭāḥ sarvāś ceṣṭāmi bhārgava
a nāgayonau yadā caiva tadā vartāmi nāgavat
c yakṣarākṣasayonīś ca yathāvad vicarāmy aham
a mānuṣye vartamāne tu kṛpaṇaṃ yācitā mayā
c na ca te jātasaṃmohā vaco gṛhṇanti me hitam
a bhayaṃ ca mahad uddiśya trāsitāḥ kuravo mayā
c kruddheva bhūtvā ca punar yathāvad anudarśitāḥ
a te 'dharmeṇeha saṃyuktāḥ parītāḥ kāladharmaṇā
c dharmeṇa nihatā yuddhe gatāḥ svargaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
a lokeṣu pāṇḍavāś caiva gatāḥ khyātiṃ dvijottama
c etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃ yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi
 uttaṅka uvāca
a abhijānāmi jagataḥ kartāraṃ tvāṃ janārdana
c nūnaṃ bhavatprasādo 'yam iti me nāsti saṃśayaḥ
a cittaṃ ca suprasannaṃ me tvadbhāvagatam acyuta
c vinivṛttaś ca me kopa iti viddhi paraṃtapa
a yadi tv anugrahaṃ kaṃ cit tvatto 'rho 'haṃ janārdana
c draṣṭum icchāmi te rūpam aiśvaraṃ tan nidarśaya
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ sa tasmai prītātmā darśayām āsa tad vapuḥ
c śāśvataṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ dhīmān dadṛśe yad dhanaṃjayaḥ
a sa dadarśa mahātmānaṃ viśvarūpaṃ mahābhujam
a   vaiṣṇavaṃ rūpam uttamam
a sumahat tejasā yuktaṃ
b sahasrasūryapratimaṃ dīptimat pāvakopamam
b sarvam ākāśam āvṛtya tiṣṭhantaṃ viśvatomukham
b tad dṛṣṭvā paramaṃ rūpaṃ viṣṇor vaiṣṇavam adbhutam
c vismayaṃ ca yayau vipras tad dṛṣṭvā rūpam aiśvaram
 uttaṅka uvāca
 namo namas te sarvātman nārāyaṇa parātpara
 paramātman padmanābha puṇḍarīkākṣa mādhava
 hiraṇyagarbharūpāya saṃsārottāraṇāya ca
 puruṣāya purāṇāya cāntaryāmāya te namaḥ
 avidyātimirādityaṃ bhavavyādhimahauṣadham
 saṃsārārṇavapāraṃ tvāṃ praṇamāmi gatir bhava
 sarvavedaikavedyāya sarvadevamayāya ca
 vāsudevāya nityāya namo bhaktipriyāya te
 dayayā duḥkhamohān māṃ samuddhartum ihārhasi
 karmabhir bahubhiḥ pāpair baddhaṃ pāhi janārdana
a viśvakarman namas te 'stu yasya te rūpam īdṛśam
c padbhyāṃ te pṛthivī vyāptā śirasā cāvṛtaṃ nabhaḥ
a dyāvāpṛthivyor yan madhyaṃ jaṭhareṇa tad āvṛtam
c bhujābhyām āvṛtāś cāśās tvam idaṃ sarvam acyuta
a saṃharasva punar deva rūpam akṣayyam uttamam
c punas tvāṃ svena rūpeṇa draṣṭum icchāmi śāśvatam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
 muniṃ vitrastamanasaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇo mahāmanāḥ
 manasā suprasannena prīyamāṇo janārdanaḥ
a tam uvāca prasannātmā govindo janamejaya
c varaṃ vṛṇīṣveti tadā tam uttaṅko 'bravīd idam
a paryāpta eṣa evādya varas tvatto mahādyute
c yat te rūpam idaṃ kṛṣṇa paśyāmi prabhavāpyayam
a tam abravīt punaḥ kṛṣṇo mā tvam atra vicāraya
c avaśyam etat kartavyam amoghaṃ darśanaṃ mama
 uttaṅka uvāca
a avaśyakaraṇīyaṃ vai yady etan manyase vibho
c toyam icchāmi yatreṣṭaṃ maruṣv etad dhi durlabham
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ saṃhṛtya tat tejaḥ provācottaṅkam īśvaraḥ
c eṣṭavye sati cintyo 'ham ity uktvā dvārakāṃ yayau
a tataḥ kadā cid bhagavān uttaṅkas toyakāṅkṣayā
c tṛṣitaḥ paricakrāma marau sasmāra cācyutam
a tato digvāsasaṃ dhīmān mātaṅgaṃ malapaṅkinam
c apaśyata marau tasmiñ śvayūthaparivāritam
a bhīṣaṇaṃ baddhanistriṃśaṃ bāṇakārmukadhāriṇam
c tasyādhaḥ srotaso 'paśyad vāri bhūri dvijottamaḥ
a smarann eva ca taṃ prāha mātaṅgaḥ prahasann iva
c ehy uttaṅka pratīcchasva matto vāri bhṛgūdvaha
e kṛpā hi me sumahatī tvāṃ dṛṣṭvā tṛṭsamāhatam
a ity uktas tena sa munis tat toyaṃ nābhyanandata
c cikṣepa ca sa taṃ dhīmān vāgbhir ugrābhir acyutam
a punaḥ punaś ca mātaṅgaḥ pibasveti tam abravīt
c na cāpibat sa sakrodhaḥ kṣubhitenāntarātmanā
a sa tathā niścayāt tena pratyākhyāto mahātmanā
c śvabhiḥ saha mahārāja tatraivāntaradhīyata
a uttaṅkas taṃ tathā dṛṣṭvā tato vrīḍitamānasaḥ
c mene pralabdham ātmānaṃ kṛṣṇenāmitraghātinā
a atha tenaiva mārgeṇa śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ
c ājagāma mahābāhur uttaṅkaś cainam abravīt
a na yuktaṃ tādṛśaṃ dātuṃ tvayā puruṣasattama
c salilaṃ vipramukhyebhyo mātaṅgasrotasā vibho
a ity uktavacanaṃ dhīmān mahābuddhir janārdanaḥ
c uttaṅkaṃ ślakṣṇayā vācā sāntvayann idam abravīt
a yādṛśeneha rūpeṇa yogyaṃ dātuṃ vṛtena vai
c tādṛśaṃ khalu me dattaṃ tvaṃ tu tan nāvabudhyase
a mayā tvadartham ukto hi vajrapāṇiḥ puraṃdaraḥ
c uttaṅkāyāmṛtaṃ dehi toyarūpam iti prabhuḥ
a sa mām uvāca devendro na martyo 'martyatāṃ vrajet
c anyam asmai varaṃ dehīty asakṛd bhṛgunandana
a amṛtaṃ deyam ity eva mayoktaḥ sa śacīpatiḥ
c sa māṃ prasādya devendraḥ punar evedam abravīt
a yadi deyam avaśyaṃ vai mātaṅgo 'haṃ mahādyute
c bhūtvāmṛtaṃ pradāsyāmi bhārgavāya mahātmane
a yady evaṃ pratigṛhṇāti bhārgavo 'mṛtam adya vai
c pradātum eṣa gacchāmi bhārgavāyāmṛtaṃ prabho
e pratyākhyātas tv ahaṃ tena na dadyām iti bhārgava
a sa tathā samayaṃ kṛtvā tena rūpeṇa vāsavaḥ
b sa tathā tena rūpeṇa vāsavas tvām upāgataḥ
c upasthitas tvayā cāpi pratyākhyāto 'mṛtaṃ dadat
e caṇḍālarūpī bhagavān sumahāṃs te vyatikramaḥ
a yat tu śakyaṃ mayā kartuṃ bhūya eva tavepsitam
c toyepsāṃ tava durdharṣa kariṣye saphalām aham
a yeṣv ahaḥsu tava brahman salilecchā bhaviṣyati
c tadā marau bhaviṣyanti jalapūrṇāḥ payodharāḥ
a rasavac ca pradāsyanti te toyaṃ bhṛgunandana
c uttaṅkameghā ity uktāḥ khyātiṃ yāsyanti cāpi te
a ity uktaḥ prītimān vipraḥ kṛṣṇena sa babhūva ha
c adyāpy uttaṅkameghāś ca marau varṣanti bhārata
 janamejaya uvāca
a uttaṅkaḥ kena tapasā saṃyuktaḥ sumahātapāḥ
c yaḥ śāpaṃ dātukāmo 'bhūd viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a uttaṅko mahatā yuktas tapasā janamejaya
c gurubhaktaḥ sa tejasvī nānyaṃ kaṃ cid apūjayat
a sarveṣām ṛṣiputrāṇām eṣa cāsīn manorathaḥ
c auttaṅkīṃ guruvṛttiṃ vai prāpnuyām iti bhārata
a gautamasya tu śiṣyāṇāṃ bahūnāṃ janamejaya
c uttaṅke 'bhyadhikā prītiḥ snehaś caivābhavat tadā
a sa tasya damaśaucābhyāṃ vikrāntena ca karmaṇā
c samyak caivopacāreṇa gautamaḥ prītimān abhūt
a atha śiṣyasahasrāṇi samanujñāya gautamaḥ
c uttaṅkaṃ parayā prītyā nābhyanujñātum aicchata
a taṃ krameṇa jarā tāta pratipede mahāmunim
c na cānvabudhyata tadā sa munir guruvatsalaḥ
a tataḥ kadā cid rājendra kāṣṭhāny ānayituṃ yayau
c uttaṅkaḥ kāṣṭhabhāraṃ ca mahāntaṃ samupānayat
a sa tu bhārābhibhūtātmā kāṣṭhabhāram ariṃdama
c niṣpipeṣa kṣitau rājan pariśrānto bubhukṣitaḥ
a tasya kāṣṭhe vilagnābhūj jaṭā rūpyasamaprabhā
c tataḥ kāṣṭhaiḥ saha tadā papāta dharaṇītale
a tataḥ sa bhāraniṣpiṣṭaḥ kṣudhāviṣṭaś ca bhārgavaḥ
c dṛṣṭvā tāṃ vayaso 'vasthāṃ rurodārtasvaraṃ tadā
a tato gurusutā tasya padmapatranibhekṣaṇā
c jagrāhāśrūṇi suśroṇī kareṇa pṛthulocanā
e pitur niyogād dharmajñā śirasāvanatā tadā
a tasyā nipetatur dagdhau karau tair aśrubindubhiḥ
c na hi tān aśrupātān vai śaktā dhārayituṃ mahī
a gautamas tv abravīd vipram uttaṅkaṃ prītamānasaḥ
c kasmāt tāta tavādyeha śokottaram idaṃ manaḥ
e sa svairaṃ brūhi viprarṣe śrotum icchāmi te vacaḥ
 uttaṅka uvāca
a bhavadgatena manasā bhavatpriyacikīrṣayā
c bhavadbhaktigateneha bhavadbhāvānugena ca
a jareyaṃ nāvabuddhā me nābhijñātaṃ sukhaṃ ca me
c śatavarṣoṣitaṃ hi tvaṃ na mām abhyanujānathāḥ
a bhavatā hy abhyanujñātāḥ śiṣyāḥ pratyavarā mayā
c upapannā dvijaśreṣṭha śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
 gautama uvāca
a tvatprītiyuktena mayā guruśuśrūṣayā tava
c vyatikrāman mahān kālo nāvabuddho dvijarṣabha
a kiṃ tv adya yadi te śraddhā gamanaṃ prati bhārgava
c anujñāṃ gṛhya mattas tvaṃ gṛhān gacchasva mā ciram
 uttaṅka uvāca
a gurvarthaṃ kaṃ prayacchāmi brūhi tvaṃ dvijasattama
c tam upākṛtya gaccheyam anujñātas tvayā vibho
 gautama uvāca
a dakṣiṇā paritoṣo vai gurūṇāṃ sadbhir ucyate
c tava hy ācarato brahmaṃs tuṣṭo 'haṃ vai na saṃśayaḥ
a itthaṃ ca parituṣṭaṃ māṃ vijānīhi bhṛgūdvaha
c yuvā ṣoḍaśavarṣo hi yad adya bhavitā bhavān
a dadāmi patnīṃ kanyāṃ ca svāṃ te duhitaraṃ dvija
c etām ṛte hi nānyā vai tvattejo 'rhati sevitum
a tatas tāṃ pratijagrāha yuvā bhūtvā yaśasvinīm
c guruṇā cābhyanujñāto gurupatnīm athābravīt
a kiṃ bhavatyai prayacchāmi gurvarthaṃ viniyuṅkṣva mām
c priyaṃ hi tava kāṅkṣāmi prāṇair api dhanair api
a yad durlabhaṃ hi loke 'smin ratnam atyadbhutaṃ bhavet
c tad ānayeyaṃ tapasā na hi me 'trāsti saṃśayaḥ
 ahalyovāca
a parituṣṭāsmi te putra nityaṃ bhagavatā saha
c paryāptaye tad bhadraṃ te gaccha tāta yathecchakam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a uttaṅkas tu mahārāja punar evābravīd vacaḥ
c ājñāpayasva māṃ mātaḥ kartavyaṃ hi priyaṃ tava
 ahalyovāca
a saudāsapatnyā vidite divye vai maṇikuṇḍale
c te samānaya bhadraṃ te gurvarthaḥ sukṛto bhavet
a sa tatheti pratiśrutya jagāma janamejaya
c gurupatnīpriyārthaṃ vai te samānayituṃ tadā
a sa jagāma tataḥ śīghram uttaṅko brāhmaṇarṣabhaḥ
c saudāsaṃ puruṣādaṃ vai bhikṣituṃ maṇikuṇḍale
a gautamas tv abravīt patnīm uttaṅko nādya dṛśyate
c iti pṛṣṭā tam ācaṣṭa kuṇḍalārthaṃ gataṃ tu vai
a tataḥ provāca patnīṃ sa na te samyag idaṃ kṛtam
c śaptaḥ sa pārthivo nūnaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ taṃ vadhiṣyati
 ahalyovāca
a ajānantyā niyuktaḥ sa bhagavan brāhmaṇo 'dya me
c bhavatprasādān na bhayaṃ kiṃ cit tasya bhaviṣyati
a ity uktaḥ prāha tāṃ patnīm evam astv iti gautamaḥ
c uttaṅko 'pi vane śūnye rājānaṃ taṃ dadarśa ha
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a sa taṃ dṛṣṭvā tathābhūtaṃ rājānaṃ ghoradarśanam
c dīrghaśmaśrudharaṃ nṝṇāṃ śoṇitena samukṣitam
a cakāra na vyathāṃ vipro rājā tv enam athābravīt
c pratyutthāya mahātejā bhayakartā yamopamaḥ
a diṣṭyā tvam asi kalyāṇa ṣaṣṭhe kāle mamāntikam
c bhakṣaṃ mṛgayamāṇasya saṃprāpto dvijasattama
 uttaṅka uvāca
a rājan gurvarthinaṃ viddhi carantaṃ mām ihāgatam
c na ca gurvartham udyuktaṃ hiṃsyam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ
 rājovāca
a ṣaṣṭhe kāle mamāhāro vihito dvijasattama
c na ca śakyaḥ samutsraṣṭuṃ kṣudhitena mayādya vai
 uttaṅka uvāca
a evam astu mahārāja samayaḥ kriyatāṃ tu me
c gurvartham abhinirvartya punar eṣyāmi te vaśam
a saṃśrutaś ca mayā yo 'rtho gurave rājasattama
c tvadadhīnaḥ sa rājendra taṃ tvā bhikṣe nareśvara
a dadāsi vipramukhyebhyas tvaṃ hi ratnāni sarvaśaḥ
c dātā tvaṃ ca naravyāghra pātrabhūtaḥ kṣitāv iha
e pātraṃ pratigrahe cāpi viddhi māṃ nṛpasattama
a upākṛtya guror arthaṃ tvadāyattam ariṃdama
c samayeneha rājendra punar eṣyāmi te vaśam
a satyaṃ te pratijānāmi nātra mithyāsti kiṃ cana
c anṛtaṃ noktapūrvaṃ me svaireṣv api kuto 'nyathā
 saudāsa uvāca
a yadi mattas tvadāyatto gurvarthaḥ kṛta eva saḥ
c yadi cāsmi pratigrāhyaḥ sāṃprataṃ tad bravīhi me
 uttaṅka uvāca
a pratigrāhyo mato me tvaṃ sadaiva puruṣarṣabha
c so 'haṃ tvām anusaṃprāpto bhikṣituṃ maṇikuṇḍale
 saudāsa uvāca
a patnyās te mama viprarṣe rucire maṇikuṇḍale
c varayārthaṃ tvam anyaṃ vai taṃ te dāsyāmi suvrata
 uttaṅka uvāca
a alaṃ te vyapadeśena pramāṇaṃ yadi te vayam
c prayaccha kuṇḍale me tvaṃ satyavāg bhava pārthiva
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a ity uktas tv abravīd rājā tam uttaṅkaṃ punar vacaḥ
c gaccha madvacanād devīṃ brūhi dehīti sattama
a saivam uktā tvayā nūnaṃ madvākyena śucismitā
c pradāsyati dvijaśreṣṭha kuṇḍale te na saṃśayaḥ
 uttaṅka uvāca
a kva patnī bhavataḥ śakyā mayā draṣṭuṃ nareśvara
c svayaṃ vāpi bhavān patnīṃ kimarthaṃ nopasarpati
 saudāsa uvāca
a drakṣyate tāṃ bhavān adya kasmiṃś cid vananirjhare
c ṣaṣṭhe kāle na hi mayā sā śakyā draṣṭum adya vai
a uttaṅkas tu tathoktaḥ sa jagāma bharatarṣabha
c madayantīṃ ca dṛṣṭvā so 'jñāpayat svaṃ prayojanam
a saudāsavacanaṃ śrutvā tataḥ sā pṛthulocanā
c pratyuvāca mahābuddhim uttaṅkaṃ janamejaya
a evam etan mahābrahman nānṛtaṃ vadase 'nagha
c abhijñānaṃ tu kiṃ cit tvaṃ samānetum ihārhasi
a ime hi divye maṇikuṇḍale me
devāś ca yakṣāś ca mahoragāś ca
c tais tair upāyaiḥ parihartukāmāś
chidreṣu nityaṃ paritarkayanti
a nikṣiptam etad bhuvi pannagās tu
ratnaṃ samāsādya parāmṛṣeyuḥ
c yakṣās tathocchiṣṭadhṛtaṃ surāś ca
nidrāvaśaṃ tvā paridharṣayeyuḥ
a chidreṣv eteṣu hi sadā hy adhṛṣyeṣu dvijarṣabha
c devarākṣasanāgānām apramattena dhāryate
a syandete hi divā rukmaṃ rātrau ca dvijasattama
c naktaṃ nakṣatratārāṇāṃ prabhām ākṣipya vartate
a ete hy āmucya bhagavan kṣutpipāsābhayaṃ kutaḥ
c viṣāgniśvāpadebhyaś ca bhayaṃ jātu na vidyate
a hrasvena caite āmukte bhavato hrasvake tadā
c anurūpeṇa cāmukte tatpramāṇe hi jāyataḥ
a evaṃvidhe mamaite vai kuṇḍale paramārcite
c triṣu lokeṣu vikhyāte tad abhijñānam ānaya
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a sa mitrasaham āsādya tv abhijñānam ayācata
c tasmai dadāv abhijñānaṃ sa cekṣvākuvaras tadā
 saudāsa uvāca
a na caivaiṣā gatiḥ kṣemyā na cānyā vidyate gatiḥ
c etan me matam ājñāya prayaccha maṇikuṇḍale
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a ity uktas tām uttaṅkas tu bhartur vākyam athābravīt
c śrutvā ca sā tataḥ prādāt tasmai te maṇikuṇḍale
a avāpya kuṇḍale te tu rājānaṃ punar abravīt
c kim etad guhyavacanaṃ śrotum icchāmi pārthiva
 saudāsa uvāca
a prajā nisargād viprān vai kṣatriyāḥ pūjayanti ha
c viprebhyaś cāpi bahavo doṣāḥ prādurbhavanti naḥ
a so 'haṃ dvijebhyaḥ praṇato viprād doṣam avāptavān
c gatim anyāṃ na paśyāmi madayantīsahāyavān
c na cānyām api paśyāmi gatiṃ gatimatāṃ vara
e svargadvārasya gamane sthāne ceha dvijottama
a na hi rājñā viśeṣeṇa viruddhena dvijātibhiḥ
c śakyaṃ nṛloke saṃsthātuṃ pretya vā sukham edhitum
a tad iṣṭe te mayaivaite datte sve maṇikuṇḍale
c yaḥ kṛtas te 'dya samayaḥ saphalaṃ taṃ kuruṣva me
 uttaṅka uvāca
a rājaṃs tatheha kartāsmi punar eṣyāmi te vaśam
c praśnaṃ tu kaṃ cit praṣṭuṃ tvāṃ vyavasiṣye paraṃtapa
 saudāsa uvāca
a brūhi vipra yathākāmaṃ prativaktāsmi te vacaḥ
c chettāsmi saṃśayaṃ te 'dya na me 'trāsti vicāraṇā
 uttaṅka uvāca
a prāhur vāksaṃgataṃ mitraṃ dharmanaipuṇyadarśinaḥ
c mitreṣu yaś ca viṣamaḥ stena ity eva taṃ viduḥ
a sa bhavān mitratām adya saṃprāpto mama pārthiva
c sa me buddhiṃ prayacchasva samāṃ buddhimatāṃ vara
a avāptārtho 'ham adyeha bhavāṃś ca puruṣādakaḥ
c bhavatsakāśam āgantuṃ kṣamaṃ mama na veti vā
 saudāsa uvāca
a kṣamaṃ ced iha vaktavyaṃ mayā dvijavarottama
c matsamīpaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha nāgantavyaṃ kathaṃ cana
a evaṃ tava prapaśyāmi śreyo bhṛgukulodvaha
c āgacchato hi te vipra bhaven mṛtyur asaṃśayam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a ity uktaḥ sa tadā rājñā kṣamaṃ buddhimatā hitam
c samanujñāpya rājānam ahalyāṃ prati jagmivān
a gṛhītvā kuṇḍale divye gurupatnyāḥ priyaṃkaraḥ
c javena mahatā prāyād gautamasyāśramaṃ prati
a yathā tayo rakṣaṇaṃ ca madayantyābhibhāṣitam
c tathā te kuṇḍale baddhvā tathā kṛṣṇājine 'nayat
a sa kasmiṃś cit kṣudhāviṣṭaḥ phalabhārasamanvitam
c bilvaṃ dadarśa kasmiṃś cid āruroha kṣudhānvitaḥ
a śākhāsv āsajya tasyaiva kṛṣṇājinam ariṃdama
b pātayām āsa bilvāni tadā sa dvijapuṃgavaḥ
b atha pātayamānasya bilvāpahṛtacakṣuṣaḥ
b nyapataṃs tāni bilvāni tasminn evājine vibho
c yasmiṃs te kuṇḍale baddhe tadā dvijavareṇa vai
d bilvaprahārais tasyātha vyaśīryād bandhanaṃ tathā
d sakuṇḍalaṃ tad ajinaṃ papāta sahasā taroḥ
a viśīrṇabandhane tasmin gate kṛṣṇājine mahīm
c apaśyad bhujagaḥ kaś cit te tatra maṇikuṇḍale
a airāvatakulotpannaḥ śīghro bhūtvā tadā sa vai
c vidaśyāsyena valmīkaṃ viveśātha sa kuṇḍale
a hriyamāṇe tu dṛṣṭvā sa kuṇḍale bhujagena ha
c papāta vṛkṣāt sodvego duḥkhāt paramakopanaḥ
a sa daṇḍakāṣṭham ādāya valmīkam akhanat tadā
b ahāni triṃśad avyagraḥ pañca cānyāni bhārata
c krodhāmarṣābhitaptāṅgas tato vai dvijapuṃgavaḥ
a tasya vegam asahyaṃ tam asahantī vasuṃdharā
c daṇḍakāṣṭhābhinunnāṅgī cacāla bhṛśam āturā
a tataḥ khanata evātha viprarṣer dharaṇītalam
c nāgalokasya panthānaṃ kartukāmasya niścayāt
a rathena hariyuktena taṃ deśam upajagmivān
c vajrapāṇir mahātejā dadarśa ca dvijottamam
a sa tu taṃ brāhmaṇo bhūtvā tasya duḥkhena duḥkhitaḥ
c uttaṅkam abravīt tāta naitac chakyaṃ tvayeti vai
a ito hi nāgaloko vai yojanāni sahasraśaḥ
b yatra te kuṇḍale nīte bhujagena dvijottama
c na daṇḍakāṣṭhasādhyaṃ ca manye kāryam idaṃ tava
 uttaṅka uvāca
a nāgaloke yadi brahman na śakye kuṇḍale mayā
c prāptuṃ prāṇān vimokṣyāmi paśyatas te dvijottama
a yadā sa nāśakat tasya niścayaṃ kartum anyathā
c vajrapāṇis tadā daṇḍaṃ vajrāstreṇa yuyoja ha
a tato vajraprahārais tair dāryamāṇā vasuṃdharā
c nāgalokasya panthānam akaroj janamejaya
a sa tena mārgeṇa tadā nāgalokaṃ viveśa ha
c dadarśa nāgalokaṃ ca yojanāni sahasraśaḥ
a prākāranicayair divyair maṇimuktābhyalaṃkṛtaiḥ
c upapannaṃ mahābhāga śātakumbhamayais tathā
a vāpīḥ sphaṭikasopānā nadīś ca vimalodakāḥ
c dadarśa vṛkṣāṃś ca bahūn nānādvijagaṇāyutān
a tasya lokasya ca dvāraṃ dadarśa sa bhṛgūdvahaḥ
c pañcayojanavistāram āyataṃ śatayojanam
a nāgalokam uttaṅkas tu prekṣya dīno 'bhavat tadā
c nirāśaś cābhavat tāta kuṇḍalāharaṇe punaḥ
a tatra provāca turagas taṃ kṛṣṇaśvetavāladhiḥ
c tāmrāsyanetraḥ kauravya prajvalann iva tejasā
a dhamasvāpānam etan me tatas tvaṃ vipra lalpsyase
c airāvatasuteneha tavānīte hi kuṇḍale
a mā jugupsāṃ kṛthāḥ putra tvam atrārthe kathaṃ cana
c tvayaitad dhi samācīrṇaṃ gautamasyāśrame tadā
 uttaṅka uvāca
a kathaṃ bhavantaṃ jānīyām upādhyāyāśramaṃ prati
c yan mayā cīrṇapūrvaṃ ca śrotum icchāmi tad dhy aham
 aśva uvāca
a guror guruṃ māṃ jānīhi jvalitaṃ jātavedasam
c tvayā hy ahaṃ sadā vatsa guror arthe 'bhipūjitaḥ
a satataṃ pūjito vipra śucinā bhṛgunandana
c tasmāc chreyo vidhāsyāmi tavaivaṃ kuru mā ciram
a ity uktaḥ sa tathākārṣīd uttaṅkaś citrabhānunā
c ghṛtārciḥ prītimāṃś cāpi prajajvāla didhakṣayā
a tato 'sya romakūpebhyo dhmāyamānasya bhārata
c ghanaḥ prādurabhūd dhūmo nāgalokabhayāvahaḥ
a tena dhūmena sahasā vardhamānena bhārata
c nāgaloke mahārāja na prajñāyata kiṃ cana
a hāhākṛtam abhūt sarvam airāvataniveśanam
c vāsukipramukhānāṃ ca nāgānāṃ janamejaya
a na prakāśanta veśmāni dhūmaruddhāni bhārata
c nīhārasaṃvṛtānīva vanāni girayas tathā
a te dhūmaraktanayanā vahnitejobhitāpitāḥ
c ājagmur niścayaṃ jñātuṃ bhārgavasyātitejasaḥ
a śrutvā ca niścayaṃ tasya maharṣes tigmatejasaḥ
c saṃbhrāntamanasaḥ sarve pūjāṃ cakrur yathāvidhi
a sarve prāñjalayo nāgā vṛddhabālapurogamāḥ
c śirobhiḥ praṇipatyocuḥ prasīda bhagavann iti
a prasādya brāhmaṇaṃ te tu pādyam arghyaṃ nivedya ca
c prāyacchan kuṇḍale divye pannagāḥ paramārcite
a tataḥ saṃpūjito nāgais tatrottaṅkaḥ pratāpavān
c agniṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā jagāma gurusadma tat
a sa gatvā tvarito rājan gautamasya niveśanam
c prāyacchat kuṇḍale divye gurupatnyai tadānagha
d vāsukipramukhānāṃ ca nāgānāṃ janamejaya
d sarvaṃ śaśaṃsa gurave yathāvad dvijasattamaḥ
a evaṃ mahātmanā tena trīṃl lokāñ janamejaya
c parikramyāhṛte divye tatas te maṇikuṇḍale
a evaṃprabhāvaḥ sa munir uttaṅko bharatarṣabha
c pareṇa tapasā yukto yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi
 janamejaya uvāca
a uttaṅkāya varaṃ dattvā govindo dvijasattama
c ata ūrdhvaṃ mahābāhuḥ kiṃ cakāra mahāyaśāḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a dattvā varam uttaṅkāya prāyāt sātyakinā saha
c dvārakām eva govindaḥ śīghravegair mahāhayaiḥ
a sarāṃsi ca nadīś caiva vanāni vividhāni ca
c atikramya sasādātha ramyāṃ dvāravatīṃ purīm
a vartamāne mahārāja mahe raivatakasya ca
c upāyāt puṇḍarīkākṣo yuyudhānānugas tadā
a alaṃkṛtas tu sa girir nānārūpavicitritaiḥ
c babhau rukmamayaiḥ kāśaiḥ sarvataḥ puruṣarṣabha
a kāñcanasragbhir agryābhiḥ sumanobhis tathaiva ca
c vāsobhiś ca mahāśailaḥ kalpavṛkṣaiś ca sarvaśaḥ
a dīpavṛkṣaiś ca sauvarṇair abhīkṣṇam upaśobhitaḥ
c guhānirjharadeśeṣu divābhūto babhūva ha
a patākābhir vicitrābhiḥ saghaṇṭābhiḥ samantataḥ
c puṃbhiḥ strībhiś ca saṃghuṣṭaḥ pragīta iva cābhavat
e atīva prekṣaṇīyo 'bhūn merur munigaṇair iva
a mattānāṃ hṛṣṭarūpāṇāṃ strīṇāṃ puṃsāṃ ca bhārata
c gāyatāṃ parvatendrasya divaspṛg iva nisvanaḥ
a pramattamattasaṃmattakṣveḍitotkṛṣṭasaṃkulā
c tathā kilakilāśabdair bhūr abhūt sumanoharā
a vipaṇāpaṇavān ramyo bhakṣyabhojyavihāravān
c vastramālyotkarayuto vīṇāveṇumṛdaṅgavān
d mālyotkarayuto vīṇāveṇuśaṅkhamṛdaṅgavān
a surāmaireyamiśreṇa bhakṣyabhojyena caiva ha
c dīnāndhakṛpaṇādibhyo dīyamānena cāniśam
e babhau paramakalyāṇo mahas tasya mahāgireḥ
a puṇyāvasathavān vīra puṇyakṛdbhir niṣevitaḥ
c vihāro vṛṣṇivīrāṇāṃ mahe raivatakasya ha
e sa nago veśmasaṃkīrṇo devaloka ivābabhau
a tadā ca kṛṣṇasāṃnidhyam āsādya bharatarṣabha
b stuvanty antarhitā devā gandharvāś ca saharṣibhiḥ
b sādhakaḥ sarvadharmāṇām asurāṇāṃ vināśakaḥ
b tvaṃ sraṣṭā sṛjyam ādhāraṃ kāraṇaṃ dharmavedavit
b tvayā yat kriyate deva na jānīmo 'tra māyayā
b kevalaṃ tv abhijānīmaḥ śaraṇaṃ parameśvaram
b brahmādīnāṃ ca govinda saṃnidhyaṃ śaraṇaṃ namaḥ
b iti stute mānuṣaiś ca pūjite devakīsute

a tataḥ saṃpūjyamānaḥ sa viveśa bhavanaṃ śubham
c govindaḥ sātyakiś caiva jagāma bhavanaṃ svakam
a viveśa ca sa hṛṣṭātmā cirakālapravāsakaḥ
c kṛtvā nasukaraṃ karma dānaveṣv iva vāsavaḥ
a upayātaṃ tu vārṣṇeyaṃ bhojavṛṣṇyandhakās tadā
c abhyagacchan mahātmānaṃ devā iva śatakratum
a sa tān abhyarcya medhāvī pṛṣṭvā ca kuśalaṃ tadā
b jaharṣa dhīmān dhīmadbhiḥ pravṛttaḥ sa mudāyutaḥ
b dṛṣṭvā samāgataṃ kṛṣṇaṃ snehena muśalāyudhaḥ
b vanamālī halī rāmaḥ paryaṣvajata keśavam
b kṛṣṇo 'pi bhrātaraṃ rāmaṃ yatnāt samabhivādya ca
c abhyavādayata prītaḥ pitaraṃ mātaraṃ tathā
a tābhyāṃ ca saṃpariṣvaktaḥ sāntvitaś ca mahābhujaḥ
c upopaviṣṭas taiḥ sarvair vṛṣṇibhiḥ parivāritaḥ
a sa viśrānto mahātejāḥ kṛtapādāvasecanaḥ
c kathayām āsa taṃ kṛṣṇaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ pitrā mahāhavam
 vasudeva uvāca
a śrutavān asmi vārṣṇeya saṃgrāmaṃ paramādbhutam
c narāṇāṃ vadatāṃ putra kathodghāteṣu nityaśaḥ
a tvaṃ tu pratyakṣadarśī ca kāryajñaś ca mahābhuja
c tasmāt prabrūhi saṃgrāmaṃ yāthātathyena me 'nagha
a yathā tad abhavad yuddhaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām
c bhīṣmakarṇakṛpadroṇaśalyādibhir anuttamam

c nānāveṣākṛtimatāṃ nānādeśanivāsinām
a ity uktaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ pitrā mātus tadantike
c śaśaṃsa kuruvīrāṇāṃ saṃgrāme nidhanaṃ yathā
 vāsudeva uvāca
a atyadbhutāni karmāṇi kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahātmanām
c bahulatvān na saṃkhyātuṃ śakyāny abdaśatair api
a prādhānyatas tu gadataḥ samāsenaiva me śṛṇu
c karmāṇi pṛthivīśānāṃ yathāvad amaradyute
a bhīṣmaḥ senāpatir abhūd ekādaśacamūpatiḥ
c kauravyaḥ kauraveyāṇāṃ devānām iva vāsavaḥ
a śikhaṇḍī pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ netā saptacamūpatiḥ
c babhūva rakṣito dhīmān dhīmatā savyasācinā
a teṣāṃ tad abhavad yuddhaṃ daśāhāni mahātmanām
c kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca sumahad romaharṣaṇam
a tataḥ śikhaṇḍī gāṅgeyam ayudhyantaṃ mahāhave
b ayudhyamānaṃ gāṅgeyaṃ śikhaṇḍī taṃ mahādyutim
c jaghāna bahubhir bāṇaiḥ saha gāṇḍīvadhanvanā

c ayanaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ hitvā saṃprāpte cottarāyaṇe

c pravīraḥ kauravendrasya kāvyo daityapater iva
a akṣauhiṇībhiḥ śiṣṭābhir navabhir dvijasattamaḥ
c saṃvṛtaḥ samaraślāghī guptaḥ kṛpavṛṣādibhiḥ
d kṛtvā vyūhaṃ mahāyuddhe pātayitvā mahārathān
d antakapratimaś cogro rātriyuddhe dahan prajāḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnas tv abhūn netā pāṇḍavānāṃ mahāstravit
c gupto bhīmena tejasvī mitreṇa varuṇo yathā
a pañcasenāparivṛto droṇaprepsur mahāmanāḥ
c pitur nikārān saṃsmṛtya raṇe karmākaron mahat
a tasmiṃs te pṛthivīpālā droṇapārṣatasaṃgare
c nānādigāgatā vīrāḥ prāyaśo nidhanaṃ gatāḥ
a dināni pañca tad yuddham abhūt paramadāruṇam
c tato droṇaḥ pariśrānto dhṛṣṭadyumnavaśaṃ gataḥ
a tataḥ senāpatir abhūt karṇo dauryodhane bale
c akṣauhiṇībhiḥ śiṣṭābhir vṛtaḥ pañcabhir āhave
a tisras tu pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ camvo bībhatsupālitāḥ
c hatapravīrabhūyiṣṭhā babhūvuḥ samavasthitāḥ
a tataḥ pārthaṃ samāsādya pataṃga iva pāvakam
c pañcatvam agamat sautir dvitīye 'hani dāruṇe
d dvitīye 'hani sa tadā phalgunena nipātitaḥ
d pratāpya pāṇḍavān sarvān pāñcālān astratejasā
d saputraḥ samare karṇaḥ saṃśāntaḥ pārthatejasā
a hate karṇe tu kauravyā nirutsāhā hataujasaḥ
c akṣauhiṇībhis tisṛbhir madreśaṃ paryavārayan
a hatavāhanabhūyiṣṭhāḥ pāṇḍavās tu yudhiṣṭhiram
c akṣauhiṇyā nirutsāhāḥ śiṣṭayā paryavārayan
a avadhīn madrarājānaṃ kururājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c tasmiṃs tathārdhadivase karma kṛtvā suduṣkaram
a hate śalye tu śakuniṃ sahadevo mahāmanāḥ
c āhartāraṃ kales tasya jaghānāmitavikramaḥ
a nihate śakunau rājā dhārtarāṣṭraḥ sudurmanāḥ
c apākrāmad gadāpāṇir hatabhūyiṣṭhasainikaḥ

c hrade dvaipāyane cāpi salilasthaṃ dadarśa tam

c upopaviviśur hṛṣṭā hradasthaṃ pañca pāṇḍavāḥ
a vigāhya salilaṃ tv āśu vāgbāṇair bhṛśavikṣataḥ
c utthāya sa gadāpāṇir yuddhāya samupasthitaḥ
a tataḥ sa nihato rājā dhārtarāṣṭro mahāmṛdhe
c bhīmasenena vikramya paśyatāṃ pṛthivīkṣitām

c nihataṃ droṇaputreṇa pitur vadham amṛṣyatā
a hataputrā hatabalā hatamitrā mayā saha
c yuyudhānadvitīyena pañca śiṣṭāḥ sma pāṇḍavāḥ
a sahaiva kṛpabhojābhyāṃ drauṇir yuddhād amucyata
c yuyutsuś cāpi kauravyo muktaḥ pāṇḍavasaṃśrayāt
a nihate kauravendre ca sānubandhe suyodhane
c viduraḥ saṃjayaś caiva dharmarājam upasthitau
a evaṃ tad abhavad yuddham ahāny aṣṭādaśa prabho
c yatra te pṛthivīpālā nihatāḥ svargam āvasan
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a śṛṇvatāṃ tu mahārāja kathāṃ tāṃ romaharṣaṇīm
c duḥkhaharṣaparikleśā vṛṣṇīnām abhavaṃs tadā
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a kathayann eva tu tadā vāsudevaḥ pratāpavān
c mahābhāratayuddhaṃ tat kathānte pitur agrataḥ
a abhimanyor vadhaṃ vīraḥ so 'tyakrāmata bhārata
c apriyaṃ vasudevasya mā bhūd iti mahāmanāḥ
a mā dauhitravadhaṃ śrutvā vasudevo mahātyayam

a tām apaśyan nipatitāṃ vasudevaḥ kṣitau tadā

a tataḥ sa dauhitravadhād duḥkhaśokasamanvitaḥ
c vasudevo mahārāja kṛṣṇaṃ vākyam athābravīt
a nanu tvaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣa satyavāg bhuvi viśrutaḥ
c yad dauhitravadhaṃ me 'dya na khyāpayasi śatruhan

c māṃ cāpi puṇḍarīkākṣa capalākṣaḥ priyo mama
a āhavaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā kaccin na nihataḥ paraiḥ
c kaccin mukhaṃ na govinda tenājau vikṛtaṃ kṛtam
a sa hi kṛṣṇa mahātejāḥ ślāghann iva mamāgrataḥ
c bālabhāvena vijayam ātmano 'kathayat prabhuḥ
a kaccin na vikṛto bālo droṇakarṇakṛpādibhiḥ
c dharaṇyāṃ nihataḥ śete tan mamācakṣva keśava
a sa hi droṇaṃ ca bhīṣmaṃ ca karṇaṃ ca rathināṃ varam
c spardhate sma raṇe nityaṃ duhituḥ putrako mama
a evaṃvidhaṃ bahu tadā vilapantaṃ suduḥkhitam
c pitaraṃ duḥkhitataro govindo vākyam abravīt
a na tena vikṛtaṃ vaktraṃ kṛtaṃ saṃgrāmamūrdhani
c na pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtaś cāpi saṃgrāmas tena dustaraḥ
a nihatya pṛthivīpālān sahasraśatasaṃghaśaḥ
c khedito droṇakarṇābhyāṃ dauḥśāsanivaśaṃ gataḥ
a eko hy ekena satataṃ yudhyamāno yadi prabho
c na sa śakyeta saṃgrāme nihantum api vajriṇā
a samāhūte tu saṃgrāme pārthe saṃśaptakais tadā
c paryavāryata saṃkruddhaiḥ sa droṇādibhir āhave

c dauhitras tava vārṣṇeya dauḥśāsanivaśaṃ gataḥ
a nūnaṃ ca sa gataḥ svargaṃ jahi śokaṃ mahāmate
c na hi vyasanam āsādya sīdante sannarāḥ kva cit
a droṇakarṇaprabhṛtayo yena pratisamāsitāḥ
c raṇe mahendrapratimāḥ sa kathaṃ nāpnuyād divam
a sa śokaṃ jahi durdharṣa mā ca manyuvaśaṃ gamaḥ
c śastrapūtāṃ hi sa gatiṃ gataḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ
a tasmiṃs tu nihate vīre subhadreyaṃ svasā mama
c duḥkhārtātho pṛthāṃ prāpya kurarīva nanāda ha
a draupadīṃ ca samāsādya paryapṛcchata duḥkhitā
c ārye kva dārakāḥ sarve draṣṭum icchāmi tān aham
a asyās tu vacanaṃ śrutvā sarvās tāḥ kuruyoṣitaḥ
c bhujābhyāṃ parigṛhyaināṃ cukruśuḥ paramārtavat
a uttarāṃ cābravīd bhadrā bhadre bhartā kva te gataḥ
c kṣipram āgamanaṃ mahyaṃ tasmai tvaṃ vedayasva ha
a nanu nāma sa vairāṭi śrutvā mama giraṃ purā
c bhavanān niṣpataty āśu kasmān nābhyeti te patiḥ
a abhimanyo kuśalino mātulās te mahārathāḥ
c kuśalaṃ cābruvan sarve tvāṃ yuyutsum ihāgatam

c kasmād eva vilapatīṃ nādyeha pratibhāṣase

c śrutvā pṛthā suduḥkhārtā śanair vākyam athābravīt
a subhadre vāsudevena tathā sātyakinā raṇe
b evaṃ vilapatīṃ tāṃ tu sātyakis tu tadābravīt
c pitrā ca pālito bālaḥ sa hataḥ kāladharmaṇā
a īdṛśo martyadharmo 'yaṃ mā śuco yadunandini
c putro hi tava durdharṣaḥ saṃprāptaḥ paramāṃ gatim
a kule mahati jātāsi kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahātmanām
c mā śucaś capalākṣaṃ tvaṃ puṇḍarīkanibhekṣaṇe
a uttarāṃ tvam avekṣasva garbhiṇīṃ mā śucaḥ śubhe
c putram eṣā hi tasyāśu janayiṣyati bhāminī
a evam āśvāsayitvaināṃ kuntī yadukulodvaha
c vihāya śokaṃ durdharṣaṃ śrāddham asya hy akalpayat
a samanujñāpya dharmajñā rājānaṃ bhīmam eva ca
c yamau yamopamau caiva dadau dānāny anekaśaḥ
a tataḥ pradāya bahvīr gā brāhmaṇebhyo yadūdvaha
c samahṛṣyata vārṣṇeyī vairāṭīṃ cābravīd idam
a vairāṭi neha saṃtāpas tvayā kāryo yaśasvini
c bhartāraṃ prati suśroṇi garbhasthaṃ rakṣa me śiśum
a evam uktvā tataḥ kuntī virarāma mahādyute
c tām anujñāpya caivemāṃ subhadrāṃ samupānayam
a evaṃ sa nidhanaṃ prāpto dauhitras tava mādhava
c saṃtāpaṃ jahi durdharṣa mā ca śoke manaḥ kṛthāḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a etac chrutvā tu putrasya vacaḥ śūrātmajas tadā
c vihāya śokaṃ dharmātmā dadau śrāddham anuttamam
a tathaiva vāsudevo 'pi svasrīyasya mahātmanaḥ
c dayitasya pitur nityam akarod aurdhvadehikam
a ṣaṣṭiṃ śatasahasrāṇi brāhmaṇānāṃ mahābhujaḥ
c vidhivad bhojayām āsa bhojyaṃ sarvaguṇānvitam
a ācchādya ca mahābāhur dhanatṛṣṇām apānudat
c brāhmaṇānāṃ tadā kṛṣṇas tad abhūd romaharṣaṇam
a suvarṇaṃ caiva gāś caiva śayanācchādanaṃ tathā
c dīyamānaṃ tadā viprāḥ prabhūtam iti cābruvan
a vāsudevo 'tha dāśārho baladevaḥ sasātyakiḥ
c abhimanyos tadā śrāddham akurvan satyakas tadā
e atīva duḥkhasaṃtaptā na śamaṃ copalebhire
a tathaiva pāṇḍavā vīrā nagare nāgasāhvaye
c nopagacchanti vai śāntim abhimanyuvinākṛtāḥ
a subahūni ca rājendra divasāni virāṭajā
c nābhuṅkta patiśokārtā tad abhūt karuṇaṃ mahat
e kukṣistha eva tasyāstu sa garbhaḥ saṃpralīyata
f dhriyamāṇe 'tha tasmiṃs tu garbhe kukṣistha eva ha
a ājagāma tato vyāso jñātvā divyena cakṣuṣā
c āgamya cābravīd dhīmān pṛthāṃ pṛthulalocanām
e uttarāṃ ca mahātejāḥ śokaḥ saṃtyajyatām ayam
a janiṣyati mahātejāḥ putras tava yaśasvini
c prabhāvād vāsudevasya mama vyāharaṇād api
e pāṇḍavānām ayaṃ cānte pālayiṣyati medinīm
a dhanaṃjayaṃ ca saṃprekṣya dharmarājasya paśyataḥ
c vyāso vākyam uvācedaṃ harṣayann iva bhārata
a pautras tava mahābāho janiṣyati mahāmanāḥ
c pṛthvīṃ sāgaraparyantāṃ pālayiṣyati caiva ha
a tasmāc chokaṃ kuruśreṣṭha jahi tvam arikarśana
c vicāryam atra na hi te satyam etad bhaviṣyati
a yac cāpi vṛṣṇivīreṇa kṛṣṇena kurunandana
c puroktaṃ tat tathā bhāvi mā te 'trāstu vicāraṇā
a vibudhānāṃ gato lokān akṣayān ātmanirjitān
c na sa śocyas tvayā tāta na cānyaiḥ kurubhis tathā
a evaṃ pitāmahenokto dharmātmā sa dhanaṃjayaḥ
c tyaktvā śokaṃ mahārāja hṛṣṭarūpo 'bhavat tadā
a pitāpi tava dharmajña garbhe tasmin mahāmate
c avardhata yathākālaṃ śuklapakṣe yathā śaśī
a tataḥ saṃcodayām āsa vyāso dharmātmajaṃ nṛpam
c aśvamedhaṃ prati tadā tataḥ so 'ntarhito 'bhavat
a dharmarājo 'pi medhāvī śrutvā vyāsasya tad vacaḥ
c vittopanayane tāta cakāra gamane matim
 janamejaya uvāca
a śrutvaitad vacanaṃ brahman vyāsenoktaṃ mahātmanā
c aśvamedhaṃ prati tadā kiṃ nṛpaḥ pracakāra ha
a ratnaṃ ca yan maruttena nihitaṃ pṛthivītale
c tad avāpa kathaṃ ceti tan me brūhi dvijottama
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a śrutvā dvaipāyanavaco dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c bhrātṝn sarvān samānāyya kāle vacanam abravīt
e arjunaṃ bhīmasenaṃ ca mādrīputrau yamāv api
f arjunaṃ nakulaṃ cāpi sahadevaṃ vṛkodaram

a āyatyāṃ ca tadātve ca sarveṣāṃ tad dhi no hitam

a te vayaṃ praṇipātena girīśasya mahātmanaḥ

a rakṣante ye ca tad dravyaṃ kiṃkarā raudradarśanāḥ
c te ca vaśyā bhaviṣyanti prasanne vṛṣabhadhvaje

a modakaiḥ pāyasenātha māṃsāpūpais tathaiva ca

d prayayuḥ pāṇḍavā vīrā niyamasthāḥ śucivratāḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tatas te prayayur hṛṣṭāḥ prahṛṣṭanaravāhanāḥ
c rathaghoṣeṇa mahatā pūrayanto vasuṃdharām
a saṃstūyamānāḥ stutibhiḥ sūtamāgadhabandibhiḥ

a jayāśiṣaḥ prahṛṣṭānāṃ narāṇāṃ pathi pāṇḍavaḥ

a adyaiva nakṣatram ahaś ca puṇyaṃ

upoṣyatāṃ cāpi bhavadbhir adya
a śrutvā tu teṣāṃ dvijasattamānāṃ

c ūṣuḥ pratītāḥ kuśasaṃstareṣu

a tato niśā sā vyagaman mahātmanāṃ

 brāhmaṇā ūcuḥ

 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a śrutvā tu vacanaṃ teṣāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c girīśasya yathānyāyam upahāram upāharat

a yakṣendrāya kuberāya maṇibhadrāya caiva ha

b odanaṃ kumbhaśaḥ kṛtvā purodhāḥ samupāharat

b naktaṃcarāṇāṃ bhūtānāṃ vyādideśa baliṃ tadā

c arcayitvā dvijāgryān sa svasti vācya ca vīryavān
a teṣāṃ puṇyāhaghoṣeṇa tejasā samavasthitaḥ
c prītimān sa kuruśreṣṭhaḥ khānayām āsa taṃ nidhim

 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a etasminn eva kāle tu vāsudevo 'pi vīryavān

c pratyagṛhṇād yathānyāyaṃ viduraś ca mahāmanāḥ

c āviśya pradiśaḥ sarvāḥ punar eva vyupāramat

c krośantīm abhidhāveti vāsudevaṃ punaḥ punaḥ

c savikrośaṃ sakaruṇaṃ bāndhavānāṃ striyo nṛpa
a tataḥ kṛṣṇaṃ samāsādya kuntī rājasutā tadā
c provāca rājaśārdūla bāṣpagadgadayā girā
a vāsudeva mahābāho suprajā devakī tvayā
c tvaṃ no gatiḥ pratiṣṭhā ca tvadāyattam idaṃ kulam

c aśvatthāmnā hato jātas tam ujjīvaya keśava

c ahaṃ saṃjīvayiṣyāmi mṛtaṃ jātam iti prabho
a so 'yaṃ jāto mṛtas tāta paśyainaṃ puruṣarṣabha
c uttarāṃ ca subhadrāṃ ca draupadīṃ māṃ ca mādhava
a dharmaputraṃ ca bhīmaṃ ca phalgunaṃ nakulaṃ tathā
c sahadevaṃ ca durdharṣa sarvān nas trātum arhasi
a asmin prāṇāḥ samāyattāḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mamaiva ca
c pāṇḍoś ca piṇḍo dāśārha tathaiva śvaśurasya me
a abhimanyoś ca bhadraṃ te priyasya sadṛśasya ca

a uttarā hi priyoktaṃ vai kathayaty arisūdana

a abravīt kila dāśārha vairāṭīm ārjuniḥ purā
c mātulasya kulaṃ bhadre tava putro gamiṣyati

a evam uktvā tu vārṣṇeyaṃ pṛthā pṛthulalocanā
c ucchritya bāhū duḥkhārtā tāś cānyāḥ prāpatan bhuvi

c bhūmau nipatitāṃ caināṃ sāntvayām āsa bhārata
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a utthitāyāṃ pṛthāyāṃ tu subhadrā bhrātaraṃ tadā
c dṛṣṭvā cukrośa duḥkhārtā vacanaṃ cedam abravīt

a bhavitātaḥ paraṃ duḥkhaṃ kiṃ nu manye janārdana

a yady evaṃ tvaṃ pratiśrutya na karoṣi vacaḥ śubham

a abhimanyoḥ suto vīra na saṃjīvati yady ayam
c jīvati tvayi durdharṣa kiṃ kariṣyāmy ahaṃ tvayā
a saṃjīvayainaṃ durdharṣa mṛtaṃ tvam abhimanyujam
c sadṛśākṣasutaṃ vīra sasyaṃ varṣann ivāmbudaḥ
a tvaṃ hi keśava dharmātmā satyavān satyavikramaḥ

a icchann api hi lokāṃs trīñ jīvayethā mṛtān imān
a   jīvati tvayi mānada
a pāṇḍavān api sarvāṃs tvaṃ
c kiṃ punar dayitaṃ jātaṃ svasrīyasyātmajaṃ mṛtam
a prabhāvajñāsmi te kṛṣṇa tasmād etad bravīmi te
c kuruṣva pāṇḍuputrāṇām imaṃ param anugraham
a svaseti vā mahābāho hataputreti vā punaḥ
c prapannā mām iyaṃ veti dayāṃ kartum ihārhasi
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktas tu rājendra keśihā duḥkhamūrchitaḥ
c tatheti vyājahāroccair hlādayann iva taṃ janam
a vākyena tena hi tadā taṃ janaṃ puruṣarṣabhaḥ
c hlādayām āsa sa vibhur gharmārtaṃ salilair iva
a tataḥ sa prāviśat tūrṇaṃ janmaveśma pitus tava
c arcitaṃ puruṣavyāghra sitair mālyair yathāvidhi
a apāṃ kumbhaiḥ supūrṇaiś ca vinyastaiḥ sarvatodiśam
c ghṛtena tindukālātaiḥ sarṣapaiś ca mahābhuja
a śastraiś ca vimalair nyastaiḥ pāvakaiś ca samantataḥ
c vṛddhābhiś cābhirāmābhiḥ paricārārtham acyutaḥ
a dakṣaiś ca parito vīra bhiṣagbhiḥ kuśalais tathā
c dadarśa ca sa tejasvī rakṣoghnāny api sarvaśaḥ
e dravyāṇi sthāpitāni sma vidhivat kuśalair janaiḥ
a tathāyuktaṃ ca tad dṛṣṭvā janmaveśma pitus tava
c hṛṣṭo 'bhavad dhṛṣīkeśaḥ sādhu sādhv iti cābravīt
a tathā bruvati vārṣṇeye prahṛṣṭavadane tadā
c draupadī tvaritā gatvā vairāṭīṃ vākyam abravīt
a ayam āyāti te bhadre śvaśuro madhusūdanaḥ
c purāṇarṣir acintyātmā samīpam aparājitaḥ
a sāpi bāṣpakalāṃ vācaṃ nigṛhyāśrūṇi caiva ha
c susaṃvītābhavad devī devavat kṛṣṇam īkṣatī
a sā tathā dūyamānena hṛdayena tapasvinī
c dṛṣṭvā govindam āyāntaṃ kṛpaṇaṃ paryadevayat
a puṇḍarīkākṣa paśyasva bālāv iha vinākṛtau
c abhimanyuṃ ca māṃ caiva hatau tulyaṃ janārdana
a vārṣṇeya madhuhan vīra śirasā tvāṃ prasādaye
c droṇaputrāstranirdagdhaṃ jīvayainaṃ mamātmajam
a yadi sma dharmarājñā vā bhīmasenena vā punaḥ
c tvayā vā puṇḍarīkākṣa vākyam uktam idaṃ bhavet
a ajānatīm iṣīkeyaṃ janitrīṃ hantv iti prabho
c aham eva vinaṣṭā syāṃ nedam evaṃgataṃ bhavet
a garbhasthasyāsya bālasya brahmāstreṇa nipātanam
b brahmāstreṇāsya bālasya garbhasthasya nikṛntanam
c kṛtvā nṛśaṃsaṃ durbuddhir drauṇiḥ kiṃ phalam aśnute
a sā tvā prasādya śirasā yāce śatrunibarhaṇa
c prāṇāṃs tyakṣyāmi govinda nāyaṃ saṃjīvate yadi
a asmin hi bahavaḥ sādho ye mamāsan manorathāḥ
c te droṇaputreṇa hatāḥ kiṃ nu jīvāmi keśava
a āsīn mama matiḥ kṛṣṇa pūrṇotsaṅgā janārdana
c abhivādayiṣye diṣṭyeti tad idaṃ vitathīkṛtam
a capalākṣasya dāyāde mṛte 'smin puruṣarṣabha
c viphalā me kṛtāḥ kṛṣṇa hṛdi sarve manorathāḥ
a capalākṣaḥ kilātīva priyas te madhusūdana
c sutaṃ paśyasva tasyemaṃ brahmāstreṇa nipātitam
a kṛtaghno 'yaṃ nṛśaṃso 'yaṃ yathāsya janakas tathā
c yaḥ pāṇḍavīṃ śriyaṃ tyaktvā gato 'dya yamasādanam
a mayā caitat pratijñātaṃ raṇamūrdhani keśava
c abhimanyau hate vīra tvām eṣyāmy acirād iti
a tac ca nākaravaṃ kṛṣṇa nṛśaṃsā jīvitapriyā
c idānīm āgatāṃ tatra kiṃ nu vakṣyati phālguniḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a saivaṃ vilapya karuṇaṃ sonmādeva tapasvinī
c uttarā nyapatad bhūmau kṛpaṇā putragṛddhinī
a tāṃ tu dṛṣṭvā nipatitāṃ hatabandhuparicchadām
c cukrośa kuntī duḥkhārtā sarvāś ca bharatastriyaḥ
a muhūrtam iva tad rājan pāṇḍavānāṃ niveśanam
c aprekṣaṇīyam abhavad ārtasvaranināditam
a sā muhūrtaṃ ca rājendra putraśokābhipīḍitā
c kaśmalābhihatā vīra vairāṭī tv abhavat tadā
a pratilabhya tu sā saṃjñām uttarā bharatarṣabha
c aṅkam āropya taṃ putram idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a dharmajñasya sutaḥ saṃs tvam adharmam avabudhyase
c yas tvaṃ vṛṣṇipravīrasya kuruṣe nābhivādanam
a putra gatvā mama vaco brūyās tvaṃ pitaraṃ tava
c durmaraṃ prāṇināṃ vīra kāle prāpte kathaṃ cana
a yāhaṃ tvayā vihīnādya patyā putreṇa caiva ha
c martavye sati jīvāmi hatasvastir akiṃcanā
a atha vā dharmarājñāham anujñātā mahābhuja
c bhakṣayiṣye viṣaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ pravekṣye vā hutāśanam
a atha vā durmaraṃ tāta yad idaṃ me sahasradhā
c patiputravihīnāyā hṛdayaṃ na vidīryate
a uttiṣṭha putra paśyemāṃ duḥkhitāṃ prapitāmahīm
c ārtām upaplutāṃ dīnāṃ nimagnāṃ śokasāgare
a āryāṃ ca paśya pāñcālīṃ sātvatīṃ ca tapasvinīm
c māṃ ca paśya suduḥkhārtāṃ vyādhaviddhāṃ mṛgīm iva
a uttiṣṭha paśya vadanaṃ lokanāthasya dhīmataḥ
c puṇḍarīkapalāśākṣaṃ pureva capalekṣaṇam
a evaṃ vipralapantīṃ tu dṛṣṭvā nipatitāṃ punaḥ
c uttarāṃ tāḥ striyaḥ sarvāḥ punar utthāpayanty uta
a utthāya tu punar dhairyāt tadā matsyapateḥ sutā
c prāñjaliḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ bhūmāv evābhyavādayat
a śrutvā sa tasyā vipulaṃ vilāpaṃ puruṣarṣabhaḥ
c upaspṛśya tataḥ kṛṣṇo brahmāstraṃ saṃjahāra tat
a pratijajñe ca dāśārhas tasya jīvitam acyutaḥ
c abravīc ca viśuddhātmā sarvaṃ viśrāvayañ jagat
a na bravīmy uttare mithyā satyam etad bhaviṣyati
c eṣa saṃjīvayāmy enaṃ paśyatāṃ sarvadehinām
a noktapūrvaṃ mayā mithyā svaireṣv api kadā cana
c na ca yuddhe parāvṛttas tathā saṃjīvatām ayam
a yathā me dayito dharmo brāhmaṇāś ca viśeṣataḥ
c abhimanyoḥ suto jāto mṛto jīvatv ayaṃ tathā
a yathāhaṃ nābhijānāmi vijayena kadā cana
c virodhaṃ tena satyena mṛto jīvatv ayaṃ śiśuḥ
a yathā satyaṃ ca dharmaś ca mayi nityaṃ pratiṣṭhitau
c tathā mṛtaḥ śiśur ayaṃ jīvatām abhimanyujaḥ
a yathā kaṃsaś ca keśī ca dharmeṇa nihatau mayā
c tena satyena bālo 'yaṃ punar ujjīvatām iha
d yadi me brahmacaryaṃ syāt satyaṃ ca mayi saṃsthitam
d avyāhataṃ mamaiśvaryaṃ tena jīvatu bālakaḥ
a ity ukto vāsudevena sa bālo bharatarṣabha
b pādena kamalābhena brahmarudrārcitena ca
b sa spṛṣṭvā puṇḍarīkākṣa āpādatalamastakam
b spṛṣṭamātras tu kṛṣṇena sa hi bālo 'bhimanyujaḥ
c śanaiḥ śanair mahārāja prāspandata sacetanaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a brahmāstraṃ tu yadā rājan kṛṣṇena pratisaṃhṛtam
c tadā tad veśma te pitrā tejasābhividīpitam
a tato rakṣāṃsi sarvāṇi neśus tyaktvā gṛhaṃ tu tat
c antarikṣe ca vāg āsīt sādhu keśava sādhv iti
a tad astraṃ jvalitaṃ cāpi pitāmaham agāt tadā
c tataḥ prāṇān punar lebhe pitā tava janeśvara
e vyaceṣṭata ca bālo 'sau yathotsāhaṃ yathābalam
a babhūvur muditā rājaṃs tatas tā bharatastriyaḥ
c brāhmaṇān vācayām āsur govindasya ca śāsanāt
a tatas tā muditāḥ sarvāḥ praśaśaṃsur janārdanam
c striyo bharatasiṃhānāṃ nāvaṃ labdhveva pāragāḥ
a kuntī drupadaputrī ca subhadrā cottarā tathā
c striyaś cānyā nṛsiṃhānāṃ babhūvur hṛṣṭamānasāḥ
a tatra mallā naṭā jhallā granthikāḥ saukhaśāyikāḥ
c sūtamāgadhasaṃghāś cāpy astuvan vai janārdanam
e kuruvaṃśas tavākhyābhir āśīrbhir bharatarṣabha
f sabhājayata saṃhṛṣṭo mahārāja mahājanaḥ
a utthāya tu yathākālam uttarā yadunandanam
c abhyavādayata prītā saha putreṇa bhārata
e tatas tasyai dadau prīto bahuratnaṃ viśeṣataḥ
a tathānye vṛṣṇiśārdūlā nāma cāsyākarot prabhuḥ
c pitus tava mahārāja satyasaṃdho janārdanaḥ
a parikṣīṇe kule yasmāj jāto 'yam abhimanyujaḥ
c parikṣid iti nāmāsya bhavatv ity abravīt tadā
a so 'vardhata yathākālaṃ pitā tava narādhipa
c manaḥprahlādanaś cāsīt sarvalokasya bhārata
d pitāmahasamāno 'yaṃ parīkṣid bhavitā nṛpaḥ
a māsajātas tu te vīra pitā bhavati bhārata
c athājagmuḥ subahulaṃ ratnam ādāya pāṇḍavāḥ
d merukūṭanibhān bhāṇḍān kalaśān bhājanāni ca
d kṛtākṛtaṃ mahad dhemam ādāya puruṣottamāḥ
d bhārārtair vāhanais tatra gorute gorute pathi
d nivasanto yayur devaṃ smarantaḥ parameṣṭhinam
d nāsīt tatra naraḥ kaś cid abhārārto nṛpaṃ vinā
d bhīmādayo 'pi yajñārthaṃ vahante kiṃ punar janāḥ
a tān samīpagatāñ śrutvā niryayur vṛṣṇipuṃgavāḥ
c alaṃcakruś ca mālyaughaiḥ puruṣā nāgasāhvayam
a patākābhir vicitrābhir dhvajaiś ca vividhair api
c veśmāni samalaṃcakruḥ paurāś cāpi janādhipa
a devatāyatanānāṃ ca pūjā bahuvidhās tathā
c saṃdideśātha viduraḥ pāṇḍuputrapriyepsayā
a rājamārgāś ca tatrāsan sumanobhir alaṃkṛtāḥ
c śuśubhe tat puraṃ cāpi samudraughanibhasvanam
a nartakaiś cāpi nṛtyadbhir gāyanānāṃ ca nisvanaiḥ
c āsīd vaiśravaṇasyeva nivāsas tat puraṃ tadā
a bandibhiś ca narai rājan strīsahāyaiḥ sahasraśaḥ
c tatra tatra vivikteṣu samantād upaśobhitam
a patākā dhūyamānāś ca śvasatā mātariśvanā
c adarśayann iva tadā kurūn vai dakṣiṇottarān
a aghoṣayat tadā cāpi puruṣo rājadhūrgataḥ
c sarvarātrivihāro 'dya ratnābharaṇalakṣaṇaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tān samīpagatāñ śrutvā pāṇḍavāñ śatrukarśanaḥ
c vāsudevaḥ sahāmātyaḥ pratyudyāto didṛkṣayā
c   prayayau sasuhṛdgaṇaḥ
c te sametya yathānyāyaṃ
a te sametya yathānyāyaṃ pāṇḍavā vṛṣṇibhiḥ saha
c viviśuḥ sahitā rājan puraṃ vāraṇasāhvayam
a mahatas tasya sainyasya khuranemisvanena ca
c dyāvāpṛthivyau khaṃ caiva śabdenāsīt samāvṛtam
a te kośam agrataḥ kṛtvā viviśuḥ svapuraṃ tadā
c pāṇḍavāḥ prītamanasaḥ sāmātyāḥ sasuhṛdgaṇāḥ
a te sametya yathānyāyaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ janādhipam
c kīrtayantaḥ svanāmāni tasya pādau vavandire
a dhṛtarāṣṭrād anu ca te gāndhārīṃ subalātmajām
c kuntīṃ ca rājaśārdūla tadā bharatasattamāḥ
a viduraṃ pūjayitvā ca vaiśyāputraṃ sametya ca
c pūjyamānāḥ sma te vīrā vyarājanta viśāṃ pate
a tatas tat param āścaryaṃ vicitraṃ mahad adbhutam
c śuśruvus te tadā vīrāḥ pitus te janma bhārata
a tad upaśrutya te karma vāsudevasya dhīmataḥ
c pūjārhaṃ pūjayām āsuḥ kṛṣṇaṃ devakinandanam
a tataḥ katipayāhasya vyāsaḥ satyavatīsutaḥ
c ājagāma mahātejā nagaraṃ nāgasāhvayam
a tasya sarve yathānyāyaṃ pūjāṃ cakruḥ kurūdvahāḥ
c saha vṛṣṇyandhakavyāghrair upāsāṃ cakrire tadā
a tatra nānāvidhākārāḥ kathāḥ samanukīrtya vai
c yudhiṣṭhiro dharmasuto vyāsaṃ vacanam abravīt
a bhavatprasādād bhagavan yad idaṃ ratnam āhṛtam
c upayoktuṃ tad icchāmi vājimedhe mahākratau
a tad anujñātum icchāmi bhavatā munisattama
c tvadadhīnā vayaṃ sarve kṛṣṇasya ca mahātmanaḥ
 vyāsa uvāca
a anujānāmi rājaṃs tvāṃ kriyatāṃ yad anantaram
c yajasva vājimedhena vidhivad dakṣiṇāvatā
a aśvamedho hi rājendra pāvanaḥ sarvapāpmanām
c teneṣṭvā tvaṃ vipāpmā vai bhavitā nātra saṃśayaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a ity uktaḥ sa tu dharmātmā kururājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c aśvamedhasya kauravya cakārāharaṇe matim
a samanujñāpya tu sa taṃ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaṃ nṛpaḥ
c vāsudevam athāmantrya vāgmī vacanam abravīt
a devakī suprajā devī tvayā puruṣasattama
c yad brūyāṃ tvāṃ mahābāho tat kṛthās tvam ihācyuta
a tvatprabhāvārjitān bhogān aśnīma yadunandana
c parākrameṇa buddhyā ca tvayeyaṃ nirjitā mahī
a dīkṣayasva tvam ātmānaṃ tvaṃ naḥ paramako guruḥ
c tvayīṣṭavati dharmajña vipāpmā syām ahaṃ vibho
e tvaṃ hi yajño 'kṣaraḥ sarvas tvaṃ dharmas tvaṃ prajāpatiḥ
 vāsudeva uvāca
a tvam evaitan mahābāho vaktum arhasy ariṃdama
c tvaṃ gatiḥ sarvabhūtānām iti me niścitā matiḥ
a tvaṃ cādya kuruvīrāṇāṃ dharmeṇābhivirājase
c guṇabhūtāḥ sma te rājaṃs tvaṃ no rājan mato guruḥ
a yajasva madanujñātaḥ prāpta eva kratur mayā
c yunaktu no bhavān kārye yatra vāñchasi bhārata
e satyaṃ te pratijānāmi sarvaṃ kartāsmi te 'nagha
a bhīmasenārjunau caiva tathā mādravatīsutau
c iṣṭavanto bhaviṣyanti tvayīṣṭavati bhārata
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktas tu kṛṣṇena dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c vyāsam āmantrya medhāvī tato vacanam abravīt
a yathā kālaṃ bhavān vetti hayamedhasya tattvataḥ
c dīkṣayasva tadā mā tvaṃ tvayy āyatto hi me kratuḥ
 vyāsa uvāca
a ahaṃ pailo 'tha kaunteya yājñavalkyas tathaiva ca
c vidhānaṃ yad yathākālaṃ tat kartāro na saṃśayaḥ
a caitryāṃ hi paurṇamāsyāṃ ca tava dīkṣā bhaviṣyati
c saṃbhārāḥ saṃbhriyantāṃ te yajñārthaṃ puruṣarṣabha
a aśvavidyāvidaś caiva sūtā viprāś ca tadvidaḥ
c medhyam aśvaṃ parīkṣantāṃ tava yajñārthasiddhaye
a tam utsṛjya yathāśāstraṃ pṛthivīṃ sāgarāmbarām
c sa paryetu yaśo nāmnā tava pārthiva vardhayan
d   mahīṃ sāgaramekhalām
d rakṣitaḥ paryaṭann eva yaśovardhana tavāyatam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a ity uktaḥ sa tathety uktvā pāṇḍavaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ
c cakāra sarvaṃ rājendra yathoktaṃ brahmavādinā
e saṃbhārāś caiva rājendra sarve saṃkalpitābhavan
a sa saṃbhārān samāhṛtya nṛpo dharmātmajas tadā
c nyavedayad ameyātmā kṛṣṇadvaipāyanāya vai
a tato 'bravīn mahātejā vyāso dharmātmajaṃ nṛpam
c yathākālaṃ yathāyogaṃ sajjāḥ sma tava dīkṣaṇe
a sphyaś ca kūrcaś ca sauvarṇo yac cānyad api kaurava
c tatra yogyaṃ bhavet kiṃ cit tad raukmaṃ kriyatām iti
a aśvaś cotsṛjyatām adya pṛthvyām atha yathākramam
c suguptaś ca caratv eṣa yathāśāstraṃ yudhiṣṭhira
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a ayam aśvo mayā brahmann utsṛṣṭaḥ pṛthivīm imām
c cariṣyati yathākāmaṃ tatra vai saṃvidhīyatām
a pṛthivīṃ paryaṭantaṃ hi turagaṃ kāmacāriṇam
c kaḥ pālayed iti mune tad bhavān vaktum arhati
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a ity uktaḥ sa tu rājendra kṛṣṇadvaipāyano 'bravīt
c bhīmasenād avarajaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarvadhanuṣmatām
a jiṣṇuḥ sahiṣṇur dhṛṣṇuś ca sa enaṃ pālayiṣyati
c śaktaḥ sa hi mahīṃ jetuṃ nivātakavacāntakaḥ
a tasmin hy astrāṇi divyāni divyaṃ saṃhananaṃ tathā
c divyaṃ dhanuś ceṣudhī ca sa enam anuyāsyati
a sa hi dharmārthakuśalaḥ sarvavidyāviśāradaḥ
c yathāśāstraṃ nṛpaśreṣṭha cārayiṣyati te hayam
a rājaputro mahābāhuḥ śyāmo rājīvalocanaḥ
c abhimanyoḥ pitā vīraḥ sa enam anuyāsyati
a bhīmaseno 'pi tejasvī kaunteyo 'mitavikramaḥ
c samartho rakṣituṃ rāṣṭraṃ nakulaś ca viśāṃ pate
a sahadevas tu kauravya samādhāsyati buddhimān
c kuṭumbatantraṃ vidhivat sarvam eva mahāyaśāḥ
a tat tu sarvaṃ yathānyāyam uktaṃ kurukulodvahaḥ
c cakāra phalgunaṃ cāpi saṃdideśa hayaṃ prati
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a ehy arjuna tvayā vīra hayo 'yaṃ paripālyatām
c tvam arho rakṣituṃ hy enaṃ nānyaḥ kaś cana mānavaḥ
a ye cāpi tvāṃ mahābāho pratyudīyur narādhipāḥ
c tair vigraho yathā na syāt tathā kāryaṃ tvayānagha
a ākhyātavyaś ca bhavatā yajño 'yaṃ mama sarvaśaḥ
c pārthivebhyo mahābāho samaye gamyatām iti
a evam uktvā sa dharmātmā bhrātaraṃ savyasācinam
c bhīmaṃ ca nakulaṃ caiva puraguptau samādadhat
a kuṭumbatantre ca tathā sahadevaṃ yudhāṃ patim
c anumānya mahīpālaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a dīkṣākāle tu saṃprāpte tatas te sumahartvijaḥ
c vidhivad dīkṣayām āsur aśvamedhāya pārthivam
a kṛtvā sa paśubandhāṃś ca dīkṣitaḥ pāṇḍunandanaḥ
c dharmarājo mahātejāḥ sahartvigbhir vyarocata
a hayaś ca hayamedhārthaṃ svayaṃ sa brahmavādinā
c utsṛṣṭaḥ śāstravidhinā vyāsenāmitatejasā
a sa rājā dharmajo rājan dīkṣito vibabhau tadā
c hemamālī rukmakaṇṭhaḥ pradīpta iva pāvakaḥ
a kṛṣṇājinī daṇḍapāṇiḥ kṣaumavāsāḥ sa dharmajaḥ
c vibabhau dyutimān bhūyaḥ prajāpatir ivādhvare
a tathaivāsyartvijaḥ sarve tulyaveṣā viśāṃ pate
c babhūvur arjunaś caiva pradīpta iva pāvakaḥ
a śvetāśvaḥ kṛṣṇasāraṃ taṃ sasārāśvaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
c vidhivat pṛthivīpāla dharmarājasya śāsanāt
a vikṣipan gāṇḍivaṃ rājan baddhagodhāṅgulitravān
c tam aśvaṃ pṛthivīpāla mudā yuktaḥ sasāra ha
a ākumāraṃ tadā rājann āgamat tat puraṃ vibho
c draṣṭukāmaṃ kuruśreṣṭhaṃ prayāsyantaṃ dhanaṃjayam
a teṣām anyonyasaṃmardād ūṣmeva samajāyata
c didṛkṣūṇāṃ hayaṃ taṃ ca taṃ caiva hayasāriṇam
a tataḥ śabdo mahārāja daśāśāḥ pratipūrayan
c babhūva prekṣatāṃ nṝṇāṃ kuntīputraṃ dhanaṃjayam
a eṣa gacchati kaunteyas turagaś caiva dīptimān
c yam anveti mahābāhuḥ saṃspṛśan dhanur uttamam

c svasti te 'stu vrajāriṣṭaṃ punaś caihīti bhārata
a athāpare manuṣyendra puruṣā vākyam abruvan
c nainaṃ paśyāma saṃmarde dhanur etat pradṛśyate
a etad dhi bhīmanirhrādaṃ viśrutaṃ gāṇḍivaṃ dhanuḥ
c svasti gacchatv ariṣṭaṃ vai panthānam akutobhayam

a evamādyā manuṣyāṇāṃ strīṇāṃ ca bharatarṣabha
c śuśrāva madhurā vācaḥ punaḥ punar udīritāḥ
a yājñavalkyasya śiṣyaś ca kuśalo yajñakarmaṇi
c prāyāt pārthena sahitaḥ śāntyarthaṃ vedapāragaḥ
a brāhmaṇāś ca mahīpāla bahavo vedapāragāḥ
c anujagmur mahātmānaṃ kṣatriyāś ca viśo 'pi ca
a pāṇḍavaiḥ pṛthivīm aśvo nirjitām astratejasā
c cacāra sa mahārāja yathādeśaṃ sa sattama
a tatra yuddhāni vṛttāni yāny āsan pāṇḍavasya ha
c tāni vakṣyāmi te vīra vicitrāṇi mahānti ca
a sa hayaḥ pṛthivīṃ rājan pradakṣiṇam ariṃdama
c sasārottarataḥ pūrvaṃ tan nibodha mahīpate
a avamṛdnan sa rāṣṭrāṇi pārthivānāṃ hayottamaḥ
c śanais tadā pariyayau śvetāśvaś ca mahārathaḥ
a tatra saṃkalanā nāsti rājñām ayutaśas tadā
c ye 'yudhyanta mahārāja kṣatriyā hatabāndhavāḥ
a kirātā vikṛtā rājan bahavo 'sidhanurdharāḥ
c mlecchāś cānye bahuvidhāḥ pūrvaṃ vinikṛtā raṇe
a āryāś ca pṛthivīpālāḥ prahṛṣṭanaravāhanāḥ
c samīyuḥ pāṇḍuputreṇa bahavo yuddhadurmadāḥ
a evaṃ yuddhāni vṛttāni tatra tatra mahīpate
c arjunasya mahīpālair nānādeśanivāsibhiḥ
a yāni tūbhayato rājan prataptāni mahānti ca
c tāni yuddhāni vakṣyāmi kaunteyasya tavānagha
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a trigartair abhavad yuddhaṃ kṛtavairaiḥ kirīṭinaḥ
c mahārathasamājñātair hatānāṃ putranaptṛbhiḥ
a te samājñāya saṃprāptaṃ yajñiyaṃ turagottamam
c viṣayānte tato vīrā daṃśitāḥ paryavārayan
a rathino baddhatūṇīrāḥ sadaśvaiḥ samalaṃkṛtaiḥ

c vārayām āsa tān vīrān sāntvapūrvam ariṃdamaḥ
a tam anādṛtya te sarve śarair abhyahanaṃs tadā
c tamorajobhyāṃ saṃchannāṃs tān kirīṭī nyavārayat
a abravīc ca tato jiṣṇuḥ prahasann iva bhārata
c nivartadhvam adharmajñāḥ śreyo jīvitam eva vaḥ
a sa hi vīraḥ prayāsyan vai dharmarājena vāritaḥ
c hatabāndhavā na te pārtha hantavyāḥ pārthivā iti
a sa tadā tad vacaḥ śrutvā dharmarājasya dhīmataḥ
c tān nivartadhvam ity āha na nyavartanta cāpi te

c śatāny amuñcad rājendra laghvastram abhidarśayan
a tathaivānye maheṣvāsā ye tasyaivānuyāyinaḥ
c mumucuḥ śaravarṣāṇi dhanaṃjayavadhaiṣiṇaḥ
a sa tāñ jyāpuṅkhanirmuktair bahubhiḥ subahūñ śarān
c ciccheda pāṇḍavo rājaṃs te bhūmau nyapataṃs tadā
a ketuvarmā tu tejasvī tasyaivāvarajo yuvā
c yuyudhe bhrātur arthāya pāṇḍavena mahātmanā

c guḍākeśo mahātejā bālasya dhṛtavarmaṇaḥ
a na saṃdadhānaṃ dadṛśe nādadānaṃ ca taṃ tadā
c kirantam eva sa śarān dadṛśe pākaśāsaniḥ
a sa tu taṃ pūjayām āsa dhṛtavarmāṇam āhave
c manasā sa muhūrtaṃ vai raṇe samabhiharṣayan
d na vivyādha raṇe kruddhaḥ kuntīputro hasann iva
d saubhadrasyeva tat karma dṛṣṭvā bālasya vismitaḥ
a taṃ pannagam iva kruddhaṃ kuruvīraḥ smayann iva
c prītipūrvaṃ mahārāja prāṇair na vyaparopayat
a sa tathā rakṣyamāṇo vai pārthenāmitatejasā
c dhṛtavarmā śaraṃ tīkṣṇaṃ mumoca vijaye tadā
a sa tena vijayas tūrṇam asyan viddhaḥ kare bhṛśam
c mumoca gāṇḍīvaṃ duḥkhāt tat papātātha bhūtale
a dhanuṣaḥ patatas tasya savyasācikarād vibho
c indrasyevāyudhasyāsīd rūpaṃ bharatasattama
d babhūva sadṛśaṃ rūpaṃ śakracāpasya bhārata
a tasmin nipatite divye mahādhanuṣi pārthiva
c jahāsa sasvanaṃ hāsaṃ dhṛtavarmā mahāhave
a tato roṣānvito jiṣṇuḥ pramṛjya rudhiraṃ karāt
c dhanur ādatta tad divyaṃ śaravarṣaṃ vavarṣa ca
a tato halahalāśabdo divaspṛg abhavat tadā
c nānāvidhānāṃ bhūtānāṃ tat karmātīva śaṃsatām
a tataḥ saṃprekṣya taṃ kruddhaṃ kālāntakayamopamam
c jiṣṇuṃ traigartakā yodhās tvaritāḥ paryavārayan
a abhisṛtya parīpsārthaṃ tatas te dhṛtavarmaṇaḥ
c parivavrur guḍākeśaṃ tatrākrudhyad dhanaṃjayaḥ
a tato yodhāñ jaghānāśu teṣāṃ sa daśa cāṣṭa ca
c mahendravajrapratimair āyasair niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ

c śarair āśīviṣākārair jaghāna svanavad dhasan
a te bhagnamanasaḥ sarve traigartakamahārathāḥ
c diśo vidudruvuḥ sarvā dhanaṃjayaśarārditāḥ
d hatāvaśiṣṭā hi purā pārthaṃ dṛṣṭaparākramāḥ
a ta ūcuḥ puruṣavyāghraṃ saṃśaptakaniṣūdanam
c tava sma kiṃkarāḥ sarve sarve ca vaśagās tava
a ājñāpayasva naḥ pārtha prahvān preṣyān avasthitān
c kariṣyāmaḥ priyaṃ sarvaṃ tava kauravanandana
a etad ājñāya vacanaṃ sarvāṃs tān abravīt tadā
c jīvitaṃ rakṣata nṛpāḥ śāsanaṃ gṛhyatām iti
d āgacchadhvaṃ nṛpatayaḥ parāṃ caitrīm upasthitām
d yudhiṣṭhirasyāśvamedho bhavadbhir anubhūyatām
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a prāgjyotiṣam athābhyetya vyacarat sa hayottamaḥ
c bhagadattātmajas tatra niryayau raṇakarkaśaḥ
a sa hayaṃ pāṇḍuputrasya viṣayāntam upāgatam
c yuyudhe bharataśreṣṭha vajradatto mahīpatiḥ
a so 'bhiniryāya nagarād bhagadattasuto nṛpaḥ
c aśvam āyāntam unmathya nagarābhimukho yayau
a tam ālakṣya mahābāhuḥ kurūṇām ṛṣabhas tadā
c gāṇḍīvaṃ vikṣipaṃs tūrṇaṃ sahasā samupādravat
a tato gāṇḍīvanirmuktair iṣubhir mohito nṛpaḥ
c hayam utsṛjya taṃ vīras tataḥ pārtham upādravat
a punaḥ praviśya nagaraṃ daṃśitaḥ sa nṛpottamaḥ
c āruhya nāgapravaraṃ niryayau yuddhakāṅkṣayā
a pāṇḍureṇātapatreṇa dhriyamāṇena mūrdhani
c dodhūyatā cāmareṇa śvetena ca mahārathaḥ
d dodhūyamānena tathā cāmareṇa mahārathaḥ
a tataḥ pārthaṃ samāsādya pāṇḍavānāṃ mahāratham
c āhvayām āsa kauravyaṃ bālyān mohāc ca saṃyuge
a sa vāraṇaṃ nagaprakhyaṃ prabhinnakaraṭāmukham
c preṣayām āsa saṃkruddhas tataḥ śvetahayaṃ prati
a vikṣarantaṃ yathā meghaṃ paravāraṇavāraṇam
c śāstravat kalpitaṃ saṃkhye trisāhaṃ yuddhadurmadam
a pracodyamānaḥ sa gajas tena rājñā mahābalaḥ
c tadāṅkuśena vibabhāv utpatiṣyann ivāmbaram
a tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya kruddho rājan dhanaṃjayaḥ
c bhūmiṣṭho vāraṇagataṃ yodhayām āsa bhārata
a vajradattas tu saṃkruddho mumocāśu dhanaṃjaye
c tomarān agnisaṃkāśāñ śalabhān iva vegitān
a arjunas tān asaṃprāptān gāṇḍīvapreṣitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c dvidhā tridhā ca ciccheda kha eva khagamais tadā
a sa tān dṛṣṭvā tathā chinnāṃs tomarān bhagadattajaḥ
c iṣūn asaktāṃs tvaritaḥ prāhiṇot pāṇḍavaṃ prati
a tato 'rjunas tūrṇataraṃ rukmapuṅkhān ajihmagān
c preṣayām āsa saṃkruddho bhagadattātmajaṃ prati
a sa tair viddho mahātejā vajradatto mahāhave
c bhṛśāhataḥ papātorvyāṃ na tv enam ajahāt smṛtiḥ
a tataḥ sa punar āruhya vāraṇapravaraṃ raṇe
c avyagraḥ preṣayām āsa jayārthī vijayaṃ prati
a tasmai bāṇāṃs tato jiṣṇur nirmuktāśīviṣopamān
c preṣayām āsa saṃkruddho jvalitān iva pāvakān
a sa tair viddho mahānāgo visravan rudhiraṃ babhau
c himavān iva śailendro bahuprasravaṇas tadā
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evaṃ trirātram abhavat tad yuddhaṃ bharatarṣabha
c arjunasya narendreṇa vṛtreṇeva śatakratoḥ
a tataś caturthe divase vajradatto mahābalaḥ
c jahāsa sasvanaṃ hāsaṃ vākyaṃ cedam athābravīt
a arjunārjuna tiṣṭhasva na me jīvan vimokṣyase
c tvāṃ nihatya kariṣyāmi pitus toyaṃ yathāvidhi

c preṣayām āsa kauravya vāraṇaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ prati

c utpatiṣyann ivākāśam abhidudrāva pāṇḍavam
a agrahastapramuktena śīkareṇa sa phalgunam
c samukṣata mahārāja śailaṃ nīla ivāmbudaḥ
a sa tena preṣito rājñā meghavan ninadan muhuḥ

c āsasāda drutaṃ rājan kauravāṇāṃ mahāratham

c gāṇḍīvam āśritya balī na vyakampata śatruhā

c kāryavighnam anusmṛtya pūrvavairaṃ ca bhārata

c nivārayām āsa tadā veleva makarālayam
a sa nāgapravaro vīryād arjunena nivāritaḥ
c tasthau śarair vitunnāṅgaḥ śvāvic chalalito yathā
a nivāritaṃ gajaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagadattātmajo nṛpaḥ
c utsasarja śitān bāṇān arjune krodhamūrchitaḥ
a arjunas tu mahārāja śaraiḥ śaravighātibhiḥ
c vārayām āsa tān astāṃs tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a tataḥ punar atikruddho rājā prāgjyotiṣādhipaḥ
c preṣayām āsa nāgendraṃ balavac chvasanopamam
a tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya balavān pākaśāsaniḥ
c nārācam agnisaṃkāśaṃ prāhiṇod vāraṇaṃ prati
a sa tena vāraṇo rājan marmaṇy abhihato bhṛśam
c papāta sahasā bhūmau vajrarugṇa ivācalaḥ
a sa patañ śuśubhe nāgo dhanaṃjayaśarāhataḥ
c viśann iva mahāśailo mahīṃ vajraprapīḍitaḥ
a tasmin nipatite nāge vajradattasya pāṇḍavaḥ
c taṃ na bhetavyam ity āha tato bhūmigataṃ nṛpam
a abravīd dhi mahātejāḥ prasthitaṃ māṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c rājānas te na hantavyā dhanaṃjaya kathaṃ cana
a sarvam etan naravyāghra bhavatv etāvatā kṛtam
c yodhāś cāpi na hantavyā dhanaṃjaya raṇe tvayā
a vaktavyāś cāpi rājānaḥ sarvaiḥ saha suhṛjjanaiḥ
c yudhiṣṭhirasyāśvamedho bhavadbhir anubhūyatām
a iti bhrātṛvacaḥ śrutvā na hanmi tvāṃ janādhipa
c uttiṣṭha na bhayaṃ te 'sti svastimān gaccha pārthiva
a āgacchethā mahārāja parāṃ caitrīm upasthitām
c tadāśvamedho bhavitā dharmarājasya dhīmataḥ
a evam uktaḥ sa rājā tu bhagadattātmajas tadā
c tathety evābravīd vākyaṃ pāṇḍavenābhinirjitaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
 jitvā prasādya rājānaṃ bhagadattasutaṃ tadā
 visṛjya yāte turage saindhavān prati bhārata
a saindhavair abhavad yuddhaṃ tatas tasya kirīṭinaḥ
c hataśeṣair mahārāja hatānāṃ ca sutair api

c pratyudyayur amṛṣyanto rājānaḥ pāṇḍavarṣabham
a aśvaṃ ca taṃ parāmṛśya viṣayānte viṣopamāḥ
c na bhayaṃ cakrire pārthād bhīmasenād anantarāt
a te 'vidūrād dhanuṣpāṇiṃ yajñiyasya hayasya ca
c bībhatsuṃ pratyapadyanta padātinam avasthitam

c jigīṣanto naravyāghrāḥ pūrvaṃ vinikṛtā yudhi

c kīrtayantas tadā pārthaṃ śaravarṣair avākiran

c raṇe jayam abhīpsantaḥ kaunteyaṃ paryavārayan

c sarve yuyudhire vīrā rathasthās taṃ padātinam

c koṣṭhakīkṛtya kaunteyaṃ saṃprahṛṣṭam ayodhayan

c jayadrathasya kauravya samare savyasācinā

c taiḥ kīrṇaḥ śuśubhe pārtho ravir meghāntare yathā
a sa śaraiḥ samavacchanno dadṛśe pāṇḍavarṣabhaḥ
c pañjarāntarasaṃcārī śakunta iva bhārata
a tato hāhākṛtaṃ sarvaṃ kaunteye śarapīḍite
c trailokyam abhavad rājan raviś cāsīd rajoruṇaḥ
a tato vavau mahārāja māruto romaharṣaṇaḥ
c rāhur agrasad ādityaṃ yugapat somam eva ca
a ulkāś ca jaghnire sūryaṃ vikīryantyaḥ samantataḥ
c vepathuś cābhavad rājan kailāsasya mahāgireḥ
a mumucuś cāsram atyuṣṇaṃ duḥkhaśokasamanvitāḥ
c saptarṣayo jātabhayās tathā devarṣayo 'pi ca

c viparītas tadā rājaṃs tasminn utpātalakṣaṇe
a rāsabhāruṇasaṃkāśā dhanuṣmantaḥ savidyutaḥ
c āvṛtya gaganaṃ meghā mumucur māṃsaśoṇitam
a evam āsīt tadā vīre śaravarṣābhisaṃvṛte
c loke 'smin bharataśreṣṭha tad adbhutam ivābhavat

c mohāt papāta gāṇḍīvam āvāpaś ca karād api

c sarve vitrastamanasas tasya śāntiparābhavan

c brahmarṣayaś ca vijayaṃ jepuḥ pārthasya dhīmataḥ
a tataḥ pradīpite devaiḥ pārthatejasi pārthiva
c tasthāv acalavad dhīmān saṃgrāme paramāstravit
a vicakarṣa dhanur divyaṃ tataḥ kauravanandanaḥ
c yantrasyeveha śabdo 'bhūn mahāṃs tasya punaḥ punaḥ
a tataḥ sa śaravarṣāṇi pratyamitrān prati prabhuḥ
c vavarṣa dhanuṣā pārtho varṣāṇīva sureśvaraḥ
a tatas te saindhavā yodhāḥ sarva eva sarājakāḥ
c nādṛśyanta śaraiḥ kīrṇāḥ śalabhair iva pāvakāḥ
a tasya śabdena vitresur bhayārtāś ca vidudruvuḥ
c mumucuś cāśru śokārtāḥ suṣupuś cāpi saindhavāḥ
a tāṃs tu sarvān naraśreṣṭhaḥ sarvato vicaran balī
c alātacakravad rājañ śarajālaiḥ samarpayat
a tad indrajālapratimaṃ bāṇajālam amitrahā
c vyasṛjad dikṣu sarvāsu mahendra iva vajrabhṛt
a meghajālanibhaṃ sainyaṃ vidārya sa raviprabhaḥ
c vibabhau kauravaśreṣṭhaḥ śaradīva divākaraḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tato gāṇḍīvabhṛc chūro yuddhāya samavasthitaḥ
c vibabhau yudhi durdharṣo himavān acalo yathā
a tataḥ saindhavayodhās te punar eva vyavasthitāḥ
c vimuñcantaḥ susaṃrabdhāḥ śaravarṣāṇi bhārata
a tān prasahya mahāvīryaḥ punar eva vyavasthitān
c tataḥ provāca kaunteyo mumūrṣūñ ślakṣṇayā girā
a yudhyadhvaṃ parayā śaktyā yatadhvaṃ ca vadhe mama
c kurudhvaṃ sarvakāryāṇi mahad vo bhayam āgatam
a eṣa yotsyāmi vaḥ sarvān nivārya śaravāgurām
c tiṣṭhadhvaṃ yuddhamanaso darpaṃ vinayitāsmi vaḥ
a etāvad uktvā kauravyo ruṣā gāṇḍīvabhṛt tadā
c tato 'tha vacanaṃ smṛtvā bhrātur jyeṣṭhasya bhārata
a na hantavyā raṇe tāta kṣatriyā vijigīṣavaḥ
c jetavyāś ceti yat proktaṃ dharmarājñā mahātmanā
e cintayām āsa ca tadā phalgunaḥ puruṣarṣabhaḥ
a ity ukto 'haṃ narendreṇa na hantavyā nṛpā iti
c kathaṃ tan na mṛṣeha syād dharmarājavacaḥ śubham
a na hanyeraṃś ca rājāno rājñaś cājñā kṛtā bhavet
c iti saṃcintya sa tadā bhrātuḥ priyahite rataḥ
e provāca vākyaṃ dharmajñaḥ saindhavān yuddhadurmadān
a bālān striyo vā yuṣmākaṃ na haniṣye vyavasthitān
c yaś ca vakṣyati saṃgrāme tavāsmīti parājitaḥ
a etac chrutvā vaco mahyaṃ kurudhvaṃ hitam ātmanaḥ
c ato 'nyathā kṛcchragatā bhaviṣyatha mayārditāḥ
a evam uktvā tu tān vīrān yuyudhe kurupuṃgavaḥ
c atvarāvān asaṃrabdhaḥ saṃrabdhair vijigīṣubhiḥ
a tataḥ śatasahasrāṇi śarāṇāṃ nataparvaṇām
c mumucuḥ saindhavā rājaṃs tadā gāṇḍīvadhanvani
a sa tān āpatataḥ krūrān āśīviṣaviṣopamān
c ciccheda niśitair bāṇair antaraiva dhanaṃjayaḥ
a chittvā tu tān āśugamān kaṅkapatrāñ śilāśitān
c ekaikam eṣa daśabhir bibheda samare śaraiḥ
a tataḥ prāsāṃś ca śaktīś ca punar eva dhanaṃjaye
c jayadrathaṃ hataṃ smṛtvā cikṣipuḥ saindhavā nṛpāḥ
a teṣāṃ kirīṭī saṃkalpaṃ moghaṃ cakre mahāmanāḥ
c sarvāṃs tān antarā chittvā mudā cukrośa pāṇḍavaḥ
a tathaivāpatatāṃ teṣāṃ yodhānāṃ jayagṛddhinām
c śirāṃsi pātayām āsa bhallaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a teṣāṃ pradravatāṃ caiva punar eva ca dhāvatām
c nivartatāṃ ca śabdo 'bhūt pūrṇasyeva mahodadheḥ
a te vadhyamānās tu tadā pārthenāmitatejasā
c yathāprāṇaṃ yathotsāhaṃ yodhayām āsur arjunam
a tatas te phalgunenājau śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c kṛtā visaṃjñā bhūyiṣṭhāḥ klāntavāhanasainikāḥ
a tāṃs tu sarvān pariglānān viditvā dhṛtarāṣṭrajā
c duḥśalā bālam ādāya naptāraṃ prayayau tadā
e surathasya sutaṃ vīraṃ rathenānāgasaṃ tadā
a śāntyarthaṃ sarvayodhānām abhyagacchata pāṇḍavam
c sā dhanaṃjayam āsādya mumocārtasvaraṃ tadā
e dhanaṃjayo 'pi tāṃ dṛṣṭvā dhanur visasṛje prabhuḥ
a samutsṛṣṭadhanuḥ pārtho vidhivad bhaginīṃ tadā
c prāha kiṃ karavāṇīti sā ca taṃ vākyam abravīt
a eṣa te bharataśreṣṭha svasrīyasyātmajaḥ śiśuḥ
c abhivādayate vīra taṃ paśya puruṣarṣabha
a ity uktas tasya pitaraṃ sa papracchārjunas tadā
c kvāsāv iti tato rājan duḥśalā vākyam abravīt
a pitṛśokābhisaṃtapto viṣādārto 'sya vai pitā
c pañcatvam agamad vīra yathā tan me nibodha ha
a sa pūrvaṃ pitaraṃ śrutvā hataṃ yuddhe tvayānagha
c tvām āgataṃ ca saṃśrutya yuddhāya hayasāriṇam
e pituś ca mṛtyuduḥkhārto 'jahāt prāṇān dhanaṃjaya
a prāpto bībhatsur ity eva nāma śrutvaiva te 'nagha
c viṣādārtaḥ papātorvyāṃ mamāra ca mamātmajaḥ
a taṃ tu dṛṣṭvā nipatitaṃ tatas tasyātmajaṃ vibho
c gṛhītvā samanuprāptā tvām adya śaraṇaiṣiṇī
a ity uktvārtasvaraṃ sā tu mumoca dhṛtarāṣṭrajā
c dīnā dīnaṃ sthitaṃ pārtham abravīc cāpy adhomukham
a svasāraṃ mām avekṣasva svasrīyātmajam eva ca
c kartum arhasi dharmajña dayāṃ mayi kurūdvaha
e vismṛtya kururājānaṃ taṃ ca mandaṃ jayadratham
a abhimanyor yathā jātaḥ parikṣit paravīrahā
c tathāyaṃ surathāj jāto mama pautro mahābhuja
a tam ādāya naravyāghra saṃprāptāsmi tavāntikam
c śamārthaṃ sarvayodhānāṃ śṛṇu cedaṃ vaco mama
a āgato 'yaṃ mahābāho tasya mandasya pautrakaḥ
c prasādam asya bālasya tasmāt tvaṃ kartum arhasi
a eṣa prasādya śirasā mayā sārdham ariṃdama
c yācate tvāṃ mahābāho śamaṃ gaccha dhanaṃjaya
a bālasya hatabandhoś ca pārtha kiṃ cid ajānataḥ
c prasādaṃ kuru dharmajña mā manyuvaśam anvagāḥ
a tam anāryaṃ nṛśaṃsaṃ ca vismṛtyāsya pitāmaham
c āgaskāriṇam atyarthaṃ prasādaṃ kartum arhasi
a evaṃ bruvatyāṃ karuṇaṃ duḥśalāyāṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
c saṃsmṛtya devīṃ gāndhārīṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ ca pārthivam
e provāca duḥkhaśokārtaḥ kṣatradharmaṃ vigarhayan
a dhik taṃ duryodhanaṃ kṣudraṃ rājyalubdhaṃ ca māninam
c yatkṛte bāndhavāḥ sarve mayā nītā yamakṣayam
a ity uktvā bahu sāntvādi prasādam akaroj jayaḥ
c pariṣvajya ca tāṃ prīto visasarja gṛhān prati
a duḥśalā cāpi tān yodhān nivārya mahato raṇāt
c saṃpūjya pārthaṃ prayayau gṛhān prati śubhānanā
a tataḥ saindhavakān yodhān vinirjitya nararṣabhaḥ
b evaṃ nirjitya tān vīrān saindhavān sa dhanaṃjayaḥ
c punar evānvadhāvat sa taṃ hayaṃ kāmacāriṇam
a sasāra yajñiyaṃ vīro vidhivat sa viśāṃ pate
c tārāmṛgam ivākāśe devadevaḥ pinākadhṛk
a sa ca vājī yatheṣṭena tāṃs tān deśān yathāsukham
c vicacāra yathākāmaṃ karma pārthasya vardhayan
a krameṇa sa hayas tv evaṃ vicaran bharatarṣabha
c maṇipūrapater deśam upāyāt sahapāṇḍavaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a śrutvā tu nṛpatir vīraṃ pitaraṃ babhruvāhanaḥ
c niryayau vinayenāryo brāhmaṇārghyapuraḥsaraḥ
a maṇipūreśvaraṃ tv evam upayātaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
c nābhyanandata medhāvī kṣatradharmam anusmaran
a uvāca cainaṃ dharmātmā samanyuḥ phalgunas tadā
c prakriyeyaṃ na te yuktā bahis tvaṃ kṣatradharmataḥ
a saṃrakṣyamāṇaṃ turagaṃ yaudhiṣṭhiram upāgatam
c yajñiyaṃ viṣayānte māṃ nāyotsīḥ kiṃ nu putraka
a dhik tvām astu sudurbuddhiṃ kṣatradharmāviśāradam
c yo māṃ yuddhāya saṃprāptaṃ sāmnaivātho tvam agrahīḥ
a na tvayā puruṣārthaś ca kaś cid astīha jīvatā
c yas tvaṃ strīvad yudhā prāptaṃ sāmnā māṃ pratyagṛhṇathāḥ
a yady ahaṃ nyastaśastras tvām āgaccheyaṃ sudurmate
c prakriyeyaṃ tato yuktā bhavet tava narādhama
a tam evam uktaṃ bhartrā tu viditvā pannagātmajā
c amṛṣyamāṇā bhittvorvīm ulūpī tam upāgamat
a sā dadarśa tataḥ putraṃ vimṛśantam adhomukham
c saṃtarjyamānam asakṛd bhartrā yuddhārthinā vibho
a tataḥ sā cārusarvāṅgī tam upetyoragātmajā
c ulūpī prāha vacanaṃ kṣatradharmaviśāradā
a ulūpīṃ māṃ nibodha tvaṃ mātaraṃ pannagātmajām
c kuruṣva vacanaṃ putra dharmas te bhavitā paraḥ
a yudhyasvainaṃ kuruśreṣṭhaṃ dhanaṃjayam ariṃdama
c evam eṣa hi te prīto bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
a evam uddharṣito mātrā sa rājā babhruvāhanaḥ
c manaś cakre mahātejā yuddhāya bharatarṣabha
a saṃnahya kāñcanaṃ varma śirastrāṇaṃ ca bhānumat
c tūṇīraśatasaṃbādham āruroha mahāratham
a sarvopakaraṇair yuktaṃ yuktam aśvair manojavaiḥ
c sucakropaskaraṃ dhīmān hemabhāṇḍapariṣkṛtam
a paramārcitam ucchritya dhvajaṃ siṃhaṃ hiraṇmayam
c prayayau pārtham uddiśya sa rājā babhruvāhanaḥ
a tato 'bhyetya hayaṃ vīro yajñiyaṃ pārtharakṣitam
c grāhayām āsa puruṣair hayaśikṣāviśāradaiḥ
a gṛhītaṃ vājinaṃ dṛṣṭvā prītātmā sa dhanaṃjayaḥ
c putraṃ rathasthaṃ bhūmiṣṭhaḥ saṃnyavārayad āhave
a tataḥ sa rājā taṃ vīraṃ śaravrātaiḥ sahasraśaḥ
c ardayām āsa niśitair āśīviṣaviṣopamaiḥ
a tayoḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ pituḥ putrasya cātulam
c devāsuraraṇaprakhyam ubhayoḥ prīyamāṇayoḥ
a kirīṭinaṃ tu vivyādha śareṇa nataparvaṇā
c jatrudeśe naravyāghraḥ prahasan babhruvāhanaḥ
a so 'bhyagāt saha puṅkhena valmīkam iva pannagaḥ
c vinirbhidya ca kaunteyaṃ mahītalam athāviśat
a sa gāḍhavedano dhīmān ālambya dhanur uttamam
c divyaṃ tejaḥ samāviśya pramīta iva saṃbabhau
a sa saṃjñām upalabhyātha praśasya puruṣarṣabhaḥ
c putraṃ śakrātmajo vākyam idam āha mahīpate
a sādhu sādhu mahābāho vatsa citrāṅgadātmaja
c sadṛśaṃ karma te dṛṣṭvā prītimān asmi putraka
a vimuñcāmy eṣa bāṇāṃs te putra yuddhe sthiro bhava
c ity evam uktvā nārācair abhyavarṣad amitrahā
d sutīkṣṇair ātmajaṃ vīraṃ prahasan pāṇḍavarṣabha
a tān sa gāṇḍīvanirmuktān vajrāśanisamaprabhān
c nārācair acchinad rājā sarvān eva tridhā tridhā
a tasya pārthaḥ śarair divyair dhvajaṃ hemapariṣkṛtam
c suvarṇatālapratimaṃ kṣureṇāpāharad rathāt
a hayāṃś cāsya mahākāyān mahāvegaparākramān
c cakāra rājño nirjīvān prahasan pāṇḍavarṣabhaḥ
a sa rathād avatīryāśu rājā paramakopanaḥ
c padātiḥ pitaraṃ kopād yodhayām āsa pāṇḍavam
a saṃprīyamāṇaḥ pāṇḍūnām ṛṣabhaḥ putravikramāt
c nātyarthaṃ pīḍayām āsa putraṃ vajradharātmajaḥ
a sa hanyamāno vimukhaṃ pitaraṃ babhruvāhanaḥ
b hṛdi vivyādha bāṇena dṛḍhena jagatīpatiḥ
c śarair āśīviṣākāraiḥ punar evārdayad balī
a tataḥ sa bālyāt pitaraṃ vivyādha hṛdi patriṇā
c niśitena supuṅkhena balavad babhruvāhanaḥ
a sa bāṇas tejasā dīpto jvalann iva hutāśanaḥ
c viveśa pāṇḍavaṃ rājan marma bhittvātiduḥkhakṛt
a sa tenātibhṛśaṃ viddhaḥ putreṇa kurunandanaḥ
c mahīṃ jagāma mohārtas tato rājan dhanaṃjayaḥ
a tasmin nipatite vīre kauravāṇāṃ dhuraṃdhare
c so 'pi mohaṃ jagāmāśu tataś citrāṅgadāsutaḥ
a vyāyamya saṃyuge rājā dṛṣṭvā ca pitaraṃ hatam
c pūrvam eva ca bāṇaughair gāḍhaviddho 'rjunena saḥ
d papāta so 'pi dharaṇīm āliṅgya raṇamūrdhani
a bhartāraṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā putraṃ ca patitaṃ bhuvi
c citrāṅgadā paritrastā praviveśa raṇājiram
a śokasaṃtaptahṛdayā rudatī sā tataḥ śubhā
c maṇipūrapater mātā dadarśa nihataṃ patim
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tato bahuvidhaṃ bhīrur vilapya kamalekṣaṇā
c mumoha duḥkhād durdharṣā nipapāta ca bhūtale
a pratilabhya ca sā saṃjñāṃ devī divyavapurdharā
c ulūpīṃ pannagasutāṃ dṛṣṭvedaṃ vākyam abravīt
a ulūpi paśya bhartāraṃ śayānaṃ nihataṃ raṇe
c tvatkṛte mama putreṇa bālena samitiṃjayam
a nanu tvam ārye dharmajñā nanu cāsi pativratā
c yat tvatkṛte 'yaṃ patitaḥ patis te nihato raṇe
a kiṃ tu sarvāparādho 'yaṃ yadi te 'dya dhanaṃjayaḥ
c kṣamasva yācyamānā me saṃjīvaya dhanaṃjayam
a nanu tvam ārye dharmajñā trailokyaviditā śubhe
c yad ghātayitvā bhartāraṃ putreṇeha na śocasi
a nāhaṃ śocāmi tanayaṃ nihataṃ pannagātmaje
c patim eva tu śocāmi yasyātithyam idaṃ kṛtam
a ity uktvā sā tadā devīm ulūpīṃ pannagātmajām
c bhartāram abhigamyedam ity uvāca yaśasvinī
a uttiṣṭha kurumukhyasya priyakāma mama priya
c ayam aśvo mahābāho mayā te parimokṣitaḥ
a nanu nāma tvayā vīra dharmarājasya yajñiyaḥ
c ayam aśvo 'nusartavyaḥ sa śeṣe kiṃ mahītale
a tvayi prāṇāḥ samāyattāḥ kurūṇāṃ kurunandana
c sa kasmāt prāṇado 'nyeṣāṃ prāṇān saṃtyaktavān asi
a ulūpi sādhu saṃpaśya bhartāraṃ nihataṃ raṇe
c putraṃ cainaṃ samutsāhya ghātayitvā na śocasi
a kāmaṃ svapitu bālo 'yaṃ bhūmau pretagatiṃ gataḥ
c lohitākṣo guḍākeśo vijayaḥ sādhu jīvatu
a nāparādho 'sti subhage narāṇāṃ bahubhāryatā
c nārīṇāṃ tu bhavaty etan mā te bhūd buddhir īdṛśī
a sakhyaṃ hy etat kṛtaṃ dhātrā śāśvataṃ cāvyayaṃ ca ha
c sakhyaṃ samabhijānīhi satyaṃ saṃgatam astu te
a putreṇa ghātayitvemaṃ patiṃ yadi na me 'dya vai
c jīvantaṃ darśayasy adya parityakṣyāmi jīvitam
a sāhaṃ duḥkhānvitā bhīru patiputravinākṛtā
c ihaiva prāyam āśiṣye prekṣantyās te na saṃśayaḥ
a ity uktvā pannagasutāṃ sapatnīṃ caitravāhinī
c tataḥ prāyam upāsīnā tūṣṇīm āsīj janādhipa
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tathā vilapyoparatā bhartuḥ pādau pragṛhya sā
c upaviṣṭābhavad devī socchvāsaṃ putram īkṣatī
a tataḥ saṃjñāṃ punar labdhvā sa rājā babhruvāhanaḥ
c mātaraṃ tām athālokya raṇabhūmāv athābravīt
a ito duḥkhataraṃ kiṃ nu yan me mātā sukhaidhitā
c bhūmau nipatitaṃ vīram anuśete mṛtaṃ patim
a nihantāraṃ raṇe 'rīṇāṃ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varam
c mayā vinihataṃ saṃkhye prekṣate durmaraṃ bata
a aho 'syā hṛdayaṃ devyā dṛḍhaṃ yan na vidīryate
c vyūḍhoraskaṃ mahābāhuṃ prekṣantyā nihataṃ patim
a durmaraṃ puruṣeṇeha manye hy adhvany anāgate
c yatra nāhaṃ na me mātā viprayujyeta jīvitāt
a aho dhik kuruvīrasya hy uraḥsthaṃ kāñcanaṃ bhuvi
c vyapaviddhaṃ hatasyeha mayā putreṇa paśyata
a bho bho paśyata me vīraṃ pitaraṃ brāhmaṇā bhuvi
c śayānaṃ vīraśayane mayā putreṇa pātitam
a brāhmaṇāḥ kurumukhyasya prayuktā hayasāriṇaḥ
c kurvantu śāntikāṃ tv adya raṇe yo 'yaṃ mayā hataḥ
a vyādiśantu ca kiṃ viprāḥ prāyaścittam ihādya me
c sunṛśaṃsasya pāpasya pitṛhantū raṇājire
a duścarā dvādaśa samā hatvā pitaram adya vai
c mameha sunṛśaṃsasya saṃvītasyāsya carmaṇā
a śiraḥkapāle cāsyaiva bhuñjataḥ pitur adya me
c prāyaścittaṃ hi nāsty anyad dhatvādya pitaraṃ mama
a paśya nāgottamasute bhartāraṃ nihataṃ mayā
c kṛtaṃ priyaṃ mayā te 'dya nihatya samare 'rjunam
a so 'ham apy adya yāsyāmi gatiṃ pitṛniṣevitām
c na śaknomy ātmanātmānam ahaṃ dhārayituṃ śubhe
a sā tvaṃ mayi mṛte mātas tathā gāṇḍīvadhanvani
c bhava prītimatī devi satyenātmānam ālabhe
a ity uktvā sa tadā rājā duḥkhaśokasamāhataḥ
c upaspṛśya mahārāja duḥkhād vacanam abravīt
a śṛṇvantu sarvabhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca
c tvaṃ ca mātar yathā satyaṃ bravīmi bhujagottame
a yadi nottiṣṭhati jayaḥ pitā me bharatarṣabhaḥ
c asminn eva raṇoddeśe śoṣayiṣye kalevaram
a na hi me pitaraṃ hatvā niṣkṛtir vidyate kva cit
c narakaṃ pratipatsyāmi dhruvaṃ guruvadhārditaḥ
a vīraṃ hi kṣatriyaṃ hatvā gośatena pramucyate
c pitaraṃ tu nihatyaivaṃ dustarā niṣkṛtir mayā
a eṣa hy eko mahātejāḥ pāṇḍuputro dhanaṃjayaḥ
c pitā ca mama dharmātmā tasya me niṣkṛtiḥ kutaḥ
a ity evam uktvā nṛpate dhanaṃjayasuto nṛpaḥ
c upaspṛśyābhavat tūṣṇīṃ prāyopeto mahāmatiḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a prāyopaviṣṭe nṛpatau maṇipūreśvare tadā
c pitṛśokasamāviṣṭe saha mātrā paraṃtapa
a ulūpī cintayām āsa tadā saṃjīvanaṃ maṇim
c sa copātiṣṭhata tadā pannagānāṃ parāyaṇam
a taṃ gṛhītvā tu kauravya nāgarājapateḥ sutā
c manaḥprahlādanīṃ vācaṃ sainikānām athābravīt
a uttiṣṭha mā śucaḥ putra naiṣa jiṣṇus tvayā hataḥ
c ajeyaḥ puruṣair eṣa devair vāpi savāsavaiḥ
a mayā tu mohinī nāma māyaiṣā saṃprayojitā
c priyārthaṃ puruṣendrasya pitus te 'dya yaśasvinaḥ
a jijñāsur hy eṣa vai putra balasya tava kauravaḥ
c saṃgrāme yudhyato rājann āgataḥ paravīrahā
a tasmād asi mayā putra yuddhārthaṃ paricoditaḥ
c mā pāpam ātmanaḥ putra śaṅkethās tv aṇv api prabho
a ṛṣir eṣa mahātejāḥ puruṣaḥ śāśvato 'vyayaḥ
c nainaṃ śakto hi saṃgrāme jetuṃ śakro 'pi putraka
a ayaṃ tu me maṇir divyaḥ samānīto viśāṃ pate
c mṛtān mṛtān pannagendrān yo jīvayati nityadā
a etam asyorasi tvaṃ tu sthāpayasva pituḥ prabho
c saṃjīvitaṃ punaḥ putra tato draṣṭāsi pāṇḍavam
a ity uktaḥ sthāpayām āsa tasyorasi maṇiṃ tadā
c pārthasyāmitatejāḥ sa pituḥ snehād apāpakṛt
a tasmin nyaste maṇau vīra jiṣṇur ujjīvitaḥ prabhuḥ
c suptotthita ivottasthau mṛṣṭalohitalocanaḥ
a tam utthitaṃ mahātmānaṃ labdhasaṃjñaṃ manasvinam
c samīkṣya pitaraṃ svasthaṃ vavande babhruvāhanaḥ
a utthite puruṣavyāghre punar lakṣmīvati prabho
c divyāḥ sumanasaḥ puṇyā vavṛṣe pākaśāsanaḥ
a anāhatā dundubhayaḥ praṇedur meghanisvanāḥ
c sādhu sādhv iti cākāśe babhūva sumahān svanaḥ
a utthāya tu mahābāhuḥ paryāśvasto dhanaṃjayaḥ
c babhruvāhanam āliṅgya samājighrata mūrdhani
a dadarśa cāvidūre 'sya mātaraṃ śokakarśitām
c ulūpyā saha tiṣṭhantīṃ tato 'pṛcchad dhanaṃjayaḥ
a kim idaṃ lakṣyate sarvaṃ śokavismayaharṣavat
c raṇājiram amitraghna yadi jānāsi śaṃsa me
a jananī ca kimarthaṃ te raṇabhūmim upāgatā
c nāgendraduhitā ceyam ulūpī kim ihāgatā
a jānāmy aham idaṃ yuddhaṃ tvayā madvacanāt kṛtam
c strīṇām āgamane hetum aham icchāmi veditum
a tam uvāca tataḥ pṛṣṭo maṇipūrapatis tadā
c prasādya śirasā vidvān ulūpī pṛcchyatām iti
 arjuna uvāca
a kim āgamanakṛtyaṃ te kauravyakulanandini
c maṇipūrapater mātus tathaiva ca raṇājire
a kaccit kuśalakāmāsi rājño 'sya bhujagātmaje
c mama vā cañcalāpāṅge kaccit tvaṃ śubham icchasi
a kaccit te pṛthulaśroṇi nāpriyaṃ śubhadarśane
c akārṣam aham ajñānād ayaṃ vā babhruvāhanaḥ
a kaccic ca rājaputrī te sapatnī caitravāhinī
c citrāṅgadā varārohā nāparādhyati kiṃ cana
a tam uvācoragapater duhitā prahasanty atha
c na me tvam aparāddho 'si na nṛpo babhruvāhanaḥ
e na janitrī tathāsyeyaṃ mama yā preṣyavat sthitā
a śrūyatāṃ yad yathā cedaṃ mayā sarvaṃ viceṣṭitam
c na me kopas tvayā kāryaḥ śirasā tvāṃ prasādaye
a tvatprītyarthaṃ hi kauravya kṛtam etan mayānagha
c yat tac chṛṇu mahābāho nikhilena dhanaṃjaya
a mahābhāratayuddhe yat tvayā śāṃtanavo nṛpaḥ
