c adharmeṇa hataḥ pārtha tasyaiṣā niṣkṛtiḥ kṛtā
a na hi bhīṣmas tvayā vīra yudhyamāno nipātitaḥ
c śikhaṇḍinā tu saṃsaktas tam āśritya hatas tvayā
a tasya śāntim akṛtvā tu tyajes tvaṃ yadi jīvitam
c karmaṇā tena pāpena patethā niraye dhruvam
a eṣā tu vihitā śāntiḥ putrād yāṃ prāptavān asi
c vasubhir vasudhāpāla gaṅgayā ca mahāmate
a purā hi śrutam etad vai vasubhiḥ kathitaṃ mayā
c gaṅgāyās tīram āgamya hate śāṃtanave nṛpe
a āplutya devā vasavaḥ sametya ca mahānadīm
c idam ūcur vaco ghoraṃ bhāgīrathyā mate tadā
a eṣa śāṃtanavo bhīṣmo nihataḥ savyasācinā
c ayudhyamānaḥ saṃgrāme saṃsakto 'nyena bhāmini
a tad anenābhiṣaṅgeṇa vayam apy arjunaṃ śubhe
c śāpena yojayāmeti tathāstv iti ca sābravīt
a tad ahaṃ pitur āvedya bhṛśaṃ pravyathitendriyā
c abhavaṃ sa ca tac chrutvā viṣādam agamat param
a pitā tu me vasūn gatvā tvadarthaṃ samayācata
c punaḥ punaḥ prasādyaināṃs ta enam idam abruvan
a punas tasya mahābhāga maṇipūreśvaro yuvā
c sa enaṃ raṇamadhyasthaṃ śaraiḥ pātayitā bhuvi
a evaṃ kṛte sa nāgendra muktaśāpo bhaviṣyati
c gaccheti vasubhiś cokto mama cedaṃ śaśaṃsa saḥ
a tac chrutvā tvaṃ mayā tasmāc chāpād asi vimokṣitaḥ
c na hi tvāṃ devarājo 'pi samareṣu parājayet
a ātmā putraḥ smṛtas tasmāt tenehāsi parājitaḥ
c nātra doṣo mama mataḥ kathaṃ vā manyase vibho
a ity evam ukto vijayaḥ prasannātmābravīd idam
c sarvaṃ me supriyaṃ devi yad etat kṛtavaty asi
a ity uktvāthābravīt putraṃ maṇipūreśvaraṃ jayaḥ
c citrāṅgadāyāḥ śṛṇvantyāḥ kauravyaduhitus tathā
a yudhiṣṭhirasyāśvamedhaḥ parāṃ caitrīṃ bhaviṣyati
c tatrāgaccheḥ sahāmātyo mātṛbhyāṃ sahito nṛpa
a ity evam uktaḥ pārthena sa rājā babhruvāhanaḥ
c uvāca pitaraṃ dhīmān idam asrāvilekṣaṇaḥ
a upayāsyāmi dharmajña bhavataḥ śāsanād aham
c aśvamedhe mahāyajñe dvijātipariveṣakaḥ
a mama tv anugrahārthāya praviśasva puraṃ svakam
c bhāryābhyāṃ saha śatrughna mā bhūt te 'tra vicāraṇā
a uṣitveha viśalyas tvaṃ sukhaṃ sve veśmani prabho
c punar aśvānugamanaṃ kartāsi jayatāṃ vara
a ity uktaḥ sa tu putreṇa tadā vānaraketanaḥ
c smayan provāca kaunteyas tadā citrāṅgadāsutam
a viditaṃ te mahābāho yathā dīkṣāṃ carāmy aham
c na sa tāvat pravekṣyāmi puraṃ te pṛthulocana
a yathākāmaṃ prayāty eṣa yajñiyaś ca turaṃgamaḥ
c svasti te 'stu gamiṣyāmi na sthānaṃ vidyate mama
a sa tatra vidhivat tena pūjitaḥ pākaśāsaniḥ
c bhāryābhyām abhyanujñātaḥ prāyād bharatasattamaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a sa tu vājī samudrāntāṃ paryetya pṛthivīm imām
c nivṛtto 'bhimukho rājan yena nāgāhvayaṃ puram
a anugacchaṃś ca tejasvī nivṛtto 'tha kirīṭabhṛt
c yadṛcchayā samāpede puraṃ rājagṛhaṃ tadā
a tam abhyāśagataṃ rājā jarāsaṃdhātmajātmajaḥ
c kṣatradharme sthito vīraḥ samarāyājuhāva ha
a tataḥ purāt sa niṣkramya rathī dhanvī śarī talī
c meghasaṃdhiḥ padātiṃ taṃ dhanaṃjayam upādravat
a āsādya ca mahātejā meghasaṃdhir dhanaṃjayam
c bālabhāvān mahārāja provācedaṃ na kauśalāt
a kim ayaṃ cāryate vājī strīmadhya iva bhārata
c hayam enaṃ hariṣyāmi prayatasva vimokṣaṇe
a adattānunayo yuddhe yadi tvaṃ pitṛbhir mama
b ārto nanu purā yuddhe
b   śilpa ity api pāragaḥ
c kariṣyāmi tavātithyaṃ prahara praharāmi vā
a ity uktaḥ pratyuvācainaṃ pāṇḍavaḥ prahasann iva
c vighnakartā mayā vārya iti me vratam āhitam
a bhrātrā jyeṣṭhena nṛpate tavāpi viditaṃ dhruvam
c praharasva yathāśakti na manyur vidyate mama
a ity uktaḥ prāharat pūrvaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ magadheśvaraḥ
c kirañ śarasahasrāṇi varṣāṇīva sahasradṛk
a tato gāṇḍīvabhṛc chūro gāṇḍīvapreṣitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c cakāra moghāṃs tān bāṇān ayatnād bharatarṣabha
a sa moghaṃ tasya bāṇaughaṃ kṛtvā vānaraketanaḥ
c śarān mumoca jvalitān dīptāsyān iva pannagān
a dhvaje patākādaṇḍeṣu rathayantre hayeṣu ca
c anyeṣu ca rathāṅgeṣu na śarīre na sārathau
a saṃrakṣyamāṇaḥ pārthena śarīre phalgunasya ha
c manyamānaḥ svavīryaṃ tan māgadhaḥ prāhiṇoc charān
a tato gāṇḍīvabhṛc chūro māgadhena samāhataḥ
c babhau vāsantika iva palāśaḥ puṣpito mahān
a avadhyamānaḥ so 'bhyaghnan māgadhaḥ pāṇḍavarṣabham
c tena tasthau sa kauravya lokavīrasya darśane
a savyasācī tu saṃkruddho vikṛṣya balavad dhanuḥ
c hayāṃś cakāra nirdehān sāratheś ca śiro 'harat
a dhanuś cāsya mahac citraṃ kṣureṇa pracakarta ha
c hastāvāpaṃ patākāṃ ca dhvajaṃ cāsya nyapātayat
a sa rājā vyathito vyaśvo vidhanur hatasārathiḥ
c gadām ādāya kaunteyam abhidudrāva vegavān
a tasyāpatata evāśu gadāṃ hemapariṣkṛtām
c śaraiś cakarta bahudhā bahubhir gṛdhravājitaiḥ
a sā gadā śakalībhūtā viśīrṇamaṇibandhanā
c vyālī nirmucyamāneva papātāsya sahasradhā
a virathaṃ taṃ vidhanvānaṃ gadayā parivarjitam
c naicchat tāḍayituṃ dhīmān arjunaḥ samarāgraṇīḥ
a tata enaṃ vimanasaṃ kṣatradharme samāsthitam
c sāntvapūrvam idaṃ vākyam abravīt kapiketanaḥ
a paryāptaḥ kṣatradharmo 'yaṃ darśitaḥ putra gamyatām
c bahv etat samare karma tava bālasya pārthiva
a yudhiṣṭhirasya saṃdeśo na hantavyā nṛpā iti
c tena jīvasi rājaṃs tvam aparāddho 'pi me raṇe
a iti matvā sa cātmānaṃ pratyādiṣṭaṃ sma māgadhaḥ
c tathyam ity avagamyainaṃ prāñjaliḥ pratyapūjayat
d parājito 'smi bhadraṃ te nāhaṃ yoddhum ihotsahe
d yac ca kṛtyaṃ mayā te 'dya tad brūhi kṛtam eva tu
a tam arjunaḥ samāśvāsya punar evedam abravīt
c āgantavyaṃ parāṃ caitrīm aśvamedhe nṛpasya naḥ
a ity uktaḥ sa tathety uktvā pūjayām āsa taṃ hayam
c phalgunaṃ ca yudhāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ vidhivat sahadevajaḥ
a tato yatheṣṭam agamat punar eva sa kesarī
c tataḥ samudratīreṇa vaṅgān puṇḍrān sakeralān
a tatra tatra ca bhūrīṇi mlecchasainyāny anekaśaḥ
c vijigye dhanuṣā rājan gāṇḍīvena dhanaṃjayaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a māgadhenārcito rājan pāṇḍavaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ
c dakṣiṇāṃ diśam āsthāya cārayām āsa taṃ hayam
a tataḥ sa punar āvṛtya hayaḥ kāmacaro balī
c āsasāda purīṃ ramyāṃ cedīnāṃ śuktisāhvayām
a śarabheṇārcitas tatra śiśupālātmajena saḥ
c yuddhapūrveṇa mānena pūjayā ca mahābalaḥ
a tatrārcito yayau rājaṃs tadā sa turagottamaḥ
c kāśīn andhrān kosalāṃś ca kirātān atha taṅgaṇān
a tatra pūjāṃ yathānyāyaṃ pratigṛhya sa pāṇḍavaḥ
c punar āvṛtya kaunteyo daśārṇān agamat tadā
a tatra citrāṅgado nāma balavān vasudhādhipaḥ
c tena yuddham abhūt tasya vijayasyātibhairavam
a taṃ cāpi vaśam ānīya kirīṭī puruṣarṣabhaḥ
c niṣādarājño viṣayam ekalavyasya jagmivān
a ekalavyasutaś cainaṃ yuddhena jagṛhe tadā
c tataś cakre niṣādaiḥ sa saṃgrāmaṃ romaharṣaṇam
a tatas tam api kaunteyaḥ samareṣv aparājitaḥ
c jigāya samare vīro yajñavighnārtham udyatam
a sa taṃ jitvā mahārāja naiṣādiṃ pākaśāsaniḥ
c arcitaḥ prayayau bhūyo dakṣiṇaṃ salilārṇavam
a tatrāpi draviḍair andhrai raudrair māhiṣakair api
c tathā kollagireyaiś ca yuddham āsīt kirīṭinaḥ
d tāṃś cāpi vijayo jitvā nātitīvreṇa karmaṇā
a turagasya vaśenātha surāṣṭrān abhito yayau
c gokarṇam api cāsādya prabhāsam api jagmivān
a tato dvāravatīṃ ramyāṃ vṛṣṇivīrābhirakṣitām
c āsasāda hayaḥ śrīmān kururājasya yajñiyaḥ
a tam unmathya hayaśreṣṭhaṃ yādavānāṃ kumārakāḥ
c prayayus tāṃs tadā rājann ugraseno nyavārayat
a tataḥ puryā viniṣkramya vṛṣṇyandhakapatis tadā
c sahito vasudevena mātulena kirīṭinaḥ
a tau sametya kuruśreṣṭhaṃ vidhivat prītipūrvakam
c parayā bharataśreṣṭhaṃ pūjayā samavasthitau
e tatas tābhyām anujñāto yayau yena hayo gataḥ
a tataḥ sa paścimaṃ deśaṃ samudrasya tadā hayaḥ
c krameṇa vyacarat sphītaṃ tataḥ pañcanadaṃ yayau
a tasmād api sa kauravya gāndhāraviṣayaṃ hayaḥ
c vicacāra yathākāmaṃ kaunteyānugatas tadā
a tatra gāndhārarājena yuddham āsīn mahātmanaḥ
c ghoraṃ śakuniputreṇa pūrvavairānusāriṇā
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a śakunes tu suto vīro gāndhārāṇāṃ mahārathaḥ
c pratyudyayau guḍākeśaṃ sainyena mahatā vṛtaḥ
e hastyaśvarathapūrṇena patākādhvajamālinā
a amṛṣyamāṇās te yodhā nṛpateḥ śakuner vadham
c abhyayuḥ sahitāḥ pārthaṃ pragṛhītaśarāsanāḥ
a tān uvāca sa dharmātmā bībhatsur aparājitaḥ
c yudhiṣṭhirasya vacanaṃ na ca te jagṛhur hitam
a vāryamāṇās tu pārthena sāntvapūrvam amarṣitāḥ
c parivārya hayaṃ jagmus tataś cukrodha pāṇḍavaḥ
a tataḥ śirāṃsi dīptāgrais teṣāṃ ciccheda pāṇḍavaḥ
c kṣurair gāṇḍīvanirmuktair nātiyatnād ivārjunaḥ
a te vadhyamānāḥ pārthena hayam utsṛjya saṃbhramāt
c nyavartanta mahārāja śaravarṣārditā bhṛśam
a vitudyamānas taiś cāpi gāndhāraiḥ pāṇḍavarṣabhaḥ
c ādiśyādiśya tejasvī śirāṃsy eṣāṃ nyapātayat
a vadhyamāneṣu teṣv ājau gāndhāreṣu samantataḥ
c sa rājā śakuneḥ putraḥ pāṇḍavaṃ pratyavārayat
a taṃ yudhyamānaṃ rājānaṃ kṣatradharme vyavasthitam
c pārtho 'bravīn na me vadhyā rājāno rājaśāsanāt
e alaṃ yuddhena te vīra na te 'sty adya parājayaḥ
a ity uktas tad anādṛtya vākyam ajñānamohitaḥ
c sa śakrasamakarmāṇam avākirata sāyakaiḥ
a tasya pārthaḥ śirastrāṇam ardhacandreṇa patriṇā
c apāharad asaṃbhrānto jayadrathaśiro yathā
a tad dṛṣṭvā vismayaṃ jagmur gāndhārāḥ sarva eva te
c icchatā tena na hato rājety api ca te viduḥ
a gāndhārarājaputras tu palāyanakṛtakṣaṇaḥ
c babhau tair eva sahitas trastaiḥ kṣudramṛgair iva
a teṣāṃ tu tarasā pārthas tatraiva paridhāvatām
c vijahārottamāṅgāni bhallaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
a ucchritāṃs tu bhujān ke cin nābudhyanta śarair hṛtān
c śarair gāṇḍīvanirmuktaiḥ pṛthubhiḥ pārthacoditaiḥ
a saṃbhrāntanaranāgāśvam atha tad vidrutaṃ balam
c hatavidhvastabhūyiṣṭham āvartata muhur muhuḥ
a na hy adṛśyanta vīrasya ke cid agre 'gryakarmaṇaḥ
c ripavaḥ pātyamānā vai ye saheyur mahāśarān
a tato gāndhārarājasya mantrivṛddhapuraḥsarā
c jananī niryayau bhītā puraskṛtyārghyam uttamam
a sā nyavārayad avyagrā taṃ putraṃ yuddhadurmadam
c prasādayām āsa ca taṃ jiṣṇum akliṣṭakāriṇam
a tāṃ pūjayitvā kaunteyaḥ prasādam akarot tadā
c śakuneś cāpi tanayaṃ sāntvayann idam abravīt
a na me priyaṃ mahābāho yat te buddhir iyaṃ kṛtā
c pratiyoddhum amitraghna bhrātaiva tvaṃ mamānagha
a gāndhārīṃ mātaraṃ smṛtvā dhṛtarāṣṭrakṛtena ca
c tena jīvasi rājaṃs tvaṃ nihatās tv anugās tava
a maivaṃ bhūḥ śāmyatāṃ vairaṃ mā te bhūd buddhir īdṛśī
c āgantavyaṃ parāṃ caitrīm aśvamedhe nṛpasya naḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a ity uktvānuyayau pārtho hayaṃ taṃ kāmacāriṇam
b te nyavartanta gāndhārā hataśiṣṭāḥ svakaṃ puram
c nyavartata tato vājī yena nāgāhvayaṃ puram
a taṃ nivṛttaṃ tu śuśrāva cāreṇaiva yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c śrutvārjunaṃ kuśalinaṃ sa ca hṛṣṭamanābhavat
a vijayasya ca tat karma gāndhāraviṣaye tadā
c śrutvānyeṣu ca deśeṣu sa suprīto 'bhavan nṛpaḥ
a etasminn eva kāle tu dvādaśīṃ māghapākṣikīm
c iṣṭaṃ gṛhītvā nakṣatraṃ dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a samānāyya mahātejāḥ sarvān bhrātṝn mahāmanāḥ
c bhīmaṃ ca nakulaṃ caiva sahadevaṃ ca kauravaḥ
a provācedaṃ vacaḥ kāle tadā dharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
c āmantrya vadatāṃ śreṣṭho bhīmaṃ bhīmaparākramam
a āyāti bhīmasenāsau sahāśvena tavānujaḥ
c yathā me puruṣāḥ prāhur ye dhanaṃjayasāriṇaḥ
a upasthitaś ca kālo 'yam abhito vartate hayaḥ
c māghī ca paurṇamāsīyaṃ māsaḥ śeṣo vṛkodara
a tat prasthāpyantu vidvāṃso brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ
c vājimedhārthasiddhyarthaṃ deśaṃ paśyantu yajñiyam
a ity uktaḥ sa tu tac cakre bhīmo nṛpatiśāsanam
c hṛṣṭaḥ śrutvā narapater āyāntaṃ savyasācinam
a tato yayau bhīmasenaḥ prājñaiḥ sthapatibhiḥ saha
c brāhmaṇān agrataḥ kṛtvā kuśalān yajñakarmasu
d yajñaślāghyaṃ tadā sthānaṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam
a taṃ saśālacayagrāmaṃ saṃpratolīviṭaṅkinam
c māpayām āsa kauravyo yajñavāṭaṃ yathāvidhi
d prāsādaśatasaṃbādhaṃ maṇipravarakuṭṭikam
a sadaḥ sapatnīsadanaṃ sāgnīdhram api cottaram
c kārayām āsa vidhivan maṇihemavibhūṣitam
a stambhān kanakacitrāṃś ca toraṇāni bṛhanti ca
c yajñāyatanadeśeṣu dattvā śuddhaṃ ca kāñcanam
a antaḥpurāṇi rājñāṃ ca nānādeśanivāsinām
c kārayām āsa dharmātmā tatra tatra yathāvidhi
a brāhmaṇānāṃ ca veśmāni nānādeśasameyuṣām
c kārayām āsa bhīmaḥ sa vividhāni hy anekaśaḥ
a tathā saṃpreṣayām āsa dūtān nṛpatiśāsanāt
c bhīmaseno mahārāja rājñām akliṣṭakarmaṇām
a te priyārthaṃ kurupater āyayur nṛpasattamāḥ
c ratnāny anekāny ādāya striyo 'śvān āyudhāni ca
a teṣāṃ niviśatāṃ teṣu śibireṣu sahasraśaḥ
c nardataḥ sāgarasyeva śabdo divam ivāspṛśat
d pratyudgamya namaskṛtya brāhmaṇāṃś ca nyavedayat
a teṣām abhyāgatānāṃ sa rājā rājīvalocanaḥ
c vyādideśānnapānāni śayyāś cāpy atimānuṣāḥ
a vāhanānāṃ ca vividhāḥ śālāḥ śālīkṣugorasaiḥ
c upetāḥ puruṣavyāghra vyādideśa sa dharmarāṭ
d varṇāḥ pṛthak saṃniviṣṭā hy uttarottarapūjitāḥ
a tathā tasmin mahāyajñe dharmarājasya dhīmataḥ
c samājagmur munigaṇā bahavo brahmavādinaḥ
a ye ca dvijātipravarās tatrāsan pṛthivīpate
c samājagmuḥ saśiṣyāṃs tān pratijagrāha kauravaḥ
a sarvāṃś ca tān anuyayau yāvad āvasathād iti
c svayam eva mahātejā dambhaṃ tyaktvā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a tataḥ kṛtvā sthapatayaḥ śilpino 'nye ca ye tadā
c kṛtsnaṃ yajñavidhiṃ rājan dharmarājñe nyavedayan
a tac chrutvā dharmarājaḥ sa kṛtaṃ sarvam aninditam
c hṛṣṭarūpo 'bhavad rājā saha bhrātṛbhir acyutaḥ
c śrīmannāmā ca bhavatu janānāṃ puṇyadaḥ prabhuḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tasmin yajñe pravṛtte tu vāgmino hetuvādinaḥ
c hetuvādān bahūn prāhuḥ parasparajigīṣavaḥ
a dadṛśus taṃ nṛpatayo yajñasya vidhim uttamam
c devendrasyeva vihitaṃ bhīmena kurunandana
a dadṛśus toraṇāny atra śātakumbhamayāni te
c śayyāsanavihārāṃś ca subahūn ratnabhūṣitān
a ghaṭān pātrīḥ kaṭāhāni kalaśān vardhamānakān
c na hi kiṃ cid asauvarṇam apaśyaṃs tatra pārthivāḥ
a yūpāṃś ca śāstrapaṭhitān dāravān hemabhūṣitān
c upakḷptān yathākālaṃ vidhivad bhūrivarcasaḥ
a sthalajā jalajā ye ca paśavaḥ ke cana prabho
c sarvān eva samānītāṃs tān apaśyanta te nṛpāḥ
a gāś caiva mahiṣīś caiva tathā vṛddhāḥ striyo 'pi ca
c audakāni ca sattvāni śvāpadāni vayāṃsi ca
a jarāyujāny aṇḍajāni svedajāny udbhidāni ca
c parvatānūpavanyāni bhūtāni dadṛśuś ca te
d sarve rājan yathānyāyam ānītā nṛpaśāsanāt
a evaṃ pramuditaṃ sarvaṃ paśugodhanadhānyataḥ
c yajñavāṭaṃ nṛpā dṛṣṭvā paraṃ vismayam āgaman
d aniśaṃ dīyate ca sma tatra bhojyaṃ pṛthagvidham
e brāhmaṇānāṃ viśāṃ caiva bahumṛṣṭānnam ṛddhimat
a pūrṇe śatasahasre tu viprāṇāṃ tatra bhuñjatām
c dundubhir meghanirghoṣo muhur muhur atāḍyata
a vinanādāsakṛt so 'tha divase divase tadā
c evaṃ sa vavṛte yajño dharmarājasya dhīmataḥ
a annasya bahavo rājann utsargāḥ parvatopamāḥ
c dadhikulyāś ca dadṛśuḥ sarpiṣaś ca hradāñjanāḥ
a jambūdvīpo hi sakalo nānājanapadāyutaḥ
c rājann adṛśyataikastho rājñas tasmin mahākratau
a tatra jātisahasrāṇi puruṣāṇāṃ tatas tataḥ
c gṛhītvā dhanam ājagmur bahūni bharatarṣabha
a rājānaḥ sragviṇaś cāpi sumṛṣṭamaṇikuṇḍalāḥ
c paryaveṣan dvijāgryāṃs tāñ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a vividhāny annapānāni puruṣā ye 'nuyāyinaḥ
c teṣāṃ nṛpopabhojyāni brāhmaṇebhyo daduḥ sma te
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a samāgatān vedavido rājñaś ca pṛthivīśvarān
c dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiro rājā bhīmasenam athābravīt
a upayātā naravyāghrā ya ime jagadīśvarāḥ
c eteṣāṃ kriyatāṃ pūjā pūjārhā hi nareśvarāḥ
a ity uktaḥ sa tathā cakre narendreṇa yaśasvinā
c bhīmaseno mahātejā yamābhyāṃ saha bhārata
a athābhyagacchad govindo vṛṣṇibhiḥ saha dharmajam
b yajñeśo yajñapuruṣaḥ sarvavedāntaveditaḥ
b devāś ca munayo viprā manasā vandya keśavam
b pratyutthitās tatas tatra praviveśa sa mādhavaḥ
c baladevaṃ puraskṛtya sarvaprāṇabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
a yuyudhānena sahitaḥ pradyumnena gadena ca
c niśaṭhenātha sāmbena tathaiva kṛtavarmaṇā
a teṣām api parāṃ pūjāṃ cakre bhīmo mahābhujaḥ
c viviśus te ca veśmāni ratnavanti nararṣabhāḥ
a yudhiṣṭhirasamīpe tu kathānte madhusūdanaḥ
c arjunaṃ kathayām āsa bahusaṃgrāmakarśitam
a sa taṃ papraccha kaunteyaḥ punaḥ punar ariṃdamam
c dharmarāḍ bhrātaraṃ jiṣṇuṃ samācaṣṭa jagatpatiḥ
a āgamad dvārakāvāsī mamāptaḥ puruṣo nṛpa
c yo 'drākṣīt pāṇḍavaśreṣṭhaṃ bahusaṃgrāmakarśitam
a samīpe ca mahābāhum ācaṣṭa ca mama prabho
c kuru kāryāṇi kaunteya hayamedhārthasiddhaye
a ity uktaḥ pratyuvācainaṃ dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c diṣṭyā sa kuśalī jiṣṇur upayāti ca mādhava
a tava yat saṃdideśāsau pāṇḍavānāṃ balāgraṇīḥ
c tad ākhyātum ihecchāmi bhavatā yadunandana
a ity ukte rājaśārdūla vṛṣṇyandhakapatis tadā
c provācedaṃ vaco vāgmī dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
a idam āha mahārāja pārthavākyaṃ naraḥ sa mām
c vācyo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kṛṣṇa kāle vākyam idaṃ mama
a āgamiṣyanti rājānaḥ sarvataḥ kauravān prati
c teṣām ekaikaśaḥ pūjā kāryety etat kṣamaṃ hi naḥ
a ity etad vacanād rājā vijñāpyo mama mānada
c na tad ātyayikaṃ hi syād yad arghyānayane bhavet
a kartum arhati tad rājā bhavāṃś cāpy anumanyatām
c rājadveṣād vinaśyeyur nemā rājan prajāḥ punaḥ
a idam anyac ca kaunteya vacaḥ sa puruṣo 'bravīt
c dhanaṃjayasya nṛpate tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu
a upayāsyati yajñaṃ no maṇipūrapatir nṛpaḥ
c putro mama mahātejā dayito babhruvāhanaḥ
a taṃ bhavān madapekṣārthaṃ vidhivat pratipūjayet
c sa hi bhakto 'nuraktaś ca mama nityam iti prabho
a ity etad vacanaṃ śrutvā dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c abhinandyāsya tad vākyam idaṃ vacanam abravīt
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a śrutaṃ priyam idaṃ kṛṣṇa yat tvam arhasi bhāṣitum
c tan me 'mṛtarasaprakhyaṃ mano hlādayate vibho
a bahūni kila yuddhāni vijayasya narādhipaiḥ
c punar āsan hṛṣīkeśa tatra tatreti me śrutam
a mannimittaṃ hi sa sadā pārthaḥ sukhavivarjitaḥ
c atīva vijayo dhīmān iti me dūyate manaḥ
a saṃcintayāmi vārṣṇeya sadā kuntīsutaṃ rahaḥ
b atīva duḥkhabhāgī sa satataṃ pāṇḍunandanaḥ
c kiṃ nu tasya śarīre 'sti sarvalakṣaṇapūjite
e aniṣṭaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ kṛṣṇa yena duḥkhāny upāśnute
a atīva duḥkhabhāgī sa satataṃ kuntinandanaḥ
c na ca paśyāmi bībhatsor nindyaṃ gātreṣu kiṃ cana
e śrotavyaṃ cen mayaitad vai tan me vyākhyātum arhasi
a ity uktaḥ sa hṛṣīkeśo dhyātvā sumahad antaram
c rājānaṃ bhojarājanyavardhano viṣṇur abravīt
a na hy asya nṛpate kiṃ cid aniṣṭam upalakṣaye
c ṛte puruṣasiṃhasya piṇḍike 'syātikāyataḥ
a tābhyāṃ sa puruṣavyāghro nityam adhvasu yujyate
c na hy anyad anupaśyāmi yenāsau duḥkhabhāg jayaḥ
a ity uktaḥ sa kuruśreṣṭhas tathyaṃ kṛṣṇena dhīmatā
c provāca vṛṣṇiśārdūlam evam etad iti prabho
a kṛṣṇā tu draupadī kṛṣṇaṃ tiryak sāsūyam aikṣata
c pratijagrāha tasyās taṃ praṇayaṃ cāpi keśihā
e sakhyuḥ sakhā hṛṣīkeśaḥ sākṣād iva dhanaṃjayaḥ
a tatra bhīmādayas te tu kuravo yādavās tathā
c remuḥ śrutvā vicitrārthā dhanaṃjayakathā vibho
a tathā kathayatām eva teṣām arjunasaṃkathāḥ
c upāyād vacanān martyo vijayasya mahātmanaḥ
a so 'bhigamya kuruśreṣṭhaṃ namaskṛtya ca buddhimān
c upāyātaṃ naravyāghram arjunaṃ pratyavedayat
a tac chrutvā nṛpatis tasya harṣabāṣpākulekṣaṇaḥ
c priyākhyānanimittaṃ vai dadau bahu dhanaṃ tadā
a tato dvitīye divase mahāñ śabdo vyavardhata
c āyāti puruṣavyāghre pāṇḍavānāṃ dhuraṃdhare
a tato reṇuḥ samudbhūto vibabhau tasya vājinaḥ
c abhito vartamānasya yathoccaiḥśravasas tathā
a tatra harṣakalā vāco narāṇāṃ śuśruve 'rjunaḥ
c diṣṭyāsi pārtha kuśalī dhanyo rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a ko 'nyo hi pṛthivīṃ kṛtsnām avajitya sapārthivām
c cārayitvā hayaśreṣṭham upāyāyād ṛte 'rjunam
a ye vyatītā mahātmāno rājānaḥ sagarādayaḥ
c teṣām apīdṛśaṃ karma na kiṃ cid anuśuśruma
a naitad anye kariṣyanti bhaviṣyāḥ pṛthivīkṣitaḥ
c yat tvaṃ kurukulaśreṣṭha duṣkaraṃ kṛtavān iha
a ity evaṃ vadatāṃ teṣāṃ nṝṇāṃ śrutisukhā giraḥ
c śṛṇvan viveśa dharmātmā phalguno yajñasaṃstaram
a tato rājā sahāmātyaḥ kṛṣṇaś ca yadunandanaḥ
c dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ puraskṛtya te taṃ pratyudyayus tadā
a so 'bhivādya pituḥ pādau dharmarājasya dhīmataḥ
c bhīmādīṃś cāpi saṃpūjya paryaṣvajata keśavam
d saumyātmany amṛtādhāre pariṣvakte sukhaṃ yayau
a taiḥ sametyārcitas tān sa pratyarcya ca yathāvidhi
c viśaśrāmātha dharmātmā tīraṃ labdhveva pāragaḥ
a etasminn eva kāle tu sa rājā babhruvāhanaḥ
c mātṛbhyāṃ sahito dhīmān kurūn abhyājagāma ha
d tatra vṛddhān yathā vatsa kurūn anyāṃś ca pārthivān
a sa sametya kurūn sarvān sarvais tair abhinanditaḥ
b abhivādya mahābāhus taiś cāpi pratinanditaḥ
c praviveśa pitāmahyāḥ kuntyā bhavanam uttamam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a sa praviśya yathānyāyaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ niveśanam
a   mātṛbhyāṃ sahito vaśī
a praśrayāvanataḥ kuntyā gāndhāryāś ca yathāvidhi
a vavande caraṇau tatra
c pitāmahīm abhyavadat sāmnā paramavalgunā
a tathā citrāṅgadā devī kauravyasyātmajāpi ca
c pṛthāṃ kṛṣṇāṃ ca sahite vinayenābhijagmatuḥ
e subhadrāṃ ca yathānyāyaṃ yāś cānyāḥ kuruyoṣitaḥ
a dadau kuntī tatas tābhyāṃ ratnāni vividhāni ca
c draupadī ca subhadrā ca yāś cāpy anyā daduḥ striyaḥ
a ūṣatus tatra te devyau mahārhaśayanāsane
c supūjite svayaṃ kuntyā pārthasya priyakāmyayā
a sa ca rājā mahāvīryaḥ pūjito babhruvāhanaḥ
c dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ mahīpālam upatasthe yathāvidhi
a yudhiṣṭhiraṃ ca rājānaṃ bhīmādīṃś cāpi pāṇḍavān
c upagamya mahātejā vinayenābhyavādayat
a sa taiḥ premṇā pariṣvaktaḥ pūjitaś ca yathāvidhi
c dhanaṃ cāsmai dadur bhūri prīyamāṇā mahārathāḥ
a tathaiva sa mahīpālaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ cakragadādharam
c pradyumna iva govindaṃ vinayenopatasthivān
a tasmai kṛṣṇo dadau rājñe mahārham abhipūjitam
c rathaṃ hemapariṣkāraṃ divyāśvayujam uttamam
a dharmarājaś ca bhīmaś ca yamajau phalgunas tathā
c pṛthak pṛthag atīvainaṃ mānārhaṃ samapūjayan
a tatas tṛtīye divase satyavatyāḥ suto muniḥ
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ samabhyetya vāgmī vacanam abravīt
a adya prabhṛti kaunteya yajasva samayo hi te
c muhūrto yajñiyaḥ prāptaś codayanti ca yājakāḥ
a ahīno nāma rājendra kratus te 'yaṃ vikalpavān
c bahutvāt kāñcanasyāsya khyāto bahusuvarṇakaḥ
a evam eva mahārāja dakṣiṇāṃ triguṇāṃ kuru
c tritvaṃ vrajatu te rājan brāhmaṇā hy atra kāraṇam
a trīn aśvamedhān atra tvaṃ saṃprāpya bahudakṣiṇān
c jñātivadhyākṛtaṃ pāpaṃ prahāsyasi narādhipa
a pavitraṃ paramaṃ hy etat pāvanānāṃ ca pāvanam
c yad aśvamedhāvabhṛthaṃ prāpsyase kurunandana
a ity uktaḥ sa tu tejasvī vyāsenāmitatejasā
c dīkṣāṃ viveśa dharmātmā vājimedhāptaye tadā
e narādhipaḥ prāyajata vājimedhaṃ mahākratum
f bahvannadakṣiṇaṃ rājā sarvakāmaguṇānvitam
a tatra vedavido rājaṃś cakruḥ karmāṇi yājakāḥ
c parikramantaḥ śāstrajñā vidhivat sādhuśikṣitāḥ
a na teṣāṃ skhalitaṃ tatra nāsīd apahutaṃ tathā
c kramayuktaṃ ca yuktaṃ ca cakrus tatra dvijarṣabhāḥ
a kṛtvā pravargyaṃ dharmajñā yathāvad dvijasattamāḥ
c cakrus te vidhivad rājaṃs tathaivābhiṣavaṃ dvijāḥ
a abhiṣūya tato rājan somaṃ somapasattamāḥ
c savanāny ānupūrvyeṇa cakruḥ śāstrānusāriṇaḥ
a na tatra kṛpaṇaḥ kaś cin na daridro babhūva ha
c kṣudhito duḥkhito vāpi prākṛto vāpi mānavaḥ
a bhojanaṃ bhojanārthibhyo dāpayām āsa nityadā
c bhīmaseno mahātejāḥ satataṃ rājaśāsanāt
a saṃstare kuśalāś cāpi sarvakarmāṇi yājakāḥ
c divase divase cakrur yathāśāstrārthacakṣuṣaḥ
a nāṣaḍaṅgavid atrāsīt sadasyas tasya dhīmataḥ
c nāvrato nānupādhyāyo na ca vādākṣamo dvijaḥ
a tato yūpocchraye prāpte ṣaḍ bailvān bharatarṣabha
c khādirān bilvasamitāṃs tāvataḥ sarvavarṇinaḥ
a devadārumayau dvau tu yūpau kurupateḥ kratau
c śleṣmātakamayaṃ caikaṃ yājakāḥ samakārayan
d sarvān etān yathāśāstraṃ yājakāḥ samayojayan
a śobhārthaṃ cāparān yūpān kāñcanān puruṣarṣabha
c sa bhīmaḥ kārayām āsa dharmarājasya śāsanāt
a te vyarājanta rājarṣe vāsobhir upaśobhitāḥ
c narendrābhigatā devān yathā saptarṣayo divi
a iṣṭakāḥ kāñcanīś cātra cayanārthaṃ kṛtābhavan
c śuśubhe cayanaṃ tatra dakṣasyeva prajāpateḥ
a catuścityaḥ sa tasyāsīd aṣṭādaśakarātmakaḥ
c sa rukmapakṣo nicitas triguṇo garuḍākṛtiḥ
a tato niyuktāḥ paśavo yathāśāstraṃ manīṣibhiḥ
c taṃ taṃ devaṃ samuddiśya pakṣiṇaḥ paśavaś ca ye
a ṛṣabhāḥ śāstrapaṭhitās tathā jalacarāś ca ye
c sarvāṃs tān abhyayuñjaṃs te tatrāgnicayakarmaṇi
a yūpeṣu niyataṃ cāsīt paśūnāṃ triśataṃ tathā
c aśvaratnottaraṃ rājñaḥ kaunteyasya mahātmanaḥ
a sa yajñaḥ śuśubhe tasya sākṣād devarṣisaṃkulaḥ
c gandharvagaṇasaṃkīrṇaḥ śobhito 'psarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ
a sa kiṃpuruṣagītaiś ca kiṃnarair upaśobhitaḥ
c siddhavipranivāsaiś ca samantād abhisaṃvṛtaḥ
a tasmin sadasi nityās tu vyāsaśiṣyā dvijottamāḥ
c sarvaśāstrapraṇetāraḥ kuśalā yajñakarmasu
a nāradaś ca babhūvātra tumburuś ca mahādyutiḥ
c viśvāvasuś citrasenas tathānye gītakovidāḥ
a gandharvā gītakuśalā nṛtteṣu ca viśāradāḥ
c ramayanti sma tān viprān yajñakarmāntareṣv atha
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a śamayitvā paśūn anyān vidhivad dvijasattamāḥ
c turagaṃ taṃ yathāśāstram ālabhanta dvijātayaḥ
a tataḥ saṃjñāpya turagaṃ vidhivad yājakarṣabhāḥ
c upasaṃveśayan rājaṃs tatas tāṃ drupadātmajām
d sarvaśāstrapraṇetāraḥ kuśalā yajñakarmasu
e kalābhis tisṛbhī rājan yathāvidhi manasvinīm
a uddhṛtya tu vapāṃ tasya yathāśāstraṃ dvijarṣabhāḥ
c śrapayām āsur avyagrāḥ śāstravad bharatarṣabha
a taṃ vapādhūmagandhaṃ tu dharmarājaḥ sahānujaḥ
c upājighrad yathānyāyaṃ sarvapāpmāpahaṃ tadā
a śiṣṭāny aṅgāni yāny āsaṃs tasyāśvasya narādhipa
c tāny agnau juhuvur dhīrāḥ samastāḥ ṣoḍaśartvijaḥ
a saṃsthāpyaivaṃ tasya rājñas taṃ kratuṃ śakratejasaḥ
c vyāsaḥ saśiṣyo bhagavān vardhayām āsa taṃ nṛpam
a tato yudhiṣṭhiraḥ prādāt sadasyebhyo yathāvidhi
c koṭīsahasraṃ niṣkāṇāṃ vyāsāya tu vasuṃdharām
a pratigṛhya dharāṃ rājan vyāsaḥ satyavatīsutaḥ
c abravīd bharataśreṣṭhaṃ dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
a pṛthivī bhavatas tv eṣā saṃnyastā rājasattama
c niṣkrayo dīyatāṃ mahyaṃ brāhmaṇā hi dhanārthinaḥ
a yudhiṣṭhiras tu tān viprān pratyuvāca mahāmanāḥ
c bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito dhīmān madhye rājñāṃ mahātmanām
a aśvamedhe mahāyajñe pṛthivī dakṣiṇā smṛtā
c arjunena jitā seyam ṛtvigbhyaḥ prāpitā mayā
a vanaṃ pravekṣye viprendrā vibhajadhvaṃ mahīm imām
c caturdhā pṛthivīṃ kṛtvā cāturhotrapramāṇataḥ
a nāham ādātum icchāmi brahmasvaṃ munisattamāḥ
c idaṃ hi me mataṃ nityaṃ bhrātṝṇāṃ ca mamānaghāḥ
a ity uktavati tasmiṃs te bhrātaro draupadī ca sā
c evam etad iti prāhus tad abhūd romaharṣaṇam
a tato 'ntarikṣe vāg āsīt sādhu sādhv iti bhārata
c tathaiva dvijasaṃghānāṃ śaṃsatāṃ vibabhau svanaḥ
a dvaipāyanas tathoktas tu punar eva yudhiṣṭhiram
c uvāca madhye viprāṇām idaṃ saṃpūjayan muniḥ
a dattaiṣā bhavatā mahyaṃ tāṃ te pratidadāmy aham
c hiraṇyaṃ dīyatām ebhyo dvijātibhyo dharās tu te
a tato 'bravīd vāsudevo dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c yathāha bhagavān vyāsas tathā tat kartum arhasi
a ity uktaḥ sa kuruśreṣṭhaḥ prītātmā bhrātṛbhiḥ saha
c koṭikoṭikṛtāṃ prādād dakṣiṇāṃ triguṇāṃ kratoḥ
a na kariṣyati tal loke kaś cid anyo narādhipaḥ
c yat kṛtaṃ kurusiṃhena maruttasyānukurvatā
a pratigṛhya tu tad dravyaṃ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ
c ṛtvigbhyaḥ pradadau vidvāṃś caturdhā vyabhajaṃś ca te
a pṛthivyā niṣkrayaṃ dattvā tad dhiraṇyaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c dhūtapāpmā jitasvargo mumude bhrātṛbhiḥ saha
a ṛtvijas tam aparyantaṃ suvarṇanicayaṃ tadā
c vyabhajanta dvijātibhyo yathotsāhaṃ yathābalam
a yajñavāṭe tu yat kiṃ cid dhiraṇyam api bhūṣaṇam
c toraṇāni ca yūpāṃś ca ghaṭāḥ pātrīs tatheṣṭakāḥ
e yudhiṣṭhirābhyanujñātāḥ sarvaṃ tad vyabhajan dvijāḥ
a anantaraṃ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ kṣatriyā jahrire vasu
c tathā viṭśūdrasaṃghāś ca tathānye mlecchajātayaḥ
e kālena mahatā jahrus tat suvarṇaṃ tatas tataḥ
a tatas te brāhmaṇāḥ sarve muditā jagmur ālayān
c tarpitā vasunā tena dharmarājñā mahātmanā
a svam aṃśaṃ bhagavān vyāsaḥ kuntyai pādābhivādanāt
c pradadau tasya mahato hiraṇyasya mahādyutiḥ
a śvaśurāt prītidāyaṃ taṃ prāpya sā prītamānasā
c cakāra puṇyaṃ loke tu sumahāntaṃ pṛthā tadā
a gatvā tv avabhṛthaṃ rājā vipāpmā bhrātṛbhiḥ saha
c sabhājyamānaḥ śuśubhe mahendro daivatair iva
a pāṇḍavāś ca mahīpālaiḥ sametaiḥ saṃvṛtās tadā
c aśobhanta mahārāja grahās tārāgaṇair iva
a rājabhyo 'pi tataḥ prādād ratnāni vividhāni ca
c gajān aśvān alaṃkārān striyo vastrāṇi kāñcanam
a tad dhanaugham aparyantaṃ pārthaḥ pārthivamaṇḍale
c visṛjañ śuśubhe rājā yathā vaiśravaṇas tathā
a ānāyya ca tathā vīraṃ rājānaṃ babhruvāhanam
c pradāya vipulaṃ vittaṃ gṛhān prāsthāpayat tadā
a duḥśalāyāś ca taṃ pautraṃ bālakaṃ pārthivarṣabha
c svarājye pitṛbhir gupte prītyā samabhiṣecayat
a rājñaś caivāpi tān sarvān suvibhaktān supūjitān
c prasthāpayām āsa vaśī kururājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d govindaṃ ca mahātmānaṃ baladevaṃ mahābalam
d tathānyān vṛṣṇivīrāṃś ca pradyumnādīn sahasraśaḥ
d pūjayitvā mahārāja yathāvidhi mahādyutiḥ
d bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito rājā prāsthāpayad ariṃdamaḥ
a evaṃ babhūva yajñaḥ sa dharmarājasya dhīmataḥ
c bahvannadhanaratnaughaḥ surāmaireyasāgaraḥ
a sarpiḥpaṅkā hradā yatra bahavaś cānnaparvatāḥ
c rasālākardamāḥ kulyā babhūvur bharatarṣabha
a bhakṣyaṣāṇḍavarāgāṇāṃ kriyatāṃ bhujyatām iti
c paśūnāṃ vadhyatāṃ cāpi nāntas tatra sma dṛśyate
a mattonmattapramuditaṃ pragītayuvatījanam
c mṛdaṅgaśaṅkhaśabdaiś ca manoramam abhūt tadā
a dīyatāṃ bhujyatāṃ ceti divārātram avāritam
a   tatra śabdo mahān abhūt
a pīyatāṃ dīyatāṃ ceti
c taṃ mahotsavasaṃkāśam atihṛṣṭajanākulam
e kathayanti sma puruṣā nānādeśanivāsinaḥ
a varṣitvā dhanadhārābhiḥ kāmai ratnair dhanais tathā
c vipāpmā bharataśreṣṭhaḥ kṛtārthaḥ prāviśat puram
 janamejaya uvāca
a pitāmahasya me yajñe dharmaputrasya dhīmataḥ
c yad āścaryam abhūt kiṃ cit tad bhavān vaktum arhati
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a śrūyatāṃ rājaśārdūla mahad āścaryam uttamam
c aśvamedhe mahāyajñe nivṛtte yad abhūd vibho
a tarpiteṣu dvijāgryeṣu jñātisaṃbandhibandhuṣu
c dīnāndhakṛpaṇe cāpi tadā bharatasattama
a ghuṣyamāṇe mahādāne dikṣu sarvāsu bhārata
c patatsu puṣpavarṣeṣu dharmarājasya mūrdhani
a bilān niṣkramya nakulo rukmapārśvas tadānagha
c vajrāśanisamaṃ nādam amuñcata viśāṃ pate
a sakṛd utsṛjya taṃ nādaṃ trāsayāno mṛgadvijān
c mānuṣaṃ vacanaṃ prāha dhṛṣṭo bilaśayo mahān
a saktuprasthena vo nāyaṃ yajñas tulyo narādhipāḥ
c uñchavṛtter vadānyasya kurukṣetranivāsinaḥ
a tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā nakulasya viśāṃ pate
c vismayaṃ paramaṃ jagmuḥ sarve te brāhmaṇarṣabhāḥ
a tataḥ sametya nakulaṃ paryapṛcchanta te dvijāḥ
c kutas tvaṃ samanuprāpto yajñaṃ sādhusamāgamam
a kiṃ balaṃ paramaṃ tubhyaṃ kiṃ śrutaṃ kiṃ parāyaṇam
c kathaṃ bhavantaṃ vidyāma yo no yajñaṃ vigarhase
a avilupyāgamaṃ kṛtsnaṃ vidhijñair yājakaiḥ kṛtam
c yathāgamaṃ yathānyāyaṃ kartavyaṃ ca yathākṛtam
a pūjārhāḥ pūjitāś cātra vidhivac chāstracakṣuṣā
c mantrapūtaṃ hutaś cāgnir dattaṃ deyam amatsaram
a tuṣṭā dvijarṣabhāś cātra dānair bahuvidhair api
c kṣatriyāś ca suyuddhena śrāddhair api pitāmahāḥ
a pālanena viśas tuṣṭāḥ kāmais tuṣṭā varastriyaḥ
c anukrośais tathā śūdrā dānaśeṣaiḥ pṛthagjanāḥ
a jñātisaṃbandhinas tuṣṭāḥ śaucena ca nṛpasya naḥ
c devā havirbhiḥ puṇyaiś ca rakṣaṇaiḥ śaraṇāgatāḥ
a yad atra tathyaṃ tad brūhi satyasaṃdha dvijātiṣu
c yathāśrutaṃ yathādṛṣṭaṃ pṛṣṭo brāhmaṇakāmyayā
a śraddheyavākyaḥ prājñas tvaṃ divyaṃ rūpaṃ bibharṣi ca
c samāgataś ca viprais tvaṃ tattvato vaktum arhasi
a iti pṛṣṭo dvijais taiḥ sa prahasya nakulo 'bravīt
c naiṣānṛtā mayā vāṇī proktā darpeṇa vā dvijāḥ
a yan mayoktam idaṃ kiṃ cid yuṣmābhiś cāpy upaśrutam
c saktuprasthena vo nāyaṃ yajñas tulyo narādhipāḥ
e uñchavṛtter vadānyasya kurukṣetranivāsinaḥ
a ity avaśyaṃ mayaitad vo vaktavyaṃ dvijapuṃgavāḥ
c śṛṇutāvyagramanasaḥ śaṃsato me dvijarṣabhāḥ
a anubhūtaṃ ca dṛṣṭaṃ ca yan mayādbhutam uttamam
c uñchavṛtter yathāvṛttaṃ kurukṣetranivāsinaḥ
a svargaṃ yena dvijaḥ prāptaḥ sabhāryaḥ sasutasnuṣaḥ
c yathā cārdhaṃ śarīrasya mamedaṃ kāñcanīkṛtam
 nakula uvāca
a hanta vo vartayiṣyāmi dānasya paramaṃ phalam
c nyāyalabdhasya sūkṣmasya vipradattasya yad dvijāḥ
a dharmakṣetre kurukṣetre dharmajñair bahubhir vṛte
c uñchavṛttir dvijaḥ kaś cit kāpotir abhavat purā
a sabhāryaḥ saha putreṇa sasnuṣas tapasi sthitaḥ
c vadhūcaturtho vṛddhaḥ sa dharmātmā niyatendriyaḥ
a ṣaṣṭhe kāle tadā vipro bhuṅkte taiḥ saha suvrataḥ
c ṣaṣṭhe kāle kadā cic ca tasyāhāro na vidyate
e bhuṅkte 'nyasmin kadā cit sa ṣaṣṭhe kāle dvijottamaḥ
a kapotadharmiṇas tasya durbhikṣe sati dāruṇe
c nāvidyata tadā viprāḥ saṃcayas tān nibodhata
e kṣīṇauṣadhisamāvāyo dravyahīno 'bhavat tadā
a kāle kāle 'sya saṃprāpte naiva vidyeta bhojanam
c kṣudhāparigatāḥ sarve prātiṣṭhanta tadā tu te
a uñchaṃs tadā śuklapakṣe madhyaṃ tapati bhāskare
c uṣṇārtaś ca kṣudhārtaś ca sa vipras tapasi sthitaḥ
e uñcham aprāptavān eva sārdhaṃ parijanena ha
a sa tathaiva kṣudhāviṣṭaḥ spṛṣṭvā toyaṃ yathāvidhi
c kṣapayām āsa taṃ kālaṃ kṛcchraprāṇo dvijottamaḥ
a atha ṣaṣṭhe gate kāle yavaprastham upārjayat
c yavaprasthaṃ ca te saktūn akurvanta tapasvinaḥ
a kṛtajapyāhvikās te tu hutvā vahniṃ yathāvidhi
c kuḍavaṃ kuḍavaṃ sarve vyabhajanta tapasvinaḥ
a athāgacchad dvijaḥ kaś cid atithir bhuñjatāṃ tadā
c te taṃ dṛṣṭvātithiṃ tatra prahṛṣṭamanaso 'bhavan
a te 'bhivādya sukhapraśnaṃ pṛṣṭvā tam atithiṃ tadā
c viśuddhamanaso dāntāḥ śraddhādamasamanvitāḥ
a anasūyavo gatakrodhāḥ sādhavo gatamatsarāḥ
c tyaktamānā jitakrodhā dharmajñā dvijasattamāḥ
a sabrahmacaryaṃ svaṃ gotraṃ samākhyāya parasparam
c kuṭīṃ praveśayām āsuḥ kṣudhārtam atithiṃ tadā
a idam arghyaṃ ca pādyaṃ ca bṛsī ceyaṃ tavānagha
c śucayaḥ saktavaś ceme niyamopārjitāḥ prabho
e pratigṛhṇīṣva bhadraṃ te mayā dattā dvijottama
a ity uktaḥ pratigṛhyātha saktūnāṃ kuḍavaṃ dvijaḥ
c bhakṣayām āsa rājendra na ca tuṣṭiṃ jagāma saḥ
a sa uñchavṛttiḥ taṃ prekṣya kṣudhāparigataṃ dvijam
c āhāraṃ cintayām āsa kathaṃ tuṣṭo bhaved iti
a tasya bhāryābravīd rājan madbhāgo dīyatām iti
c gacchatv eṣa yathākāmaṃ saṃtuṣṭo dvijasattamaḥ
a iti bruvantīṃ tāṃ sādhvīṃ dharmātmā sa dvijarṣabhaḥ
c kṣudhāparigatāṃ jñātvā saktūṃs tān nābhyanandata
d ātmānumānato vidvān sa tu viprarṣabhas tadā
a jānan vṛddhāṃ kṣudhārtāṃ ca śrāntāṃ glānāṃ tapasvinīm
c tvagasthibhūtāṃ vepantīṃ tato bhāryām uvāca tām
a api kīṭapataṃgānāṃ mṛgāṇāṃ caiva śobhane
c striyo rakṣyāś ca poṣyāś ca naivaṃ tvaṃ vaktum arhasi
a anukampito naro nāryā puṣṭo rakṣita eva ca
c prapated yaśaso dīptān na ca lokān avāpnuyāt
d dharmakāmārthakāryāṇi śuśrūṣā kulasaṃtatiḥ
d dāreṣv adhīno dharmaś ca pitṝṇām ātmanas tathā
d na vetti karmato bhāryārakṣaṇe yo 'kṣamaḥ pumān
d ayaśo mahad āpnoti narakāṃś caiva gacchati
a ity uktā sā tataḥ prāha dharmārthau nau samau dvija
c saktuprasthacaturbhāgaṃ gṛhāṇemaṃ prasīda me
a satyaṃ ratiś ca dharmaś ca svargaś ca guṇanirjitaḥ
c strīṇāṃ patisamādhīnaṃ kāṅkṣitaṃ ca dvijottama
a ṛtur mātuḥ pitur bījaṃ daivataṃ paramaṃ patiḥ
c bhartuḥ prasādāt strīṇāṃ vai ratiḥ putraphalaṃ tathā
a pālanād dhi patis tvaṃ me bhartāsi bharaṇān mama
c putrapradānād varadas tasmāt saktūn gṛhāṇa me
a jarāparigato vṛddhaḥ kṣudhārto durbalo bhṛśam
c upavāsapariśrānto yadā tvam api karśitaḥ
a ity uktaḥ sa tayā saktūn pragṛhyedaṃ vaco 'bravīt
c dvija saktūn imān bhūyaḥ pratigṛhṇīṣva sattama
a sa tān pragṛhya bhuktvā ca na tuṣṭim agamad dvijaḥ
c tam uñchavṛttir ālakṣya tataś cintāparo 'bhavat
d tam uvāca tataḥ putraḥ pitaraṃ dīnamānasam
d praśrayāvanato bhūtvā hetuyuktam idaṃ vacaḥ
 putra uvāca
a saktūn imān pragṛhya tvaṃ dehi viprāya sattama
c ity evaṃ sukṛtaṃ manye tasmād etat karomy aham
a bhavān hi paripālyo me sarvayatnair dvijottama
c sādhūnāṃ kāṅkṣitaṃ hy etat pitur vṛddhasya poṣaṇam
a putrārtho vihito hy eṣa sthāvirye paripālanam
c śrutir eṣā hi viprarṣe triṣu lokeṣu viśrutā
a prāṇadhāraṇamātreṇa śakyaṃ kartuṃ tapas tvayā
c prāṇo hi paramo dharmaḥ sthito deheṣu dehinām
 pitovāca
a api varṣasahasrī tvaṃ bāla eva mato mama
c utpādya putraṃ hi pitā kṛtakṛtyo bhavaty uta
a bālānāṃ kṣud balavatī jānāmy etad ahaṃ vibho
c vṛddho 'haṃ dhārayiṣyāmi tvaṃ balī bhava putraka
a jīrṇena vayasā putra na mā kṣud bādhate 'pi ca
c dīrghakālaṃ tapas taptaṃ na me maraṇato bhayam
 putra uvāca
a apatyam asmi te putras trāṇāt putro hi viśrutaḥ
c ātmā putraḥ smṛtas tasmāt trāhy ātmānam ihātmanā
d putro 'haṃ tava viprarṣe tvayā pālyo 'smi sarvadā
d idānīṃ tu imān saktūn dīyatāṃ kṣudhitāya ca
 pitovāca
a rūpeṇa sadṛśas tvaṃ me śīlena ca damena ca
c parīkṣitaś ca bahudhā saktūn ādadmi te tataḥ
d praśrayeṇa tathā buddhyā vṛttyā kṣāntyā tathaiva ca
a ity uktvādāya tān saktūn prītātmā dvijasattamaḥ
c prahasann iva viprāya sa tasmai pradadau tadā
a bhuktvā tān api saktūn sa naiva tuṣṭo babhūva ha
c uñchavṛttis tu savrīḍo babhūva dvijasattamaḥ
a taṃ vai vadhūḥ sthitā sādhvī brāhmaṇapriyakāmyayā
c saktūn ādāya saṃhṛṣṭā guruṃ taṃ vākyam abravīt
a saṃtānāt tava saṃtānaṃ mama vipra bhaviṣyati
c saktūn imān atithaye gṛhītvā tvaṃ prayaccha me
a tava prasavanirvṛtyā mama lokāḥ kilākṣayāḥ
c pautreṇa tān avāpnoti yatra gatvā na śocati
a dharmādyā hi yathā tretā vahnitretā tathaiva ca
c tathaiva putrapautrāṇāṃ svarge tretā kilākṣayā
a pitṝṃs trāṇāt tārayati putra ity anuśuśruma
c putrapautraiś ca niyataṃ sādhulokān upāśnute
 śvaśura uvāca
a vātātapaviśīrṇāṅgīṃ tvāṃ vivarṇāṃ nirīkṣya vai
c karśitāṃ suvratācāre kṣudhāvihvalacetasam
a kathaṃ saktūn grahīṣyāmi bhūtvā dharmopaghātakaḥ
c kalyāṇavṛtte kalyāṇi naivaṃ tvaṃ vaktum arhasi
a ṣaṣṭhe kāle vratavatīṃ śīlaśaucasamanvitām
c kṛcchravṛttiṃ nirāhārāṃ drakṣyāmi tvāṃ kathaṃ nv aham
a bālā kṣudhārtā nārī ca rakṣyā tvaṃ satataṃ mayā
c upavāsapariśrāntā tvaṃ hi bāndhavanandinī
 snuṣovāca
a guror mama gurus tvaṃ vai yato daivatadaivatam
c devātidevas tasmāt tvaṃ saktūn ādatsva me vibho
a dehaḥ prāṇaś ca dharmaś ca śuśrūṣārtham idaṃ guroḥ
c tava vipra prasādena lokān prāpsyāmy abhīpsitān
a avekṣyā iti kṛtvā tvaṃ dṛḍhabhaktyeti vā dvija
c cintyā mameyam iti vā saktūn ādātum arhasi
 śvaśura uvāca
a anena nityaṃ sādhvī tvaṃ śīlavṛttena śobhase
c yā tvaṃ dharmavratopetā guruvṛttim avekṣase
a tasmāt saktūn grahīṣyāmi vadhūr nārhasi vañcanām
c gaṇayitvā mahābhāge tvaṃ hi dharmabhṛtāṃ varā
a ity uktvā tān upādāya saktūn prādād dvijātaye
c tatas tuṣṭo 'bhavad vipras tasya sādhor mahātmanaḥ
a prītātmā sa tu taṃ vākyam idam āha dvijarṣabham
c vāgmī tadā dvijaśreṣṭho dharmaḥ puruṣavigrahaḥ
a śuddhena tava dānena nyāyopāttena yatnataḥ
c yathāśakti vimuktena prīto 'smi dvijasattama
a aho dānaṃ ghuṣyate te svarge svarganivāsibhiḥ
c gaganāt puṣpavarṣaṃ ca paśyasva patitaṃ bhuvi
d gantāśu devavarṣāṇi anantāni mahāmate
a surarṣidevagandharvā ye ca devapuraḥsarāḥ
c stuvanto devadūtāś ca sthitā dānena vismitāḥ
a brahmarṣayo vimānasthā brahmalokagatāś ca ye
c kāṅkṣante darśanaṃ tubhyaṃ divaṃ gaccha dvijarṣabha
a pitṛlokagatāḥ sarve tāritāḥ pitaras tvayā
c anāgatāś ca bahavaḥ subahūni yugāni ca
a brahmacaryeṇa yajñena dānena tapasā tathā
c agahvareṇa dharmeṇa tasmād gaccha divaṃ dvija
a śraddhayā parayā yas tvaṃ tapaś carasi suvrata
c tasmād devās tavānena prītā dvijavarottama
c prītātmā devatāḥ sarve yate na tapasā tathā
a sarvasvam etad yasmāt te tyaktaṃ śuddhena cetasā
c kṛcchrakāle tataḥ svargo jito 'yaṃ tava karmaṇā
a kṣudhā nirṇudati prajñāṃ dharmyāṃ buddhiṃ vyapohati
c kṣudhāparigatajñāno dhṛtiṃ tyajati caiva ha
a bubhukṣāṃ jayate yas tu sa svargaṃ jayate dhruvam
c yadā dānarucir bhavati tadā dharmo na sīdati
a anavekṣya sutasnehaṃ kalatrasneham eva ca
c dharmam eva guruṃ jñātvā tṛṣṇā na gaṇitā tvayā
a dravyāgamo nṛṇāṃ sūkṣmaḥ pātre dānaṃ tataḥ param
c kālaḥ parataro dānāc chraddhā cāpi tataḥ parā
a svargadvāraṃ susūkṣmaṃ hi narair mohān na dṛśyate
c svargārgalaṃ lobhabījaṃ rāgaguptaṃ durāsadam
a tat tu paśyanti puruṣā jitakrodhā jitendriyāḥ
c brāhmaṇās tapasā yuktā yathāśaktipradāyinaḥ
a sahasraśaktiś ca śataṃ śataśaktir daśāpi ca
c dadyād apaś ca yaḥ śaktyā sarve tulyaphalāḥ smṛtāḥ
a rantidevo hi nṛpatir apaḥ prādād akiṃcanaḥ
c śuddhena manasā vipra nākapṛṣṭhaṃ tato gataḥ
a na dharmaḥ prīyate tāta dānair dattair mahāphalaiḥ
c nyāyalabdhair yathā sūkṣmaiḥ śraddhāpūtaiḥ sa tuṣyati
a gopradānasahasrāṇi dvijebhyo 'dān nṛgo nṛpaḥ
c ekāṃ dattvā sa pārakyāṃ narakaṃ samavāptavān
a ātmamāṃsapradānena śibir auśīnaro nṛpaḥ
c prāpya puṇyakṛtāṃl lokān modate divi suvrataḥ
a vibhave na nṛṇāṃ puṇyaṃ svaśaktyā svarjitaṃ satām
b nṛṇāṃ puṇyaṃ sa śaktyā ca varjitaṃ garjanaṃ tadā
c na yajñair vividhair vipra yathānyāyena saṃcitaiḥ
a krodho dānaphalaṃ hanti lobhāt svargaṃ na gacchati
c nyāyavṛttir hi tapasā dānavit svargam aśnute
a na rājasūyair bahubhir iṣṭvā vipuladakṣiṇaiḥ
c na cāśvamedhair bahubhiḥ phalaṃ samam idaṃ tava
a saktuprasthena hi jito brahmalokas tvayānagha
c virajo brahmabhavanaṃ gaccha vipra yathecchakam
a sarveṣāṃ vo dvijaśreṣṭha divyaṃ yānam upasthitam
c ārohata yathākāmaṃ dharmo 'smi dvija paśya mām
a pāvito hi tvayā deho loke kīrtiḥ sthirā ca te
c sabhāryaḥ sahaputraś ca sasnuṣaś ca divaṃ vraja
a ity uktavākyo dharmeṇa yānam āruhya sa dvijaḥ
c sabhāryaḥ sasutaś cāpi sasnuṣaś ca divaṃ yayau
a tasmin vipre gate svargaṃ sasute sasnuṣe tadā
c bhāryācaturthe dharmajñe tato 'haṃ niḥsṛto bilāt
a tatas tu saktugandhena kledena salilasya ca
c divyapuṣpāvamardāc ca sādhor dānalavaiś ca taiḥ
e viprasya tapasā tasya śiro me kāñcanīkṛtam
a tasya satyābhisaṃdhasya sūkṣmadānena caiva ha
c śarīrārdhaṃ ca me viprāḥ śātakumbhamayaṃ kṛtam
e paśyatedaṃ suvipulaṃ tapasā tasya dhīmataḥ
a katham evaṃvidhaṃ me syād anyat pārśvam iti dvijāḥ
c tapovanāni yajñāṃś ca hṛṣṭo 'bhyemi punaḥ punaḥ
a yajñaṃ tv aham imaṃ śrutvā kururājasya dhīmataḥ
c āśayā parayā prāpto na cāhaṃ kāñcanīkṛtaḥ
a tato mayoktaṃ tad vākyaṃ prahasya dvijasattamāḥ
c saktuprasthena yajño 'yaṃ saṃmito neti sarvathā
a saktuprasthalavais tair hi tadāhaṃ kāñcanīkṛtaḥ
c na hi yajño mahān eṣa sadṛśas tair mato mama
d saktuprasthena vo nāyaṃ yajñas tulyo matir mama
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a ity uktvā nakulaḥ sarvān yajñe dvijavarāṃs tadā
c jagāmādarśanaṃ rājan viprās te ca yayur gṛhān
a etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃ mayā parapuraṃjaya
c yad āścaryam abhūt tasmin vājimedhe mahākratau
a na vismayas te nṛpate yajñe kāryaḥ kathaṃ cana
c ṛṣikoṭisahasrāṇi tapobhir ye divaṃ gatāḥ
a adrohaḥ sarvabhūteṣu saṃtoṣaḥ śīlam ārjavam
c tapo damaś ca satyaṃ ca dānaṃ ceti samaṃ matam
 janamejaya uvāca
a yajñe saktā nṛpatayas tapaḥsaktā maharṣayaḥ
c śāntivyavasitā viprāḥ śamo dama iti prabho
a tasmād yajñaphalais tulyaṃ na kiṃ cid iha vidyate
c iti me vartate buddhis tathā caitad asaṃśayam
a yajñair iṣṭvā hi bahavo rājāno dvijasattama
c iha kīrtiṃ parāṃ prāpya pretya svargam ito gatāḥ
a devarājaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ kratubhir bhūridakṣiṇaiḥ
c devarājyaṃ mahātejāḥ prāptavān akhilaṃ vibhuḥ
d yajñais tapobhir vipulai rājāno dvijasattamāḥ
d iha loke parāṃ kīrtiṃ vimucya divi saṃsthitāḥ
a yathā yudhiṣṭhiro rājā bhīmārjunapuraḥsaraḥ
c sadṛśo devarājena samṛddhyā vikrameṇa ca
a atha kasmāt sa nakulo garhayām āsa taṃ kratum
c aśvamedhaṃ mahāyajñaṃ rājñas tasya mahātmanaḥ
d iti hetor mahārāja nakulo 'garhayac ca tat
d karma rājño mahābuddhe dharmaḥ sūkṣmo mahīpate
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a yajñasya vidhim agryaṃ vai phalaṃ caiva nararṣabha
c gadataḥ śṛṇu me rājan yathāvad iha bhārata
a purā śakrasya yajataḥ sarva ūcur maharṣayaḥ
c ṛtvikṣu karmavyagreṣu vitate yajñakarmaṇi
a hūyamāne tathā vahnau hotre bahuguṇānvite
c deveṣv āhūyamāneṣu sthiteṣu paramarṣiṣu
a supratītais tadā vipraiḥ svāgamaiḥ susvanair nṛpa
c aśrāntaiś cāpi laghubhir adhvaryuvṛṣabhais tathā
a ālambhasamaye tasmin gṛhīteṣu paśuṣv atha
c maharṣayo mahārāja saṃbabhūvuḥ kṛpānvitāḥ
a tato dīnān paśūn dṛṣṭvā ṛṣayas te tapodhanāḥ
c ūcuḥ śakraṃ samāgamya nāyaṃ yajñavidhiḥ śubhaḥ
a apavijñānam etat te mahāntaṃ dharmam icchataḥ
c na hi yajñe paśugaṇā vidhidṛṣṭāḥ puraṃdara
a dharmopaghātakas tv eṣa samārambhas tava prabho
c nāyaṃ dharmakṛto dharmo na hiṃsā dharma ucyate
a āgamenaiva te yajñaṃ kurvantu yadi hecchasi
c vidhidṛṣṭena yajñena dharmas te sumahān bhavet
a yaja bījaiḥ sahasrākṣa trivarṣaparamoṣitaiḥ
c eṣa dharmo mahāñ śakra cintyamāno 'dhigamyate
a śatakratus tu tad vākyam ṛṣibhis tattvadarśibhiḥ
c uktaṃ na pratijagrāha mānamohavaśānugaḥ
a teṣāṃ vivādaḥ sumahāñ jajñe śakramaharṣiṇām
c jaṅgamaiḥ sthāvarair vāpi yaṣṭavyam iti bhārata
a te tu khinnā vivādena ṛṣayas tattvadarśinaḥ
c tataḥ saṃdhāya śakreṇa papracchur nṛpatiṃ vasum
d dharmasaṃśayam āpannān satyaṃ brūhi mahāmate
a mahābhāga kathaṃ yajñeṣv āgamo nṛpate smṛtaḥ
c yaṣṭavyaṃ paśubhir medhyair atho bījair ajair api
a tac chrutvā tu vacas teṣām avicārya balābalam
c yathopanītair yaṣṭavyam iti provāca pārthivaḥ
a evam uktvā sa nṛpatiḥ praviveśa rasātalam
c uktveha vitathaṃ rājaṃś cedīnām īśvaraḥ prabhuḥ
d tasmān na vācyaṃ hy ekena bahujñenāpi saṃśaye
d prajāpatim apāhāya svayaṃbhuvam ṛte prabhum
a anyāyopagataṃ dravyam atītaṃ yo hy apaṇḍitaḥ
c dharmābhikāṅkṣī yajate na dharmaphalam aśnute
a dharmavaitaṃsiko yas tu pāpātmā puruṣas tathā
c dadāti dānaṃ viprebhyo lokaviśvāsakārakam
a pāpena karmaṇā vipro dhanaṃ labdhvā niraṅkuśaḥ
c rāgamohānvitaḥ so 'nte kaluṣāṃ gatim āpnute
a tena dattāni dānāni pāpena hatabuddhinā
c tāni sattvam anāsādya naśyanti vipulāny api
a tasyādharmapravṛttasya hiṃsakasya durātmanaḥ
c dāne na kīrtir bhavati pretya ceha ca durmateḥ
a api saṃcayabuddhir hi lobhamohavaśaṃgataḥ
c udvejayati bhūtāni hiṃsayā pāpacetanaḥ
a evaṃ labdhvā dhanaṃ lobhād yajate yo dadāti ca
c sa kṛtvā karmaṇā tena na sidhyati durāgamāt
d   yo hi dadyād yajeta vā
d na tasya sa phalaṃ pretya bhuṅkte pāpadhanāgamāt
a uñchaṃ mūlaṃ phalaṃ śākam udapātraṃ tapodhanāḥ
c dānaṃ vibhavato dattvā narāḥ svar yānti dharmiṇaḥ
a eṣa dharmo mahāṃs tyāgo dānaṃ bhūtadayā tathā
c brahmacaryaṃ tathā satyam anukrośo dhṛtiḥ kṣamā
e sanātanasya dharmasya mūlam etat sanātanam
a śrūyante hi purā viprā viśvāmitrādayo nṛpāḥ
c viśvāmitro 'sitaś caiva janakaś ca mahīpatiḥ
e kakṣasenārṣṭiṣeṇau ca sindhudvīpaś ca pārthivaḥ
a ete cānye ca bahavaḥ siddhiṃ paramikāṃ gatāḥ
c nṛpāḥ satyaiś ca dānaiś ca nyāyalabdhais tapodhanāḥ
a brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrā ye cāśritās tapaḥ
c dānadharmāgninā śuddhās te svargaṃ yānti bhārata
 janamejaya uvāca
a dharmāgatena tyāgena bhagavan sarvam asti cet
c etan me sarvam ācakṣva kuśalo hy asi bhāṣitum
a tatoñchavṛtter yad vṛttaṃ saktudāne phalaṃ mahat
c kathitaṃ me mahad brahmaṃs tathyam etad asaṃśayam
a kathaṃ hi sarvayajñeṣu niścayaḥ paramo bhavet
c etad arhasi me vaktuṃ nikhilena dvijarṣabha
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c agastyasya mahāyajñe purāvṛttam ariṃdama
a purāgastyo mahātejā dīkṣāṃ dvādaśavārṣikīm
c praviveśa mahārāja sarvabhūtahite rataḥ
a tatrāgnikalpā hotāra āsan satre mahātmanaḥ
c mūlāhārā nirāhārāḥ sāśmakuṭṭā marīcipāḥ
a parighṛṣṭikā vaighasikāḥ saṃprakṣālās tathaiva ca
c yatayo bhikṣavaś cātra babhūvuḥ paryavasthitāḥ
a sarve pratyakṣadharmāṇo jitakrodhā jitendriyāḥ
c dame sthitāś ca te sarve dambhamohavivarjitāḥ
a vṛtte śuddhe sthitā nityam indriyaiś cāpy avāhitāḥ
c upāsate sma taṃ yajñaṃ bhuñjānās te maharṣayaḥ
a yathāśaktyā bhagavatā tad annaṃ samupārjitam
c tasmin satre tu yat kiṃ cid ayogyaṃ tatra nābhavat
e tathā hy anekair munibhir mahāntaḥ kratavaḥ kṛtāḥ
a evaṃvidhes tv agastyasya vartamāne mahādhvare
c na vavarṣa sahasrākṣas tadā bharatasattama
a tataḥ karmāntare rājann agastyasya mahātmanaḥ
c katheyam abhinirvṛttā munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanām
a agastyo yajamāno 'sau dadāty annaṃ vimatsaraḥ
c na ca varṣati parjanyaḥ katham annaṃ bhaviṣyati
a satraṃ cedaṃ mahad viprā muner dvādaśavārṣikam
c na varṣiṣyati devaś ca varṣāṇy etāni dvādaśa
a etad bhavantaḥ saṃcintya maharṣer asya dhīmataḥ
c agastyasyātitapasaḥ kartum arhanty anugraham
a ity evam ukte vacane tato 'gastyaḥ pratāpavān
c provācedaṃ vaco vāgmī prasādya śirasā munīn
a yadi dvādaśavarṣāṇi na varṣiṣyati vāsavaḥ
c cintāyajñaṃ kariṣyāmi vidhir eṣa sanātanaḥ
a yadi dvādaśavarṣāṇi na varṣiṣyati vāsavaḥ
b sparśayajñaṃ kariṣyāmi vidhir eṣa sanātanaḥ
b yadi dvādaśavarṣāṇi na varṣiṣyati vāsavaḥ
c vyāyāmenāhariṣyāmi yajñān anyān ativratān
d dhyeyātmanā hariṣyāmi yajñān etān yatavrataḥ
a bījayajño mayāyaṃ vai bahuvarṣasamācitaḥ
c bījaiḥ kṛtaiḥ kariṣye ca nātra vighno bhaviṣyati
a nedaṃ śakyaṃ vṛthā kartuṃ mama satraṃ kathaṃ cana
c varṣiṣyatīha vā devo na vā devo bhaviṣyati
a atha vābhyarthanām indraḥ kuryān na tv iha kāmataḥ
c svayam indro bhaviṣyāmi jīvayiṣyāmi ca prajāḥ
a yo yad āhārajātaś ca sa tathaiva bhaviṣyati
c viśeṣaṃ caiva kartāsmi punaḥ punar atīva hi
a adyeha svarṇam abhyetu yac cānyad vasu durlabham
c triṣu lokeṣu yac cāsti tad ihāgacchatāṃ svayam
a divyāś cāpsarasāṃ saṃghāḥ sagandharvāḥ sakiṃnarāḥ
c viśvāvasuś ca ye cānye te 'py upāsantu vaḥ sadā
a uttarebhyaḥ kurubhyaś ca yat kiṃ cid vasu vidyate
c sarvaṃ tad iha yajñe me svayam evopatiṣṭhatu
e svargaṃ svargasadaś caiva dharmaś ca svayam eva tu
a ity ukte sarvam evaitad abhavat tasya dhīmataḥ
b tasya dīptāgnimahasas tv agastyasyātitejasaḥ
c tatas te munayo dṛṣṭvā munes tasya tapobalam
e vismitā vacanaṃ prāhur idaṃ sarve mahārthavat
a prītāḥ sma tava vākyena na tv icchāmas tapovyayam
c svair eva yajñais tuṣṭāḥ smo nyāyenecchāmahe vayam
a yajñān dīkṣās tathā homān yac cānyan mṛgayāmahe
c tan no 'stu svakṛtair yajñair nānyato mṛgayāmahe
a nyāyenopārjitāhārāḥ svakarmaniratā vayam
c vedāṃś ca brahmacaryeṇa nyāyataḥ prārthayāmahe
a nyāyenottarakālaṃ ca gṛhebhyo niḥsṛtā vayam
c dharmadṛṣṭair vidhidvārais tapas tapsyāmahe vayam
a bhavataḥ samyag eṣā hi buddhir hiṃsāvivarjitā
c etām ahiṃsāṃ yajñeṣu brūyās tvaṃ satataṃ prabho
a prītās tato bhaviṣyāmo vayaṃ dvijavarottama
c visarjitāḥ samāptau ca satrād asmād vrajāmahe
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tathā kathayatām eva devarājaḥ puraṃdaraḥ
c vavarṣa sumahātejā dṛṣṭvā tasya tapobalam
a asamāptau ca yajñasya tasyāmitaparākramaḥ
c nikāmavarṣī devendro babhūva janamejaya
a prasādayām āsa ca tam agastyaṃ tridaśeśvaraḥ
c svayam abhyetya rājarṣe puraskṛtya bṛhaspatim
a tato yajñasamāptau tān visasarja mahāmunīn
b vipine tatra nakulo nakulo 'ntarhitas tadā
c agastyaḥ paramaprītaḥ pūjayitvā yathāvidhi
 janamejaya uvāca
a ko 'sau nakularūpeṇa śirasā kāñcanena vai
c prāha mānuṣavad vācam etat pṛṣṭo vadasva me
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a etat pūrvaṃ na pṛṣṭo 'haṃ na cāsmābhiḥ prabhāṣitam
c śrūyatāṃ nakulo yo 'sau yathā vāg asya mānuṣī
a śrāddhaṃ saṃkalpayām āsa jamadagniḥ purā kila
c homadhenus tam āgāc ca svayaṃ cāpi dudoha tām
a tat kṣīraṃ sthāpayām āsa nave bhāṇḍe dṛḍhe śucau
c tac ca krodhaḥ svarūpeṇa piṭharaṃ paryavartayat
a jijñāsus tam ṛṣiśreṣṭhaṃ kiṃ kuryād vipriye kṛte
c iti saṃcintya durmedhā dharṣayām āsa tat payaḥ
a tam ājñāya muniḥ krodhaṃ naivāsya cukupe tataḥ
c sa tu krodhas tam āhedaṃ prāñjalir mūrtimān sthitaḥ
d jite tasmin bhṛguśreṣṭham abhyabhāṣad amarṣaṇaḥ
a jito 'smīti bhṛguśreṣṭha bhṛgavo hy atiroṣaṇāḥ
c loke mithyāpravādo 'yaṃ yat tvayāsmi parājitaḥ
a so 'haṃ tvayi sthito hy adya kṣamāvati mahātmani
c bibhemi tapasaḥ sādho prasādaṃ kuru me vibho
 janamejaya uvāca
a sākṣād dṛṣṭo 'si me krodha gaccha tvaṃ vigatajvaraḥ
c na mamāpakṛtaṃ te 'dya na manyur vidyate mama
a yān uddiśya tu saṃkalpaḥ payaso 'sya kṛto mayā
c pitaras te mahābhāgās tebhyo budhyasva gamyatām
a ity ukto jātasaṃtrāsaḥ sa tatrāntaradhīyata
c pitṝṇām abhiṣaṅgāt tu nakulatvam upāgataḥ
a sa tān prasādayām āsa śāpasyānto bhaved iti
b tenāpy ukto mahārāja dharmarājasya vai tadā
b aśvamedhe tadāgantā śāpān mukto bhaviṣyati
c taiś cāpy ukto yadā dharmaṃ kṣepsyase mokṣyase tadā
a taiś cokto yajñiyān deśān dharmāraṇyāni caiva ha
c jugupsan paridhāvan sa yajñaṃ taṃ samupāsadat
a dharmaputram athākṣipya saktuprasthena tena saḥ
c muktaḥ śāpāt tataḥ krodho dharmo hy āsīd yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a evam etat tadā vṛttaṃ tasya yajñe mahātmanaḥ
c paśyatāṃ cāpi nas tatra nakulo 'ntarhitas tadā
d sa cāpi bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ
d yajñiyo yajñanāthaś ca puṇḍarīko janārdanaḥ
d vāsudevo harir viṣṇur ananto bhaktavatsalaḥ
d ā samāpter jagannātho yajñaṃ rakṣitavān hariḥ
d rakṣitvā sa mahābāhur jagāma dvārakāṃ purīm
d etat puṇyaṃ mahārāja śṛṇvatāṃ bhuktimuktidam
d śrotā ca śrāvako yaś ca sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
d janamejayaḥ
d aśvamedhe purā vṛtte keśavaṃ keśisūdanam
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d dharmasaṃśayam uddiśya kim apṛcchat pitāmahaḥ
d paścimenāśvamedhena yadā snāto yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d tadā rājan namaskṛtya keśavaṃ punar abravīt
d bhagavan vaiṣṇavā dharmāḥ kiṃphalāḥ kiṃparāyaṇāḥ
d kiṃ dharmam adhikṛtyātha bhavatotpāditāḥ purā
d yadi te 'ham anugrāhyaḥ priyo 'smi madhusūdana
d śrotavyā yadi me kṛṣṇa tan me kathaya suvrata
d pavitrāḥ kila te dharmāḥ sarvapāpapraṇāśanāḥ
d sarvadharmottamāḥ puṇyā bhagavaṃs tvanmukhodgatāḥ
d yāñ śrutvā brahmahā goghno mātṛhā gurutalpagaḥ
d pākabhedī kṛtaghnaś ca surāpo brahmavikrayī
d mitraviśvāsaghātī ca vīrahā bhrūṇahā tathā
d tapovikrayiṇaś caiva dānavikrayiṇas tathā
d ātmavikrayiṇo mūḍhā jīved yaś ca vikarmabhiḥ
d pāpāḥ śaṭhā naikṛtikā ḍāmbhikā dūṣakās tathā
d rasabhedakarā ye ca ye ca syur brahmaghātakāḥ
d śūdrapreṣyakarāś corā viprā ye ca purohitāḥ
d nikṣepahāriṇaḥ strīghnās tathā ye pāradārikāḥ
d ete cānye ca pāpās te mucyante te 'pi kilbiṣāt
d tān ācakṣva suraśreṣṭha tvadbhaktasya mamācyuta
d ity evaṃ kathite deve dharmaputreṇa saṃsadi
d vasiṣṭhādyās tapoyuktā munayas tattvadarśinaḥ
d śrotukāmāḥ paraṃ guhyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ dharmam uttamam
d yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d tathā bhāgavatāś caiva tatas taṃ paryavārayan
d tattvatas tu bhavān eva pādamūlam upāgatam
d yadi jānāsi māṃ bhaktaṃ snigdhaṃ vā bhaktavatsala
d dharmaguhyāni sarvāṇi vettum icchāmi tattvataḥ
d dharmān kathaya deveśa yady anugrahabhāg aham
d śrutā me mānavā dharmā vāsiṣṭhāḥ kāśyapās tathā
d gārgīyā gautamīyāś ca tathā gopālakasya ca
d parāśarakṛtāḥ pūrvaṃ maitreyasya ca dhīmataḥ
d aumā māheśvarāś caiva nandidharmāś ca pāvanāḥ
d brahmaṇā kathitā ye ca kaumārāś ca śrutā mayā
d dhūmrāyaṇakṛtā dharmāḥ kāṇḍavaiśvānarā api
d bhārgavyā yājñavalkyāś ca mārkaṇḍeyakṛtās tathā
d bhāradvājakṛtā ye ca bṛhaspatikṛtāś ca ye
d kuṇeś ca kuṇibāhoś ca viśvāmitrakṛtāś ca ye
d sumantujaiminikṛtāḥ śākuneyās tathaiva ca
d pulastyapulahodgītāḥ pāvakīyās tathaiva ca
d agastyagītā maudgalyāḥ śāṇḍilyāś caiva pāvanāḥ
d vālakhilyakṛtā ye ca ye ca saptarṣibhiḥ kṛtāḥ
d āpastambakṛtā dharmāḥ śaṅkhasya likhitasya ca
d prājāpatyās tathā yāmyā māhendrāś ca śrutā mayā
d vaiyyāghrā vyāsagītāś ca vibhāṇḍakakṛtāś ca ye
d nāradīyāḥ śrutā dharmāḥ kāpotāś ca śrutā mayā
d tathā viduravākyāni bhṛgor aṅgirasas tathā
d krauñcā mṛdaṅgagītāś ca sauryā hārītakāś ca ye
d ye piśaṅgakṛtāś cāpi kautupā haṃsapālakāḥ
d uddālakakṛtā dharmā auśanasyās tathaiva ca
d vaiśaṃpāyanagītāś ca ye cānye 'py evamādayaḥ
d etebhyaḥ sarvadharmebhyo deva tvanmukhaniḥsṛtāḥ
d pāvanatvāt pavitratvād viśiṣṭā iti me matiḥ
d tasmād dhi tvāṃ prapannasya tvadbhaktasya ca bhāvataḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d yuṣmadīyān varān dharmān puṇyān kathaya me 'cyuta
d evaṃ pṛṣṭas tu dharmajño dharmaputreṇa keśavaḥ
d uvāca dharmān sūkṣmārthān dharmaputrasya harṣitaḥ
d evaṃ te yasya kaunteya yatno dharmeṣu suvrata
d tvatsamo durlabho loke na kaś cid iha vidyate
d dharmaḥ śruto vā dṛṣṭo vā kathito vā kṛto 'pi vā
d anumodito vā rājendra punātīha naraṃ sadā
d dharmaḥ pitā ca mātā ca dharmo nāthaḥ suhṛt tathā
d dharmo bhrātā sakhā caiva dharmaḥ svāmī paraṃtapa
d dharmād arthaś ca kāmaś ca dharmād bhogāḥ sukhāni ca
d dharmād aiśvaryam evāgryaṃ dharmāt svargagatiḥ parā
d dharmo yaḥ sevitaḥ śuddhas trāyate mahato bhayāt
d dharmād dvijatvaṃ devatvaṃ dharmaḥ prāpayate naram
d yadā ca kṣīyate pāpaṃ kālena puruṣasya tu
d tadā saṃjāyate buddhir dharmaṃ kartuṃ yudhiṣṭhira
d janmāntarasahasrais tu manuṣyatvaṃ hi durlabham
d tad gatvāpīha yo dharmaṃ na karoti sa vañcitaḥ
d kutsitā ye daridrāś ca virūpā vyādhitās tathā
d parapreṣyāś ca mūrkhāś ca na tair dharmaḥ kṛtaḥ purā
d ye ca dīrghāyuṣaḥ śūrāḥ paṇḍitā bhoginas tathā
d nīrogā rūpasaṃpannās tair dharmaḥ sukṛtaḥ purā
d evaṃ dharmaḥ kṛtaḥ śuddho nayate gatim uttamām
d adharmaṃ sevamānas tu tiryag yonyāṃ pataty asau
d idaṃ rahasyaṃ kaunteya śṛṇu dharmam anuttamam
d kathayiṣye paraṃ dharmaṃ mama bhaktasya pāṇḍava
d iṣṭas tvam asi me 'tyarthaṃ prapannaś cāpi māṃ sadā
d paramārtham api brūmaḥ kiṃ punar dharmasaṃhitām
d idaṃ me mānuṣaṃ janma kṛtam ātmani māyayā
d dharmasaṃsthāpanārthāya duṣṭānāṃ śāsanāya ca
d mānuṣyaṃ bhāvam āpannaṃ ye māṃ gṛhṇanty avajñayā
d saṃsarantīha te mūḍhās tiryag yoniṣv anekaśaḥ
d ye ca māṃ sarvabhūtasthaṃ paśyanti jñānacakṣuṣā
d madbhaktāṃs tān sadā yuktān matsamīpaṃ nayāmy aham
d madbhaktā na vinaśyanti madbhaktā vītakalmaṣāḥ
d madbhaktānāṃ tu mānuṣye saphalaṃ janma pāṇḍava
d api pāpeṣv abhiratā madbhaktāḥ pāṇḍunandana
d mucyante pāpakaiḥ sarvaiḥ padmapatram ivāmbhasā
d janmāntarasahasreṣu tapasā bhāvitātmanām
d bhaktir utpadyate tāta manuṣyāṇāṃ na saṃśayaḥ
d yac ca rūpaṃ paraṃ guhyaṃ kūṭastham acalaṃ dhruvam
d na dṛśyate tathā devair madbhaktair dṛśyate yathā
d aparaṃ yac ca me rūpaṃ prādurbhāveṣu dṛśyate
d tad arcayanti sarvārthaiḥ sarvabhūtāni pāṇḍava
d kalpakoṭisahasreṣu vyatīteṣv āgateṣu ca
d darśayāmīha tad rūpaṃ tat prapaśyanti me surāḥ
d sthityutpattivyayakaraṃ yo māṃ jñātvā prapadyate
d anugṛhṇāmy ahaṃ taṃ vai saṃsārān mocayāmi ca
d aham ādir hi devānāṃ sṛṣṭā brahmādayo mayā
d prakṛtiṃ svām avaṣṭabhya jagat sarvaṃ sṛjāmy aham
d tamomūlo 'ham avyakto rajo madhye pratiṣṭhitaḥ
d ūrdhvaṃ sattvaviśālo 'haṃ brahmādistambasaṃjñitaḥ
d mūrdhānaṃ me divaṃ viddhi candrādityau ca locane
d devāgnir brāhmaṇā vaktraṃ mārutaḥ śvasanaś ca me
d diśo me bāhavaś cāṣṭau nakṣatrāṇi ca bhūṣaṇam
d antarikṣam uro viddhi sarvabhūtāvakāśakam
d mārgo meghānilābhyāṃ tu yan mamodaram avyayam
d pṛthivīmaṇḍalaṃ yad vai dvīpārṇavanagair yutam
d sarvasaṃdhāraṇopetaṃ pādau mama yudhiṣṭhira
d sthito hy ekaguṇaḥ khe 'haṃ dviguṇaś cāsmi mārute
d triguṇo 'gnau sthito 'haṃ vai salile tu caturguṇaḥ
d śabdādyā ye guṇāḥ pañca mahābhūteṣu pañcasu
d tanmātrasaṃsthitaḥ so 'haṃ pṛthivyāṃ pañcadhā sthitaḥ
d ahaṃ sahasraśīrṣas tu sahasravadanekṣaṇaḥ
d sahasrabāhūdaradṛk sahasroruḥ sahasrapāt
d dhṛtvorvīṃ sarvataḥ samyag atyatiṣṭhad daśāṅgulam
d sarvabhūtātmabhūtasthaḥ sarvavyāpī tato hy aham
d acintyo 'ham ananto 'ham ajaro 'ham ajo hy aham
d anadyo 'ham avadhyo 'ham aprameyo 'ham avyayaḥ
d nirguṇo 'ham agūḍhātmā nirdvandvo nirmamo nṛpa
d niṣkalo nirvikāro 'haṃ nidānam amṛtasya tu
d sudhā cāhaṃ svadhā cāhaṃ svāhā cāhaṃ narādhipa
d tejasā tapasā cāhaṃ bhūtagrāmaṃ caturvidham
d snehapāśaguṇair baddhvā dhārayāmy ātmamāyayā
d caturāśramadharmo 'haṃ cāturhotraphalāśanaḥ
d caturmūrtiś caturvyūhaś caturāśramabhāvanaḥ
d saṃhṛtyāhaṃ jagat sarvaṃ kṛtvā vai garbham ātmanaḥ
d śayāmi divyayogena pralayeṣu yudhiṣṭhira
d sahasrayugaparyantāṃ brāhmīṃ rātriṃ mahārṇave
d sthitvā sṛjāmi bhūtāni jaṅgamāni sthirāṇi ca
d kalpe kalpe ca bhūtāni saṃharāmi sṛjāmi ca
d na ca māṃ tāni jānanti māyayā mohitāni me
d mama caivāndhakārasya mārgitavyasya nityaśaḥ
d praśāntasyeva dīpasya gatir naivopalabhyate
d na tad asti kva cid rājan yatrāhaṃ na pratiṣṭhitaḥ
d na ca tad vidyate bhūtaṃ mayi yan na pratiṣṭhitam
d yāvanmātraṃ bhaved bhūtaṃ sthūlaṃ sūkṣmam idaṃ jagat
d jīvabhūto hy ahaṃ tasmiṃs tāvanmātraṃ pratiṣṭhitam
d kiṃ cātra bahunoktena satyam eva bravīmi te
d yad bhūtaṃ yad bhaviṣyac ca tat sarvam aham eva tu
d mayā sṛṣṭāni bhūtāni manmayāni ca bhārata
d mām eva na vijānanti māyayā mohitāni me
d evaṃ sarvaṃ jagad idaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam
d mattaḥ prabhavate rājan mayy eva pravilīyate
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d evam ātmodbhavaṃ sarvaṃ jagad uddiśya keśavaḥ
d bhagavān uvāca
d dharmān dharmātmajasyātha puṇyān akathayat prabhuḥ
d śṛṇu pāṇḍava tattvena pavitraṃ pāpanāśanam
d kathyamānaṃ mayā puṇyaṃ dharmaśāstraphalaṃ mahat
d yaḥ śṛṇoti śucir bhūtvā ekacittas tapoyutaḥ
d svargyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ dharmyaṃ jñeyaṃ yudhiṣṭhira
d śraddadhānasya tasyeha yat pāpaṃ pūrvasaṃcitam
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d vinaśyaty āśu tat sarvaṃ madbhaktasya viśeṣataḥ
d evaṃ śrutvā vacaḥ puṇyaṃ satyaṃ keśavabhāṣitam
d prahṛṣṭamanaso bhūtvā cintayanto 'dbhutaṃ param
d devā brahmarṣayaḥ sarve gandharvāpsarasas tathā
d bhūtā yakṣagrahāś caiva guhyakā bhujagās tathā
d vālakhilyā mahātmāno yoginas tattvadarśinaḥ
d tathā bhāgavatāś cāpi pañcakālam upāsakāḥ
d kautūhalasamāyuktāḥ prahṛṣṭendriyamānasāḥ
d śrotukāmāḥ paraṃ dharmaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ dharmaśāsanāt
d hṛdi kartuṃ ca tad vākyaṃ praṇemuḥ śirasā natāḥ
d tatas te vāsudevena dṛṣṭāḥ saumyena cakṣuṣā
d vimuktapāpān ālokya praṇamya śirasā harim
d papraccha keśavaṃ dharmaṃ dharmaputraḥ pratāpavān
d kīdṛśī brāhmaṇasyātha kṣatriyasyāpi kīdṛśī
d vaiśyasya kīdṛśī deva gatiḥ śūdrasya kīdṛśī
d kathaṃ badhyeta pāśena brāhmaṇas tu yamālaye
d kṣatriyo vātha vaiśyo vā śūdro vā badhyate katham
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d etat karmaphalaṃ brūhi lokanātha namo 'stu te
d pṛṣṭo 'tha keśavo hy evaṃ dharmaputreṇa dhīmatā
d uvāca saṃsāragatiṃ cāturvarṇyasya karmajām
d bhagavān uvāca
d śṛṇu varṇakrameṇaiva dharmaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ vara
d nāsti kiṃ cin naraśreṣṭha duṣkṛtaṃ brāhmaṇasya tu
d ye sthitāḥ syuḥ sadādhyātme saṃdhyāṃ ye cāpy upāsate
d yaiś ca pūrṇāhutiḥ prāptā vidhivaj juhvate ca ye
d vaiśvadevaṃ ca ye kuryuḥ pūjayanty atithīṃś ca ye
d nityaṃ svādhyāyaśīlāś ca japayajñaparāś ca ye
d sāyaṃprātar hutāśāś ca śūdrabhojanavarjitāḥ
d ḍambhānṛtavimuktāś ca svadāraniratāś ca ye
d pañcayajñaratā ye ca ye 'gnihotram upāsate
d dahanti duṣkṛtaṃ yeṣāṃ hūyamānāgnayas trayaḥ
d naṣṭaduṣkṛtakarmāṇo brahmalokaṃ vrajanti te
d brahmaloke punaḥ kāmaṃ gandharvair brahmagāyakaiḥ
d udgīyamānāḥ prayataiḥ pūjyamānāḥ svayaṃbhuvā
d brahmaloke pramodante yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam
d kṣatriyo 'pi sthito rājye svadharmaparipālakaḥ
d samyak prajāḥ pālayitā ṣaḍbhāganirataḥ sadā
d yajñadānarato dhīraḥ svadāranirataḥ sadā
d śāstrānusārī tattvajñaḥ prajākāryaparāyaṇaḥ
d viprebhyaḥ kāmado nityaṃ bhṛtyānāṃ bharaṇe rataḥ
d satyasaṃdhaḥ śucir nityaṃ lobhaḍambhavivarjitaḥ
d kṣatriyo 'py uttamāṃ yāti gatiṃ devaniṣevitām
d tatra divyāpsarobhis tu gandharvaiś ca viśeṣataḥ
d sevyamāno mahātejāḥ krīḍate śakrapūjitaḥ
d caturyugāni vai triṃśat krīḍitvā tatra devavat
d iha mānuṣaloke tu caturvedī dvijo bhavet
d kṛṣigopālanirato dharmānveṣaṇatatparaḥ
d dānadharme 'pi nirato vipraśuśrūṣakas tathā
d satyasaṃdhaḥ śucir nityaṃ lobhaḍambhavivarjitaḥ
d ṛjuḥ svadāranirato hiṃsādrohavivarjitaḥ
d vaṇigdharmān namuñcan vai devabrāhmaṇapūjakaḥ
d vaiśyaḥ svargatim āpnoti pūjyamāno 'psarogaṇaiḥ
d caturyugāni vai triṃśat krīḍitvā daśa pañca ca
d iha mānuṣyaloke ca rājā bhavati vīryavān
d suvarṇakoṭyaḥ pañcāśad ratnānāṃ ca śataṃ tathā
d hastyaśvarathasaṃyuktān mahābhogāṃś ca sevate
d trayāṇām api varṇānāṃ śuśrūṣānirataḥ sadā
d viśeṣatas tu viprāṇāṃ dāsavad yas tu tiṣṭhati
d ayācitapradātā ca satyaśaucasamanvitaḥ
d gurudevārcanarataḥ paradāravivarjitaḥ
d parapīḍām akṛtvaiva bhṛtyavargaṃ bibharti yaḥ
d śūdro 'pi svargam āpnoti jīvānām abhayapradaḥ
d sa svargaloke krīḍitvā varṣakoṭiṃ mahātapāḥ
d iha mānuṣaloke tu vaiśyo dhanapatir bhavet
d evaṃ dharmāt paraṃ nāsti mahat saṃsāramokṣaṇam
d na ca dharmāt paraṃ kiṃ cit pāpakarmavyapohanam
d tasmād dharmaḥ sadā kāryo mānuṣyaṃ prāpya durlabham
d na hi dharmānuraktānāṃ loke kiṃ cin na durlabham
d svayaṃbhuvihito dharmo yo yasyeha nareśvara
d sa tena kṣapayet pāpaṃ samyag ācaritena ca
d sahajaṃ yad bhavet karma na tat tyājyaṃ hi kena cit
d sa eva tasya dharmo hi tena siddhiṃ sa gacchati
d viguṇo 'pi svadharmas tu pāpakarma vyapohati
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d evam eva tu dharmo 'pi kṣīyate pāpavardhanāt
d bhagavan devadeveśa śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me
d bhagavān uvāca
d śubhasyāpy aśubhasyāpi kṣayavṛddhī yathākramam
d śṛṇu pārthiva tat sarvaṃ dharmaṃ sūkṣmaṃ sanātanam
d durvijñeyatamaṃ nityam atra bhagnā mahājanāḥ
d yathaiva śītam udakam uṣṇena bahunāvṛtam
d bhavet tu tatkṣaṇād uṣṇaṃ śītatvaṃ ca vinaśyati
d yathoṣṇaṃ vā bhaved alpaṃ śītena bahunāvṛtam
d śītalaṃ tad bhavet sarvam uṣṇatvaṃ ca vinaśyati
d evaṃ tu yad bhaved bhūri sukṛtaṃ vātha duṣkṛtam
d tad alpaṃ kṣapayec chīghraṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
d samatve sati rājendra tayoḥ sukṛtapāpayoḥ
d gūhitasya bhaved vṛddhiḥ kīrtitasya bhavet kṣayaḥ
d khyāpanenānutāpena prāyaḥ pāpaṃ vinaśyati
d tathā kṛtas tu rājendra dharmo naśyati mānada
d tāv ubhau gūhitau samyag vṛddhiṃ yātau na saṃśayaḥ
d tasmāt sarvaprayatnena na pāpaṃ gūhayed budhaḥ
d tasmād etat prayatnena kīrtayet kṣayakāraṇāt
d tasmāt saṃkīrtayet pāpaṃ satyaṃ dharmaṃ ca gūhayet
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d evaṃ śrutvā vacas tasya dharmaputro 'cyutasya tu
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d papraccha punar apy anyān dharmān dharmātmajo harim
d vṛthā ca kati janmāni vṛthā dānāni yāni ca
d vṛthā ca jīvitaṃ keṣāṃ narāṇāṃ puruṣottama
d kīdṛśāsu vyavasthāsu dānaṃ dattaṃ janārdana
d iha loke 'nubhavati puruṣaḥ puruṣottama
d garbhasthe kiṃ samaśnāti kiṃ bālye vāpi keśava
d yauvanasthe 'pi kiṃ kṛṣṇa vārdhake vāpi kiṃ bhavet
d sāttvikaṃ kīdṛśaṃ dānaṃ rājasaṃ kīdṛśaṃ bhavet
d tāmasaṃ kīdṛśaṃ deva tarpayiṣyati kiṃ prabho
d uttamaṃ kīdṛśaṃ dānaṃ madhyamaṃ kīdṛśaṃ bhavet
d adhamaṃ kīdṛśaṃ dānaṃ teṣāṃ vā vada kiṃ phalam
d kiṃ dānaṃ nayati hy ūrdhvaṃ kiṃ gatiṃ madhyamāṃ bhavet
d gatiṃ jaghanyām atha vā devadeva bravīhi me
d etad icchāmi vijñātuṃ paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me
d tvadīyaṃ vacanaṃ satyaṃ puṇyaṃ ca madhusūdana
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d evaṃ dharmaṃ prayatnena pṛṣṭaḥ pāṇḍusutena vai
d uvāca vāsudevo 'tha dharmān dharmātmajasya ca
d śṛṇu rājan yathānyāyaṃ vacanaṃ tathyam uttamam
d kathyamānaṃ mayā puṇyaṃ sarvapāpavyapohanam
d vṛthā ca daśa janmāni catvāri ca narādhipa
d vṛthā dānāni pañcāśat pañcaiva ca yathākramam
d vṛthā ca jīvitaṃ yeṣāṃ te ca ṣaṭ parikīrtitāḥ
d anukrameṇa sarvāṇi tāni vakṣyāmi pārthiva
d dharmaghnānāṃ vṛthā janma lubdhānāṃ pāpināṃ tathā
d vṛthā pākaṃ ca ye 'śnanti paradāraratāś ca ye
d pākabhedakarā ye ca ye ca syuḥ satyavarjitāḥ
d mṛṣṭam aśnāti yaś caiko dṛśyamānas tu bāndhavaiḥ
d pitaraṃ mātaraṃ caiva upādhyāyaṃ guruṃ tathā
d mātulaṃ mātulānīṃ ca yo nihanyāc chapeta vā
d brāhmaṇaś caiva yo bhūtvā saṃdhyopāsanavarjitaḥ
d nirbrahmo niḥsvadhaś caiva śūdrāṇām annabhug dvijaḥ
d mama vā śaṃkarasyāpi brahmaṇo vā yudhiṣṭhira
d atha vā brāhmaṇānāṃ tu ye na bhaktā narādhamāḥ
d vṛthā janmāny athaiteṣāṃ pāpināṃ viddhi pāṇḍava
d aśraddhayā ca yad dattam avamānena vāpi yat
d ḍambhārtham api yad dattaṃ yat pāṣaṇḍihṛtaṃ nṛpa
d śūdrācārāya yad dattaṃ yad dattvā cānukīrtitam
d roṣayuktaṃ tu yad dattaṃ yad dattam anuśocitam
d ḍambhārjitaṃ ca yad dattaṃ yac ca vāpy anṛtārjitam
d brāhmaṇasvaṃ ca yad dattaṃ cauryeṇāpy ārjitaṃ ca yat
d abhiśastāhṛtaṃ yat tu yad dattaṃ patite dvije
d nirbrahmābhihṛtaṃ yat tu yad dhṛtaṃ sarvayācakaiḥ
d vrātyais tu yad dhṛtaṃ dānam ārūḍhapatitaiś ca yat
d yad dattaṃ svairiṇībhartuḥ śvaśurān anuvartine
d yad grāmayācakahṛtaṃ yat kṛtaghnahṛtaṃ tathā
d upapātakine dattaṃ vedavikrayiṇe ca yat
d strījitāya ca yad dattaṃ vyālagrāhihṛtaṃ ca yat
d purohitāya yad dattaṃ cikitsakahṛtaṃ ca yat
d yad vaṇikkarmiṇe dattaṃ kṣudramantropajīvine
d yac chūdrajīvine dattaṃ yac ca devalakāya ca
d devadravyāśine yac ca yad dattaṃ citrakarmiṇe
d raṅgopajīvine dattaṃ yac ca māṃsopajīvine
d sevakāya ca yad dattaṃ yad dattaṃ brāhmaṇabruve
d agnihīne ca yad dattaṃ dattaṃ vārdhuṣikāya ca
d yad anācāriṇe dattaṃ yat tu dattam anagnaye
d asaṃdhyopāsine dattaṃ yac chūdragrāmavāsine
d yan mithyāliṅgine dattaṃ dattaṃ sarvāśine ca yat
d nāstikāya ca yad dattaṃ dharmavikrayiṇe ca yat
d cārakāya ca yad dattaṃ yad dattaṃ kūṭasākṣiṇe
d grāmakūṭāya yad dattaṃ dānaṃ pārthivapuṃgava
d vṛthā bhavati tat sarvaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
d vipranāmadharā hy ete lolupā brāhmaṇādhamāḥ
d nātmānaṃ tārayanty ete na dātāraṃ yudhiṣṭhira
d etebhyo dattamātrāṇi dānāni ca bahūny api
d vṛthā bhavanti rājendra bhasmany ājyāhutir yathā
d eteṣu yat phalaṃ kiṃ cid bhaviṣyati kathaṃ cana
d rākṣasāś ca piśācāś ca tad vilumpanti harṣitāḥ
d vṛthā hy etāni dattāni kathitāni samāsataḥ
d jīvitaṃ tu vṛthā yeṣāṃ tac chṛṇuṣva yudhiṣṭhira
d ye māṃ na pratipadyante śaṃkaraṃ vā narādhamāḥ
d brāhmaṇān vā mahīdevān vṛthā jīvanti te narāḥ
d hetuśāstreṣu ye saktāḥ kudṛṣṭipatham āśritāḥ
d vedān nindanty anācārā vṛthā jīvanti te narāḥ
d kuśalaiḥ kṛtaśāstrāṇi paṭhitvā ye narādhamāḥ
d viprān nindanti yajñāṃś ca vṛthā jīvanti te narāḥ
d ye ca durgāṃ kumāraṃ vā vāyum agniṃ jalaṃ ravim
d pitaraṃ mātaraṃ caiva gurum indraṃ niśākaram
d mūḍhā nindanty anācārā vṛthā jīvanti te narāḥ
d vidyamāne dhane yas tu dānadharmavivarjitaḥ
d mṛṣṭam aśnāti yaś caiko vṛthā jīvati so 'pi ca
d vṛthā jīvitam ākhyātaṃ dānakālaṃ bravīmi te
d tamoniviṣṭacittena dattaṃ dānaṃ tu yad bhavet
d sa tasya phalam aśnāti naro garbhagato nṛpa
d īrṣyāmātsaryasaṃyukto ḍambhārthaṃ cārthakāraṇāt
d dadāti dānaṃ yo martyo bālabhāve tad aśnute
d bhoktuṃ bhogaṃ na śaktas tu vyādhibhiḥ pīḍito bhṛśam
d dadāti dānaṃ yo martyo vṛddhabhāve tad aśnute
d śraddhāyuktaḥ śuciḥ snātaḥ prasannendriyamānasaḥ
d dadāti dānaṃ yo martyo yauvane sa tad aśnute
d svayaṃ nītvā tu yad dānaṃ bhaktyā pātre pradīyate
d tat sārvakālikaṃ viddhi dānam āmaraṇāntikam
d sāttvikaṃ rājasaṃ caiva tāmasaṃ ca yudhiṣṭhira
d dānaṃ dānaphalaṃ caiva gatiṃ ca trividhāṃ śṛṇu
d dānaṃ dātavyam ity eva matiṃ kṛtvā dvijāya vai
d upakāraviyuktāya yad dattaṃ tad dhi sāttvikam
d śrotriyāya daridrāya bahubhṛtyāya pāṇḍava
d dīyate yat prahṛṣṭena tat sāttvikam udāhṛtam
d vedākṣaravihīnāya yat tu pūrvopakāriṇe
d samṛddhāya ca yad dattaṃ tad dānaṃ rājasaṃ smṛtam
d saṃbandhine ca yad dattaṃ pramattāya ca pāṇḍava
d phalārthibhir apātrāya tad dānaṃ rājasaṃ smṛtam
d vaiśvadevavihīnāya dānam aśrotriyāya ca
d dīyate taskarāyāpi tad dānaṃ tāmasaṃ smṛtam
d saroṣam avadhūtaṃ ca kleśayuktam avajñayā
d sevakāya ca yad dattaṃ tat tāmasam udāhṛtam
d devāḥ pitṛgaṇāś caiva munayaś cāgnayas tathā
d sāttvikaṃ dānam aśnanti tuṣyanti ca nareśvara
d dānavā daityasaṃghāś ca grahā yakṣāḥ sarākṣasāḥ
d rājasaṃ dānam aśnanti varjitaṃ pitṛdaivataiḥ
d piśācāḥ pretasaṃghāś ca kaśmalā ye malīmasāḥ
d tāmasaṃ dānam aśnanti gatiṃ ca trividhāṃ śṛṇu
d sāttvikānāṃ tu dānānām uttamaṃ phalam ucyate
d madhyamaṃ rājasānāṃ tu tāmasānāṃ tu paścimam
d abhigamyopanītānāṃ dānānām uttamaṃ phalam
d madhyamaṃ tu samāhūya jaghanyaṃ yācate phalam
d ayācitapradātā yaḥ sa yāti gatim uttamām
d samāhūya tu yo dadyān madhyamāṃ sa gatiṃ vrajet
d yācito yaś ca vai dadyāj jaghanyāṃ sa gatiṃ vrajet
d uttamā daivikā jñeyā madhyamā mānuṣī gatiḥ
d gatiṃ jaghanyāṃ tiryakṣu gatir eṣā tridhā smṛtā
d pātrabhūteṣu vipreṣu susthiteṣv āhitāgniṣu
d yat tu nikṣipyate dānam akṣayyaṃ saṃprakīrtitam
d śrotriyāṇāṃ daridrāṇāṃ bharaṇaṃ kuru pārthiva
d samṛddhānāṃ dvijātīnāṃ kuryāt teṣāṃ ca rakṣaṇam
d daridrān vṛttihīnāṃś ca pradānaiḥ suṣṭhu pūjaya
d āturasyauṣadhaiḥ kāryaṃ nīrujasya kim auṣadhaiḥ
d pāpaṃ pratigrahītāraṃ pradātur upagacchati
d pratigrahītur yat puṇyaṃ pradātāram upaiti tat
d tasmād dānaṃ sadā kāryaṃ paratra hitam icchatā
d vedavidyāvadāteṣu sadā śūdrānnavarjiṣu
d prayatnena vidhātavyo mahādānamayo nidhiḥ
d yeṣāṃ dārāḥ pratīkṣante sahasrasyeva lambhanam
d bhuktaśeṣasya bhaktasya tān nimantraya pāṇḍava
d āmantrya tu nirāśāni na kartavyāni bhārata
d kulāni sudaridrāṇāṃ teṣām āśā hatā bhavet
d madbhaktā ye naraśreṣṭha madgatā matparāyaṇāḥ
d madyājino manniyamās tān prayatnena pūjayet
d teṣāṃ tu pāvanāyāhaṃ nityam eva yudhiṣṭhira
d ubhe saṃdhye 'pi tiṣṭhāmi hy askannaṃ tad vrataṃ mama
d tasmād aṣṭākṣaraṃ mantraṃ madbhaktair vītakalmaṣaiḥ
d saṃdhyākāleṣu japtavyaṃ satataṃ cātmaśuddhaye
d anyeṣām api viprāṇāṃ kilbiṣaṃ hi praṇaśyati
d ubhe saṃdhye 'py upāsīta tasmād vipro viśuddhaye
d daive śrāddhe ca vipraḥ sa niyoktavyo 'jugupsayā
d jugupsitas tu yaḥ śrāddhaṃ dahaty agnir ivendhanam
d bhārataṃ mānavo dharmo vedāḥ sāṅgāś cikitsitam
d ājñāsiddhāni catvāri na hantavyāni hetubhiḥ
d na brāhmaṇān parīkṣeta daive karmaṇi dharmavit
d mahān bhavet parīvādo brāhmaṇānāṃ parīkṣaṇe
d brāhmaṇānāṃ parīvādaṃ yaḥ kuryāt puruṣādhamaḥ
d rāsabhānāṃ śunāṃ yoniṃ gacchet puruṣadūṣakaḥ
d śvatvaṃ prāpnoti ninditvā parīvādāt kharo bhavet
d kṛmir bhavaty abhibhavāt kīṭo bhavati matsarī
d durvṛttā vā suvṛttā vā prākṛtā vā susaṃskṛtāḥ
d brāhmaṇā nāvamantavyā bhasmacchannā ivāgnayaḥ
d kṣatriyaṃ caiva sarpaṃ ca brāhmaṇaṃ ca bahuśrutam
d nāvamanyeta medhāvī kṛśān api kadā cana
d etat trayaṃ hi puruṣaṃ nirdahed avamānitam
d tasmād etat prayatnena nāvamanyeta buddhimān
d yathā sarvāsv avasthāsu pāvako daivataṃ mahat
d tathā sarvāsv avasthāsu brāhmaṇo daivataṃ mahat
d vyaṅgāḥ kāṇāś ca kubjāś ca vāmanāṅgās tathaiva ca
d sarve daive niyoktavyā vyāmiśrā vedapāragaiḥ
d manyuṃ notpādayet teṣāṃ na cāriṣṭān samācaret
d manyupraharaṇā viprā na viprāḥ śastrapāṇayaḥ
d manyunā ghnanti te śatrūn vajreṇendra ivāsurān
d brāhmaṇo hi mahad daivaṃ jātimātreṇa jāyate
d īśvaraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ dharmakośasya guptaye
d kiṃ punar ye ca kaunteya saṃdhyāṃ nityam upāsate
d yasyāsyena samaśnanti havyāni tridivaukasaḥ
d kavyāni caiva pitaraḥ kiṃ bhūtam adhikaṃ tathā
d utpattir eva viprasya mūrtir dharmasya śāśvatī
d sa hi dharmārtham utpanno brahmabhūyāya kalpate
d svam eva brāhmaṇo bhuṅkte svaṃ vaste svaṃ dadāti ca
d ānṛśaṃsyād brāhmaṇasya bhuñjate hītare janāḥ
d tasmāt te nāvamantavyā madbhaktā hi dvijāḥ sadā
d āraṇyakopaniṣadi ye tu paśyanti māṃ dvijāḥ
d nigūḍhaṃ niṣkalāvasthaṃ tān prayatnena pūjaya
d svagṛhe vā pravāse vā divārātram athāpi vā
d śraddhayā brāhmaṇāḥ pūjyā madbhaktā ye ca pāṇḍava
d nāsti viprasamaṃ daivaṃ nāsti viprasamo guruḥ
d nāsti viprāt paro bandhur nāsti viprāt paro nidhiḥ
d nāsti viprāt paraṃ tīrthaṃ na puṇyaṃ brāhmaṇāt param
d na pavitraṃ paraṃ viprān na dvijāt pāvanaṃ param
d nāsti viprāt paro dharmo nāsti viprāt parā gatiḥ
d pāpakarmasamākṣiptaṃ patantaṃ narake naram
d trāyate dānam apy ekaṃ pātrabhūte kṛtaṃ dvije
d bālāhitāgnayo ye ca śāntāḥ śūdrānnavarjitāḥ
d mām arcayanti madbhaktās tebhyo dattam ihākṣayam
d pradānaiḥ pūjito vipro vandito vāpi saṃstutaḥ
d saṃbhāṣito vā dṛṣṭo vā madbhakto divam unnayet
d ye paṭhanti namasyanti dhyāyanti puruṣottamam
d tān spṛṣṭvā vātha vā dṛṣṭvā naraḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyate
d madbhaktā madgataprāṇā madgatā matparāyaṇāḥ
d bījayoniviśuddhā ye śrotriyāḥ saṃyatendriyāḥ
d śūdrānnaviratā nityaṃ te punantīha darśanāt
d svayaṃ nītvā viśeṣeṇa dānaṃ teṣāṃ gṛheṣv atha
d nivāpayet tu yad bhaktyā tad dānaṃ koṭisaṃmitam
d jāgrataḥ svapato vāpi pravāseṣu gṛheṣv atha
d hṛdaye na praṇaśyāmi yasya viprasya bhāvataḥ
d saṃpūjito vā dṛṣṭo vā spṛṣṭo vāpi dvijottamaḥ
d saṃbhāṣito vā rājendra punāty eva naraṃ sadā
d evaṃ sarvāsv avasthāsu sarvadānāni pāṇḍava
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d madbhaktebhyaḥ pradattāni svargamārgapradāni vai
d śrutvaiva sāttvikaṃ dānaṃ rājasaṃ tāmasaṃ tathā
d pṛthak pṛthak tv eva gatiṃ phalaṃ cāpi pṛthak pṛthak
d avitṛptaḥ prahṛṣṭātmā puṇyaṃ dharmāmṛtaṃ punaḥ
d yudhiṣṭhiro dharmarataḥ keśavaṃ punar abravīt
d bījayoniviśuddhānāṃ lakṣaṇāni vadasva me
d bījadoṣeṇa lokeśa jāyante ca kathaṃ narāḥ
d ācāradoṣaṃ deveśa vaktum arhasy aśeṣataḥ
d brāhmaṇānāṃ viśeṣaṃ ca guṇadoṣau ca keśava
d cāturvarṇasya kṛtsnasya vartamānāḥ pratigrahe
d kena viprā viśeṣeṇa tarante tārayanti ca
d bhagavān uvāca
d etān kathaya deveśa tvadbhaktasya namo 'stu te
d śṛṇu rājan yathāvṛttaṃ bījayoniśubhāśubham
d yena tiṣṭhati loko 'yaṃ vinaśyati ca pāṇḍava
d aviplutabrahmacaryo yas tu vipro yathāvidhi
d subījaṃ nāma vijñeyaṃ tasya bījaṃ śubhaṃ bhavet
d kanyā cākṣatayoniḥ syāt kulīnā pitṛmātṛtaḥ
d brāhmādiṣu vivāheṣu pariṇītā yathāvidhi
d sā praśastā varārohā tasyā yoniḥ praśasyate
d manasā karmaṇā vācā yā bhavet svairacāriṇī
d sā kulaghnīti vijñeyā tasyāṃ jātaḥ śvapācakaḥ
d daive pitrye tathā dāne bhojane sahabhāṣaṇe
d śayane sahasaṃbandhe na yogyā duṣṭayonijāḥ
d na tasmād duṣṭayonyāṃ tu garbham utpādayed budhaḥ
d mohena kurute yas tu kulaṃ hanti tripūruṣam
d kānīnaś ca sahoḍhaś ca tathobhau kuṇḍagolakau
d ārūḍhapatitāj jātaḥ patitasyāpi yaḥ sutaḥ
d ṣaḍ ete viśvacaṇḍālā nikṛṣṭāḥ śvapacād api
d yo yatra tatra vā retaḥ siktvā śūdrāsu vā caret
d kāmacārī sa pāpātmā bījaṃ tasyāśubhaṃ bhavet
d aśubhaṃ tad bhaved bījaṃ śuddhāṃ yoniṃ na cārhati
d dūṣayaty api tāṃ yoniṃ śunā līḍhaṃ havir yathā
d śūdrayonau pated bījaṃ hāhāśabdaṃ dvijanmanaḥ
d kuryāt purīṣagarteṣu patito 'smīti duḥkhitaḥ
d mām adhaḥ pātayaty eṣa pāpātmā kāmamohitaḥ
d adhogatiṃ vrajet kṣipram iti śaptvā patet tu tat
d ātmā hi śuklam uddiṣṭaṃ daivataṃ paramaṃ mahat
d tasmāt sarvaprayatnena nirundhyāc chuklam ātmanaḥ
d āyus tejo balaṃ vīryaṃ prajñā śrīś ca mahad yaśaḥ
d puṇyaṃ ca matpriyatvaṃ ca labhate brahmacaryayā
d aviplutabrahmacaryair gṛhasthāśramam āśritaiḥ
d pañcayajñaparair dharmaḥ sthāpyate pṛthivītale
d sāyaṃ prātas tu ye saṃdhyāṃ samyaṅ nityam upāsate
d nāvaṃ vedamayīṃ kṛtvā tarante tārayanti ca
d yo japet pāvanīṃ devīṃ gāyatrīṃ vedamātaram
d na sīdet pratigṛhṇānaḥ pṛthivīṃ ca sasāgarām
d ye cāsya duḥsthitāḥ ke cid grahāḥ sūryādayo divi
d te cāsya saumyā jāyante śivāḥ śubhakarās tathā
d yatra yatra sthitāś caiva dāruṇāḥ piśitāśanāḥ
d ghorarūpā mahākāyā dharṣayanti na taṃ dvijam
d punantīha pṛthivyāṃ ca cīrṇavedavratā narāḥ
d caturṇām api vedānāṃ sā ca rājan garīyasī
d acīrṇavratavedā ye vikarmapatham āśritāḥ
d brāhmaṇā nāmamātreṇa te 'pi pūjyā yudhiṣṭhira
d kiṃ punar yas tu saṃdhye dve nityam evopatiṣṭhati
d śīlam adhyayanaṃ dānaṃ śaucaṃ mārdavam ārjavam
d tasmād vedād viśiṣṭāni manur āha prajāpatiḥ
d bhūr bhuvaḥ svar iti brahma yo vedaparamaṃ dvijaḥ
d svadāranirato dāntaḥ sa vidvān sa ca bhūsuraḥ
d saṃdhyām upāsate viprā nityam eva dvijottamāḥ
d te yānti naraśārdūla brahmalokaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
d sāvitrīmātrasāro 'pi varo vipraḥ suyantritaḥ
d nāyantritaś caturvedī sarvāśī sarvavikrayī
d sāvitrīṃ caiva vedāṃś ca tulayātolayan purā
d sadevarṣigaṇāś caiva sarve brahmapuraḥsarāḥ
d caturṇām api vedānāṃ sā hi rājan garīyasī
d yathā vikasite puṣpe madhu gṛhṇati ṣaṭpadāḥ
d samutsṛjya rasaṃ sarvaṃ nirarthakam asāravat
d evaṃ gṛhītā sāvitrī sarvavede ca pāṇḍava
d tasmāt tu sarvavedānāṃ sāvitrī prāṇa ucyate
d nirjīvā hītare vedā vinā sāvitriyā nṛpa
d nāyantritaś caturvedī śīlabhraṣṭaḥ sa kutsitaḥ
d śīlavṛttasamāyuktaḥ sāvitrīpāṭhako varaḥ
d sahasraparamāṃ devīṃ śatamadhyāṃ daśāvarām
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d sāvitrīṃ japa kaunteya sarvapāpapraṇāśinīm
d trailokyanātha he kṛṣṇa sarvabhūtātmako hy asi
d nānāyogapara śreṣṭha tuṣyase kena karmaṇā
d bhagavān uvāca
d yadi bhārasahasraṃ tu guggulvādi pradhūpayet
d karoti cen namaskāram upahāraṃ ca kārayet
d stauti yaḥ stutibhir māṃ ca ṛgyajuḥsāmabhiḥ sadā
d na toṣayati ced viprān nāhaṃ tuṣyāmi bhārata
d brāhmaṇe pūjite nityaṃ pūjito 'smi na saṃśayaḥ
d ākruṣṭe cāham ākruṣṭo bhavāmi bharatarṣabha
d parā mayi gatis teṣāṃ pūjayanti ca māṃ hi te
d yad ahaṃ dvijarūpeṇa vasāmi vasudhātale
d yas tān pūjayati prājño madgatenāntarātmanā
d tam ahaṃ svena rūpeṇa paśyāmi narapuṃgava
d kubjāḥ kāṇā vāmanāś ca daridrā vyādhitās tathā
d nāvamānyā dvijāḥ prājñair mama rūpā hi te dvijāḥ
d ye ke cit sāgarāntāyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ dvijasattamāḥ
d mama rūpaṃ hi teṣv evam arciteṣv arcito 'smy aham
d bahavas tu na jānanti narā jñānabahiṣkṛtāḥ
d yathāhaṃ dvijarūpeṇa vasāmi vasudhātale
d avamanyanti ye viprān svadharmāt pātayanti te
d preṣaṇaiḥ preṣayante ca śuśrūṣāṃ kārayanti ca
d mṛtāś cātra paratremān yamadūtā mahābalāḥ
d nikṛntanti yathākāmaṃ sūtramārgeṇa śilpinaḥ
d ākrośaparivādābhyāṃ ye ramante dvijātiṣu
d tān mṛtān yamalokasthān nipātya pṛthivītale
d ākramyorasi pādena krūraḥ saṃraktalocanaḥ
d agnivarṇais tu saṃdaṃśair yamo jihvāṃ samuddharet
d ye ca viprān nirīkṣante pāpāḥ pāpena cakṣuṣā
d abrahmaṇyāḥ śruter bāhyā nityaṃ brahmadviṣo narāḥ
d teṣāṃ ghorā mahākāyā vakratuṇḍā mahābalāḥ
d uddharanti muhūrtena khagāś cakṣur yamājñayā
d yaḥ prahāraṃ dvijendrāya dadyāt kuryāc ca śoṇitam
d asthibhaṅgaṃ ca yaḥ kuryāt prāṇair vā viprayojayet
d so 'nupūrvyeṇa yātīmān narakān ekaviṃśatim
d śūlam āropito gatvā jvalane paripacyate
d bahuvarṣasahasrāṇi pacyamānas tv avākśirāḥ
d nāvamucyeta durmedhā na tasya kṣīyate gatiḥ
d brāhmaṇāyāvicāryaivaṃ vrajan vai vadhakāṅkṣayā
d śatavarṣasahasrāṇi tāmisre paripacyate
d utpādya śoṇitaṃ gātrāt saṃrambhān matipūrvakam
d sa paryāyeṇa yātīmān narakān ekaviṃśatim
d tasmān nākuśalaṃ brūyān na śuṣkāṃ giram īrayet
d na brūyāt paruṣāṃ vāṇīṃ na caivaitān atikramet
d ye viprāñ śraddhayā vācā pūjayanti narottamāḥ
d arcitaś ca tataś caiva tair bhavāmi na saṃśayaḥ
d tarjayanti ca ye viprān krośayanti ca bhārata
d ākruṣṭas tarjitaś cāhaṃ tair bhavāmi na saṃśayaḥ
d yaś candanaiś cāgarudhūpadīpair
d abhyarcayet kāṣṭhamayīṃ mamārcām
d tenārcito naiva bhavāmi samyag
d viprārcanād asmi samarcito 'ham
d vipraprasādād dharaṇīdharo 'haṃ
d vipraprasādād asurāñ jayāmi
d vipraprasādāc ca sadakṣiṇo 'haṃ
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d vipraprasādād ajito 'ham asmi
d devadeveśa daityaghna paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me
d etat kathaya sarvajña tvadbhaktasya ca keśava
d mānuṣasya ca lokasya dharmalokasya cāntaram
d kīdṛśaṃ kiṃpramāṇaṃ vā kim adhiṣṭhānam eva ca
d taranti mānuṣā deva kenopāyena mādhava
d tvagasthimāṃsanirmukte pañcabhūtavivarjite
d kathayasva mahādeva sukhaduḥkham aśeṣataḥ
d jīvasya karmalokeṣu karmabhis tu śubhāśubhaiḥ
d anubaddhasya taiḥ pāśair nīyamānasya dāruṇaiḥ
d mṛtyudūtair durādharṣair ghorair ghoraparākramaiḥ
d vadhyasyākṣipyamāṇasya vidrutasya yamājñayā
d puṇyapāpakṛtaṃ tiṣṭhet sukhaduḥkham aśeṣataḥ
d yamadūtair durādharṣair nīyate vā kathaṃ punaḥ
d kiṃ vā tatra gatā deva karma kurvanti mānavāḥ
d kathaṃ dharmaparā yānti devatādvijapūjakāḥ
d kathaṃ vā pāpakarmāṇo yānti pretapuraṃ narāḥ
d kiṃ rūpaṃ kiṃ pramāṇaṃ vā varṇaḥ ko vāsya keśava
d bhagavān uvāca
d jīvasya gacchato nityaṃ yamalokaṃ bravīhi me
d śṛṇu rājan yathāvṛttaṃ yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi
d tat te 'haṃ kathayiṣyāmi madbhaktasya nareśvara
d ṣaḍaśītisahasrāṇi yojanānāṃ yudhiṣṭhira
d mānuṣyasya ca lokasya yamalokasya cāntaram
d na tatra vṛkṣacchāyā vā na taṭākaṃ saro 'pi vā
d na vāpyo dīrghikā vāpi na kūpo vā yudhiṣṭhira
d na maṇṭapaṃ sabhā vāpi na prapā na niketanam
d na parvato nadī vāpi na bhūmer vivaraṃ kva cit
d na grāmo vāśramo vāpi nodyānaṃ vā vanāni ca
d na kiṃ cid āśrayasthānaṃ pathi tasmin yudhiṣṭhira
d jantor hi prāptakālasya vedanārtasya vai bhṛśam
d karaṇais tyaktadehasya prāṇaiḥ kaṇṭhagataiḥ punaḥ
d śarīrāc cālyate jīvo hy avaśo mātariśvanā
d nirgato vāyubhūtas tu ṣaṭkośāt tu kalevarāt
d śarīram anyat tadrūpaṃ tadvarṇaṃ tatpramāṇakam
d adṛśyaṃ tat praviṣṭas tu so 'py adṛṣṭena kena cit
d so 'ntarātmā dehavatām aṣṭāṅgo yas tu saṃcaret
d chedanād bhedanād dāhāt tāḍanād vā na naśyati
d nānārūpadharair ghoraiḥ pracaṇḍaiś caṇḍasādhanaiḥ
d nīyamāno durādharṣair yamadūtair yamājñayā
d putradāramayaiḥ pāśaiḥ saṃniruddho 'vaśo balāt
d svakarmabhiś cānugataḥ kṛtaiḥ sukṛtaduṣkṛtaiḥ
d ākrandamānaḥ karuṇaṃ bandhubhir duḥkhapīḍitaiḥ
d tyaktvā bandhujanaṃ sarvaṃ nirapekṣas tu gacchati
d mātṛbhiḥ pitṛbhiś cāpi bhrātṛbhir mātulais tathā
d dāraiḥ putrair vayasyaiś ca rudadbhis tyajyate punaḥ
d adṛśyamānas tair dīnair aśrupūrṇamukhekṣaṇaiḥ
d svaśarīraṃ parityajya vāyubhūtas tu gacchati
d andhakāram apāraṃ taṃ mahāghoraṃ tamovṛtam
d duḥkhāntaṃ duṣpratāraṃ ca durgamaṃ pāpakarmaṇām
d duḥsahāyaṃ durantaṃ ca durnirīkṣaṃ durāsadam
d durāpam atiduḥkhaṃ ca pāpiṣṭhānāṃ narottama
d ṛṣibhiḥ kathyamānaṃ tat pāraṃparyeṇa pārthiva
d trāsaṃ janayati prāyaḥ śrūyamāṇaṃ kathāsv api
d avaśyaṃ caiva gantavyaṃ tadadhvānaṃ yudhiṣṭhira
d prāptakālena saṃtyajya bandhūn bhogān dhanāni ca
