d jarāyujair aṇḍajaiś ca svedajair udbhijjais tathā
d jaṅgamaiḥ sthirajaiś caiva gantavyaṃ yamasādanam
d devāsurair manuṣyādyair vaivasvatavaśānugaiḥ
d strīpuṃnapuṃsakaiś cāpi pṛthivyāṃ jīvasaṃjñitaiḥ
d madhyamair yuvabhir vāpi bālair vṛddhais tathaiva ca
d jātamātraiś ca garbhasthair gantavyaḥ sa mahāpathaḥ
d pūrvāhṇe vāparāhṇe vā saṃdhyākāle 'tha vā punaḥ
d pradoṣe vārdharātre vā pratyūṣe vāpy upasthite
d pravāsasthair vanasthair vā parvatasthair jalasthitaiḥ
d kṣetrasthair vā nabhaḥsthair vā gṛhamadhyagatair api
d bhuñjadbhir vā pibadbhir vā khādadbhir vā narottama
d āsīnair vā sthitair vāpi śayanīyagatair api
d jāgradbhir vā prasuptair vā gantavyas tu mahāpathaḥ
d mṛtyudūtair durādharṣaiḥ pracaṇḍaiś caṇḍaśāsanaiḥ
d ākṣipyamāṇā hy avaśāḥ prayānti yamasādanam
d kva cid bhītaiḥ kva cit trastaiḥ praskhaladbhiḥ kva cit kva cit
d krandadbhir vedanārtais tu gantavyaṃ yamasādanam
d nirbhartsyamānair udvignair vidhūtair bhayavihvalaiḥ
d tudyamānaśarīraiś ca gantavyaṃ tarjanaiḥ sadā
d kaṇṭakākīrṇamārgeṇa taptavālukapāṃsunā
d dahyamānais tu gantavyaṃ narair dānavivarjitaiḥ
d kāṣṭhopalaśilāghātair daṇḍolmukakaśāṅkuśaiḥ
d hanyamānair yamapuraṃ gantavyaṃ dharmavarjitaiḥ
d medaḥśoṇitapūyārdrair vaktragātraiś ca savraṇaiḥ
d dagdhakṣatajakīrṇaiś ca gantavyaṃ jīvaghātakaiḥ
d krandadbhiś ca rudadbhiś ca krośadbhiś cāpi visvanam
d vedanārtaiś ca kūjadbhir vikrośadbhiś ca visvaram
d vedanārtaiḥ patadbhiś ca gantavyaṃ jīvaghātakaiḥ
d bhagnapādoruhastāṅgair bhagnadantaśirodharaiḥ
d chinnakaṇṭhoṣṭhanāsaiś ca gantavyaṃ jīvaghātakaiḥ
d śaktibhir bhiṇḍipālaiś ca śaṅkutomarasāyakaiḥ
d tudyamānais tu śūlāgrair gantavyaṃ jīvaghātakaiḥ
d śvabhir vyāghrair vṛkaiḥ kākair bhakṣyamāṇāḥ samantataḥ
d tudyamānāś ca gacchanti rākṣasair māṃsakhādibhiḥ
d mahiṣaiś ca mṛgaiś cāpi sūkaraiḥ pṛṣatais tathā
d bhakṣyamāṇais tadadhvānaṃ gantavyaṃ māṃsakhādibhiḥ
d sūcīsutīkṣṇatuṇḍābhir makṣikābhiḥ samantataḥ
d tudyamānais tu gantavyaṃ pāpiṣṭhair bālaghātakaiḥ
d visrabdhaṃ svāminaṃ mitraṃ striyaṃ vā ghnanti ye narāḥ
d śastrair nirbhidyamānais tair gantavyaṃ yamasādanam
d ghātayanti ca ye jīvān duḥkham āpādayanti ca
d rākṣasaiś ca śvabhiś caiva bhakṣyamāṇā vrajanti te
d ye haranti ca vastrāṇi śayyāḥ prāvaraṇāni ca
d te yānti vidrutā nagnāḥ piśācā iva tatpatham
d gāś ca dhānyaṃ hiraṇyaṃ ca balāt kṣetragṛhaṃ tathā
d ye haranti durātmānaḥ parasvaṃ pāpakāriṇaḥ
d pāṣāṇair ulmukair daṇḍaiḥ kāṣṭhaghātaiś ca jharjharaiḥ
d hanyamānaiḥ kṣatākīrṇair gantavyaṃ tair yamālayam
d brahmasvaṃ ye harantīha narā narakanirbhayāḥ
d ākrośantīha vā nityaṃ praharanti ca ye dvijān
d śuṣkakaṇṭhā nibaddhās te chinnajihvākṣināsikāḥ
d pūyaśoṇitadurgandhā bhakṣyante kākajambukaiḥ
d caṇḍālair bhīṣaṇaiś caṇḍais tudyamānāḥ samantataḥ
d krośantaḥ karuṇaṃ ghoraṃ gacchanti yamasādanam
d tatra cāpi gatāḥ pāpā viṣṭhākūpeṣv anekaśaḥ
d jīvanto varṣakoṭīs tu kliśyante vedanārditāḥ
d tataś ca muktāḥ kālena loke cāsmin narādhamāḥ
d viṣṭhākrimitvaṃ gacchanti janmakoṭiśataṃ nṛpa
d vidyamānadhanair yas tu lobhaḍambhānṛtānvitaiḥ
d śrotriyebhyo na dattāni dānāni kurupuṃgava
d grīvāpāśanibaddhās te hanyamānāś ca rākṣasaiḥ
d kṣutpipāsāśramārtās tu yānti pretapuraṃ narāḥ
d adattadānā gacchanti śuṣkakaṇṭhāsyatālukāḥ
d annaṃ pānīyasahitaṃ prārthayantaḥ punaḥ punaḥ
d svāmin bubhukṣātṛṣṇārtā gantuṃ naivādya śaknumaḥ
d mamānnaṃ dīyatāṃ svāmin pānīyaṃ dīyatāṃ mama
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d iti bruvantas tair dūtair yāpayanti yamālayam
d tac chrutvā vacanaṃ viṣṇoḥ papāta bhuvi pāṇḍavaḥ
d niḥsaṃjño 'pi bhayatrasto mūrchayā samabhiplutaḥ
d tato labdhvā śanaiḥ saṃjñāṃ samāśvasto 'cyutena saḥ
d netre prakṣālya toyena bhūyaḥ keśavam abravīt
d bhīto 'smy ahaṃ mahādeva śrutvā mārgasya vistaram
d bhagavān uvāca
d kenopāyena tanmārgaṃ taranti puruṣāḥ sukham
d iha ye dhārmikā loke jīvaghātavivarjitāḥ
d guruśuśrūṣaṇe yuktā devabrāhmaṇapūjakāḥ
d asmān mānuṣyakāl lokāt sabhāryāḥ sahabāndhavāḥ
d yam adhvānaṃ tu gacchanti yathāvat taṃ nibodha me
d brāhmaṇebhyaḥ pradānāni nānārūpāṇi pārthiva
d ye prayacchanti vidvadbhyas te sukhaṃ yānti tatpatham
d annaṃ ye ca prayacchanti brāhmaṇebhyaḥ susaṃskṛtam
d śrotriyebhyo viśeṣeṇa prītyā paramayā yutāḥ
d te vimānair mahātmāno yānti citrair yamālayam
d sevyamānā varastrībhir apsarobhir mahāpatham
d ye ca nityaṃ prabhāṣante satyaṃ niṣkalmaṣaṃ vacaḥ
d te 'pi yānty amalābhrābhair vimānais taṃ yamālayam
d kapilādyāni puṇyāni gopradānāni ye narāḥ
d brāhmaṇebhyaḥ prayacchanti śrotriyebhyo viśeṣataḥ
d te yānty amalavarṇābhair vimānair vṛṣayojitaiḥ
d vaivasvatapuraṃ prāpya apsarobhir niṣevitāḥ
d upānahau ca chattraṃ ca śayanāny āsanāni ca
d viprebhyo ye prayacchanti vastrāṇy ābharaṇāni ca
d te yānty aśvair vṛṣair vāpi kuñjarair apy alaṃkṛtāḥ
d dharmarājapuraṃ ramyaṃ sauvarṇacchattraśobhitāḥ
d ye ca bhakṣyāṇi dāsyanti bhojyaṃ peyaṃ tathaiva ca
d snigdhānnāny api viprebhyaḥ śraddhayā parayā yutāḥ
d te yānti kāñcanair yānaiḥ sukhaṃ vaivasvatālayam
d varastrībhir yathākāmaṃ sevyamānāḥ sahasraśaḥ
d ye ca kṣīraṃ prayacchanti ghṛtaṃ dadhi guḍaṃ madhu
d brāhmaṇebhyaḥ prayatnena śraddadhānāḥ susaṃskṛtāḥ
d cakravākaprayuktais tu yānai rukmamayaiḥ śubhaiḥ
d yānti gandharvavāditraiḥ sevyamānā yamālayam
d ye phalāni prayacchanti puṣpāṇi surabhīṇi ca
d haṃsayuktair vimānais tu yānti dharmapuraṃ narāḥ
d ye prayacchanti viprebhyo vicitrānnaṃ ghṛtāplutam
d te vrajanty amalābhrābhair vimānair vāyuvegibhiḥ
d puraṃ tat pretanāthasya nānājanasamākulam
d pānīyaṃ ye prayacchanti sarvabhūtaprajīvanam
d te sutṛptāḥ sukhaṃ yānti vimānair haṃsacoditaiḥ
d ye tilāṃs tiladhenuṃ vā ghṛtadhenum athāpi vā
d śrotriyebhyaḥ prayacchanti saumyabhāvasamanvitāḥ
d somamaṇḍalasaṃkāśair yānais te yānti nirmalaiḥ
d gīyamānais tu gandharvair vaivasvatapuraṃ nṛpa
d yeṣāṃ vāpyaś ca kūpāś ca taṭākāni sarāṃsi ca
d dīrghikāḥ puṣkariṇyaś ca sajalāś ca jalāśayāḥ
d yānais te yānti candrābhair divyaghaṇṭānināditaiḥ
d cāmarais tālavṛntaiś ca vījyamānā mahāprabhāḥ
d nityatṛptā mahātmāno gacchanti yamasādanam
d yeṣāṃ devagṛhāṇīha citrāṇy āyatanāni ca
d manoharāṇi kāntāni darśanīyāni bhānti ca
d te vrajanty amalābhrābhair vimānair vāyuvegibhiḥ
d puraṃ tat pretanāthasya nānājanasamākulam
d vaivasvataṃ ca paśyanti sukhacittaṃ sukhasthitam
d yamena pūjitā yānti devasālokyatāṃ tataḥ
d devān uddiśya lokeṣu prapāsu karakoddhṛtam
d śītalaṃ salilaṃ ramyaṃ tṛṣitebhyo diśanti ye
d te tu tṛptiṃ parāṃ prāpya sukhaṃ yānti mahāpatham
d kāṣṭhapādukadā yānti tadadhvānaṃ sukhaṃ narāḥ
d sauvarṇamaṇipīṭheṣu pādau kṛtvā rathottame
d ārāmān vṛkṣaṣaṇḍāṃś ca ropayanti ca ye narāḥ
d saṃvardhayanti cāvyagrāḥ phalapuṣpopaśobhitān
d vṛkṣacchāyāsu ramyāsu śītalāsu svalaṃkṛtāḥ
d yānti te vāhanair divyaiḥ pūjyamānā muhur muhuḥ
d sevyamānāḥ surūpābhir uttamābhiḥ prayatnataḥ
d strībhiḥ kanakavarṇābhir yathākāmaṃ yathāsukham
d aśvayānaṃ tu goyānaṃ hastiyānam athāpi vā
d ye prayacchanti viprebhyo vimānaiḥ kanakopamaiḥ
d suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ vāpi vidrumaṃ mauktikaṃ tathā
d ye prayacchanti te yānti vimānaiḥ kāñcanojjvalaiḥ
d te vrajanti varastrībhiḥ sevyamānā yathāsukham
d bhūmidā yānti taṃ lokaṃ sarvakāmaiḥ sutarpitāḥ
d uditādityasaṃkāśair vimānair vṛṣayojitaiḥ
d kanyāṃ ye ca prayacchanti viprāya śrotriyāya ca
d divyakanyāvṛtā yānti vimānais te yamālayam
d sugandhān gandhasaṃyogān puṣpāṇi surabhīṇi ca
d prayacchanti dvijāgrebhyo bhaktyā paramayā yutāḥ
d sugandhāḥ suṣṭhuveṣāś ca suprabhāḥ sragvibhūṣaṇāḥ
d yānti dharmapuraṃ yānair vicitrair apy alaṃkṛtāḥ
d dīpadā yānti yānaiś ca dyotayanto diśo daśa
d ādityasadṛśākārair dīpyamānā ivāgnayaḥ
d gṛhāvasathadātāro grahaiḥ kāñcanavedikaiḥ
d vrajanti bālasūryābhair dharmarājapuraṃ narāḥ
d jalabhājanadātāraḥ kuṇḍikākarakapradāḥ
d pūjyamānā varastrībhir yānti tṛptā mahāgajaiḥ
d pādābhyaṅgaṃ śirobhyaṅgaṃ pānaṃ pādodakaṃ tathā
d ye prayacchanti viprebhyas te yānty aśvair yamālayam
d viśrāmayanti ye viprāñ śrāntān adhvani karśitān
d cakravākaprayuktena yānti yānena te 'pi ca
d svāgatena ca yo viprān pūjayed āsanena ca
d sa gacchati tadadhvānaṃ sukhaṃ paramanirvṛtaḥ
d namo brahmaṇyadeveti yo māṃ dṛṣṭvābhivādayet
d vratavat prayato nityaṃ sa sukhaṃ yāti tatpatham
d namaḥ sarvasabhābhyaś cety abhikhyāya dine dine
d namaskaroti gobhyo yaḥ sa sukhaṃ yāti tatpatham
d namo 'stu priyadattāyety evaṃvādī dine dine
d bhūmim ākramate prātaḥ śayanād utthitaś ca yaḥ
d sarvakāmaiḥ sa tṛptātmā sarvabhūṣaṇabhūṣitaḥ
d yāti yānena divyena sukhaṃ vaivasvatālayam
d anantarāśino ye tu ḍambhāhaṃkāravarjitāḥ
d te 'pi sārasayuktena yānti yānena vai sukham
d ye cāpy ekena bhuktena vartante ḍambhavarjitāḥ
d haṃsayuktair vimānais tu sukhaṃ yānti yamālayam
d caturthena ca bhuktena vartante ye jitendriyāḥ
d yānti te dharmanagaraṃ yānair barhiṇayojitaiḥ
d tṛtīyadivaseneha bhuñjate ye jitendriyāḥ
d te 'pi hastirathaṃ yānti tatpathaṃ kanakojjvalaiḥ
d ṣaṣṭhāhnakāliko yas tu varṣam ekaṃ tu vartate
d kāmakrodhavinirmuktaḥ śucir nityaṃ jitendriyaḥ
d sa yāti kuñjarasthas tu jayaśabdaravair yutaḥ
d pakṣopavāsino yānti yānaiḥ śārdūlayojitaiḥ
d dharmarājapuraṃ ramyaṃ divyastrīgaṇasevitam
d ye ca māsopavāsaṃ vai kurvate saṃyatendriyāḥ
d te 'pi sūryodayaprakhyair yānti yānair yamālayam
d agnipraveśaṃ yaś cāpi kurute madgatātmanā
d sa yāty agniprakāśena vimānena yamālayam
d prāṇāṃs tyajati yo vipro māṃ prapanno hy anāśakaḥ
d sa bālārkaprakāśena vrajed yānena tatpatham
d praviṣṭo 'ntarjale yas tu prāṇāṃs tyajati mānavaḥ
d somamaṇḍalakalpena yāti yānena tatpatham
d svaśarīraṃ hi gṛdhrāṇāṃ manmanā yaḥ prayacchati
d sa yāti rathamukhyena kāñcanena yamālayam
d gokṛte strīkṛte caiva hatā viprakṛte 'pi ca
d te yānty amarakanyābhiḥ sevyamānā raviprabhāḥ
d ye ca kurvanti madbhaktās tīrthayātrāṃ jitendriyāḥ
d te panthānaṃ mahātmāno yānair yānti sunirvṛtāḥ
d ye yajanti dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ kratubhir bhūridakṣiṇaiḥ
d haṃsasārasasaṃyuktair yānais te yānti tatpatham
d parapīḍām akṛtvaiva bhṛtyān bibhrati ye narāḥ
d tatpathaṃ te sukhaṃ yānti vimānaiḥ kāñcanojjvalaiḥ
d ye samāḥ sarvabhūteṣu jīvānām abhayapradāḥ
d krodhalobhavinirmuktā nigṛhītendriyās tathā
d pūrṇacandrapratīkāśair vimānais te mahāprabhāḥ
d yānti vaivasvatapuraṃ devagandharvasevitāḥ
d ye mām ekāntabhāvena devaṃ tryambakam eva ca
d pūjayanti namasyanti stuvanti ca dine dine
d dharmarājapuraṃ yānti yānais te 'rkasamaprabhaiḥ
d pūjitās tatra dharmeṇa svayaṃ mālyādibhiḥ śubhaiḥ
d yānty eva mama lokaṃ vā rudralokam athāpi vā
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d śrutvā yamapurādhvānaṃ jīvānāṃ gamanaṃ tathā
d dharmaputraḥ prahṛṣṭātmā keśavaṃ punar abravīt
d devadeveśa daityaghna ṛṣisaṃghair abhiṣṭuta
d bhavān bhavakaraḥ śrīmān sahasrādityasaprabha
d sarvasaṃbhava sarvajña sarvadharmapravartaka
d sarvadānaphalaṃ saumya kathayasva mamācyuta
d dānaṃ deyaṃ kathaṃ kṛṣṇa kīdṛśāya dvijāya vai
d kīdṛśaṃ vā tapaḥ kṛtvā tatphalaṃ kutra bhujyate
d evam ukto hṛṣīkeśo dharmaputreṇa dhīmatā
d uvāca dharmaputrāya puṇyān dharmān mahodayān
d śṛṇuṣvāvahito rājan pūtaṃ pāpaghnam uttamam
d sarvadānaphalaṃ saumya na śrāvyaṃ pāpakarmaṇām
d yac chrutvā puruṣaḥ strī vā naṣṭapāpaḥ samāhitaḥ
d tatkṣaṇāt pūtatāṃ yāti pāpakarmarato 'pi vā
d ekāham api kaunteya bhūmāv utpāditaṃ jalam
d sapta tārayate pūrvān vitṛṣṇā yatra gaur bhavet
d pānīyaṃ paramaṃ loke jīvānāṃ jīvanaṃ smṛtam
d pānīyasya pradānena tṛptir bhavati pāṇḍava
d pānīyasya guṇā divyāḥ paraloke sukhāvahāḥ
d tatra puṣpodakī nāma nadī paramapāvanī
d kāmān dadāti rājendra toyadānaṃ yamālaye
d śītalaṃ salilaṃ tasyā akṣayyam amṛtopamam
d śītatoyapradātṝṇāṃ bhaven nityaṃ sukhāvahā
d ye cāpy atoyadātāraḥ pūyas teṣāṃ vidhīyate
d praṇaśyaty ambupānena bubhukṣā ca yudhiṣṭhira
d tṛṣitasya na cānnena pipāsāpi praṇaśyati
d tasmāt toyaṃ sadā deyaṃ tṛṣitebhyo vijānatā
d agner mūrtiḥ kṣiter yonir amṛtasya ca saṃbhavaḥ
d ato 'mbhaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ mūlam ity ucyate budhaiḥ
d adbhiḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni jīvanti prabhavanti ca
d tasmāt sarveṣu dāneṣu toyadānaṃ viśiṣyate
d sarvadānatapoyajñair yat prāpyaṃ phalam uttamam
d tat sarvaṃ toyadānena prāpyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
d ye prayacchanti viprebhyas tv annadānaṃ susaṃskṛtam
d tais tu dattā svayaṃ prāṇā bhavanti bharatarṣabha
d annād raktaṃ ca śuklaṃ ca anne jīvaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ
d indriyāṇi ca buddhiś ca puṣṇanty annena nityaśaḥ
d annahīnāni sīdanti sarvabhūtāni pāṇḍava
d tejo balaṃ ca vīryaṃ ca sattvaṃ rūpaṃ dyutir dhṛtiḥ
d jñānaṃ medhā tathāyuś ca sarvam anne pratiṣṭhitam
d devamānavatiryakṣu sarvalokeṣu sarvadā
d sarvakālaṃ hi sarveṣām anne prāṇāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ
d annaṃ prajāpate rūpam annaṃ prajananaṃ smṛtam
d sarvabhūtamayaṃ cānnaṃ jīvaś cānnamayaṃ smṛtam
d annenādhiṣṭhitaḥ prāṇa apāno vyāna eva ca
d udānaś ca samānaś ca dhārayanti śarīriṇām
d śayanotthānagamanaṃ grahaṇākarṣaṇāni ca
d sarvasattvakṛtaṃ karma cānnād eva pravartate
d caturvidhāni bhūtāni jaṅgamāni sthirāṇi ca
d annād bhavanti rājendra sṛṣṭir eṣā prajāpateḥ
d vidyāsthānāni sarvāṇi sarvayajñāś ca pāvanāḥ
d annād yasmāt pravartante tasmād annaṃ paraṃ smṛtam
d devā rudrādayaḥ sarve pitaro 'py agnayas tathā
d yasmād annena tuṣyanti tasmād annaṃ viśiṣyate
d yasmād annāt prajāḥ sarvāḥ kalpe kalpe 'sṛjat prabhuḥ
d tasmād annāt paraṃ dānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati
d yasmād annāt pravartante dharmārthau kāma eva ca
d tasmād annāt paraṃ dānaṃ nāmutreha ca pāṇḍava
d yakṣarakṣograhā nāgā bhūtā daityāś ca dānavāḥ
d tuṣyanty annena yasmāt tu tasmād annaṃ paraṃ bhavet
d parānnam upabhuñjāno yat karma kurute śubham
d tacchubhasyaikabhāgas tu kartur bhavati bhārata
d annadasya trayo bhāgā bhavanti puruṣarṣabha
d tasmād annaṃ pradātavyaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo viśeṣataḥ
d brāhmaṇāya daridrāya yo 'nnaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ nṛpa
d śrotriyāya prayacched vai pākabhedavivarjitaḥ
d ḍambhānṛtavimuktas tu parāṃ bhaktim upāgataḥ
d svadharmeṇārjitaphalaṃ tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d śataṃ varṣasahasrāṇi kāmagaḥ kāmarūpadhṛk
d modate 'maralokasthaḥ pūjyamāno 'psarogaṇaiḥ
d tataś cāpi cyutaḥ kālān naraloke dvijo bhavet
d agrabhikṣāṃ ca yo dadyād daridrāya dvijātaye
d ṣaṇmāsād vārṣikaṃ śrāddhaṃ tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d gosahasrapradānena yat puṇyaṃ samudāhṛtam
d tat puṇyaphalam āpnoti naro vai nātra saṃśayaḥ
d atha saṃvatsaraṃ dadyād agrabhaikṣyam ayācate
d pracchādyaiva svayaṃ nītvā tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d kapilānāṃ sahasrais tu yad deyaṃ puṇyam ucyate
d tat sarvam akhilaṃ prāpya śakraloke mahīyate
d sa śakrabhavane ramye varṣakoṭiśataṃ nṛpa
d yathākāmaṃ mahātejāḥ krīḍaty apsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ
d agrānnaṃ yas tu vai dadyād dvijāya niyatavrataḥ
d daśavarṣāṇi rājendra tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d kapilāśatasahasrasya vidhidattasya yat phalam
d tat puṇyaphalam āsādya puraṃdarapuraṃ vrajet
d sa śakrabhavane ramye kāmarūpī yathāsukham
d śatakoṭisamā rājan krīḍate 'marapūjitaḥ
d śakralokāvatīrṇaś ca iha loke mahādyutiḥ
d caturvedī dvijaḥ śrīmāñ jāyate rājapūjitaḥ
d adhvaśrāntāya viprāya kṣudhitāyānnakāṅkṣiṇe
d deśakālābhiyātāya dīyate pāṇḍunandana
d yācate 'nnaṃ na dadyād yo vidyamāne dhanāgame
d sa lubdho narakaṃ yāti kṛmīṇāṃ kālasūtrakam
d sa tatra narake ghore lobhamohitacetanaḥ
d daśavarṣasahasrāṇi kliśyate vedanārditaḥ
d tasmāc ca narakān muktaḥ kālena mahatā hi saḥ
d daridro mānuṣo loke caṇḍāleṣv api jāyate
d yas tu pāṃsulapādaś ca dūrādhvaśramakarśitaḥ
d kṣutpipāsāśramaḥ śrānta ārtaḥ khinnagatir dvijaḥ
d pṛcchan vai hy annadātāraṃ gṛham abhyetya yācayet
d taṃ pūjayet tu yatnena so 'tithiḥ svargasaṃkramaḥ
d tasmiṃs tuṣṭe naraśreṣṭha tuṣṭāḥ syuḥ sarvadevatāḥ
d na tathā haviṣā homair na puṣpair nānulepanaiḥ
d agnayaḥ pārtha tuṣyanti yathā hy atithipūjanāt
d kapilāyāṃ tu dattāyāṃ vidhivaj jyeṣṭhapuṣkare
d na tat phalam avāpnoti yat phalaṃ viprabhojanāt
d dvijapādodakaklinnā yāvat tiṣṭhati medinī
d tāvat puṣkaraparṇena pibanti pitaro jalam
d devamālyāpanayanaṃ dvijocchiṣṭāpamārjanam
d śrāntasaṃvāhanaṃ caiva tathā pādāvasecanam
d pratiśrayapradānaṃ ca tathā śayyāsanasya ca
d ekaikaṃ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha gopradānād viśiṣyate
d pādodakaṃ pādaghṛtaṃ dīpam annaṃ pratiśrayam
d ye prayacchanti viprebhyo nopasarpanti te yamam
d viprātithye kṛte rājan bhaktyā śuśrūṣite 'pi ca
d devāḥ śuśrūṣitāḥ sarve trayastriṃśad bhavanti te
d abhyāgato jñātapūrvo hy ajñāto 'tithir ucyate
d tayoḥ pūjāṃ dvijaḥ kuryād iti paurāṇikī śrutiḥ
d pādābhyaṅgānnapānais tu yo 'tithiṃ pūjayen naraḥ
d pūjitas tena rājendra bhavāmīha na saṃśayaḥ
d śīghraṃ pāpād vinirmukto mayā cānugrahīkṛtaḥ
d vimānenendukalpena mama lokaṃ sa gacchati
d abhyāgataṃ śrāntam anuvrajanti
d devāś ca sarve pitaro 'gnayaś ca
d tasmin dvije pūjite pūjitāḥ syur
d gate nirāśāḥ pitaro vrajanti
d atithir yasya bhagnāśo gṛhāt pratinivartate
d pitaras tasya nāśnanti daśa varṣāṇi pañca ca
d varjitaḥ pitṛbhir lubdhaḥ sa devair agnibhiḥ saha
d nirayaṃ rauravaṃ gatvā daśa varṣāṇi pacyate
d tataś cāpi cyutaḥ kālād iha cocchiṣṭabhug bhavet
d vaiśvadevāntike prāptam atithiṃ yo na pūjayet
d sa caṇḍālatvam āpnoti sadya eva na saṃśayaḥ
d nirvāsayati yo vipraṃ deśakālāgataṃ gṛhāt
d patitas tatkṣaṇād eva jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
d narake raurave ghore varṣakoṭiṃ sa pacyate
d tataś cāpi cyutaḥ kālād iha loke narādhamaḥ
d śvā vai dvādaśa janmāni jāyate kṣutpipāsitaḥ
d caṇḍālo 'py atithiḥ prāpto deśakāle 'nnakāṅkṣayā
d abhyudgamya gṛhasthena pūjanīyaś ca sarvadā
d anarcayitvā yo 'śnāti lobhamohavicetanaḥ
d sa caṇḍālatvam āpnoti daśa janmāni pāṇḍava
d nirāśam atithiṃ kṛtvā bhuñjāno yaḥ prahṛṣṭavān
d na jānāty ātmanātmānaṃ viṣṭhākūpe nipātitam
d moghaṃ dhruvaṃ prorṇayati mogham asya tu pacyate
d mogham annaṃ sadāśnāti yo 'tithiṃ na ca pūjayet
d sāṅgopāṅgāṃs tu yo vedān paṭhatīha dine dine
d na cātithiṃ pūjayati vṛthā bhavati sa dvijaḥ
d pākayajñamahāyajñaiḥ somasaṃsthābhir eva ca
d ye yajanti na cārcanti gṛheṣv atithim āgatam
d teṣāṃ yaśobhikāmānāṃ dattam iṣṭaṃ ca yad bhavet
d vṛthā bhavati tat sarvam āśayā hi tayā hatam
d deśakālaṃ ca pātraṃ ca svaśaktiṃ ca nirīkṣya ca
d alpaṃ samaṃ mahad vāpi kuryād ātithyam ātmavān
d sumukhaḥ suprasannātmā dhīmān atithim āgatam
d svāgatenāsanenādbhir annādyena ca pūjayet
d hitaḥ priyo vā dveṣyo vā mūrkhaḥ paṇḍita eva vā
d prāpto yo vaiśvadevānte so 'tithiḥ svargasaṃkramaḥ
d kṣutpipāsāśramārtāya deśakālāgatāya ca
d satkṛtyānnaṃ pradātavyaṃ yajñasya phalam icchatā
d bhojayed ātmanaḥ śreṣṭhān vidhivad dhavyakavyayoḥ
d annaṃ prāṇo manuṣyāṇām annadaḥ prāṇado bhavet
d tasmād annaṃ viśeṣeṇa dātavyaṃ bhūtim icchatā
d annadaḥ sarvakāmais tu sutṛptaḥ suṣṭhv alaṃkṛtaḥ
d pūrṇacandraprakāśena vimānena virājatā
d sevyamāno varastrībhir mama lokaṃ sa gacchati
d krīḍitvā tu tatas tasmin varṣakoṭiṃ yathāmaraḥ
d tataś cāpi cyutaḥ kālād iha loke mahāyaśāḥ
d vedaśāstrārthatattvajño bhogavān brāhmaṇo bhavet
d yathāśraddhaṃ tu yaḥ kuryān manuṣyeṣu prajāyate
d mahādhanapatiḥ śrīmān vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ
d sarvaśāstrārthatattvajño bhogavān brāhmaṇo bhavet
d sarvātithyaṃ tu yaḥ kuryād varṣam ekam akalmaṣaḥ
d dharmārjitadhano bhūtvā pāpabhedavivarjitaḥ
d devān iva svayaṃ viprān arcayitvā pitṝn api
d viprānagrāśanāśī yas tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d varṣeṇaikena yāvanti piṇḍān aśnanti vai dvijāḥ
d tāvad varṣāṇi rājendra mama loke mahīyate
d tataś cāpi cyutaḥ kālād iha loke mahāyaśāḥ
d vedaśāstrārthatattvajño bhogavān brāhmaṇo bhavet
d sarvātithyaṃ ca yaḥ kuryād yathāśraddhaṃ nareśvara
d akālaniyamenāpi satyavādī jitendriyaḥ
d satyasaṃdho jitakrodhaḥ śākhādharmavivarjitaḥ
d adharmabhīrur dharmiṣṭho māyāmātsaryavarjitaḥ
d śraddadhānaḥ śucir nityaṃ pākabhedavivarjitaḥ
d sa vimānena divyena divyarūpī mahāyaśāḥ
d puraṃdarapuraṃ yāti gīyamāno 'psarogaṇaiḥ
d manvantaraṃ tu tatraiva krīḍitvā devapūjitaḥ
d mānuṣyalokam āgamya bhogavān brāhmaṇo bhavet
d daśa janmāni vipratvam āpnuyād rājapūjitaḥ
d bhagavān uvāca
d jātismaraś ca bhavati yatra tatropajāyate
d ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi bhūmidānam anuttamam
d yaḥ prayacchati viprāya bhūmiṃ ramyāṃ sadakṣiṇām
d śrotriyāya daridrāya sāgnihotrāya pāṇḍava
d sa sarvakāmatṛptātmā sarvaratnavibhūṣitaḥ
d sarvapāpavinirmukto dīpyamāno 'rkavat sadā
d bālasūryaprakāśena vicitradhvajaśobhinā
d yāti yānena divyena mama lokaṃ mahāyaśāḥ
d tatra divyāṅganābhis tu sevyamāno yathāsukham
d kāmagaḥ kāmarūpī ca krīḍaty apsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ
d yāvad bibharti lokān vai bhūmiḥ kurukulodvaha
d tāvad bhūmipradaḥ kāmaṃ mama loke mahīyate
d na hi bhūmipradānād vai dānam anyad viśiṣyate
d na cāpi bhūmiharaṇāt pāpam anyad viśiṣyate
d dānāny anyāni hīyante kālena kurupuṃgava
d bhūmidānasya puṇyasya kṣayo naivopapadyate
d brāhmaṇāya daridrāya bhūmiṃ dattāṃ tu yo naraḥ
d na hiṃsati naravyāghra tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d saptadvīpasamudrāntā ratnadhānyasamākulā
d sa śailavanadurgāḍhyā tena dattā mahī bhavet
d bhūmiṃ dṛṣṭvā dīyamānāṃ śrotriyāyāgnihotriṇe
d sarvabhūtāni manyante māṃ dadātīti harṣavat
d suvarṇamaṇiratnāni dhanadhānyavasūni ca
d sarvadānāni vai rājan dadāti vasudhāṃ dadan
d sāgarān saritaḥ śailān samāni viṣamāṇi ca
d sarvagandharasāṃś caiva dadāti vasudhāṃ dadan
d oṣadhīḥ phalasaṃpannā nānāpuṣpaphalānvitāḥ
d kamalotpalaṣaṇḍāṃś ca dadāti vasudhāṃ dadan
d dharmaṃ kāmaṃ tathārthaṃ ca vedān yajñāṃs tathaiva ca
d svargamārgagatiṃ caiva dadāti vasudhāṃ dadan
d agniṣṭomādibhir yajñair ye yajante sadakṣiṇaiḥ
d na tat phalaṃ labhante te bhūmidānasya yat phalam
d śrotriyāya mahīṃ dattvā yo na hiṃsati pāṇḍava
d tad dānaṃ kathayiṣyanti yāval lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ
d tāvat svargopabhogānāṃ bhoktāraḥ pāṇḍunandana
d sasyapūrṇāṃ mahīṃ yas tu śrotriyāya prayacchati
d pitaras tasya tṛpyanti yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam
d mama rudrasya savitus tridaśānāṃ tathaiva ca
d prītaye viddhi rājendra bhūmir dattā dvijāya vai
d tena puṇyena pūtātmā dātā bhūmer yudhiṣṭhira
d mama sālokyam āyāti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
d yat kiṃ cit kurute pāpaṃ puruṣo vṛttikarśitaḥ
d sa ca gokarṇamātreṇa bhūmidānena śudhyati
d māsopavāse yat puṇyaṃ kṛcchre cāndrāyaṇe 'pi ca
d bhūmigokarṇamātreṇa tat puṇyaṃ tu vidhīyate
d sarvatīrthābhiṣeke ca yat puṇyaṃ samudāhṛtam
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d bhūmigokarṇamātreṇa tat puṇyaṃ tu vidhīyate
d devadeva namas te 'stu vāsudeva sureśvara
d bhagavān uvāca
d gokarṇasya pramāṇaṃ vai vaktum arhasi tattvataḥ
d śṛṇu gokarṇamātrasya pramāṇaṃ pāṇḍunandana
d triṃśaddaṇḍapramāṇena pramitaṃ sarvatodiśam
d pratyak prāg api rājendra tat tathā dakṣiṇottaram
d gokarṇaṃ tadvidaḥ prāhuḥ pramāṇaṃ dharaṇer nṛpa
d savṛṣaṃ gośataṃ yatra sukhaṃ tiṣṭhaty ayantritam
d savatsaṃ kuruśārdūla tac ca gokarṇam ucyate
d kiṃkarā mṛtyudaṇḍāś ca kumbhīpākāś ca dāruṇāḥ
d ghorāś ca vāruṇāḥ pāśā nopasarpanti bhūmidam
d nirayā rauravādyāś ca tathā vaitaraṇī nadī
d tīvrāś ca yātanāḥ kaṣṭā nopasarpanti bhūmidam
d citraguptaḥ kaliḥ kālaḥ kṛtānto mṛtyur eva ca
d yamaś ca bhagavān sākṣāt pūjayanti mahīpradam
d rudraḥ prajāpatiḥ śakraḥ surā ṛṣigaṇās tathā
d ahaṃ ca prītimān rājan pūjayāmo mahīpradam
d kṛśabhṛtyasya kṛśagoḥ kṛśāśvasya kṛśātitheḥ
d bhūmir deyā naraśreṣṭha sa nidhiḥ pāralaukikaḥ
d sīdamānakuṭumbāya śrotriyāyāgnihotriṇe
d vratasthāya daridrāya bhūmir deyā narādhipa
d yathā hi dhātrī kṣīreṇa putraṃ vardhayati svayam
d dātāram anugṛhṇāti dattā hy evaṃ vasuṃdharā
d yathā bibharti gaur vatsaṃ sṛjantī kṣīram ātmanaḥ
d tathā sarvaguṇopetā bhūmir vahati bhūmidam
d yathā bījāni rohanti jalasiktāni bhūpate
d tathā kāmāḥ prarohanti bhūmidasya dine dine
d yathodayas tu sūryasya tamaḥ sarvaṃ vyapohati
d tathā pāpaṃ narasyeha bhūmidānaṃ vyapohati
d dātā daśānugṛhṇāti yo hared daśa hanti ca
d atītānāgatānīha kulāni kurupuṃgava
d āśrutya bhūmidānaṃ tu dattvā yo vā haret punaḥ
d sa baddho vāruṇaiḥ pāśaiḥ kṣipyate pūyaśoṇite
d svadattāṃ paradattāṃ vā yo hareta vasuṃdharām
d na tasya narakād ghorād vidyate niṣkṛtiḥ kva cit
d brāhmaṇasya hate kṣetre hanyād dvādaśa pūrvajān
d sa gacchet kṛmiyoniṃ ca na ca mucyeta jātu saḥ
d dattvā bhūmiṃ dvijendrāya yas tām evopajīvati
d gavāṃ śatasahasrasya hantuḥ sa labhate phalam
d so 'dhaḥśirās tu pāpātmā kumbhīpākeṣu pacyate
d divyair varṣasahasrais tu kumbhīpākād viniḥsṛtaḥ
d iha loke bhavet sa śvā śatajanmāni pāṇḍava
d dattvā bhūmiṃ dvijendrāṇāṃ yas tām evopajīvati
d sa mūḍho yāti duṣṭātmā narakān ekaviṃśatim
d narakebhyo vinirmuktaḥ śunāṃ yoniṃ sa gacchati
d halakṛṣṭā mahī deyā sabījā sasyamālinī
d atha vā sodakā deyā daridrāya dvijātaye
d evaṃ dattā mahī rājan prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā
d sarvān kāmān avāpnoti manasā cintitāni ca
d bahubhir vasudhā dattā dīyate ca narādhipaiḥ
d yasya yasya yadā bhūmis tasya tasya tadā phalam
d yaḥ prayacchati kanyāṃ vai surūpāṃ śrotriyāya vai
d sa brahmadevo rājendra tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d balīvardasahasrāṇāṃ dattānāṃ dhuryavāhinām
d yat phalaṃ labhate rājan kanyādānena tat phalam
d gavāṃ śatasahasrasya samyag dattasya yat phalam
d tat phalaṃ samavāpnoti yaḥ prayacchati kanyakām
d yāvanti caiva romāṇi kanyāyāḥ kurupuṃgava
d tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi mama loke mahīyate
d tataś cāpi cyutaḥ kālād iha loke sa jāyate
d ṣaḍaṅgavic caturvedī sarvalokārcito dvijaḥ
d yaḥ suvarṇaṃ daridrāya brāhmaṇāya prayacchati
d śrotriyāya daridrāya bahuputrāya pāṇḍava
d vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyo bālasūryasamaprabhaḥ
d vimānaṃ divyam ārūḍhaḥ kāmagaḥ kāmabhogavān
d varṣakoṭiṃ mahātejā mama loke pramodate
d tataḥ kālāvatīrṇaś ca sosmiṃl loke hi jāyate
d vedavedāṅgavid vipraḥ koṭīdhanapatir bhavet
d yaś ca rūpyaṃ prayacched vai daridrāya dvijāya vai
d kṛśavṛtte kṛśagave sa muktaḥ sarvakilbiṣaiḥ
d pūrṇacandraprakāśena vimānena virājatā
d kāmarūpī yathā kāmaṃ svargaloke mahīyate
d tato 'vatīrṇaḥ kālena loke cāsmin mahāyaśāḥ
d sarvalokārcitaḥ śrīmān rājā bhavati vīryavān
d tilaparvatakaṃ yas tu śrotriyāya prayacchati
d viśeṣeṇa daridrāya tasyāpi śṛṇu yat phalam
d puṇyaṃ vṛṣāyutotsarge yat proktaṃ pāṇḍunandana
d tat puṇyaṃ samanuprāpya tatkṣaṇād virajo bhavet
d yathā tvaco bhujaṅgo vai tyaktvā śuddhatanur bhavet
d tathā tilapradānād vai pāpaṃ tyaktvā viśudhyati
d tilaṣaṇḍaṃ prayuñjāno jāmbūnadavibhūṣitam
d vimānaṃ divyam ārūḍhaḥ pitṛloke mahīyate
d ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi kāmarūpī mahāyaśāḥ
d tilapradātā ramate pitṛloke yathāsukham
d yaḥ prayacchati viprāya tiladhenuṃ narādhipa
d śrotriyāya daridrāya śṛṇu tasyāpi yat phalam
d gosahasrapradānena yat puṇyaṃ samudāhṛtam
d tat puṇyaphalam āpnoti tiladhenuprado naraḥ
d tilānāṃ kuḍavair yas tu tiladhenuṃ prayacchati
d tāvat koṭisamā rājan svargaloke mahīyate
d aṣṭāḍhakatilaiḥ kṛtvā tiladhenuṃ narādhipa
d dvātriṃśan niṣkasaṃyuktaṃ viṣuve yaḥ prayacchati
d madbhaktyā madgatātmā vai tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d kanyādānasahasrasya vidhidattasya yat phalam
d tat puṇyaṃ samanuprāpto mama loke mahīyate
d mama lokāvatīrṇaś ca so 'smiṃl loke 'bhijāyate
d ṛgyajuḥsāmavedānāṃ pārago brāhmaṇarṣabhaḥ
d gāṃ tu yas tu daridrāya śrotriyāya prayacchati
d prasannāṃ kṣīriṇīṃ puṇyāṃ savatsāṃ kāṃsyadohinīm
d yat kiṃ cid duṣkṛtaṃ karma tasya pūrvakṛtaṃ nṛpa
d tat sarvaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva vinaśyati na saṃśayaḥ
d yānaṃ ca vṛṣasaṃyuktaṃ dīpyamānaṃ svalaṃkṛtam
d ārūḍhaḥ kāmagaṃ divyaṃ golokam adhigacchati
d yāvanti caiva romāṇi tasyā gos tu narādhipa
d tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi gavāṃ loke mahīyate
d golokād avatīrṇas tu loke 'smin brāhmaṇo bhavet
d satrayājī vadānyaś ca sarvarājabhir arcitaḥ
d tilaṃ gāvaḥ suvarṇaṃ cāpy annaṃ kanyā vasuṃdharā
d tārayantīha dattāni brāhmaṇebhyo mahābhuja
d brāhmaṇaṃ vṛttasaṃpannam āhitāgnim alolupam
d tarpayed vidhivad rājan sa nidhiḥ pāralaukikaḥ
d āhitāgniṃ daridraṃ ca śrotriyaṃ ca jitendriyam
d śūdrānnavarjitaṃ caiva dvijaṃ yatnena pūjayet
d āhitāgniḥ sadā pātram agnihotraś ca vedavit
d pātrāṇām api tat pātraṃ śūdrānnaṃ yasya nodare
d yac ca vedamayaṃ pātraṃ yac ca pātraṃ tapomayam
d asaṃkīrṇaṃ ca yat pātraṃ tat pātraṃ tārayiṣyati
d nityaṃ svādhyāyaniratās tv aprakīrṇendriyāś ca ye
d pañcayajñaratā nityaṃ pūjitās tārayanti te
d ye kṣāntidāntāḥ śrutipūrṇakarṇā
d jitendriyā prāṇivadhe nivṛttāḥ
d pratigrahe saṃkucitā gṛhasthās
d te brāhmaṇās tārayituṃ samarthāḥ
d nityodakī nityayajñopavītī
d nityasvādhyāyī vṛṣalānnavarjī
d ṛtau gacchan vidhivac cāpi juhvan
d sa brāhmaṇas tārayituṃ samarthaḥ
d brāhmaṇo yas tu madbhakto madyājī matparāyaṇaḥ
d mayi saṃnyastakarmā ca sa vipras tārayed dhruvam
d dvādaśākṣaratattvajñaś caturvyūhavibhāgavit
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d acchidrapañcakālajñaḥ sa vipras tārayiṣyati
d vāsudevena dāneṣu kathiteṣu yathākramam
d avitṛptas tu dharmeṣu keśavaṃ punar abravīt
d deva dharmāmṛtam idaṃ śṛṇvato 'pi paraṃtapa
d na vidyate suraśreṣṭha mama tṛptir hi mādhava
d anaḍutsaṃpradānasya yat phalaṃ tu vidhīyate
d tat phalaṃ kathayasveha tava bhaktasya me 'cyuta
d yāni cānyāni dānāni tvayā noktāni kāni cit
d tāny ācakṣva suraśreṣṭha teṣāṃ cānukramāt phalam
d bhagavān uvāca
d pavitratvāt supuṇyatvāt pāvanatvāt tathaiva ca
d śṛṇu dharmāmṛtaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ dattasyānaḍuhaḥ phalam
d daśadhenusamo 'naḍvān eko 'pi kurupuṃgava
d medomāṃsavipuṣṭāṅgo nīrogaḥ kopavarjitaḥ
d yuvā bhadraḥ suśīlaś ca sarvadoṣavivarjitaḥ
d dhuraṃ dhārayate kṣipraṃ datto viprāya pāṇḍava
d sa tena puṇyadānena varṣakoṭiṃ yudhiṣṭhira
d yathākāmaṃ mahātejā gavāṃ loke mahīyate
d yaś ca dadyād anaḍuhau dvau yuktau ca dhuraṃdharau
d suvṛttāya daridrāya śrotriyāya viśeṣataḥ
d tasya yat puṇyam ākhyātaṃ tac chṛṇuṣva yudhiṣṭhira
d sahasragopradānena yat proktaṃ phalam uttamam
d tat puṇyaphalam āpnoti yāti lokān sa māmakān
d yāvanti caiva romāṇi tayor anaḍuhor nṛpa
d tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi mama loke mahīyate
d daridrāyaiva dātavyaṃ na samṛddhāya pāṇḍava
d varṣāṇāṃ hi taṭākeṣu phalaṃ naiva payodhiṣu
d yas tu dadyād anaḍuhaṃ daridrāya dvijātaye
d sa tena puṇyadānena pūtātmā kurupuṃgava
d vimānaṃ divyam ārūḍho divyarūpī yathāsukham
d mama lokeṣu ramate yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam
d gṛhaṃ dīpaprabhāyuktaṃ śayyāsanavibhūṣitam
d bhājanopaskarair yuktaṃ dhānyapūrṇam alaṃkṛtam
d dāsīgobhūmisaṃyuktaṃ saphalaṃ sarvasādhanaiḥ
d brāhmaṇāya daridrāya śrotriyāya yudhiṣṭhira
d dadyāt sadakṣiṇaṃ yas tu tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d devāḥ pitṛgaṇāś caiva agnayo ṛṣayas tathā
d prayacchanti prahṛṣṭā vai yānam ādityasaṃnibham
d tena gacchec chriyā yukto brahmalokam anuttamam
d strīsahasrāvṛte divye bhavane tatra kāñcane
d modate brahmalokastho yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam
d śayyāṃ prastaraṇopetāṃ yaḥ prayacchati pāṇḍava
d arcayitvā dvijaṃ bhaktyā vastramālyānulepanaiḥ
d bhojayitvā vicitrānnaṃ tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d dhenudānasya yat puṇyaṃ vidhidattasya pāṇḍava
d tat puṇyaṃ tam anuprāpya pitṛloke mahīyate
d śilpam adhyayanaṃ vāpi vidyāmantrauṣadhāni ca
d yaḥ prayacchati viprāya tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d āhitāgnisahasrasya pūjitasyaiva yat phalam
d tat puṇyaphalam āpnoti yas tu vidyāṃ prayacchati
d chandobhiḥ saṃprayuktena vimānena virājatā
d saptarṣilokān vrajati pūjyate brahmavādibhiḥ
d caturyugāni vai triṃśat krīḍitvā tatra devavat
d iha mānuṣyake loke vipro bhavati vedavit
d viśrāmayati yo vipraṃ śrāntam adhvani karśitam
d vinaśyati tadā pāpaṃ tasya varṣakṛtaṃ nṛpa
d atha prakṣālayet pādau tasya toyena bhaktimān
d daśavarṣakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ vyapohati na saṃśayaḥ
d ghṛtena vātha tailena pādau tasya tu pūjayet
d tad dvādaśasamārūḍhaṃ pāpam āśu vyapohati
d dhenukāñcanadattasya yac ca puṇyam udāhṛtam
d tat puṇyaphalam āpnoti yas tv evaṃ vipram arcayet
d svāgatena ca yo vipraṃ pūjayed āsanena ca
d pratyutthānena vā rājan sa devānāṃ priyo bhavet
d svāgatenāgnayo rājann āsanena śatakratuḥ
d pratyutthānena pitaraḥ prītiṃ yānty atithipriyāḥ
d agniśakrapitṝṇāṃ ca teṣāṃ prītyā narādhipa
d saṃvatsarakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tasya sadyo vinaśyati
d yaḥ prayacchati viprāya āsanaṃ mālyabhūṣitam
d sa yāti maṇicitreṇa rathenendraniketanam
d puraṃdarapure tatra divyanārīvibhūṣitaḥ
d ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇi krīḍaty apsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ
d vāhanaṃ yaḥ prayaccheta brāhmaṇāya yudhiṣṭhira
d sa yāti ratnacitreṇa vāhanena surālayam
d sa tatra kāmaṃ krīḍitvā sevyamāno 'psarogaṇaiḥ
d iha rājā bhaved rājan nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
d pādapaṃ pallavākīrṇaṃ puṣpitaṃ phalitaṃ tathā
d gandhamālyair athābhyarcya vastrābharaṇabhūṣitam
d yaḥ prayacchati viprāya śrotriyāya sadakṣiṇam
d bhojayitvā yathākāmaṃ tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d jāmbūnadavicitreṇa vimānena virājatā
d puraṃdarapuraṃ yāti jayaśabdaravair yutaḥ
d tataḥ śakrapure ramye tasya kalpakapādapaḥ
d dadāti cepsitaṃ sarvaṃ manasā yad yad icchati
d yāvanti tasya patrāṇi puṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca
d tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate
d śakralokāvatīrṇaś ca mānuṣyaṃ lokam āgataḥ
d rathāśvagajasaṃpūrṇaṃ puraṃ rājyaṃ ca rakṣati
d sthāpayitvā tu madbhaktyā yo matpratikṛtiṃ naraḥ
d ālayaṃ vidhivat kṛtvā pūjākarma ca kārayet
d svayaṃ vā pūjayed bhaktyā tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d aśvamedhasahasrasya yat puṇyaṃ samudāhṛtam
d tat phalaṃ samavāpnoti matsālokyaṃ prapadyate
d na jāne nirgamaṃ tasya mama lokād yudhiṣṭhira
d devālaye vipragṛhe govāṭe catvare 'pi vā
d prajvālayati yo dīpaṃ tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d āruhya kāñcanaṃ yānaṃ dyotayan sarvatodiśam
d gacched ādityalokaṃ sa sevyamānaḥ surottamaiḥ
d tatra prakāmaṃ krīḍitvā varṣakoṭiṃ mahātapāḥ
d iha loke bhaved vipro vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ
d devālayeṣu vā rājan brāhmaṇāvasatheṣu vā
d catvare vā catuṣke vā rātrau vā yadi vā divā
d nānāgandharvavādyāni dharmaśrāvaṇikāni ca
d yas tu kārayate bhaktyā madgatenāntarātmanā
d tasya devā naraśreṣṭha pitaraś cāpi harṣitāḥ
d suprītāḥ saṃprayacchanti vimānaṃ kāmagaṃ śubham
d sa ca tena vimānena yāti devapuraṃ naraḥ
d tatra divyāpsarobhis tu sevyamānaḥ pramodate
d devalokāvatīrṇas tu so 'smiṃl loke narādhipa
d vedavedāṅgatattvajño bhogavān brāhmaṇo bhavet
d catvare vā sabhāyāṃ vā vistīrṇe vā sabhāṅgaṇe
d kṛtvāgnikuṇḍaṃ vipulaṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ vā yudhiṣṭhira
d tatrāgniṃ caturo māsāñ jvalayed yas tu bhaktimān
d samāpteṣu ca māseṣu pauṣyādiṣu tato dvijān
d bhojayet pāyasaṃ mṛṣṭaṃ madgatenāntarātmanā
d dakṣiṇāṃ ca yathāśakti brāhmaṇebhyo nivedayet
d evam agniṃ tu yaḥ kuryān nityam evārcayaṃs tu mām
d tasya puṇyaphalaṃ yad vai tan nibodha yudhiṣṭhira
d tenāhaṃ śaṃkaraś caiva pitaro hy agnayas tathā
d yāsyāmaḥ paramāṃ prītiṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
d ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣaśatāni ca
d so 'smat prītikaraḥ śrīmān mama loke mahīyate
d mama lokāvatīrṇaś ca so 'smiṃl loke mahāyaśāḥ
d vedavedāṅgavid vipro jāyate rājapūjitaḥ
d yaḥ karoti naraśreṣṭha bharaṇaṃ brāhmaṇasya tu
d śrotriyasyābhijātasya daridrasya viśeṣataḥ
d tasya puṇyaphalaṃ yad vai tan nibodha yudhiṣṭhira
d gavāṃ koṭipradānena yat puṇyaṃ samudāhṛtam
d tatpuṇyaphalam āpnoti varṣeṇaikena pāṇḍava
d kāñcanena vicitreṇa yānenāmbaraśobhinā
d sa yāti māmakaṃ lokaṃ divyastrīgaṇasevitaḥ
d gīyamāno varastrībhir varṣāṇāṃ koṭiviṃśatim
d krīḍitvā māmake loke tatra devair abhiṣṭutaḥ
d mānuṣyam avatīrṇas tu vedavid brāhmaṇo bhavet
d karakaṃ kuṇḍikāṃ vāpi mahad vā jalabhājanam
d yaḥ prayacchati viprāya tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d brahmakūrcena yat pīte phalaṃ proktaṃ yathāvidhi
d tat puṇyaphalam āpnoti jalabhājanado naraḥ
d sutṛptaḥ suprabhaḥ saumyaḥ prahṛṣṭendriyamānasaḥ
d haṃsasārasayuktena vimānena virājatā
d sa yāti vāruṇaṃ lokaṃ divyagandharvasevitaḥ
d pānīyaṃ yaḥ prayacched vai jīvānāṃ jīvanaṃ param
d grīṣmakeṣu ca māseṣu tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d kapilākoṭidānasya yat puṇyaṃ tu vidhīyate
d tatpuṇyaphalam āpnoti pānīyaṃ yaḥ prayacchati
d pūrṇacandraprakāśena vimānena virājatā
d sa gacchec cendrasadanaṃ sevyamāno 'psarogaṇaiḥ
d triṃśatkoṭiyugaṃ tatra divyagandharvasevitaḥ
d krīḍitvā mānuṣe loke caturvedī dvijo bhavet
d śiro 'bhyaṅgapradānena tejasvī priyadarśanaḥ
d subhago rūpavāñ śūraḥ paṇḍitaś ca bhaved dvijaḥ
d vastradāyī tu tejasvī sarvatra priyadarśanaḥ
d sukhabhogapatiḥ śrīmān strīṇāṃ nityaṃ manoramaḥ
d upānahau ca chattraṃ ca yo dadāti narottamaḥ
d sa yāti naramukhyena kāñcanena virājatā
d śakralokaṃ mahātejāḥ sevyamāno 'psarogaṇaiḥ
d kāṣṭhapādukado yāti vimānair vṛṣanirmitaiḥ
d dharmarājapuraṃ ramyaṃ sevyamāno 'psarottamaiḥ
d dantakāṣṭhapradānena priyavākyo bhaven naraḥ
d sugandhavadanaḥ śrīmān medhāsaubhāgyasaṃyutaḥ
d kṣīraṃ dadhi ghṛtaṃ vāpi guḍaṃ madhurasaṃ tathā
d ye prayacchanti viprebhyaḥ parāṃ bhaktiṃ gatā narāḥ
d te vṛṣair aśvayānaiś ca śvetasragdāmabhūṣitāḥ
d upagīyamānā gandharvair yāntīśvarapuraṃ narāḥ
d tatra divyāpsarobhis tu sevyamānā yathāsukham
d ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇi modante devasaṃnibhāḥ
d tataḥ kālāvatīrṇāś ca jāyante tv iha mānavāḥ
d prabhūtadhanadhānyāś ca bhogavanto narottamāḥ
d vaiśākhe māsi vaiśākhe divase pāṇḍunandana
d vaivasvataṃ samuddiśya parāṃ bhaktim upāgatāḥ
d abhyarcya vidhivad viprāṃs tilān guḍasamāyutān
d ye prayacchanti viprebhyas teṣāṃ puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d gopradānena yat puṇyaṃ vidhivat pāṇḍunandana
d tat puṇyaṃ samanuprāpto yamaloke mahīyate
d tataś cāpi cyutaḥ kālād iha rājā bhaviṣyati
d tasminn eva dine viprān bhojayitvā sadakṣiṇam
d toyapūrṇāni divyāni bhājanāni diśanti ye
d te yānty ādityavarṇābhair vimānair varuṇālayam
d tatra divyāṅganābhis tu ramante kāmakāminaḥ
d tato 'vatīrṇāḥ kālena te cāsmin mānuṣe punaḥ
d bhogavanto dvijaśreṣṭhā bhaviṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ
d anantarāśī yaś cāpi vartate vratavat sadā
d satyavāk krodharahitaḥ śuciḥ snānarataḥ sadā
d sa vimānena divyena yāti śakrapuraṃ naraḥ
d tatra divyāpsarobhis tu varṣakoṭiṃ mahātapāḥ
d krīḍitvā mānuṣe loke jāyate vedavid dvijaḥ
d ekabhuktena yaś cāpi varṣam ekaṃ tu vartate
d brahmacārī jitakrodhaḥ satyaśaucasamanvitaḥ
d sa vimānena divyena yāti śakrapuraṃ naraḥ
d daśakoṭisahasrāṇi krīḍitvāpsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ
d iha mānuṣyake loke brāhmaṇo vedavid bhavet
d caturthakālaṃ yo bhuṅkte brahmacārī jitendriyaḥ
d vartate caikavarṣaṃ tu tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d citrabarhiṇayuktena vicitradhvajaśobhinā
d yāti yānena divyena sa mahendrapuraṃ naraḥ
d akṛśābhir varastrībhiḥ sevyamāno yathāsukham
d tato dvādaśakoṭiṃ sa samāḥ samyak pramodate
d śakralokāvatīrṇaś ca loke cāsmin narādhipa
d bhaved vai brāhmaṇo vidvān kṣamāvān vedapāragaḥ
d ṣaṣṭhakāle tu yo 'śnāti varṣam ekam akalmaṣaḥ
d brahmacaryavratair yuktaḥ śuciḥ krodhavivarjitaḥ
d tapoyuktasya tasyātha śṛṇuṣva phalam uttamam
d atyādityaprakāśena vimānenārkasaṃnibhaḥ
d sa yāti mama lokān vai divyanārīniṣevitaḥ
d tatra sādhyair marudbhiś ca pūjyamāno yathāsukham
d paśyann eva sadā māṃ tu krīḍaty apsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ
d pakṣopavāsaṃ yaś cāpi kurute madgatātmanā
d samāpte tu vrate tasmiṃs tarpayec chrotriyān dvijān
d so 'pi gacchati divyena vimānena mahātapāḥ
d dyotayan prabhayā vyoma mama lokaṃ prapadyate
d sa tatra modate kāmaṃ kāmarūpī yathāsukham
d triṃśatkoṭisamā rājan krīḍitvā tatra devavat
d iha mānuṣyake loke pūjanīyo dvijo bhavet
d trayāṇām api vedānāṃ sāṅgānāṃ pārago bhavet
d yaś ca māsopavāsaṃ vai kurute madgatātmanā
d jitendriyo jitakrodho jitadhīḥ snānatatparaḥ
d samāpte niyame tatra bhojayitvā dvijottamān
d dakṣiṇāṃ ca tato dadyāt prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā
d sa gacchati mahātejā brahmalokam anuttamam
d siṃhayuktena yānena divyastrīgaṇasevitaḥ
d sa tatra brahmaṇo loke divyarṣigaṇasevitaḥ
d śatakoṭisamā rājan yathākāmaṃ pramodate
d tataḥ kālāvatīrṇaś ca so 'smiṃl loke dvijo bhavet
d ṣaḍaṅgavic caturvedī triṃśaj janmāny arogavān
d yas tyaktvā sarvakarmāṇi śuciḥ krodhavivarjitaḥ
d mahāprasthānam ekāgro yāti madgatamānasaḥ
d sa gacched indrasadanaṃ vimānena mahātapāḥ
d mahāmaṇivicitreṇa sauvarṇena virājatā
d śatakoṭisamās tatra surādhipatipūjitaḥ
d nākapṛṣṭhe nivasati divyastrīgaṇasevitaḥ
d śakralokāvatīrṇaś ca mānuṣeṣūpajāyate
d rājñāṃ rājā mahātejāḥ sarvalokārcitaḥ prabhuḥ
d prāyopaveśaṃ yaś cāpi kurute madgatātmanā
d namo brahmaṇyadevāyety uktvā mantraṃ samāhitaḥ
d antaḥsvastho jitakrodhas tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d kāmagaḥ kāmarūpī ca bālasūryasamaprabhaḥ
d sa vimānena divyena yāti lokān anāmayān
d svargāt svargaṃ mahātejā gatvā caiva yathāsukham
d mama lokeṣu ramate yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam
d agnipraveśaṃ yaś cāpi kurute madgatātmanā
d so 'pi yānena divyena mama lokaṃ prapadyate
d tataḥ sarvaguṇopetaḥ paśyann api sa māṃ sadā
d triṃśatkoṭisamā rājan modate mama saṃnidhau
d tato 'vatīrṇaḥ kālena vedavid brāhmaṇo bhavet
d karṣaṇaṃ sādhayan yas tu māṃ prasannaḥ śucivrataḥ
d namo brahmaṇyadevāyety etaṃ mantram udāharan
d bālasūryaprakāśena vimānena virājatā
d mama lokaṃ samāsādya ṣaṭkoṭiṃ tu pramodate
d mama lokāvatīrṇaś ca so 'smiṃl loke nṛpo bhavet
d niveśayati manmūrtyā ātmānaṃ madgataḥ śuciḥ
d rudradakṣiṇamūrtyāṃ vā caturdaśyāṃ viśeṣataḥ
d siddhair brahmarṣibhiś caiva devalokaiś ca pūjitaḥ
d gandharvair bhūtasaṃghaiś ca gīyamāno mahātapāḥ
d praviśet sa mahātejā māṃ vā śaṃkaram eva vā
d tasyāpunarbhavaṃ sic
rājan nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
d gokṛte strīkṛte caiva guruviprakṛte 'pi vā
d hanyante ye tu rājendra śakralokaṃ vrajanti te
d tatra jāmbūnadamaye vimāne kāmagāmini
d manvantaraṃ pramodante divyanārīniṣevitāḥ
d āśrutasyāpradānena dattasya haraṇena ca
d janmaprabhṛti yad dattaṃ sarvaṃ naśyati bhārata
d nāgopradās tatra payaḥ pibanti
d nābhūmidā bhūmim athāśnuvanti
d yān yān kāmān brāhmaṇebhyo dadāti
d tāṃs tān kāmān svargaloke ca bhuṅkte
d yad yad iṣṭatamaṃ dravyaṃ nyāyenopārjitaṃ ca yat
d tat tad guṇavate deyaṃ tad evākṣayam icchatā
d anupoṣya trirātrāṇi tīrthāny anabhigamya ca
d adattvā kāñcanaṃ gāṃ ca daridro nāma jāyate
d dānaṃ yat tat phalaṃ naiti śrotriyāya na dīyate
d śrotriyā yatra nāśnanti na devās tatra bhuñjate
d śrotriyebhyaḥ paraṃ nāsti paramaṃ daivataṃ mahat
d nidhānaṃ cāpi rājendra tasmāc chrotriyabhojanāt
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d viprayoge śarīrasya sendriyasya viśeṣataḥ
d bhagavān uvāca
d antarā vartamānasya gatiḥ prāṇasya kīdṛśī
d śubhāśubhakṛtaṃ sarvaṃ prāpnotīha phalaṃ naraḥ
d na tu sarvasya bhūtasya pañcatvaṃ vāpi vidyate
d pañcatvaṃ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha bhūribhūtikaraṃ nṛṇām
d teṣāṃ pañca mahāyajñān ye kurvanti dvijottamāḥ
d pañcatvaṃ pañcabhir bhūtair viyogaṃ saṃpracakṣate
d na jāyate na mriyate puruṣaḥ śāśvataḥ sadā
d prāyeṇa maraṇaṃ nāma pāpinām eva pāṇḍava
d yeṣāṃ tu na gatiḥ puṇyā teṣāṃ maraṇam ucyate
d prāyeṇākṛtakṛtyās tu mṛtyor udvijate janaḥ
d kṛtakṛtyāḥ pratīkṣante mṛtyuṃ priyam ivātithim
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d pañca yajñāḥ kathaṃ deva kriyante 'tra dvijātibhiḥ
d bhagavān uvāca
d teṣāṃ nāma ca deveśa vaktum arhasy aśeṣataḥ
d śṛṇu pañca mahāyajñān kīrtyamānān yudhiṣṭhira
d yair eva brahmasālokyaṃ labhyate gṛhamedhinā
d ṛṣiyajñaṃ brahmayajñaṃ bhūtayajñaṃ ca pārthiva
d nṛyajñaṃ pitṛyajñaṃ ca pañca yajñān pracakṣate
d tarpaṇaṃ ṛṣiyajñaṃ syāt svādhyāyo brahmayajñakaḥ
d bhūtayajño balir yajño nṛyajño 'tithipūjanam
d pitṝn uddiśya yat karma pitṛyajñaḥ prakīrtitaḥ
d hutaṃ cāpy ahutaṃ caiva tathā prahutam eva ca
d prāśitaṃ balidānaṃ ca pākayajñān pracakṣate
d vaiśvadevādayo homā hutam ity ucyate budhaiḥ
d ahutaṃ ca bhaved dattaṃ prahutaṃ brāhmaṇāśitam
d prāṇāgnihotrahomaṃ ca prāśitaṃ vidhivad viduḥ
d balikarma ca rājendra pākayajñāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
d ke cit pañca mahāyajñān pākayajñān pracakṣate
d apare brahmayajñādīn mahāyajñavido viduḥ
d sarva ete mahāyajñāḥ sarvathā parikīrtitāḥ
d bubhukṣitān brāhmaṇāṃs tu yathāśakti na hāpayet
d ahany ahani ye tv etān akṛtvā bhuñjate svayam
d kevalaṃ malam aśnanti te narā na ca saṃśayaḥ
d tasmāt snātvā dvijo vidvān kuryād etān dine dine
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d ato 'nyathā tu bhuñjan vai prāyaścittīyate dvijaḥ
d devadeva namas te 'stu tvadbhaktasya janārdana
d bhagavān uvāca
d vaktum arhasi deveśa snānasya ca vidhiṃ mama
d śṛṇu pāṇḍava tat sarvaṃ pavitraṃ pāpanāśanam
d snātvā yena vidhānena mucyante kilbiṣād dvijāḥ
d mṛdaṃ ca gomayaṃ caiva tilān darbhāṃs tathaiva ca
d puṣpāṇy api yathānyāyam ādāya tu jalaṃ vrajet
d nadyāṃ satyāṃ na ca snāyād anyatra dvijasattama
d sati prabhūte payasi nālpe snāyāt kadā cana
d gatvodakasamīpaṃ tu śucau deśe manohare
d tato mṛdgomayādīni tatra prokṣya vinikṣipet
d bahiḥ prakṣālya pādau ca dvir ācamya prayatnataḥ
d pradakṣiṇaṃ samāvṛtya namaskuryāt tu taj jalam
d na ca prakṣālayet tīrtham adbhir vidvān kadā cana
d na ca pādena vā hanyād dhastenānyena taj jalam
d sarvadevamayā hy āpo manmayāḥ pāṇḍunandana
d tasmāt tās tu na hantavyās tv adbhiḥ prakṣālayet sthalam
d kevalaṃ prathamaṃ majjen nāṅgāni vimṛjed budhaḥ
d tat tu tīrthaṃ samāsādya kuryād ācamanaṃ punaḥ
d gokarṇākṛtivat kṛtvā karaṃ triḥ prapibej jalam
d dvis tat parimṛjed vaktraṃ pādāv abhyukṣya cātmanaḥ
d śīrṣaṇyāṃs tu tataḥ prāṇān sakṛd eva tu saṃspṛśet
d bāhū dvau ca tataḥ spṛṣṭvā hṛdayaṃ nābhim eva ca
d pratyaṅgam udakaṃ spṛṣṭvā mūrdhānaṃ tu punaḥ spṛśet
d āpaḥ punāntv ity uktvā ca punar ācamanaṃ caret
d soṃkārā vyāhṛtīr vāpi sadasaspatim ity ṛcam
d ācamya mṛttikāḥ paścāt tridhā kṛtvā samālabhet
d ṛcedaṃ viṣṇur ity aṅgam uttamādhamamadhyamam
d ālabhya vāruṇaiḥ sūktair namaskṛtya jalaṃ tataḥ
d sravantī cet pratisrotaḥ pratyarkaṃ cānyavāriṣu
d majjed om ity udāhṛtya na ca prakṣobhayej jalam
d gomayaṃ ca tridhā kṛtvā jale pūrvaṃ samālabhet
d savyāhṛtiṃ sapraṇavāṃ gāyatrīṃ ca japet punaḥ
d punar ācamanaṃ kṛtvā madgatenāntarātmanā
d āpo hi ṣṭheti tisṛbhir darbhapūtena vāriṇā
d tathā tarat samandībhiḥ siñcec catasṛbhiḥ kramāt
d gosūktenāśvasūktena śuddhavargeṇa cāpy atha
d vaiṣṇavair vāruṇaiḥ sūktaiḥ sāvitrair indradevataiḥ
d vāmadevena cātmānam anyair manmayasāmabhiḥ
d sthitvāntaḥsalile sūktaṃ japed vācāghamarṣaṇam
d savyāhṛtiṃ sapraṇavāṃ gāyatrīṃ vā tato japet
d ā śvāsamokṣāt praṇavaṃ japed vā mām anusmaran
d utplutya tīrtham āsādya dhaute śukle ca vāsasī
d śuddhe cācchādayet kakṣe na kuryāt paripāśake
d pāśe nibaddhakakṣyo yat kurute karma vaidikam
d rākṣasā dānavā daityās tad vilumpanti harṣitāḥ
d tasmāt sarvaprayatnena kakṣyāṃ pāśe na dhārayet
d tataḥ prakṣālya pādau ca hastau caiva mṛdā śanaiḥ
d ācamya punar ācāmet tataḥ sāvitriyā dvijaḥ
d jale jalagataḥ śuddhaḥ sthala eva sthale sthitaḥ
d ubhayatra sthitas tasmād ācāmed ātmaśuddhaye
d darbheṣu darbhapāṇiḥ san prāṅmukhaḥ susamāhitaḥ
d prāṇāyāmāṃs tataḥ kuryān madgatenāntarātmanā
d sahasrakṛtvaḥ sāvitrīṃ śatakṛtvas tu vā japet
d samāpte tu jape tasmin sāvitryā cābhimantrya ca
d mandehānāṃ vināśāya rakṣasāṃ vikṣipej jalam
d udvargo 'sīty athācāntaḥ prāyaścittajalaṃ kṣipet
d athādāya sapuṣpāṇi toyāny añjalinā dvijaḥ
d prakṣipya pratisūryaṃ ca vyomamudrāṃ prakalpayet
d tato dvādaśakṛtvas tu sūryasyaikākṣaraṃ japet
d tataḥ ṣaḍakṣarādīni ṣaṭkṛtvaḥ parivartayet
d pradakṣiṇaṃ parāmṛśya mudrayā svamukhaṃ tayā
d ūrdhvabāhus tato bhūtvā sūryam īkṣet samāhitaḥ
d tanmaṇḍalasthaṃ māṃ dhyāyet tejomūrtiṃ caturbhujam
d ud u tyaṃ ca japen mantraṃ citraṃ taccakṣur ity api
d sāvitrīṃ ca yathāśakti japtvā sūktaṃ ca māmakam
d manmayāni ca sāmāni puruṣavratam eva ca
d tataś cālokayed arkaṃ haṃsaḥ śuciṣad ity ṛcā
d pradakṣiṇaṃ samāvṛtya namaskṛtya divākaram
d tatas tu tarpayed adbhiḥ brahmāṇaṃ māṃ ca śaṃkaram
d prajāpatiṃ ca devāṃś ca tathā devamunīn api
d sāṅgān api tathā vedān itihāsān kratūṃs tathā
d purāṇāni ca divyāni kulāny apsarasāṃ tathā
d ṛtūn saṃvatsarāṃś caiva kalākāṣṭhāntakaṃ tathā
d bhūtagrāmāṃś ca bhūtāni saritaḥ sāgarāṃs tathā
d śailāñ śailasthitān devān oṣadhīḥ savanaspatīḥ
d tarpayed upavītī tu pratyekaṃ tṛpyatām iti
d anvārabhya ca savyena pāṇinā dakṣiṇena tu
d nivītī tarpayet paścād ṛṣīn mantrakṛtas tathā
d marīcyādīn ṛṣīṃś caiva nāradāntān samāhitaḥ
d prācīnāvīty athaitāṃs tu tarpayed devatāḥ pitṝn
d tatas tu kavyavāḍ agniṃ somaṃ vaivasvataṃ tathā
d tataś cāryamaṇaṃ cāpi agniṣv āttāṃs tathaiva ca
d somapāṃś caiva darbhais tu satilair eva vāribhiḥ
d tṛpyadhvam iti paścāt tu svapitṝṃs tarpayet tataḥ
d pitṝn pitāmahāṃś caiva tathaiva prapitāmahān
d pitāmahīṃ tathā cāpi tathaiva prapitāmahīm
d tathā pitṛṣvasṝś caiva mātṛṣvasṝs tathaiva ca
d mātaraṃ cātmanaś caiva tathā mātāmahīm api
d mātur mātāmahīṃ caiva gurum ācāryam eva ca
d upādhyāyān sakhīn bandhūñ śiṣyartvigjñātiputrakān
d pramītān ānṛśaṃsyārthaṃ tarpayet tān amatsaraḥ
d tarpayitvā tathācamya snānavastraṃ prapīḍayet
d vṛddhiṃ bhṛtyajanasyāhuḥ snātakānāṃ ca tadvidaḥ
d atarpayitvā tān pūrvaṃ snānavastraṃ na pīḍayet
d pīḍayec cet purā mohād devāḥ sarṣigaṇās tathā
d pitaras tu nirāśāś ca śaptvā yānti yathāgatam
d prakṣālya tu mṛdā pādāv ācamya prayataḥ punaḥ
d darbheṣu darbhapāṇiḥ san svādhyāyaṃ tu samārabhet
d vedam ādau samārabhya tatopari padakramān
d yad adhīte svayaṃ śaktyā tat svādhyāyaṃ pracakṣate
d ṛcaṃ vātha yajur vāpi sāmagāthām athāpi vā
d itihāsapurāṇāni yathāśakti na hāpayet
d utthāya ca namaskṛtvā diśo digdevatā api
d brahmāṇaṃ ca tataś cāgniṃ pṛthivīm oṣadhīs tathā
d vācaṃ vācaspatiṃ caiva māṃ caiva saritas tathā
d namaskṛtvā tathādbhis tu praṇavādi ca pūjayet
d tato namo 'dbhya ity uktvā namaskuryāt tu taj jalam
d ghṛṇiḥ sūryas tathādityas tān praṇamya svamūrdhani
d tatas tv ālokayann arkaṃ praṇavena samāhitaḥ
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d tato mām arcayet puṣpair matpriyair eva nityaśaḥ
d tvatpriyāṇi prasūnāni tvadadhiṣṭhāni mādhava
d bhagavān uvāca
d sarvāṇy ācakṣva deveśa tvadbhaktasya mamācyuta
d śṛṇuṣvāvahito rājan puṣpāṇi prītikṛnti me
d kumudaṃ karavīraṃ ca caṇakaṃ campakaṃ tathā
d mallikājātipuṣpaṃ ca nandyāvartaṃ ca nandikam
d palāśapuṣpapatrāṇi dūrvā bhṛṅgakam eva ca
d vanamālā ca rājendra matpriyāṇi viśeṣataḥ
d sarveṣām api puṣpāṇāṃ sahasraguṇam utpalam
d tasmāt padmaṃ tathā rājan padmāt tu śatapatrakam
d tasmāt sahasrapatraṃ tu puṇḍarīkaṃ tataḥ param
d puṇḍarīkasahasrāt tu tulasī guṇato 'dhikā
d bakapuṣpaṃ tatas tasmāt sauvarṇaṃ tu tato 'dhikam
d sauvarṇāt tu prasūnāc ca matpriyaṃ nāsti pāṇḍava
d puṣpālābhe tulasyāstu patrair mām arcayed budhaḥ
d patrālābhe tu śākhābhiḥ śākhālābhe śiphāphalaiḥ
d śiphālābhe mṛdā tatra bhaktimān arcayed budhaḥ
d varjanīyāni puṣpāṇi śṛṇu rājan samāhitaḥ
d kiṅkiṇī munipuṣpaṃ ca duttūraṃ pāṭalaṃ tathā
d tathātimuktakaṃ caiva puṃnāgaṃ naktamālikā
d yaudhikaṃ kṣīrikāpuṣpaṃ nirguṇḍī lāṅgalī japā
d karṇikāraṃ tathāśokaṃ śalmalīpuṣpam eva ca
d kakubhāḥ kovidārāś ca vaibhītakam athāpi vā
d kuraṇṭakaprasūnāṃ ca tilvakaṃ lāṅgalī tathā
d aṅkolaṃ girikarṇī ca nīlāny eva ca sarvaśaḥ
d ekavarṇāni cānyāni sarvāṇy eva vivarjayet
d arkapuṣpāṇi varjyāni cārkapatrasthitāni ca
d vyāghātapicumandāni sarvāṇy eva vivarjayet
d anyais tu śuklapatrais tu gandhavadbhir narādhipa
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d avarjyais tair yathālābhaṃ madbhakto māṃ samarcayet
d kathaṃ tvam arcanīyo 'si mūrtayaḥ kīdṛśās tu te
d vaikhānasāḥ kathaṃ brūyuḥ kathaṃ vā pāñcarātrikāḥ
d bhagavān uvāca
d śṛṇu pāṇḍava tat sarvam arcanākramam ātmanaḥ
d sthaṇḍile padmakaṃ kṛtvā cāṣṭapatraṃ sakarṇikam
d aṣṭākṣaravidhānena hy atha vā dvādaśākṣaraiḥ
d vaidikair atha vā mantrair mama sūktena vā punaḥ
d sthāpitaṃ māṃ tatas tasminn arcayitvā vicakṣaṇaḥ
d puruṣaṃ ca tataḥ satyam acyutaṃ ca yudhiṣṭhira
d aniruddhaṃ ca māṃ prāhur vaikhānasavido janāḥ
d anye tv evaṃ vijānanti māṃ rājan pāñcarātrikāḥ
d vāsudevaṃ ca rājendra saṃkarṣaṇam athāpi vā
d pradyumnaṃ cāniruddhaṃ ca caturmūrtiṃ pracakṣate
d etāś cānyāś ca rājendra saṃjñābhedena mūrtayaḥ
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d viddhy anarthāntarā eva mām evaṃ cārcayed budhaḥ
d tvadbhaktāḥ kīdṛśā deva kāni teṣāṃ vratāni ca
d bhagavān uvāca
d etat kathaya deveśa tvadbhaktasya mamācyuta
d ananyadevatābhaktā ye madbhaktajanapriyāḥ
d mām eva śaraṇaṃ prāptās te madbhaktāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
d svargāṇy api yaśasyāni matpriyāṇi viśeṣataḥ
d madbhaktaḥ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha vratānīmāni dhārayet
d nānyad ācchādayed vastraṃ madbhakto jalatāraṇe
d svasthas tu na divā svapyān madhumāṃsāni varjayet
d pradakṣiṇaṃ vrajed viprān gām aśvatthaṃ hutāśanam
d na dhāvet patite varṣe nāgrabhikṣāṃ ca lopayet
d pratyakṣalavaṇaṃ nādyāt saubhañjanakagṛñjanau
d grāsamuṣṭiṃ gave dadyād dhānyāmlaṃ caiva varjayet
d tathā paryuṣitaṃ cāpi pakvaṃ parigṛhāgatam
d aniveditaṃ ca yad dravyaṃ tat prayatnena varjayet
d vibhītakakarañjānāṃ chāyāṃ dūraṃ vivarjayet
d vipradevaparīvādaṃ na vadet pīḍito 'pi san
d sāttvikā rājasāś cāpi tāmasāś cāpi pāṇḍava
d mām arcayanti madbhaktās teṣām īdṛgvidhā gatiḥ
d tāmasās timiraṃ yānti rājasā raja eva tat
d sāttvikāḥ sattvasaṃpannāḥ sattvam eva prayānti te
d ye siddhāḥ santi sāṃkhyena yogasattvabalena ca
d nabhasādityacandrābhyāṃ paśyanti padavistaram
d ekastambhe navadvāre tristhūṇe pañcadhātuke
d etasmin dehanagare rājasas tu sadā bhavet
d udite savitary asya kriyāyuktasya dhīmataḥ
d caturvedavidaś cāpi dehe ṣaḍ vṛṣalāḥ smṛtāḥ
d kṣatriyāḥ sapta vijñeyā vaiśyās tv aṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ
d niyatāḥ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha śūdrāṇām ekaviṃśatiḥ
d kāmaḥ krodhaś ca lobhaś ca mohaś ca mada eva ca
d mahāmohaś ca ity ete dehe ṣaḍ vṛṣalāḥ smṛtāḥ
d garvaḥ stambho hy ahaṃkāra īrṣyā ca droha eva ca
d pāruṣyaṃ krūratā ceti saptaite kṣatriyāḥ smṛtāḥ
d tīkṣṇatā nikṛtir māyā śāṭhyaṃ ḍambho hy anārjavam
d paiśunyam anṛtaṃ caiva vaiśyās tv aṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ
d tṛṣṇā bubhukṣā nidrā ca ālasyaṃ cāghṛṇādayā
d ādhiś cāpi vivādaś ca pramādo hīnasattvatā
d bhayaṃ viklabatā jāḍyaṃ pāpakaṃ manyur eva ca
d āśā cāśraddadhānatvam anavasthāpy ayantraṇam
d āśaucaṃ malinatvaṃ ca śūdrā hy ete prakīrtitāḥ
d yasminn ete na dṛśyante sa vai brāhmaṇa ucyate
d yeṣu yeṣu hi bhāveṣu yatkālaṃ vartate dvijaḥ
d tattatkālaṃ sa vijñeyaḥ brāhmaṇo jñānadurbalaḥ
d prāṇān āyamya yatkālaṃ yena māṃ cāpi cintayet
d tatkāle vai dvijo jñeyaḥ śeṣakālo hy athetaraḥ
d tasmāt tu sāttviko bhūtvā śuciḥ krodhavivarjitaḥ
d mām arcayet tu satataṃ matpriyatvaṃ yad icchati
d alolajihvaḥ samupasthito dhṛtir
d nidhāya cakṣur yugamātram eva ca
d manaś ca vācaṃ ca nigṛhya cañcalaṃ
d bhayān nivṛtto mama bhakta ucyate
d īdṛśādhyātmino ye tu brāhmaṇā niyatendriyāḥ
d teṣāṃ śrāddheṣu tṛpyanti tena tṛptāḥ pitāmahāḥ
d dharmo jayati nādharmaḥ satyaṃ jayati nānṛtam
d kṣamā jayati na krodhaḥ kṣamāvān brāhmaṇo bhavet
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d dānapuṇyaphalaṃ śrutvā tapaḥ puṇyaphalāni ca
d dharmaputraḥ prahṛṣṭātmā keśavaṃ punar abravīt
d yā caiṣā kapilā deva pūrvam utpāditā vibho
d homadhenuḥ sadā puṇyā caturvaktreṇa mādhava
d sā kathaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo hi deyā kasmin dine 'pi vā
d kīdṛśāya ca viprāya dātavyā puṇyalakṣaṇā
d kati vā kapilāḥ proktāḥ svayam eva svayaṃbhuvā
d kair vā deyāś ca tā deva śrotum icchāmi tattvataḥ
d evam ukto hṛṣīkeśo dharmaputreṇa saṃsadi
d abravīt kapilāsaṃkhyāṃ tāsāṃ māhātmyam eva ca
d śṛṇu pāṇḍava tattvena pavitraṃ pāvanaṃ param
d yac chrutvā pāpakarmāpi naraḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyate
d agnimadhyodbhavāṃ divyām agnijvālāsamaprabhām
d agnijvālojjvalacchṛṅgīṃ pradīptāṅgāralocanām
d agnipucchām agnikhurām agniromaprabhānvitām
d tām āgneyīm agnijihvām agnigrīvāṃ jvalatprabhām
d bhuñjate kapilāṃ ye tu śūdrā lobhena mohitāḥ
d patitāṃs tān vijānīyāc caṇḍālasadṛśā hi te
d na teṣāṃ brāhmaṇaḥ kaś cid gṛhe kuryāt pratigraham
d dūrāc ca parihartavyā mahāpātakino 'pi te
d sarvakālaṃ hi te sarvair varjitāḥ pitṛdaivataiḥ
d te sadā hy apratigrāhyā hy asaṃbhāṣyāś ca pāpinaḥ
d pibanti kapilāṃ yāvat tāvat teṣāṃ pitāmahāḥ
d amedhyam upabhuñjanti bhūmyāṃ vai śvasṛgālavat
d kapilāyā ghṛtaṃ kṣīraṃ dadhi takram athāpi vā
d ye śūdrā upabhuñjanti teṣāṃ gatim imāṃ śṛṇu
d kapilopajīvī śūdras tu mṛto gacchati rauravam
d kliśyate raurave ghore varṣakoṭiśataṃ vasan
d rauravāc ca paribhraṣṭo viṣṭhāyāṃ jāyate krimiḥ
d viṣṭhāgarteṣu saṃviṣṭo durgandheṣu sahasraśaḥ
d tatraiva jāyamāno 'sau nottāraṃ tatra vindati
d brāhmaṇaś caiva yas teṣāṃ gṛhe kuryāt pratigraham
d tataḥ prabhṛti tasyāpi pitaraḥ syur amedhyapāḥ
d na tena sārdhaṃ saṃbhāṣen na cāpy ekāsanaṃ vrajet
d sa nityaṃ varjanīyo hi dūrāt tu brāhmaṇādhamaḥ
d yas tena saha saṃbhāṣed ekaśayyāṃ vrajeta vā
d prājāpatyaṃ caret kṛcchraṃ sa ca tenaiva śudhyati
d kapilopajīvinaḥ śūdrād yaḥ karoti pratigraham
d prāyaścittaṃ bhavet tasya viprasyaitan na saṃśayaḥ
d brahmakūrcaṃ tu kurvīta cāndrāyaṇam athāpi vā
d mucyate kilbiṣāt tasmād etena brāhmaṇo hi saḥ
d kapilā hy agnihotrārthe yajñārthe ca svayaṃbhuvā
d sarvatas teja uddhṛtya brahmaṇā nirmitā purā
d pavitraṃ ca pavitrāṇāṃ maṅgalānāṃ ca maṅgalam
d puṇyānāṃ paramaṃ puṇyaṃ kapilā pāṇḍunandana
d tapasāṃ tapa evāgryaṃ vratānāṃ vratam uttamam
d dānānāṃ paramaṃ dānaṃ nidānaṃ hy etad akṣayam
d pṛthivyāṃ yāni tīrthāni puṇyāny āyatanāni ca
d pavitrāṇi ca ramyāṇi sarvalokeṣu pāṇḍava
d tebhyas tejaḥ samuddhṛtya brahmaṇā lokakartṛṇā
d lokanistāraṇāyaiva nirmitāḥ kapilāḥ svayam
d sarvatejomayī hy eṣā kapilā pāṇḍunandana
d sadāmṛtamayī medhyā śuciḥ pāvanam uttamam
d kṣīreṇa kapilāyās tu dadhnā vai saghṛtena vā
d hotavyāny agnihotrāṇi sāyaṃ prātar dvijātibhiḥ
d kapilāyā ghṛtenāpi dadhnā kṣīreṇa vā punaḥ
d juhvate ye 'gnihotrāṇi brāhmaṇā vidhivat prabho
d pūjayanty atithīṃś caiva parāṃ bhaktim upāgatāḥ
d śūdrānnād viratā nityaṃ ḍambhānṛtavivarjitāḥ
d te yānty ādityasaṃkāśair vimānair dvijasattamāḥ
d sūryamaṇḍalamadhyena brahmalokam anuttamam
d brahmaṇo bhavane divye kāmagāḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
d brahmaṇā pūjyamānās tu modante kalpam akṣayam
d evaṃ hi kapilā rājan puṇyā mantrāmṛtāraṇiḥ
d ādāv evāgnimadhyāt tu maitreyī brahmanirmitā
d śṛṅgāgre kapilāyās tu sarvatīrthāni pāṇḍava
d brahmaṇo hi niyogena nivasanti dine dine
d prātar utthāya yo martyaḥ kapilāśṛṅgamastakāt
d cyutā āpas tu śīrṣeṇa prayato dhārayec chuciḥ
d sa tena puṇyatīrthena sahasā dagdhakilbiṣaḥ
d varṣatrayakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ pradahaty agnivat tṛṇam
d mūtreṇa kapilāyās tu yas tu prātar upaspṛśet
d snānena tena puṇyena naṣṭapāpaḥ sa mānavaḥ
d triṃśadvarṣakṛtāt pāpān mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
d prātar utthāya yo bhaktyā prayacchet tṛṇamuṣṭikam
d tasya naśyati tat pāpaṃ triṃśadrātrikṛtaṃ nṛpa
d prātar utthāya madbhaktyā kuryād yas tāṃ pradakṣiṇam
d pradakṣiṇīkṛtā tena pṛthivī nātra saṃśayaḥ
d pradakṣiṇena caikena śraddhāyuktasya pāṇḍava
d daśarātrakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tasya tan naśyati dhruvam
d kapilāpañcagavyena yaḥ snāyāt tu śucir naraḥ
d sa gaṅgādyeṣu tīrtheṣu snāto bhavati pāṇḍava
d tena snānena tasyāpi śraddhāyuktasya pāṇḍava
d daśarātrakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva naśyati
d dṛṣṭvā tu kapilāṃ bhaktyā śrutvā humbhāravaṃ tathā
d vyapohati naraḥ pāpam ahorātrakṛtaṃ nṛpa
d yatra vā tatra vā cāṅge kapilāṃ yaḥ spṛśec chuciḥ
d saṃvatsarakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ vināśayati pāṇḍava
d gosahasraṃ ca yo dadyād ekāṃ ca kapilāṃ naraḥ
d samaṃ tasya phalaṃ prāha brahmaloke pitāmahaḥ
d yas tv ekāṃ kapilāṃ hanyān naraḥ kiṃ cit pramādataḥ
d gosahasraṃ hataṃ tena bhaven nātra vicāraṇā
d yaś caikāṃ kapilāṃ dadyāc chrotriyāyāhitāgnaye
d gavāṃ śatasahasraṃ tu dattaṃ bhavati pāṇḍava
d daśaiva kapilāḥ proktāḥ svayam eva svayaṃbhuvā
d yo dadyāc chrotriyebhyo vai svargaṃ gacchati tac chṛṇu
d prathamā svarṇakapilā dvitīyā gaurapiṅgalā
d tṛtīyā raktapiṅgākṣī caturthī galapiṅgalā
d pañcamī babhruvarṇābhā ṣaṣṭhī ca śvetapiṅgalā
d saptamī raktapiṅgākṣī aṣṭamī khurapiṅgalā
d navamī pāṭalā jñeyā daśamī pucchapiṅgalā
d daśaitāḥ kapilāḥ proktās tārayanti narān sadā
d maṅgalyāś ca pavitrāś ca sarvapāpapraṇāśanāḥ
d evam eva hy anaḍvāho daśa proktā nareśvara
d brāhmaṇo vāhayet tāṃs tu nānyo varṇaḥ kathaṃ cana
d na ghātayet tu daṇḍena kṣetre vādhvani vā dvijaḥ
d vāhayed dhuṃkṛtenaiva śākhayā vā sapatrayā
d na daṇḍena na yaṣṭyā vā na pāśena ca vā punaḥ
d na kṣuttṛṣṇāśramaśrāntān vāhayed vikalendriyān
d atṛpteṣu na bhuñjīyāt pibet pīteṣu codakam
d śuśrūṣor mātaraś caitāḥ pitaras te prakīrtitāḥ
d ahnāṃ pūrve tribhāge tu dhuryāṇāṃ vāhanaṃ smṛtam
d viśrāmen madhyame bhāge bhāge cānte yathāsukham
d yatra vā tvarayā kṛtyaṃ saṃśayo yatra vādhvani
d vāhayet tatra dhuryāṃs tu na sa pāpena lipyate
d anyathā vāhayan rājan nirayaṃ yāti rauravam
d rudhiraṃ pātayet teṣāṃ yas tu mohān narādhipa
d brahmahatyāsamaṃ pāpaṃ tasya syāt pāṇḍunandana
d tena pāpena pāpātmā nirayaṃ yāty asaṃśayam
d narakeṣu ca sarveṣu samāsthitvā śataṃ śatam
d iha mānuṣyake loke balīvardo bhaviṣyati
d tasmāt tu muktim anvicchan dadyāt tu kapilāṃ naraḥ
d kapilāṃ vāhayed yas tu vṛṣalo lobhamohitaḥ
d tena devās trayastriṃśat pitaraś cāpi vāhitāḥ
d sa devaiḥ pitṛbhir nityaṃ vadhyamānaḥ sudurmatiḥ
d narakān narakaṃ ghoraṃ gacched āpralayaṃ nṛpa
d brahmā rudras tathāgniś ca kapilānāṃ gatiṃ gatāḥ
d tasmāt te tu na hantavyāḥ pūjyās te tu viśeṣataḥ
d niḥśvasanti yadā śrāntās tadā hanyuś ca tat kulam
d yāvanti teṣāṃ romāṇi tāvad varṣaśataṃ nṛpa
d narake paripacyante tatra tadvāhakā narāḥ
d kapilā sarvayajñeṣu dakṣiṇārthaṃ vidhīyate
d tasmāt tā dakṣiṇā deyā yajñeṣv eva dvijātibhiḥ
d homārthaṃ cāgnihotrasya yāṃ prayacchet prayatnataḥ
d śrotriyāya daridrāya śrāntāyāmitatejase
d tena dānena pūtātmā so 'gniloke mahīyate
d yāvanti caiva romāṇi kapilāṅge yudhiṣṭhira
d tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi naraḥ svarge ca vartate
d suvarṇakhuraśṛṅgīṃ ca kapilāṃ yaḥ prayacchati
d viṣuve cāyane vāpi so 'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet
d tenāśvamedhatulyena mama lokaṃ sa gacchati
d svarṇaśṛṅgīṃ rūpyakhurāṃ savatsāṃ kāṃsyadohinīm
d vastrair alaṃkṛtāṃ puṣṭāṃ gandhair mālyaiś ca śobhitām
d pavitraṃ hi pavitrāṇāṃ suvarṇam iti me matiḥ
d tasmāt suvarṇābharaṇā dātavyā cāgnihotriṇe
d evaṃ dattvā tu rājendra saptapūrvān parān api
d tārayiṣyati rājendra nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
d agniṣṭomasahasrasya vājapeyasamaṃ bhavet
d vājapeyasahasrasya aśvamedhaṃ ca tatsamam
d aśvamedhasahasraṃ ca rājasūyaṃ ca tatsamam
d kapilānāṃ sahasreṇa vidhidattena pāṇḍava
d rājasūyaphalaṃ prāpya mama loke mahīyate
d na tasya punarāvṛttir vidyate kurupuṃgava
d prayacchate yaḥ kapilāṃ savatsāṃ kāṃsyadohinīm
d tais tair guṇaiḥ kāmadughā ca bhūtvā
d naraṃ pradātāram upaiti sā gauḥ
d svakarmabhiś cāpy anubadhyamānaṃ
d tīvrāndhakāre narake patantam
d mahārṇave naur iva vāyunītā
d dattā hi gaus tārayate manuṣyam
d putrāṃś ca pautrāṃś ca kulaṃ ca sarvam
d āsaptamaṃ tārayate paratra
d yāvan manuṣyān pṛthivīṃ bibharti
d tāvat pradātāram ito 'paratra
d yathauṣadhaṃ mantrakṛtaṃ narasya
d prayuktamātraṃ vinihanti rogān
d tathaiva dattā kapilā supātre
d pāpaṃ narasyāśu nihanti sarvam
d yathaiva dṛṣṭvā bhujagāḥ suparṇaṃ
d naśyanti dūrād vivaśā bhayārtāḥ
d tathaiva dṛṣṭvā kapilāpradānaṃ
d naśyanti pāpāni narasya śīghram
d yathā tvacaṃ svāṃ bhujago vihāya
d punar navaṃ rūpam upaiti puṇyam
d tathaiva muktaḥ puruṣaḥ svapāpair
d virājate vai kapilāpradānāt
d yathāndhakāraṃ bhavane vilagnaṃ
d dīpto hi niryātayati pradīpaḥ
d tathā naraḥ pāpam api pralīnaṃ
d niṣkrāmayed vai kapilāpradānam
d yāvanti romāṇi bhavanti tasyā
d vatsānvitāyāś ca śarīrajāni
d tāvat pradātā yugavarṣakoṭiṃ
d sa brahmaloke ramate manuṣyaḥ
d yasyāhitāgner atithipriyasya
d śūdrānnadūrasya jitendriyasya
d satyavratasyādhyayanānvitasya
d dattā hi gaus tārayate paratra
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d evaṃ śrutvā paraṃ puṇyaṃ kapilādānam uttamam
d dharmaputraḥ prahṛṣṭātmā keśavaṃ punar abravīt
d devadeveśa kapilā yadā viprāya dīyate
d kathaṃ sarveṣu cāṅgeṣu tasyās tiṣṭhanti devatāḥ
d yāś caitāḥ kapilāḥ proktā daśa caiva tvayā mama
d tāsāṃ kati suraśreṣṭha kapilāḥ puṇyalakṣaṇāḥ
d kathaṃ vānugṛhītās tāḥ suraiḥ pitṛgaṇair api
d kena yuktāś ca varṇena śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me
d yudhiṣṭhireṇaivam uktaḥ keśavaḥ satyavāk tadā
d guhyānāṃ paramaṃ guhyaṃ vaktum evopacakrame
d śṛṇu rājan pavitraṃ vai rahasyaṃ dharmam uttamam
d grahaṇīyaṃ satyam idaṃ na śrāvyaṃ hetuvādinām
d yadā vatsasya pādau dvau prasave śirasā saha
d dṛśyete dānakālaṃ tam āhuḥ kālavido janāḥ
d antarikṣagato vatso yāvad bhūmiṃ na yāsyati
d gaus tāvat pṛthivī jñeyā tasmād deyā tu tādṛśī
d yāvanti dhenvā romāṇi savatsāyā yudhiṣṭhira
d yāvantyaḥ sikatāś cāpi garbhodakapariplutāḥ
d tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi dātā svarge mahīyate
d suvarṇābharaṇāṃ kṛtvā savatsāṃ kapilāṃ tilaiḥ
d pracchādya tāṃ tu dadyād vai sarvaratnair alaṃkṛtām
d sasamudrā mahī tena saśailavanakānanā
d caturantā bhaved dattā nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
d pṛthivīdānatulyena tena dānena mānavaḥ
d saṃsārasāgarāt tīrṇo yāti lokaṃ prajāpateḥ
d brahmahā yadi vā goghno bhrūṇahā gurutalpagaḥ
d mahāpātakayukto 'pi dānenānena śudhyati
d idaṃ paṭhati yaḥ puṇyaṃ kapilādānam uttamam
d prātar utthāya madbhaktyā tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d manasā karmaṇā vācā matipūrvaṃ yudhiṣṭhira
d pāpaṃ rātrikṛtaṃ hanyād asyādhyāyasya pāṭhakaḥ
d idam āvartamānas tu śrāddhe yas tarpayed dvijān
d tasyāpy amṛtam aśnanti pitaro 'tyantaharṣitāḥ
d yaś cedaṃ śṛṇuyād bhaktyā madgatenāntarātmanā
d tasya rātrikṛtaṃ sarvaṃ pāpam āśu praṇaśyati
d ataḥ paraṃ viśeṣaṃ tu kapilānāṃ bravīmi te
d yāś caitāḥ kapilāḥ proktā daśa rājan mayā tava
d tāsāṃ catasraḥ pravarāḥ pavitrāḥ pāpanāśanāḥ
d suvarṇakapilā puṇyā tathā raktākṣipiṅgalā
d piṅgalākṣī ca yā gauś ca yad vā piṅgalapiṅgalā
d etāś catasraḥ pravarāḥ puṇyāḥ pāpapraṇāśanāḥ
d namaskṛtā vā spṛṣṭā vā ghnanti pāpaṃ narasya tu
d yasyaitāḥ kapilāḥ santi gṛhe pāpapraṇāśanāḥ
d tatra śrīr vijayaḥ kīrtiḥ sthitā nityaṃ yudhiṣṭhira
d etāsāṃ prītim āyāti kṣīreṇa tu vṛṣadhvajaḥ
d dadhnā tu tridaśāḥ sarve ghṛtena tu hutāśanaḥ
d pitaraḥ pitāmahāś caiva tathaiva prapitāmahāḥ
d sakṛd dattena tuṣyanti varṣakoṭiṃ yudhiṣṭhira
d kapilāyā ghṛtaṃ kṣīraṃ dadhi pāyasam eva vā
d śrotriyebhyaḥ sakṛd dattvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
d upavāsaṃ tu yat kṛtvā ahorātraṃ jitendriyaḥ
d kapilāpañcagavyaṃ tu pītvā cāndrāyaṇāt param
d saumye muhūrte tat prāśya śuddhātmā śuddhamānasaḥ
d krodhānṛtavinirmukto madgatenāntarātmanā
d kapilāpañcagavyena samantreṇa pṛthak pṛthak
d yo matpratikṛtiṃ vāpi śaṃkarākṛtim eva vā
d snāpayed viṣuve yas tu so 'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet
d sa muktapāpaḥ śuddhātmā yānenāmbaraśobhinā
d mama lokaṃ vrajen martyo rudralokam athāpi vā
d brahmaṇā tu purā sṛṣṭā kapilā kāñcanaprabhā
d agnikuṇḍāt parair mantrair homadhenur mahāprabhā
d sṛṣṭamātrāṃ tu tāṃ dṛṣṭvā devā rudrādayo divi
d siddhā brahmarṣayaś caiva vedāḥ sāṅgāḥ sahādhvarāḥ
d sāgarāḥ saritaś cāpi parvatāḥ sabalāhakāḥ
d gandharvāpsaraso yakṣāḥ pannagāś cāpy upasthitāḥ
d sarve vismayam āpannāḥ śikhimadhye mahāprabhām
d mantraiś ca vividhaiḥ sarvais tuṣṭuvus tām anekaśaḥ
d kṛtāñjalipuṭāḥ sarve tāmraśṛṅgīṃ trilocanām
d śirobhiḥ patitā bhūmau savatsām amṛtāraṇim
d ūcuḥ prāñjalayaḥ sarve caturvaktraṃ pitāmaham
d ājñāpaya mahādeva kiṃ te karma priyaṃ vibho
d evam uktaḥ suraiḥ sarvair brahmā vacanam abravīt
d bhavanto 'py anugṛhṇantu dogdhrīm enāṃ payasvinīm
d homadhenur iyaṃ jñeyā hy agniṃ saṃtarpayiṣyati
d tato 'gnis tarpitaḥ sarvān bhavatas tarpayiṣyati
d prītāḥ kṣīrāmṛtenāsyā jātavīryaparākramāḥ
d jayiṣyatha yathākāmaṃ dānavān sarva eva tu
d jātavīryabalaiśvaryāḥ sattvavanto jitārayaḥ
d asaṃkhyeyabalāḥ sarve pālayiṣyatha vai prajāḥ
d pālitāś ca prajāḥ sarvā bhavadbhir iha dharmataḥ
d pūjayiṣyanti vo nityaṃ yajñair vividhadakṣiṇaiḥ
d evam uktāḥ surāḥ sarve brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā
d tataḥ saṃhṛṣṭamanasaḥ kapilāyai varaṃ daduḥ
d yasmāl lokahitāyādya brahmaṇā tvaṃ vinirmitā
d tasmāt pūtā pavitrā ca bhava pāpavyapohinī
d ye tvāṃ dṛṣṭvā namasyanti spṛṣṭvā cāpi karair narāḥ
d teṣāṃ varṣakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tvadbhaktānāṃ praṇaśyati
d akāmakṛtam ajñātam adṛṣṭaṃ yac ca pātakam
d tvāṃ dṛṣṭvā ye namasyanti narāḥ sarvaṃsaheti ca
d teṣāṃ tad vilayaṃ yāti tamaḥ sūryodaye yathā
d ity uktvāsyai varaṃ dattvā prayayus te yathāgatam
d lokanistāraṇārthāya sā ca lokāṃś cacāra ha
d tasyām eva samudbhūtā hy etāś ca kapilānagha
d vicaranti mahīm enāṃ lokānugrahakāraṇāt
d tasmāt tu kapilā deyā paratra hitam icchatā
d yathā ca dīyate rājan kapilā hy agnihotriṇe
d tathāgraśṛṅgayos tasyā viṣṇur indraś ca tiṣṭhataḥ
d candravajradharau cāpi tiṣṭhataḥ śṛṅgamūlayoḥ
d śṛṅgamadhye tathā brahmā lalāṭe govṛṣadhvajaḥ
d karṇayor aśvinau devau cakṣuṣoḥ śaśibhāskarau
d danteṣu maruto devā jihvāyāṃ vāk sarasvatī
d romānte munayaḥ sarve carmaṇy eva prajāpatiḥ
d niśvāseṣu sthitā vedāḥ saṣaḍaṅgapadakramāḥ
d nāsāpuṭe sthitā gandhāḥ puṣpāṇi surabhīṇi ca
d adhare vasavaḥ sarve mukhe cāgniḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ
d sādhyā devāḥ sthitāḥ kakṣe grīvāyāṃ pārvatī sthitā
d pṛṣṭhe ca nakṣatragaṇāḥ kakuddeśe nabhaḥsthalam
d apāne sarvatīrthāni gomūtre jāhnavī svayam
d iṣṭatuṣṭamayī lakṣmīr gomaye vasate sadā
d nāsikāyāṃ tadā devī jyeṣṭhā vasati bhāminī
d śroṇītaṭasthāḥ pitaro ramā lāṅgūlam āśritāḥ
d pārśvayor ubhayoḥ sarve viśve devāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ
d tiṣṭhaty urasi tāsāṃ tu prītaḥ śaktidharo guhaḥ
d jānujaṅghorudeśeṣu pañca tiṣṭhanti vāyavaḥ
d khuramadhyeṣu gandharvāḥ khurāgreṣu ca pannagāḥ
d catvāraḥ sāgarāḥ pūrṇās tasyā eva payodharāḥ
d ratir medhā kṣamā svāhā śraddhā śāntir dhṛtiḥ smṛtiḥ
d kīrtir dīptiḥ kriyā kāntis tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭiś ca saṃtatiḥ
d diśaś ca vidiśaś caiva sevante kapilāṃ sadā
d devāḥ pitṛgaṇāś cāpi gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ
d lokā dvīpārṇavāś caiva gaṅgādyāḥ saritas tathā
d grahāḥ pitṛgaṇāś cāpi vedāḥ sāṅgāḥ sahādhvaraiḥ
d vedoktair vividhair mantraiḥ stuvanti hṛṣitās tathā
d vidyādharāś ca ye siddhā bhūtās tārāgaṇās tathā
d puṣpavṛṣṭiṃ ca varṣanti pranṛtyanti ca harṣitāḥ
d brahmaṇotpāditā devī vahnikuṇḍān mahāprabhā
d namas te kapile puṇye sarvadevair namaskṛte
d kapile 'tha mahāsattve sarvatīrthamaye śubhe
d dātāraṃ svajanopetaṃ brahmalokaṃ naya svayam
d aho ratnam idaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvaduḥkhaghnam uttamam
d aho dharmārjitaṃ śuddham idam agryaṃ mahādhanam
d ity ākāśe sthitā devā jalpanti ca namanti ca
d tasyāḥ pratigṛhītā ca bhuṅkte yāvad dvijottamaḥ
d tāvad devagaṇāḥ sarve kapilām arcayanti ca
d svarṇaśṛṅgī raupyakhurā gandhaiḥ puṣpaiś ca pūjitā
d vastrābhyām ahatābhyāṃ tu yāvat tiṣṭhaty alaṃkṛtā
d tāvad yad icchet kapilā mantrapūtā susaṃskṛtā
d bhūlokavāsinaḥ sarvān brahmalokaṃ nayet svayam
d bhūr aśvaḥ kanakaṃ gāvo raupyam annaṃ tilā yavāḥ
d dīyamānāni viprāya prahṛṣyanti dine dine
d atha tv aśrotriyebhyo vai tāni dattāni pāṇḍava
d tathā nindanty athātmānam aśubhaṃ kiṃ nu naḥ kṛtam
d aho rakṣaḥpiśācaiś ca lupyamānāḥ samantataḥ
d yāsyāmo nirayaṃ śīghram iti śocanti tāni vai
d etāny api dvijebhyo vai śrotriyebhyo viśeṣataḥ
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d dīyamānāni vardhante dātāraṃ tārayanti ca
d devadeveśa daityaghna kālaḥ ko havyakavyayoḥ
d bhagavān uvāca
d ke tatra pūjām arhanti varjanīyāś ca ke dvijāḥ
d daivaṃ pūrvāhṇikaṃ jñeyaṃ paitṛkaṃ cāparāhṇikam
d kālahīnaṃ ca yad dānaṃ tad dānaṃ rākṣasaṃ viduḥ
d avaghuṣṭaṃ ca yad bhuktam anṛtena ca bhārata
d parāmṛṣṭaṃ śunā vāpi tadbhāgaṃ rākṣasaṃ viduḥ
d yāvantaḥ patitā viprā jaḍonmattādayo 'pi ca
d daive ca pitrye ye cāpi rājan nārhanti satkriyām
d klībaḥ plīhī ca kuṣṭhī ca rājayakṣmānvitaś ca yaḥ
d apasmārī ca yaś cāpi pitrye nārhati satkriyām
d cikitsakā devalakā vṛthā niyamadhāriṇaḥ
d somavikrayiṇaś cāpi śrāddhe nārhanti satkṛtim
d ekoddiṣṭasya ye cānnaṃ bhuñjate vidhivad dvijāḥ
d cāndrāyaṇam akṛtvā te punar nārhanti satkṛtim
d gāyakā nartakāś caiva plavakā vādakās tathā
d kathakā yaudhikāś caiva śrāddhe nārhanti satkṛtim
d anagnayaś ca ye viprāḥ pretaniryātakāś ca ye
d stenāś cāpi vikarmasthā rājan nārhanti satkṛtim
d aparijñātapūrvāś ca gaṇaputrāś ca ye dvijāḥ
d putrikāputrakāś cāpi śrāddhe nārhanti satkṛtim
d ṛṇakartā ca yo vipro yaś ca vāṇijyako dvijaḥ
d prāṇivikrayavṛttiś ca śrāddhe nārhanti satkṛtim
d cīrṇavratā guṇair yuktā nityaṃ svādhyāyatatparāḥ
d sāvitrījñāḥ kriyāvantas te śrāddhe satkṛtikṣamāḥ
d śrāddhasya brāhmaṇaḥ kālaḥ prāpto dadhi ghṛtaṃ tadā
d darbhāḥ sumanasaḥ kṣetraṃ tatkāle śrāddhado bhavet
d cāritraniyatā rājan kṛśā ye kṛśavṛttayaḥ
d arthinaś copagacchanti tebhyo dattaṃ mahat phalam
d tapasvinaś ca ye viprās tathā bhaikṣacarāś ca ye
d arthinaḥ ke cid icchanti teṣāṃ dattaṃ mahat phalam
d evaṃ dharmavidāṃ śreṣṭha jñātvā sarvātmanā tadā
d śrotriyāya daridrāya prayacchānupakāriṇe
d dānaṃ yat te priyaṃ kiṃ cic chrotriyāṇāṃ ca yat priyam
d tat prayacchasva dharmajña yad icchasi tad akṣayam
d nirayaṃ ye ca gacchanti tac chṛṇuṣva yudhiṣṭhira
d gurvarthaṃ vā bhayārthaṃ vā no ced anyatra pāṇḍava
d vadanti ye 'nṛtaṃ viprās te vai nirayagāminaḥ
d paradārābhihartāraḥ paradārābhimarśakāḥ
d paradāraprayoktāras te vai nirayagāminaḥ
d sūcakāḥ saṃdhibhettāraḥ paradravyopajīvinaḥ
d akṛtajñāś ca mitrāṇāṃ te vai nirayagāminaḥ
d varṇāśramāṇāṃ ye bāhyāḥ pāṣaṇḍasthāś ca pāṇḍava
d upāsate ca tān ye tu te sarve narakālayāḥ
d vedavikrayiṇaś caiva vedānāṃ caiva dūṣakāḥ
d vedānāṃ lekhakāś caiva te vai nirayagāminaḥ
d rasavikrayiṇo rājan viṣavikrayiṇaś ca ye
d kṣīravikrayiṇaś cāpi te vai nirayagāminaḥ
d caṇḍālebhyas tu ye kṣīraṃ prayacchanti narādhamāḥ
d arthārtham atha vā snehāt te vai nirayagāminaḥ
d paśūnāṃ damakāś caiva tathā nāsānuvedhakāḥ
d puṃstvasya hiṃsakāś caiva te vai nirayagāminaḥ
d adātāraḥ samarthā ye dravyāṇāṃ lobhakāraṇāt
d dīnānāthān na paśyanti te vai nirayagāminaḥ
d kṣāntān dāntān kṛśān prājñān dīrghakālaṃ sadoṣitān
d tyajanti kṛtakṛtyā ye te vai nirayagāminaḥ
d bālānām atha vṛddhānāṃ śrāntānāṃ cāpi ye narāḥ
d adattvāśnanti ye mṛṣṭaṃ te vai nirayagāminaḥ
d ete pūrvarṣibhiḥ proktā narā nirayagāminaḥ
d ye svargaṃ samanuprāptās tāñ śṛṇuṣva yudhiṣṭhira
d dānena tapasā caiva satyena ca damena ca
d ye dharmam anuvartante te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ
d śuśrūṣayāpy upādhyāyāc chrutam ādāya pāṇḍava
d ye pratigrahaniḥsnehās te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ
d madhumāṃsāsavebhyas tu nivṛttā vṛttavat tu ye
d paradāranivṛttāś ca te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ
d mātaraṃ pitaraṃ caiva śuśrūṣanti ca ye narāḥ
d bhrātṝṇām api sasnehās te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ
d ye tu bhojanakāle tu niyatāś cātithipriyāḥ
d dvārarodhaṃ na kurvanti te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ
d vaivāhikaṃ tu kanyānāṃ daridrāṇāṃ ca ye narāḥ
d kārayanti ca kurvanti te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ
d rasānām atha bījānām oṣadhīnāṃ tathaiva ca
d dātāraḥ śraddhayopetās te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ
d kṣemākṣemaṃ ca mārgeṣu samāni viṣamāṇi ca
d arthināṃ ye ca vakṣyanti te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ
d parvadvaye caturdaśyām aṣṭamyāṃ saṃdhyayor dvayoḥ
d ārdrāyāṃ janmanakṣatre viṣuve śravaṇe tathā
d ye grāmyadharmaviratās te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ
d havyakavyavidhānaṃ ca narakasvargagāminau
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d dharmādharmau ca kathitau bhūyaḥ kiṃ śrotum icchasi
d idaṃ me tattvato deva vaktum arhasy aśeṣataḥ
d hiṃsām akṛtvā yo martyo brahmahatyām avāpnuyāt
d bhagavān uvāca
d brāhmaṇaṃ svayam āhūya bhikṣārthaṃ kṛśavṛttinam
d brūyān nāstīti yaḥ paścāt tam āhur brahmaghātakam
d madhyasthasyeha viprasya yo 'nūcānasya bhārata
d vṛttiṃ harati durbuddhis tam āhur brahmaghātakam
d gokulasya tṛṣārtasya jalānte vasudhādhipa
d utpādayati yo vighnaṃ tam āhur brahmaghātakam
d yaḥ pravṛttāṃ śrutiṃ satyāṃ śāstraṃ vā munibhiḥ kṛtam
d dūṣayaty anabhijño yas taṃ vidyād brahmaghātakam
d āśrame vā vane vāpi grāme vā nagare 'pi vā
d agniṃ yaḥ prakṣipet kruddhas tam āhur brahmaghātakam
d cakṣuṣā vāpi hīnasya paṅgor vāpi jaḍasya ca
d hared vai yas tu sarvasvaṃ taṃ vidyād brahmaghātakam
d krodhād vā yadi vā dveṣād ākruṣṭas tarjito 'pi vā
d ṛtau striyaṃ vā nopeyāt tam āhur brahmaghātakam
d yāvat sāro bhaved dhīras tannāśe yasya duḥsthitiḥ
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d tat sarvasvaṃ hared yo vai tam āhur brahmaghātakam
d sarveṣām api dānānāṃ yat tu dānaṃ viśiṣyate
d bhagavān uvāca
d abhojyānnāś ca ye viprās tān bravīhi surottama
d annam eva praśaṃsanti devā brahmapuraḥsarāḥ
d annena sadṛśaṃ dānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati
d annam ūrjaskaraṃ loke annāt prāṇāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ
d abhojyānnān imān rājan vakṣyamāṇān nibodha me
d dīkṣitasya kadaryasya baddhasya nikṛtasya ca
d abhiśastasya ṣaṇḍasya pākabhedakarasya ca
d cikitsakasya sarvasya tathā cocchiṣṭabhojinaḥ
d ugrānnaṃ sūtakānnaṃ ca śūdroccheṣaṇam eva ca
d dviṣadannaṃ na bhoktavyaṃ patitānnaṃ ca yac chrutam
d tathā ca piśunasyānnaṃ yajñavikrayiṇas tathā
d śailūṣatantuvāyānnaṃ kṛtaghnasyānnam eva ca
d ambaṣṭhasya niṣādasya raṅgāvatarakasya ca
d suvarṇakartur vaiṇasya śastravikrayiṇas tathā
d sūtānāṃ śauṇḍikānāṃ ca vaidyasya rajakasya ca
d strījitasya nṛśaṃsasya tathā māhiṣikasya ca
d anirdaśānāṃ pretānāṃ gaṇikānāṃ tathaiva ca
d vandino dyūtakartuś ca tathā dyūtavidām api
d parivittasya yac cānnaṃ parivettus tathaiva ca
d yaś cāgradidhiṣur vipro didhiṣūpapatis tathā
d tayor apy ubhayor annaṃ rājñaś cāpi vivarjayet
d rājānnaṃ teja ādatte śūdrānnaṃ brahmavarcasam
d āyuḥ suvarṇakārānnaṃ yaśaś carmāvakṛntinaḥ
d gaṇānnaṃ gaṇikānnaṃ ca lokebhyaḥ parikṛntati
d āyuś cikitsakasyānnaṃ śuklaṃ tu vṛṣalīpateḥ
d viṣṭhā vārdhuṣikasyānnaṃ tasmāt tat parivarjayet
d teṣāṃ tvagasthiromāṇi bhuṅkte yo 'nnaṃ tu bhakṣayet
d amātyānnam athaiteṣāṃ bhuktvā tu triyahaṃ kṣipet
d matyā bhuktvā sakṛd vāpi prājāpatyaṃ cared dvijaḥ
d dānānāṃ ca phalaṃ yad vai śṛṇu pāṇḍava tattvataḥ
d jaladas tṛptim āpnoti sukham akṣayam annadaḥ
d tiladas tu prajām iṣṭāṃ dīpadaś cakṣur uttamam
d bhūmido bhūmim āpnoti dīrgham āyur hiraṇyadaḥ
d gṛhado 'gryāṇi veśmāni rūpyado rūpam uttamam
d vāsodaś candrasālokyam aśvisālokyam aśvadaḥ
d anaḍuddaḥ śriyaṃ juṣṭāṃ godaś ca bradhnaviṣṭapam
d yānaśayyāprado bhāryām aiśvaryam abhayapradaḥ
d dhānyadaḥ śāśvataṃ saukhyaṃ brahmado brahmasāmyatām
d sarveṣām eva dānānāṃ brahmadānaṃ viśiṣyate
d hiraṇyabhūgavāśvājavastraśayyāsanādiṣu
d yo 'rcitaṃ pratigṛhṇāti dadāty arcitam eva ca
d tāv ubhau gacchataḥ svargaṃ narakaṃ ca viparyaye
d anṛtaṃ na vaded iṣṭvā tapas taptvā na vismayet
d nārto 'py apavaded viprān na dattvā parikīrtayet
d yajño 'nṛtena kṣarati tapaḥ kṣarati vismayāt
d āyurviprāpavādena dānaṃ tu parikīrtanāt
d ekaḥ prajāyate jantur eka eva pramīyate
d eko 'nubhuṅkte sukṛtam ekaś cāpnoti duṣkṛtam
d mṛtaṃ śarīram utsṛjya kāṣṭhaloṣṭasamaṃ kṣitau
d vimukhā bāndhavā yānti dharmas tam anuvartate
d anāgatāni kāryāṇi kartuṃ gaṇayate manaḥ
d śarīrakaṃ samuddiśya smayate nūnam antakaḥ
d tasmād dharmasahāyo 'stu dharmaṃ saṃcinuyāt sadā
d dharmeṇa hi sahāyena tamas tarati dustaram
d yeṣāṃ taṭākāni bahūdakāni
d sabhāś ca kūpāś ca pratiśrayāś ca
d annapradānaṃ madhurā ca vāṇī
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d yamasya te nirviṣayā bhavanti
d anekāntaṃ bahudvāraṃ dharmam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ
d bhagavān uvāca
d kiṃlakṣaṇo 'sau bhavati tan me brūhi janārdana
d śṛṇu rājan samāsena dharmaśaucavidhikramam
d ahiṃsā satyam asteyam ānṛśaṃsyaṃ damaḥ śamaḥ
d ārjavaṃ caiva rājendra niścitaṃ dharmalakṣaṇam
d brahmacaryaṃ tapaḥ kṣāntir madhumāṃsasya varjanam
d maryādāyāṃ sthitiś caiva śamaḥ śaucasya lakṣaṇam
d bālye vidyāṃ niṣeveta yauvane dārasaṃgraham
d vārdhakye maunam ātiṣṭhet sarvadā dharmam ācaret
d brāhmaṇān nāvamanyeta gurūn parivaden na ca
d yatīnām anukūlaḥ syād eṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ
d yatir gurur dvijātīnāṃ varṇānāṃ brāhmaṇo guruḥ
d patir eva guruḥ strīṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ pārthivo guruḥ
d yad gṛhasthārjitaṃ pāpaṃ jñānato 'jñānato 'pi vā
d nirdahiṣyati tat sarvam ekarātroṣito yatiḥ
d durvṛttā vā suvṛttā vā jñānino 'jñānino 'pi vā
d gṛhasthair yatayaḥ pūjyāḥ paratra hitakāṅkṣibhiḥ
d ekadaṇḍī tridaṇḍī vā śikhaṇḍī muṇḍito 'pi vā
d kāṣāyadaṇḍadhāro 'pi yatiḥ pūjyo yudhiṣṭhira
d apūjito gṛhasthair vā tathā cāpy avamānitaḥ
d yatir vāpy atithir vāpi narake pātayiṣyataḥ
d tasmāt tu yatnataḥ pūjyā madbhaktā matparāyaṇāḥ
d mayi saṃnyastakarmāṇaḥ paratra hitakāṅkṣibhiḥ
d praharen na dvijān prājño gāṃ na hanyāt kadā cana
d bhrūṇahatyāsamaṃ caitad ubhayaṃ yo niṣevate
d nāgniṃ mukhenopadhamen na ca pādau pratāpayet
d nādhaḥ kuryāt kadā cit tu na pṛṣṭhaṃ paritāpayet
d nāntarāgamanaṃ kuryān na cāmedhyaṃ vinikṣipet
d ucchiṣṭo na spṛśed agnim āśaucastho na jātu cit
d śvacaṇḍālādibhiḥ spṛṣṭo nāṅgam agnau pratāpayet
d sarvadevamayo vahnis tasmāc chuddhaḥ sadā spṛśet
d prāptamūtrapurīṣas tu na spṛśed vahnim ātmavān
d yāvat tu dhārayed vegaṃ tāvad aprayato bhavet
d pacanāgniṃ na gṛhṇīyāt paraveśmani jātu cit
d tena pakvena cānnena yat karma kurute śubham
d tac chubhasya phalasyārdham agnidasya bhaven nṛpa
d tasmāc chubhataraṃ karma prakuryād avināśitam
d pramādād yadi vājñānāt tasya nāśo bhaviṣyati
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d gṛhṇīyāt tu mathitvā vā śrotriyāgārato 'pi vā
d kīdṛśāḥ sādhavo viprāḥ kebhyo dattaṃ mahat phalam
d bhagavān uvāca
d kīdṛśebhyo hi dātavyaṃ tan me brūhi janārdana
d akrodhanāḥ satyaparā dharmanityā jitendriyāḥ
d tādṛśāḥ sādhavo viprās tebhyo dattaṃ mahat phalam
d amāninaḥ sarvasahā dṛṣṭārthā vijitendriyāḥ
d sarvabhūtahitā maitrās tebhyo dattaṃ mahat phalam
d alubdhāḥ śucayo vaidyā hrīmantaḥ satyavādinaḥ
d svadharmaniratā ye tu tebhyo dattaṃ mahat phalam
d sāṅgāṃś ca caturo vedān yo 'dhīyīta dine dine
d śūdrānnaṃ yasya dehe na tatpātram ṛṣayo viduḥ
d prajñāśrutābhyāṃ vṛttena śīlena ca samanvitaḥ
d tārayet tat kulaṃ sarvam eko 'pīha yudhiṣṭhira
d gām aśvam annaṃ vittaṃ vā tadvidhe pratipādayet
d niśamya ca guṇopetaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ sādhusaṃmatam
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d dūrād āhṛtya satkṛtya taṃ prayatnena pūjayet
d dharmādharmavidhir deva mama bhīṣmeṇa bhāṣitaḥ
d bhīṣmavākyāt sārabhūtaṃ vada dharmaṃ sureśvara
d bhagavān uvāca
d annena dhāryate sarvaṃ jagad etac carācaram
d annāt prabhavati prāṇaḥ pratyakṣaṃ nāsti saṃśayaḥ
d kalatraṃ pīḍayitvāpi deśe kāle ca śaktitaḥ
d dātavyaṃ bhikṣave cānnam ātmano bhūtim icchatā
d vipram adhvapariśrāntaṃ bālaṃ vṛddham athāpi vā
d arcayed guruvat prīto gṛhastho gṛham āgatam
d krodham utpatitaṃ hitvā suśīlo vītamatsaraḥ
d arcayed atithiṃ prītaḥ paratra hitabhūtaye
d atithiṃ nāvamanyeta nānṛtāṃ giram īrayet
d na pṛcched gotracaraṇaṃ nādhītaṃ vā kadā cana
d caṇḍālo vā śvapāko vā kāle yaḥ kaś cid āgataḥ
d annena pūjanīyaḥ sa paratra hitam icchatā
d pidhāya tu gṛhadvāraṃ bhuṅkte hy ekaḥ prahṛṣṭavat
d svargadvārapidhānaṃ vai kṛtaṃ tena yudhiṣṭhira
d pitṝn devān ṛṣīn viprān atithīṃś ca nirāśrayān
d yo naraḥ prīṇayaty annais tasya puṇyaphalaṃ mahat
d kṛtvāpi pāpaṃ bahuśo yo dadyād annam arthine
d brāhmaṇāya viśeṣeṇa sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
d annadaḥ prāṇado loke prāṇadaḥ sarvado bhavet
d tasmād annaṃ viśeṣeṇa dātavyaṃ bhūtim icchatā
d annaṃ hy amṛtam ity āhur annaṃ prajananaṃ smṛtam
d annapraṇāśe sīdanti śarīre pañca dhātavaḥ
d balaṃ balavato naśyed annahīnasya dehinaḥ
d tasmād annaṃ pradātavyaṃ śraddhayāśraddhayāpi vā
d ādatte hi rasaṃ sarvam ādityaḥ svagabhastibhiḥ
d vāyus tasmāt samādāya rasaṃ megheṣu dhārayet
d tat tu meghagataṃ bhūmau śakro varṣati tādṛśam
d tena digdhā bhaved devī mahī prītā ca pāṇḍava
d tasyāṃ sasyāni rohanti yair jīvanty akhilāḥ prajāḥ
d māṃsamedosthimajjānāṃ saṃbhavas tebhya eva hi
d evaṃ sūryaś ca pavano meghaḥ śakras tathaiva ca
d eka eva smṛto rāśir yato bhūtāni jajñire
d bhavanāni ca divyāni divi teṣāṃ mahātmanām
d nānāsaṃsthānarūpāṇi nānābhūtayutāni ca
d candramaṇḍalaśubhrāṇi kiṅkiṇījālavanti ca
d taruṇādityavarṇāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca
d anekaśatasaṃkhyāni sāntarjalavanāni ca
d tatra puṣpaphalopetāḥ kāmadāḥ surapādapāḥ
d vāpyo vīthyaḥ sabhāḥ kūpā dīrghikāś ca sahasraśaḥ
d ghoṣavanti ca yānāni yuktāny atha sahasraśaḥ
d bhakṣyabhojyamayāḥ śailā vāsāṃsy ābharaṇāni ca
d kṣīrasravantyaḥ saritas tathā caivānnaparvatāḥ
d prāsādāḥ pāṇḍarāḥ śubhrāḥ śayyāś ca kanakojjvalāḥ
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d annadās tatra tiṣṭhanti tasmād annaprado bhavet
d annadānaphalaṃ śrutvā prīto 'smi madhusūdana
d bhagavān uvāca
