d bhojanasya vidhiṃ vaktuṃ devadeva tvam arhasi
d bhojanasya dvijātīnāṃ vidhānaṃ śṛṇu pāṇḍava
d snātaḥ śuciḥ śucau deśe nirjane hutapāvakaḥ
d maṇḍalaṃ kārayitvā tu caturaśraṃ dvijottamaḥ
d kṣatriyaś cet tato vṛttaṃ vaiśyo 'rdhendusamākṛtim
d ārdrapādas tu bhuñjīyāt prāṅmukhaś cāsane śucau
d pādābhyāṃ dharaṇīṃ spṛṣṭvā pādenaikena vā punaḥ
d naikavāsās tu bhuñjīyān na cāntardhāya vā dvijaḥ
d na bhinnapātre bhuñjīta parṇapṛṣṭhe tathaiva ca
d annaṃ pūrvaṃ namaskuryāt prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā
d nānyad ālokayed annān na jugupseta tatparaḥ
d jugupsitaṃ ca yac cānnaṃ rākṣasā eva bhuñjate
d pāṇinā jalam uddhṛtya kuryād annaṃ pradakṣiṇam
d apeyaṃ tad vijānīyāt pītvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret
d pariveṣajalād anyat peyam etat tu mantravat
d pañca prāṇāhutīḥ kuryāt samaṃ tu pṛthak pṛthak
d yathā rasaṃ na jānāti jihvā prāṇāhutau nṛpa
d tathā samāhitaḥ kuryāt prāṇāhutim atandritaḥ
d viditvānnam athānnādaṃ pañca prāṇāṃś ca pāṇḍava
d yaḥ kuryād āhutīḥ pañca teneṣṭāḥ pañca vāyavaḥ
d ato 'nyathā tu bhuñjāno brāhmaṇo jñānadurbalaḥ
d tenānnenāsurān pretān rākṣasāṃs tarpayiṣyati
d vaktrapramāṇān piṇḍāṃś ca grased ekaikaśaḥ punaḥ
d vaktrādhikaṃ tu yat piṇḍam ātmocchiṣṭaṃ tad ucyate
d piṇḍāvaśiṣṭam anyac ca vaktraniḥsṛtam eva ca
d abhojyaṃ tad vijānīyād bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret
d svam ucchiṣṭaṃ tu yo bhuṅkte yo bhuṅte muktabhojanam
d cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret kṛcchraṃ prājāpatyam athāpi vā
d pibataḥ patite toye bhojane mukhaniḥsṛte
d abhojyaṃ tad vijānīyād bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret
d pītaśeṣaṃ tu tan nāma na peyaṃ pāṇḍunandana
d pibed yadi hi tan mohād dvijaś cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret
d pānīyāni pibed yena tat pātraṃ dvijasattamaḥ
d anucchiṣṭaṃ bhavet tāvad yāvad bhūmau na nikṣipet
d maunī vāpy atha vāmaunī prahṛṣṭaḥ saṃyatendriyaḥ
d bhuñjīta vidhivad vipro na cocchiṣṭaṃ pradāpayet
d sadā cātyāśanaṃ nādyān nātihīnaṃ ca karhi cit
d yathānnena vyathā na syāt tathā bhuñjīta nityaśaḥ
d udakyām api caṇḍālaṃ śvānaṃ vā rurum eva vā
d bhuñjāno yadi vā paśyet tad annaṃ ca parityajet
d bhuñjāno hy atyajan mohād dvijaś cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret
d keśakīṭāvapannaṃ ca mukhamārutavījitam
d abhojyaṃ tad vijānīyād bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret
d utthāya ca punaḥ spṛṣṭaṃ pādaspṛṣṭaṃ ca laṅghitam
d annaṃ tad rākṣasaṃ vidyāt tasmāt tat parivarjayet
d rākṣasocchiṣṭabhug vipraḥ sapta pūrvān parān api
d niraye raurave ghore svapitṝn pātayiṣyati
d tasminn ācamanaṃ kuryād yasmin pātre sa bhuktavān
d yady uttiṣṭhaty anācānto bhuktavān āsanāt tataḥ
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d snānaṃ sadyaḥ prakurvīta so 'nyathāprayato bhavet
d tṛṇamuṣṭividhānaṃ ca tṛṇamāhātmyam eva ca
d ikṣoḥ somasamudbhūtiṃ vaktum arhasi mānada
d bhagavān uvāca
d pitaro vṛṣabhā jñeyā gāvo lokasya mātaraḥ
d tāsāṃ tu pūjayā rājan pūjitāḥ pitṛmātaraḥ
d sabhā prapā gṛhaṃ cāpi devatāyatanāni ca
d śudhyanti śakṛdā yāsāṃ kiṃ pūtam adhikaṃ tataḥ
d grāsamuṣṭiṃ paragave dadyāt saṃvatsaraṃ tu yaḥ
d akṛtvā svayam āhāraṃ vrataṃ tat sārvakālikam
d gāvo me mātaraḥ sarvāḥ pitaraś caiva govṛṣāḥ
d grāsamuṣṭiṃ mayā dattāṃ pratigṛhṇantu mātaraḥ
d ity uktvānena mantreṇa sāvitryā vā samāhitaḥ
d abhimantrya grāsamuṣṭiṃ tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d yat kṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ tena jñānato 'jñānato 'pi vā
d tasya naśyati tat sarvaṃ duḥsvapnaṃ ca vinaśyati
d tilāḥ pavitrāḥ pāpaghnā nārāyaṇasamudbhavāḥ
d tilāñ śrāddhe praśaṃsanti dānam etad anuttamam
d tilān dadyāt tilān bhakṣyāt tilān prātar upaspṛśet
d tilaṃ tilam iti brūyāt tilāḥ pāpaharā hi te
d krītāḥ pratigṛhītā vā na vikreyā dvijātibhiḥ
d bhojanābhyañjanād dānād yo 'nyat tu kurute tilaiḥ
d kṛmir bhūtvā śvaviṣṭhāyāṃ pitṛbhiḥ saha majjati
d tilān na pīḍayed vipro yantracakre svayaṃ nṛpa
d pīḍayan hi dvijo mohān narakaṃ yāti rauravam
d ikṣuvaṃśodbhavaḥ somaḥ somavaṃśodbhavā dvijāḥ
d ikṣūn na pīḍayet tasmād ikṣughātyātmaghātakaḥ
d ikṣudaṇḍasahasrāṇām ekaikena yudhiṣṭhira
d brahmahatyām avāpnoti brāhmaṇo yantrapīḍakaḥ
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d tasmān na pīḍayed ikṣūn yantracakre dvijottamaḥ
d samuccayaṃ tu dharmāṇāṃ bhojyābhojyaṃ tathaiva ca
d bhagavān uvāca
d śrutaṃ mayā tvatprasādād āpaddharmaṃ bravīhi me
d durbhikṣe rāṣṭrasaṃbādhe tvāśauce mṛtasūtake
d dharmakāle 'dhvani tathā niyamo naiva lupyate
d dūrādhvagamanāt khinno dvijālābhe 'tha śūdrataḥ
d akṛtānnaṃ ca yat kiṃ cid gṛhṇīyād ātmavṛttaye
d āturo duḥkhito vāpi bhayārto vā bubhukṣitaḥ
d bhuñjann avidhinā vipraḥ prāyaścittīyate na ca
d nimantritas tu yo vipro vidhivad dhavyakavyayoḥ
d māṃsāny api ca bhuñjānaḥ prāyaścittīyate na ca
d aṣṭau tāny avrataghnāni āpo mūlaṃ ghṛtaṃ payaḥ
d havir brāhmaṇakāmāya guror vacanam auṣadham
d aśakto vidhivat kartuṃ prāyaścittāni yo naraḥ
d viduṣāṃ vacanenāpi dānenāpi viśudhyati
d anṛtāv ṛtukāle vā divā rātrau tathāpi vā
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d proṣitas tu striyaṃ gacchet prāyaścittīyate na ca
d praśasyāḥ kīdṛśā viprā nindyāś cāpi sureśvara
d bhagavān uvāca
d aṣṭakāyāś ca kaḥ kālas tan me kathaya suvrata
d satyasandhaṃ dvijaṃ dṛṣṭvā sthānād vepati bhāskaraḥ
d eṣa me maṇḍalaṃ bhittvā yāti brahma sanātanam
d kulīnaḥ karmakṛd vaidyas tathā cāpy ānṛśaṃsyavān
d hrīmān ṛjuḥ satyavādī pātraṃ sarva ime dvijāḥ
d ete cāgrāsanasthās tu bhuñjānāḥ prathamaṃ dvijāḥ
d tasyāṃ paṅktyāṃ ca ye cānye tān punanty eva darśanāt
d madbhaktā ye dvijaśreṣṭhā madgatā matparāyaṇāḥ
d tān paṅktipāvanān viddhi pūjyāṃś caiva viśeṣataḥ
d nindyāñ śṛṇu dvijān rājann api vā vedapāragān
d brāhmaṇacchadmanā loke carataḥ pāpakāriṇaḥ
d anagnir anadhīyānaḥ pratigraharucis tu yaḥ
d yatra kutra tu bhuñjānas taṃ vidyāt paṅktidūṣakam
d mṛtasūtakapuṣṭāṅgo yaś ca śūdrānnabhug dvijaḥ
d ahaṃ cāpi na jānāmi gatiṃ tasya narādhipa
d śūdrānnarasapuṣṭāṅgo hy adhīyāno 'pi nityaśaḥ
d japato juhvato vāpi gatir ūrdhvā na vidyate
d āhitāgniś ca yo vipraḥ śūdrānnān na nivartate
d pañca tasya praṇaśyanti ātmā brahma trayo 'gnayaḥ
d śūdrapreṣaṇakartuś ca brāhmaṇasya viśeṣataḥ
d bhūmāv annaṃ pradātavyaṃ śvasṛgālasamo hi saḥ
d pretabhūtaṃ tu yaḥ śūdraṃ brāhmaṇo jñānadurbalaḥ
d anugacchen nīyamānaṃ trirātram aśucir bhavet
d trirātre tu tataḥ pūrṇe nadīṃ gatvā samudragām
d prāṇāyāmaśataṃ kṛtvā ghṛtaṃ prāśya viśudhyati
d anāthaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ pretaṃ ye vahanti dvijottamāḥ
d pade pade 'śvamedhasya phalaṃ te prāpnuvanti hi
d na teṣām aśubhaṃ kiṃ cit pāpaṃ vāśubhakarmaṇām
d jalāvagāhanād eva sadyaḥ śaucaṃ vidhīyate
d śūdraveśmani vipreṇa kṣīraṃ vā yadi vā dadhi
d nirvṛtena na bhoktavyaṃ viddhi śūdrānnam eva tat
d viprāṇāṃ bhoktukāmānām atyantaṃ cānnakāṅkṣayā
d yo vighnaṃ kurute martyas tato nānyo 'sti pāpakṛt
d sarve ca vedāḥ saha ṣaḍbhir aṅgaiḥ
d sāṃkhyaṃ purāṇaṃ ca kule ca janma
d naitāni sarvāṇi gatir bhavanti
d śīlavyapetasya nṛpa dvijasya
d grahoparāge viṣuve 'yanānte
d pitrye maghāsu svasute ca jāte
d gayeṣu piṇḍeṣu ca pāṇḍuputra
d dattaṃ bhaven niṣkasahasratulyam
d vaiśākhamāsasya ca yā tṛtīyā
d navamy asau kārtikaśuklapakṣe
d nabhasyamāsasya ca kṛṣṇapakṣe
d trayodaśī pañcadaśī ca māghe
d upaplave candramaso raveś ca
d śrāddhasya kālo hy ayanadvaye ca
d yas tv ekapaṅktyāṃ viṣayaṃ dadāti
d snehād bhayād vā yadi vārthahetoḥ
d krūraṃ durācāram anātmavantaṃ
d brahmaghnam enaṃ munayo vadanti
d ihaivaikasya nāmutra amutraikasya no iha
d iha cāmutra caikasya nāmutraikasya no iha
d dhanāni yeṣāṃ vipulāni santi
d nityaṃ ramante paralokamūḍhāḥ
d teṣām ayaṃ śatruvaraghnaloko
d nānyaḥ sadā dehasukhe ratānām
d ye yogayuktās tapasi prasaktāḥ
d svādhyāyaśīlā jarayanti deham
d jitendriyā bhūtahite niviṣṭās
d teṣām asau nāyam arighnalokaḥ
d ye dharmam eva prathamaṃ caranti
d dharmeṇa labdhvāpi dhanāni kāle
d dārān avāpya kratubhir jayante
d teṣām ayaṃ caiva paraś ca lokaḥ
d ye naiva vidyāṃ na tapo na dānaṃ
d na cāpi mūḍhāḥ prajane yatante
d na cāpi gacchanti sukhāni bhogāṃs
d teṣām ayaṃ caiva paraś ca nāsti
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d nārāyaṇa purāṇeśa yogāvāsa namo 'stu te
d śrotum icchāmi kārtsnyena dharmasārasamuccayam
d bhagavān uvāca
d dharmasāraṃ mahārāja manunā proktam āditaḥ
d pravakṣyāmi manuproktaṃ paurāṇaṃ śrutisaṃhitam
d agnicit kapilā satrī rājā bhikṣur mahodadhiḥ
d dṛṣṭamātrāḥ punanty ete tasmāt paśyeta tān sadā
d gaur ekasyaiva dātavyā na bahūnāṃ yudhiṣṭhira
d sā gaur vikrayam āpannā dahaty āsaptamaṃ kulam
d bahūnāṃ na pradātavyā gaur vastraṃ śayanaṃ striyaḥ
d tādṛgbhūtaṃ tu tad dānaṃ dātāraṃ nopatiṣṭhati
d ākramya brāhmaṇair bhuktam anāryāṇāṃ tu veśmani
d gobhiś ca puṇyaṃ tat teṣāṃ rājasūyād viśiṣyate
d mā dadātv iti yo brūyād gavyagnau brāhmaṇeṣu ca
d tiryagyoniśataṃ gatvā caṇḍāleṣūpajāyate
d brāhmaṇasvaṃ tu devasvaṃ daridrasya ca yad dhanam
d guroś cāpi hṛtaṃ rājan svargastham api pātayet
d dharmaṃ jijñāsamānānāṃ pramāṇaṃ paramaṃ śrutiḥ
d dvitīyaṃ dharmaśāstrāṇi tṛtīyaṃ lokasaṃgrahaḥ
d ā samudrāc ca yat pūrvād ā samudrāc ca paścimāt
d himavadvindhyayor madhyam āryāvartaṃ pracakṣate
d sarasvatīdṛṣadvatyor devanadyor yad antaram
d tad devanirmitaṃ deśaṃ brahmāvartaṃ pracakṣate
d yasmin deśe ya ācāraḥ pāraṃparyakramāgataḥ
d varṇānāṃ sāntarālānāṃ sa sadācāra ucyate
d kurukṣetraṃ ca matsyāś ca pāñcālāḥ śūrasenayaḥ
d ete brahmarṣideśās tu brahmāvartād anantarāḥ
d etaddeśaprasūtasya sakāśād agrajanmanaḥ
d svaṃ cāritraṃ tu gṛhṇīyuḥ pṛthivyāṃ sarvamānavāḥ
d himavadvindhyayor madhyaṃ yat prāg viśasanād api
d pratyag eva prayāgāt tu madhyadeśaḥ prakīrtitaḥ
d kṛṣṇasāras tu carati mṛgo yatra svabhāvataḥ
d sa jñeyo yajñiyo deśo mlecchadeśas tataḥ param
d etān vijñāya deśāṃs tu saṃśrayeyur dvijātayaḥ
d śūdras tu yasmin kasmin vā nivased vṛttikarśitaḥ
d ācāraprabhavo dharmo hy ahiṃsā satyam eva ca
d dānaṃ caiva yathāśakti niyamāś ca yamaiḥ saha
d vaidikaiḥ karmabhiḥ puṇyair niṣekādir dvijanmanām
d kāryaḥ śarīrasaṃskāraḥ pāvanaḥ pretya ceha ca
d garbhahomair jātakarmanāmacaulopanāyanaiḥ
d svādhyāyais tadvrataiś caiva vivāhasnātakavrataiḥ
d mahāyajñaiś ca yajñaiś ca brāhmīyaṃ kriyate tanuḥ
d dharmārthau yatra na syātāṃ śuśrūṣā vāpi tadvidhā
d vidyā tasmin na vaptavyā śubhaṃ bījam ivoṣare
d laukikaṃ vaidikaṃ vāpi tathādhyātmikam eva vā
d yasmāj jñānam idaṃ prāptaṃ taṃ pūrvam abhivādayet
d savyena savyaṃ saṃgṛhya dakṣiṇena tu dakṣiṇam
d na kuryād ekahastena guroḥ pādābhivādanam
d niṣekādīni karmāṇi yaḥ karoti yathāvidhi
d adhyāpayati caivainaṃ sa vipro gurur ucyate
d kṛtvopanayanaṃ vedān yo 'dhyāpayati nityaśaḥ
d sakalpān sarahasyāṃś ca sa copādhyāya ucyate
d sāṅgāṃś ca vedān adhyāpya śikṣayitvā vratāni ca
d vivṛṇoti ca mantrārthān ācāryaḥ so 'bhidhīyate
d upādhyāyād daśācārya ācāryāṇāṃ śataṃ pitā
d pituḥ śataguṇaṃ mātā gauraveṇātiricyate
d tasmāt teṣāṃ vaśe tiṣṭhet tacchuśrūṣāparo bhavet
d avamānād dhi teṣāṃ tu narakaṃ syād asaṃśayaḥ
d hīnāṅgān atiriktāṅgān vidyāhīnān vayodhikān
d rūpadraviṇahīnāṃś ca jātihīnāṃś ca nākṣipet
d śapatā yat kṛtaṃ puṇyaṃ śapyamānaṃ tu gacchati
d śapyamānasya yat pāpaṃ śapantam anugacchati
d nāstikyaṃ vedanindāṃ ca devatānāṃ ca kutsanam
d dveṣaṃ ḍambhaṃ ca mānaṃ ca krodhaṃ taikṣṇyaṃ ca varjayet
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d bhagavaṃs tava bhaktasya mama dharmajanapriya
d bhagavān uvāca
d dharmaṃ puṇyatamaṃ deva pṛcchataḥ kathayasva me
d yad etad agnihotraṃ vai sṛṣṭaṃ varṇatrayasya tu
d mantravad yad dhutaṃ samyag vidhinā cāpy upāsitam
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d āhitāgniṃ nayaty ūrdhvaṃ sapatnīkaṃ sabāndhavam
d kathaṃ tad brāhmaṇair deva hotavyaṃ kṣatriyaiḥ katham
d vaiśyair vā devadeveśa kathaṃ vā suhutaṃ bhavet
d kasmin kāle 'tha vā kasya ādheyo 'gniḥ surottama
d āhitasya kathaṃ vāpi samyag ācaraṇaṃ bhavet
d katy agnayaḥ kim ātmānaḥ sthānaṃ kiṃ kasya vā vibho
d katarasmin hute sthāne kiṃ vrajed āgnihotrikaḥ
d agnihotranimittaṃ ca kim utpannaṃ purānagha
d katham evātha hūyante prīyante ca surāḥ katham
d vidhivan mantravad bhaktyā pūjitās tv agnayaḥ katham
d kāṃ gatiṃ vadatāṃ śreṣṭha nayanti hy agnihotriṇaḥ
d durhutāś cāpi bhagavann avijñātās trayo 'gnayaḥ
d kim āhitāgneḥ kurvanti duścīrṇā vāpi keśava
d utsannāgnis tu pāpātmā kāṃ yoniṃ deva gacchati
d etat sarvaṃ samāsena bhaktyā hy upagatasya me
d bhagavān uvāca
d vaktum arhasi sarvajña sarvāvāsa namo 'stu te
d śṛṇu rājan mahāpuṇyam idaṃ dharmāmṛtaṃ param
d yat tu tārayate yuktān brāhmaṇān agnihotriṇaḥ
d brahmatvenāsṛjaṃ lokān aham ādau mahādyute
d sṛṣṭo 'gnir mukhataḥ pūrvaṃ lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā
d yasmād agre sa bhūtānāṃ sarveṣāṃ nirmito mayā
d tasmād agnīty abhihitaḥ purāṇajñair manīṣiṇaḥ
d yasmāt tu sarvakṛtyeṣu pūrvam asmai pradīyate
d āhutir dīpyamānāya tasmād agnīti kīrtyate
d yasmāc ca nayati hy agryāṃ gatiṃ viprān supūjitaḥ
d tasmāc ca nayanād rājan vedeṣv agnīti kīrtyate
d yasmāc ca durhutaḥ so 'yam alaṃ bhakṣayituṃ kṣaṇāt
d yajamānaṃ naraśreṣṭha kravyādo 'gnis tataḥ smṛtaḥ
d sarvabhūtātmako rājan devānām eṣa vai mukham
d prathamaṃ manmukhāt sṛṣṭo lokārthe pacanaḥ prabhuḥ
d sṛṣṭamātro jagat sarvam attum aicchat purā khalu
d tataḥ praśamitaḥ so 'gnir upāsyaiva mayā purā
d satatopāsanāt so 'yam aupāsana iti smṛtaḥ
d āhutiḥ sarvam ākhyātaṃ tasmin vasati so 'nalaḥ
d āvasathya iti khyātas tenāsau brahmavādibhiḥ
d tasmin pañca mahāyajñā vartante yasya dharmataḥ
d somamaṇḍalamadhyena gatis tasya dvijanmanaḥ
d te ca saptarṣayaḥ siddhāḥ saṃyatendriyabuddhayaḥ
d gatā hy amarasāyujyam ekāgnyarcanatatparāḥ
d apare cāvasathyaṃ ca pacanāgniṃ pracakṣate
d tasmin pañca mahāyajñā vaiśvadevaś ca vartate
d sthālīpāka ca gārhaṃ ca sarve hy asmin pratiṣṭhitāḥ
d gṛhyakarmavaho yasmāt tasmād gṛhapatis tu saḥ
d aupāsanaṃ cāvasathyaṃ sabhyaṃ pacanapāvakam
d āhur brahmavidaḥ ke cin matam etan mamāpi ca
d agnihotraprakāraṃ tu śṛṇu rājan samāhitaḥ
d trayāṇāṃ guṇanāmāni vahnīnām ucyate mayā
d gṛhāṇāṃ hi patitvaṃ hi gṛhapatyam iti smṛtam
d gṛhapatyaṃ tu yasyāsīt tasyāsīd gārhapatyatā
d yajamānaṃ tu yasmāt tu dakṣiṇāṃ tu gatiṃ nayet
d dakṣiṇāgniṃ tam āhus taṃ dakṣiṇāyatanaṃ dvijāḥ
d āhutiḥ sarvam ākhyātaṃ havanaṃ havyavāhanam
d sarvahavyavaho vahnir gataś cāhavanīyatām
d yas tv āvasathyaṃ juhuyān mūlāgniṃ vidhivad dvijaḥ
d āvasathyaṃ tu ye cāgniṃ pacanāgniṃ pracakṣate
d teṣāṃ sa bhāgato vahniḥ sabhya ity abhidhīyate
d āvasathyas tu yo vahniḥ prathamaḥ sa prajāpatiḥ
d brahmā ca gārhapatyo 'gnis tasmād eva tu so bhavet
d dakṣiṇāgnis tv ayaṃ rudraḥ krodhātmā caṇḍa eva saḥ
d aham āhavanīyo 'gnir ā homād yasya vai mukhe
d sabhyo 'gniḥ pañcamo yas tu skanda eva narādhipa
d pṛthivī gārhapatyo 'gnir antarikṣaṃ ca dakṣiṇaḥ
d svarga āhavanīyo 'gnir evam agnitrayaṃ smṛtam
d vṛtto hi gārhapatyo 'gnir yasmād vṛttā ca medinī
d ardhacandrākṛtiḥ khaṃ vai dakṣiṇāgnis tathā bhavet
d caturaśraṃ tataḥ svargaṃ nirmalaṃ yan nirāmayam
d tasmād āhavanīyo 'gniś caturaśro bhaven nṛpa
d juhuyād gārhapatyaṃ yo bhuvaṃ jayati sa dvijaḥ
d juhoti dakṣiṇāgniṃ yaḥ sa jayaty antarikṣakam
d pṛthivīm antarikṣaṃ ca divaṃ carṣigaṇaiḥ saha
d jayaty āhavanīyaṃ yo juhuyād bhaktimān dvijaḥ
d ābhimukhyena homas tu yasya yajñeṣu vartate
d tenāpy āhavanīyatvaṃ gato vahnir mahādyutiḥ
d ā homād yo 'gnihotreṣu yajñe vā yatra sarvaśaḥ
d yasmād asmin pravartante tato hy āhavanīyatā
d yas tv āvasathyaṃ juhuyān mūlāgniṃ vidhivad dvijaḥ
d sa tu saptarṣilokeṣu sapatnīkaḥ pramodate
d yaś cāpy upāsate sabhyaṃ vidhivat prayatātmavān
d jayet sa vāṅmayaṃ sarvaṃ tathā tv ṛṣisabhām api
d agnīnām atha vāgnes tu yasya homaḥ pradīyate
d iṣṭo bhavati sarvāgner agnihotraṃ ca tad bhavet
d trayāṇāṃ yajamānasya cāturhotram iti smṛtam
d ho ity eva viṣādo vai viṣādo duḥkham ucyate
d duḥkhaṃ tāpatrayaṃ proktaṃ tāpaṃ hi narakaṃ viduḥ
d tasmād vai trāyate duḥkhād yajamānaṃ huto 'nalaḥ
d tasmāt tu vidhivat proktam agnihotram iti śrutau
d tad agnihotraṃ sṛṣṭaṃ vai brahmaṇā lokakartṛṇā
d vedāś cāpy agnihotrārthaṃ jajñire svayam eva tu
d agnihotraphalā vedā śīlavṛttaphalaṃ śrutam
d ratiputraphalā dārā dānabhogaphalaṃ dhanam
d trivedamantrasaṃyogād agnihotraṃ pravartate
d ṛgyajuḥsāmabhiḥ puṇyaiḥ sthāpyate sūtrasaṃyutaiḥ
d vasante brāhmaṇasya syād ādheyo 'gnir narādhipa
d vasanto brāhmaṇaḥ prokto vedayoniḥ sa ucyate
d agnyādheyaṃ tu yenātha vasante kriyate nṛpa
d tasya śrīr brahmavṛddhiś ca brāhmaṇasya vivardhate
d kṣatriyasyāgnir ādheyo grīṣme śreṣṭhaḥ sa vai nṛpa
d yenādhānaṃ tu vai grīṣme kriyate tasya vardhate
d śrīḥ prajāḥ paśavaś caiva vittaṃ tejo balaṃ yaśaḥ
d śaradrātre 'tha vaiśyasya hy ādhānīyo hutāśanaḥ
d śaradrātraṃ svayaṃ vaiśyo vaiśyayoniḥ sa ucyate
d śarady ādhānam evaṃ vai kriyate yena pāṇḍava
d tasyāpi śrīḥ prajāyuś ca paśavo 'rthaś ca vardhate
d paśavaḥ sarva evaite tribhir vedair alaṃkṛtāḥ
d agnihotrāt pravartante yair idaṃ dhriyate jagat
d grāmyāraṇyāś ca paśavas tathā vṛkṣās tṛṇāni ca
d phalāny oṣadhayaś cāpi hy agnihotrakṛte hi tāḥ
d rasāḥ snehās tathā gandhā ratnāni maṇayas tathā
d kāñcanāni ca lohāni hy agnihotrakṛte 'bhavan
d āyurvedo dhanurvedo mīmāṃsā nyāyavistaraḥ
d dharmaśāstraṃ ca tat sarvam agnihotrakṛte kṛtam
d chandaḥ śikṣāś ca kalpāś ca tathā vyākaraṇaṃ nṛpa
d śāstraṃ jyotir niruktaṃ cāpy agnihotrakṛte kṛtam
d itihāsapurāṇaṃ ca gāthāś copaniṣat tathā
d ātharvaṇāni karmāṇi cāgnihotrakṛte kṛtam
d yac caitasyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ hi kiṃ cid asti carācaram
d tat sarvam agnihotrasya kṛte sṛṣṭaṃ svayaṃbhuvā
d agnihotrasya darśasya paurṇamāsasya cāpy atha
d yūpeṣṭipaśubandhānāṃ somapānakriyāvatām
d tithinakṣatrayogānāṃ muhūrtakaraṇātmanām
d kālasya vedanārthaṃ tu jyotirjñānaṃ kṛtaṃ purā
d ṛgyajuḥsāmamantrāṇāṃ ślokatattvārthacintanāt
d pratyāpattivikalpānāṃ chando jñānaṃ prakalpitam
d varṇākṣarapadārthānāṃ saṃdhiliṅgaṃ vivakṣitam
d nāmadhātuvivekārthaṃ purā vyākaraṇaṃ kṛtam
d yūpavedy adhvarārthaṃ tu prokṣaṇaśravaṇāya tu
d yajñadaivatayogārthaṃ śikṣājñānaṃ prakalpitam
d yajñapātrapavitrārthaṃ dravyasaṃbhāraṇāya ca
d sarvayajñavikalpāya purākalpaṃ prakalpitam
d nāmadhātuvibhaktīnāṃ tattvārthaniyamāya ca
d sarvavedaniruktānāṃ niruktam ṛṣibhiḥ kṛtam
d vedyarthaṃ pṛthivī sṛṣṭā saṃbhārārthaṃ tathaiva ca
d idhmārtham atha yūpārthaṃ brahmā cakre vanaspatim
d grāmyāraṇyāś ca paśavo jāyante yajñakāraṇāt
d mantrāṇāṃ viniyogaṃ ca proṣitā śrāvaṇaṃ tathā
d anūyājaprayājāṃś ca marutāṃ śaṃsinas tathā
d udgātṝṃś caiva sāmnāṃ vai baliprasthānam eva ca
d viṣṇukramāṇāṃ kramaṇaṃ dakṣiṇāvabhṛthaṃ tathā
d trikālam arcanaṃ caiva sthāneṣūpahṛtaṃ tathā
d devatāgrahaṇaṃ mokṣaṃ haviṣāṃ śravaṇaṃ tathā
d nāvabudhyanti ye viprā nindanti ca paśor vadham
d te yānti narakaṃ ghoraṃ rauravaṃ tamasāvṛtam
d śatavarṣasahasrāṇi tatra sthitvā narādhamāḥ
d krimibhir bhakṣyamāṇāś ca tiṣṭheyuḥ pūyaśoṇite
d yūpās tu mantrasaṃskārair eṣāṃ vai paśavas tathā
d yajamānena sahitāḥ svargaṃ yānti nareśvara
d yāvat kālaṃ hi yajvā vai svargaloke mahīyate
d tāvat kālaṃ pramodante paśavo hy adhvare hatāḥ
d vṛkṣā yūpatvam icchanti paśutvaṃ paśavas tathā
d tṛṇānīcchanti darbhatvam oṣadhyaś ca haviṣyatām
d somatvaṃ ca latāḥ sarvā veditvaṃ vai vasuṃdharā
d yasmāt paśutvam icchanti paśavaḥ svargalipsayā
d tasmāt paśuvadhe hiṃsā nāsti yajñeṣu pāṇḍava
d ahiṃsā vaidikaṃ karma brahmakarmeti tat smṛtam
d vedoktaṃ ye na kurvanti hiṃsābuddhyā kratuṃ dvijāḥ
d sadyaḥ śūdratvam āyānti pretya caṇḍālatām api
d gāvo yajñārtham utpannā dakṣiṇārthaṃ tathaiva ca
d suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ caiva pātrī kumbhārtham eva ca
d darbhāḥ saṃstaraṇārthaṃ tu rakṣasāṃ rakṣaṇāya ca
d yajanārthaṃ dvijāḥ sṛṣṭās tārakā divi devatāḥ
d kṣatriyā rakṣaṇārthaṃ tu vaiśyā vārtānimittataḥ
d śuśrūṣārthaṃ trayāṇāṃ tu śūdrāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ svayaṃbhuvā
d evam etaj jagat sarvam agnihotrakṛte kṛtam
d nāvabudhyanti ye caitan narās tu tamasā vṛtāḥ
d te yānti narakaṃ ghoraṃ rauravaṃ nāma viśrutam
d rauravād vipramuktās tu krimiyoniṃ vrajanti te
d yathoktam agnihotrāṇāṃ śuśrūṣanti ca ye dvijāḥ
d tair dattaṃ suhutaṃ ceṣṭaṃ dattam adhyāpitaṃ bhavet
d evam iṣṭaṃ ca pūrtaṃ ca yad vipraiḥ kriyate nṛpa
d tat sarvaṃ samyag āhṛtya cāditye sthāpayāmy aham
d mayā sthāpitam āditye lokasya sukṛtaṃ hi tat
d dhārayet tat sahasrāṃśuḥ sukṛtaṃ hy agnihotriṇām
d yāvat kālaṃ tu tiṣṭhanti loke cāpy agnihotriṇaḥ
d tāvat teṣāṃ hi puṇyena dīpyante raviṇāmbare
d svarge svargaṃ gatānāṃ tu vīryād bhavati vīryavān
d tatra te hy upayuñjanti hy agnihotrasya yat phalam
d samānarūpā devānāṃ tiṣṭhanty ābhūtasaṃplavam
d vṛthāgninā ca ye ke cid dahyante hy agnihotriṇaḥ
d na te 'gnihotriṇāṃ lokaṃ manasāpi vrajanti vai
d vīraghnās te durācārāḥ sudaridrā narādhamāḥ
d vikalā vyādhitāś cāpi jāyante śūdrayoniṣu
d tasmād aproṣitair nityam agnihotraṃ dvijātibhiḥ
d hotavyaṃ vidhivad rājann ūrdhvam icchanti ye gatim
d ātmavat tatra mantavyam agnihotraṃ yudhiṣṭhira
d na tyājyaṃ kṣaṇam apy etad gṛhītavyaṃ dvijātibhiḥ
d vṛddhatve 'py agnihotraṃ vai gṛhṇanti vidhivad dvijāḥ
d śūdrānnād viratā dāntāḥ saṃyatendriyabuddhayaḥ
d pañcayajñaparā nityaṃ krodhalobhavivarjitāḥ
d dvikālam atithīṃś caiva pūjayanti ca bhaktitaḥ
d te 'pi sūryodayaprakhyair vimānair vāyuvegibhiḥ
d mama loke pramodante dṛṣṭvā māṃ ca yudhiṣṭhira
d manvantaraṃ ca tatraikaṃ moditvā dvijasattamāḥ
d iha mānuṣyake loke jāyante dvijasattamāḥ
d bālāhitāgnayo ye ca śūdrānnād viratāḥ sadā
d krodhalobhavinirmuktāḥ prātaḥsnānaparāyaṇāḥ
d yathoktam agnihotraṃ vai juhvate vijitendriyāḥ
d ātitheyāḥ sadā saumyā dvikālaṃ matparāyaṇāḥ
d te yānty apunarāvṛttiṃ bhittvā cādityamaṇḍalam
d mama lokaṃ sapatnīkā yānaiḥ sūryodayaprabhaiḥ
d tatra bālārkasaṃkāśāḥ kāmagāḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
d aiśvaryaguṇasaṃpannāḥ krīḍanti ca yathāsukham
d ity eṣā hy āhitāgnīnāṃ vibhūtiḥ pāṇḍunandana
d ye ca devaśrutiṃ ke cin nindamānā hy abuddhayaḥ
d pramāṇaṃ na ca kurvanti te yānti hy akṣayaṃ tamaḥ
d pramāṇam itihāsaṃ ca vedān kurvanti ye dvijāḥ
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d te yānty amarasāyujyaṃ nityam āstikyabuddhayaḥ
d cakrāyudha namas te 'stu deveśa garuḍadhvaja
d cāndrāyaṇavidhiṃ puṇyam ākhyāhi bhagavan mama
d bhagavān uvāca
d śṛṇu pāṇḍava tattvena sarvapāpapraṇāśanam
d pāpino yena śudhyanti tat te vakṣyāmi sarvaśaḥ
d brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vāpi vaiśyo vā caritavrataḥ
d yathāvat kartukāmo yas tasyeyaṃ prathamā kriyā
d śodhayet tu śarīraṃ svaṃ pañcagavyena yantritaḥ
d śarīraṃ kakṣapakṣāntaṃ tataḥ kurvīta pāvanam
d śuddhavāsāḥ śucir bhūtvā mauñjīṃ badhnīta mekhalām
d pālāśadaṇḍam ādāya brahmacārivrate sthitaḥ
d kṛtopavāsaḥ pūrvaṃ tu śuklapratipadi dvijaḥ
d nadīsaṃgamatīrtheṣu śucau deśe gṛhe 'pi vā
d gomayenopalipte 'tha sthaṇḍile 'gniṃ nidhāpayet
d āghārāv ājyabhāgau ca praṇavaṃ vyāhṛtīs tathā
d vāruṇaiś cāpi pañcaiva hutvā sarvān yathākramam
d satyāya viṣṇave ceti brahmarṣibhyo 'tha brahmaṇe
d viśvebhyaś caiva devebhyaḥ prajāpataya eva ca
d ṣaṭkṛtvo juhuyāt paścāt prāyaścittāhutiṃ dvijaḥ
d tataḥ samāpayed agniṃ śāntiṃ kṛtvātha pauṣṭikam
d praṇamyāgniṃ ca somaṃ ca bhasma dhṛtvā tathātmani
d nadīṃ gatvā viviktātmā somāya varuṇāya ca
d ādityāya namaskṛtvā tataḥ snāyāt samāhitaḥ
d uttīryodakam ācamya tv āsīnaḥ pūrvatomukhaḥ
d prāṇāyāmaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā pavitrair abhiṣecanam
d ācāntas tv abhivīkṣeta cordhvabāhur divākaram
d kṛtāñjalipuṭaḥ paścāt kuryāc caiva pradakṣiṇam
d nārāyaṇaṃ vā rudraṃ vā brahmāṇam atha vāpi vā
d vāruṇaṃ mantrasūktaṃ vā prāgbhojanam athāpi vā
d vīraghnam ṛṣabhaṃ vāpi tathā cāpy aghamarṣaṇam
d gāyatrīṃ mama vā devīṃ sāvitrīṃ vā japet tataḥ
d tataś cāṣṭādaśaṃ vāpi sahasram atha vāparam
d tato madhyāhnakāle vai pāyasaṃ yāvakaṃ hi vā
d pācayitvā prayatnena prayataḥ susamāhitaḥ
d pātraṃ tu susamādāya sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tu vā
d tāmraṃ vā mṛnmayaṃ vāpi audumbaram athāpi vā
d vṛkṣāṇāṃ yājñiyānāṃ tu parṇair ārdrair akutsitaiḥ
d puṭakena tu guptena cared bhaikṣaṃ samāhitaḥ
d brāhmaṇānāṃ gṛhāṇāṃ tu saptānāṃ nāparaṃ vrajet
d godohamātraṃ tiṣṭhet tu vāgyataḥ saṃyatendriyaḥ
d na hasec ca na vīkṣec ca nābhibhāṣeta vā striyam
d dṛṣṭvā mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca caṇḍālaṃ vā rajasvalām
d patitaṃ ca tathā śvānam ādityam avalokayet
d yo hi pādukam āruhya sarvadā pracared dvijaḥ
d taṃ dṛṣṭvā pāpakarmāṇam ādityam avalokayet
d tatas tv āvasathaṃ prāpto bhikṣāṃ nikṣipya bhūtale
d prakṣālya pādāv ā jānvor hastāv ākūrparaṃ punaḥ
d ācamya vāriṇā tena vahniṃ viprāṃś ca pūjayet
d pañca saptātha vā kuryād bhāgān bhaikṣasya tasya vai
d teṣām anyatamaṃ piṇḍam ādityāya nivedayet
d brahmaṇe cāgnaye caiva somāya varuṇāya ca
d viśvebhyaś caiva devebhyo dadyād annaṃ yathākramam
d avaśiṣṭam athaikaṃ tu vaktramātraṃ prakalpayet
d aṅgulyagre sthitaṃ piṇḍaṃ gāyatryā cābhimantrayet
d aṅgulībhis tribhiḥ piṇḍaṃ prāśnīyāt prāṅmukhaḥ śuciḥ
d yathā ca vardhate somo hrasate ca yathā punaḥ
d tathā piṇḍāś ca vardhante hasante ca dine dine
d trikālaṃ snānam asyoktaṃ dvikālam atha vā sakṛt
d brahmacārī sadā vāpi na ca vastraṃ prapīḍayet
d sthāne na divasaṃ tiṣṭhed rātrau vīrāsanaṃ vrajet
d bhavet sthaṇḍilaśāyī vāpy atha vā vṛkṣamūlikaḥ
d valkalaṃ yadi vā kṣaumaṃ śāṇaṃ kārpāsakaṃ tu vā
d ācchādanaṃ bhavet tasya vastrārthaṃ pāṇḍunandana
d evaṃ cāndrāyaṇe pūrṇe māsasyānte prayatnavān
d brāhmaṇān bhojayed bhaktyā dadyāc caiva ca dakṣiṇām
d cāndrāyaṇena cīrṇena yat kṛtaṃ tena duṣkṛtam
d tat sarvaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva bhasmībhavati kāṣṭhavat
d brahmahatyātha gohatyā suvarṇastainyam eva ca
d bhrūṇahatyā surāpānaṃ guror dāravyatikramaḥ
d evam anyāni pāpāni pātakīyāni yāni ca
d cāndrāyaṇena naśyanti vāyunā pāṃsavo yathā
d anirdaśāyā goḥ kṣīram auṣṭram āvikam eva ca
d mṛtasūtakayoś cānnaṃ bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret
d upapātakinaś cānnaṃ patitānnaṃ tathaiva ca
d śūdrasyoccheṣaṇaṃ caiva bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret
d ākāśasthaṃ tu hastastham āsanasthaṃ tathaiva ca
d parahastasthitaṃ caiva bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret
d athāgredidhiṣor annaṃ didhiṣūpapates tathā
d parivettus tathā cānnaṃ parivittānnam eva ca
d kuṇḍānnaṃ golakānnaṃ ca devalānnaṃ tathaiva ca
d tathā purohitasyānnaṃ bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret
d surāsavaṃ viṣaṃ sarpir lākṣā lavaṇam eva ca
d tailaṃ cāpi ca vikrīṇan dvijaś cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret
d ekoddiṣṭaṃ tu yo bhuṅkte dinamadhyagato 'pi yaḥ
d bhinnabhāṇḍe tu yo bhuṅkte dvijaś cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret
d yo bhuṅkte 'nupanītena yo bhuṅkte ca striyā saha
d yo bhuṅkte kanyayā sārdhaṃ dvijaś cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret
d ucchiṣṭaṃ sthāpayed vipro yo mohād bhojanāntare
d dadyād vā yadi saṃmohād dvijaś cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret
d tumbakośātakaṃ caiva palaṇḍuṃ gṛñjanaṃ tathā
d chattrākaṃ laghunaṃ caiva bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret
d tathā paryuṣitaṃ cānnaṃ pakvaṃ paragṛhāgatam
d vipakvaṃ ca tathā māṃsaṃ bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret
d udakyayā śunā vāpi caṇḍālair vā dvijottamaḥ
d dṛṣṭam annaṃ tu bhuñjāno dvijaś cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret
d etat purā viśuddhyartham ṛṣibhiś caritaṃ vratam
d pāvanaṃ sarvapāpānāṃ puṇyaṃ pāṇḍava coditam
d etena vasavo rudrāś cādityāś ca divaṃ gatāḥ
d etad ādyaṃ paraṃ guhyaṃ pavitraṃ pāvanaṃ smṛtam
d yathoktam etad yaḥ kuryād dvijaḥ pāpapraṇāśanam
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d sa divaṃ yāti pūtātmā nirmalādityasaṃnibhaḥ
d keśavenaivam ukte tu cāndrāyaṇavidhikrame
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d apṛcchat punar anyāṃś ca dharmān dharmātmajo nṛpa
d sarvabhūtapate śrīman sarvabhūtanamaskṛta
d sarvabhūtahitaṃ dharmaṃ sarvajña kathayasva me
d bhagavān uvāca
d yad daridrajanasyāpi svargyaṃ sukhakaraṃ bhavet
d sarvapāpapraśamanaṃ tac chṛṇuṣva yudhiṣṭhira
d kārttikādyās tu ye māsā dvādaśaiva prakīrtitāḥ
d teṣv ekabhuktaniyamaḥ sarveṣām ucyate mayā
d kārttike yas tu vai māse nandāyāṃ saṃyatendriyaḥ
d ekabhuktena madbhakto māsam ekaṃ tu vartate
d jalaṃ vā na piben māse nāntaraṃ bhojanāt param
d ādityarūpaṃ māṃ nityam arcayan susamāhitaḥ
d vratānte bhojayed viprān dakṣiṇāṃ saṃpradāya ca
d krodhalobhavinirmuktas tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d vidhivat kapilādāne yat puṇyaṃ samudāhṛtam
d tat puṇyaṃ samanuprāpya sūryaloke mahīyate
d tataś cāpi cyutaḥ kālāt puruṣeṣūpajāyate
d mārgaśīrṣaṃ tu yo māsam ekabhuktena vartate
d kāmaṃ krodhaṃ ca lobhaṃ ca parityajya yathāvidhi
d snātvā cādityarūpaṃ mām arcayen niyatendriyaḥ
d japann eva tu gāyatrīṃ māmikāṃ vāg yataḥ śuciḥ
d māse parisamāpte tu bhojayitvā dvijāñ śucīn
d tān arcayati madbhaktyā tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d agnihotre kṛte puṇyam āhitāgnes tu yad bhavet
d tat puṇyaphalam āsādya yānenāmbaraśobhinā
d saptarṣiloke carati yathākāmaṃ yathāsukham
d tataś cāpi cyutaḥ kālād dharivarṣeṣu jāyate
d tatra prakāmaṃ krīḍitvā rājā paścād bhaviṣyati
d pauṣamāsaṃ kṣaped evam ekabhuktena yo naraḥ
d arcayann eva māṃ nityaṃ madgatenāntarātmanā
d ahiṃsāsatyasahitaḥ krodhaharṣavivarjitaḥ
d evaṃ yuktasya rājendra śṛṇu yat phalam uttamam
d viprātithyasahasreṣu yat puṇyaṃ samudāhṛtam
d tat puṇyaṃ samanuprāpya śakraloke mahīyate
d avakīrṇas tataḥ kālād ilāvarṣeṣu jāyate
d tatra sthitvā ciraṃ kālam asmin vipro bhaviṣyati
d māghamāsaṃ tathā yas tu vartate caikabhuktataḥ
d madarcanaparo bhūtvā ḍambhakrodhavivarjitaḥ
d māmikām api gāyitrīṃ saṃdhyāyāṃ tu japed budhaḥ
d dattvā tu dakṣiṇām ante bhojayitvā dvijān api
d namaskaroti tān bhaktyā madgatenāntarātmanā
d trikālaṃ snānayuktasya tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d nīlakaṇṭhaprayuktena yānenāmbaraśobhinā
d pitṛlokaṃ vrajec chrīmān sevyamāno 'psarogaṇaiḥ
d tatra prakāmaṃ krīḍitvā bhadrāśveṣūpajāyate
d tataś cyutaś caturvedī vipro bhavati bhūtale
d yaḥ kṣapet phālgunaṃ māsam ekabhukto jitendriyaḥ
d namo brahmaṇyadevāyety etan mantraṃ japet sadā
d pāyasaṃ bhojayed viprān vratānte saṃyatendriyaḥ
d madarcanaparo 'krodhas tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d vimānaṃ sārasair yuktam ārūḍhaḥ kāmagāmi ca
d nakṣatraloke ramate nakṣatrasadṛśākṛtiḥ
d tataś cāpi cyutaḥ kālāt ketumāleṣu jāyate
d tatra prakāmaṃ krīḍitvā mānuṣeṣu munir bhavet
d caitramāsaṃ tu yo rājann ekabhuktena vartate
d brahmacārī tu madbhaktyā tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d yad agnihotriṇaḥ puṇyaṃ yathoktaṃ vratacāriṇaḥ
d tat puṇyaphalam āsādya candraloke mahīyate
d tato 'vatīrṇo jāyeta varṣe ramaṇake punaḥ
d bhuktvā kāmāṃs tatas tasminn iha rājā bhaviṣyati
d vaiśākhaṃ yas tu vai māsam ekabhuktena vartate
d dvijam agrāsane kṛtvā bhuñjan bhūmau ca vāgyataḥ
d namo brahmaṇyadevāyety arcayitvā divākaram
d vratānte bhojayed viprāṃs tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d phalaṃ yad vidhivat proktam agniṣṭomātirātrayoḥ
d tat puṇyaṃ phalam āsādya devaloke mahīyate
d tato haimavate varṣe jāyate kālaparyayāt
d tatra prakāmaṃ krīḍitvā vipraḥ paścād bhaviṣyati
d jyeṣṭhamāsaṃ tu yo rājann ekabhuktena vartate
d vipram agrāsane kṛtvā bhūmau bhuñjan yathāvidhi
d namo brahmaṇyadevāyety arcayan māṃ samāhitaḥ
d ḍambhānṛtavinirmuktas tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d cīrṇe cāndrāyaṇe samyag yat puṇyaṃ samudāhṛtam
d tat puṇyaphalam āsādya devaloke mahīyate
d athottarakuruṣv eva jāyate nirgatas tataḥ
d tataś cāpi cyutaḥ kālād iha loke dvijo bhavet
d āṣāḍhamāsaṃ yo rājann ekabhuktena vartate
d brahmacārī jitakrodho madarcanaparāyaṇaḥ
d vipram agrāsane kṛtvā bhūmau bhuñjan jitendriyaḥ
d kṛtvā triṣavaṇaṃ snānam aṣṭākṣaravidhānataḥ
d vratānte bhojayed viprān pāyasena yudhiṣṭhira
d guḍodanena vā rājaṃs tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d kapilāśatadānasya yat puṇyaṃ pāṇḍunandana
d tat puṇyaphalam āsādya devaloke mahīyate
d tato 'vatīrṇaḥ kāle tu śākadvīpe prajāyate
d tataś cāpi cyutaḥ kālād iha vipro bhaviṣyati
d śrāvaṇaṃ yaḥ kṣapen māsam ekabhuktena vartate
d namo brahmaṇyadevāyety uktvā mām arcayet sadā
d vipram agrāsane kṛtvā bhūmau bhuñjan yathāvidhi
d pāyasenārcayed viprāñ jitakrodho jitendriyaḥ
d lobhamohavinirmuktas tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d kapilādānasya yat puṇyaṃ vidhidattasya pāṇḍava
d tat puṇyaṃ samanuprāpya śakraloke mahīyate
d tataś cāpi cyutaḥ kālāt kuśadvīpe prajāyate
d tatra prakāmaṃ krīḍitvā vipro bhavati mānuṣe
d yas tu bhādrapadaṃ māsam ekabhuktena vartate
d brahmacārī jitakrodhaḥ satyasaṃdho jitendriyaḥ
d vipram agrāsane kṛtvā pākabhedavivarjitaḥ
d namo brahmaṇyadevāyety uktvāsya caraṇau spṛśet
d tilān vāpi ghṛtaṃ vāpi vratānte dakṣiṇāṃ dadat
d madbhaktasya naraśreṣṭha tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d yat phalaṃ vidhivat proktaṃ rājasūyāśvamedhayoḥ
d tat puṇyaphalam āsādya śakraloke mahīyate
d tataś cāpi cyutaḥ kālāj jāyate dhanadālaye
d tatra prakāmaṃ krīḍitvā rājā bhavati mānuṣe
d yaś cāpy āśvayujaṃ māsam ekabhuktena vartate
d madgāyatrīṃ japed bhaktyā madgatenāntarātmanā
d dvisaṃdhyaṃ vā trisaṃdhyaṃ vā śatam aṣṭottaraṃ tu vā
d vipram agrāsane kṛtvā saṃyatendriyamānasaḥ
d vratānte bhojayed viprāṃs tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d aśvamedhasya yat puṇyaṃ vidhivat pāṇḍunandana
d tat puṇyaphalam āsādya mama loke mahīyate
d tataś cāpi cyutaḥ kālāc chvetadvīpe prajāyate
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān atra vipraparo bhavet
d evaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ pūrṇam ekabhuktena yaḥ kṣipet
d bhagavān uvāca
d tasya puṇyaphalaṃ yad vai tan mamācakṣva keśava
d śṛṇu pāṇḍava satyaṃ me vacanaṃ puṇyam uttamam
d yad akṛtvātha vā kṛtvā naraḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyate
d ekabhuktena varteta naraḥ saṃvatsaraṃ tu yaḥ
d brahmacārī hy adhaḥśāyī jitakrodho jitendriyaḥ
d śuciḥ snānarato vyagraḥ satyavāg anasūyakaḥ
d arcayann eva māṃ nityaṃ madgatenāntarātmanā
d saṃdhyayos tu japen nityaṃ madgāyatrīṃ samāhitaḥ
d namo brahmaṇyadevāyety asakṛn māṃ praṇamya ca
d vipram agrāsane kṛtvā yāvakaṃ bhaikṣam eva ca
d bhuktvā tu vāgyato bhūmāv ācāntasya dvijanmanaḥ
d namo 'stu vāsudevāyety uktvā tu caraṇau spṛśet
d māse māse samāpte tu bhojayitvā dvijāñ śucīn
d saṃvatsare tataḥ pūrṇe dadyāt tu vratadakṣiṇām
d navanītamayīṃ gāṃ vā tiladhenum athāpi vā
d viprahastacyutais toyaiḥ sahiraṇyaiḥ samukṣitaḥ
d tasya puṇyaphalaṃ rājan kathyamānaṃ mayā śṛṇu
d daśajanmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ jñānato 'jñānato 'pi vā
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d tad vinaśyati tasyāśu nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
d sarveṣām upavāsānāṃ yac chreyaḥ sumahat phalam
d bhagavān uvāca
d yac ca niḥśreyasaṃ loke tad bhavān vaktum arhati
d śṛṇu rājan yathāpūrvaṃ yathā gītaṃ tu nārade
d tathā te kathayiṣyāmi madbhaktāya yudhiṣṭhira
d yas tu bhaktyā śucir bhūtvā pañcamyāṃ me narādhipa
d upavāsavrataṃ kuryāt trikālaṃ cārcayaṃs tu mām
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d sarvakratuphalaṃ labdhvā mama loke mahīyate
d bhagavan devadeveśa pañcamī nāma kā tava
d bhagavān uvāca
d tām ahaṃ śrotum icchāmi kathayasva mamācyuta
d parvadvayaṃ ca dvādaśyāṃ śravaṇaṃ ca narādhipa
d tat pañcamīti vikhyātā matpriyā ca viśeṣataḥ
d tasmāt tu brāhmaṇaśreṣṭhair manniveśitabuddhibhiḥ
d upavāsas tu kartavyo matpriyārthaṃ yudhiṣṭhira
d dvādaśyām eva vā kuryād upavāsam aśaknuvan
d tenāhaṃ paramāṃ prītiṃ yāsyāmi narapuṃgava
d ahorātreṇa dvādaśyāṃ mārgaśīrṣe tu keśavam
d upoṣya pūjayed yo māṃ so 'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet
d dvādaśyāṃ puṣyamāse tu nāmnā nārāyaṇaṃ tu mām
d upoṣya pūjayed yo māṃ vājapeyaphalaṃ labhet
d dvādaśyāṃ māghamāse tu mām upoṣya tu mādhavam
d pūjayed yaḥ samāpnoti rājasūyaphalaṃ labhet
d dvādaśyāṃ phālgune māsi govindākhyam upoṣya mām
d arcayed yaḥ samāpnoti hy atirātraphalaṃ nṛpa
d dvādaśyāṃ māsi caitre tu māṃ viṣṇuṃ samupoṣya yaḥ
d pūjayaṃs tad avāpnoti pauṇḍarīkasya yat phalam
d dvādaśyāṃ māsi vaiśākhe madhusūdanasaṃjñitam
d upoṣya pūjayed yo māṃ so 'gniṣṭomasya pāṇḍava
d dvādaśyāṃ jyeṣṭhamāse tu mām upoṣya trivikramam
d arcayed yaḥ samāpnoti gavāṃ medhaphalaṃ nṛpa
d āṣāḍhe vāmanākhyaṃ māṃ dvādaśyāṃ samupoṣya ca
d naramedhasya sa phalaṃ prāpnoti bharatarṣabha
d dvādaśyāṃ śrāvaṇe māsi śrīdharākhyam upoṣya mām
d pūjayed yaḥ samāpnoti pañcayajñaphalaṃ nṛpa
d māse bhādrapade yo māṃ hṛṣīkeśākhyam arcayet
d upoṣya sa samāpnoti sautrāmaṇiphalaṃ nṛpa
d dvādaśyām āśvayuṅmāse padmanābham upoṣya mām
d arcayed yaḥ samāpnoti gosahasraphalaṃ nṛpa
d dvādaśyāṃ kārttike māsi māṃ dāmodarasaṃjñitam
d upoṣya pūjayed yas tu sarvakratuphalaṃ labhet
d kevalenopavāsena dvādaśyāṃ pāṇḍunandana
d yat phalaṃ pūrvam uddiṣṭaṃ tasyārdhaṃ labhate phalam
d śravaṇe 'py evam evaṃ māṃ yo 'rcayed bhaktimān naraḥ
d mama sālokyam āpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
d māse māse samabhyarcya kramaśo mām atandritaḥ
d pūrṇe saṃvatsare kuryāt punaḥ saṃvatsarārcanam
d evaṃ dvādaśavarṣaṃ yo madbhakto matparāyaṇaḥ
d avighnam arcayānas tu mama sālokyam āpnuyāt
d arcayet prītimān yo māṃ dvādaśyāṃ vedasaṃhitām
d sa pūrvoktaphalaṃ rājaṃl labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ
d gandhaṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ toyaṃ patraṃ vā phalam eva vā
d dvādaśyāṃ mama yo dadyāt tato nānyo 'sti matpriyaḥ
d etena vidhinā sarve devāḥ śakrapurogamāḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d madbhaktā naraśārdūla svargabhogāṃs tu bhuñjate
d evaṃ vadati deveśe keśave pāṇḍunandanaḥ
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d kṛtāñjaliḥ stotram idaṃ bhaktyā dharmātmajo 'bravīt
d sarvalokeśa deveśa hṛṣīkeśa namo 'stu te
d sahasraśirase tubhyaṃ sahasrākṣa namo namaḥ
d trayīmaya trayīnātha trayīstuta namo namaḥ
d yajñātman yajñasaṃbhūta yajñanātha namo namaḥ
d caturmūrte caturbāho caturvyūha namo namaḥ
d lokātmaṃl lokakṛn nātha lokāvāsa namo namaḥ
d sṛṣṭisaṃhārakartre te narasiṃha namo namaḥ
d bhaktapriya namas te 'stu bhaktavatsala te namaḥ
d brahmāvāsa namas te 'stu brahmanātha namo namaḥ
d rudrarūpa namas te 'stu rudrakarmaratāya te
d pañcayajña namas te 'stu sarvayajña namo namaḥ
d kṛṣṇapriya namas te 'stu kṛṣṇa nātha namo namaḥ
d yogāvāsa namas te 'stu yoganātha namo namaḥ
d hayavaktra namas te 'stu cakrapāṇe namo namaḥ
d pañcabhūta namas te 'stu pañcāyudha namo namaḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d bhaktigadgadayā vācā stuvaty evaṃ yudhiṣṭhire
d gṛhītvā keśavo haste prītātmā taṃ nyavārayat
d nivārya ca punar vācā bhaktinamraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
d vaktum evaṃ naraśreṣṭhaṃ dharmaputraṃ pracakrame
d bhagavān uvāca
d anyavat kim idaṃ rājan māṃ stauṣi narapuṃgava
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d tiṣṭha pṛccha yathāpūrvaṃ dharmān eva yudhiṣṭhira
d bhagavaṃs tvatprasādāt tu smṛtvā smṛtvā punaḥ punaḥ
d na śāntir asti deveśa nṛtyatīva ca me manaḥ
d idaṃ ca mama saṃpraśnaṃ vaktum arhasi mādhava
d bhagavān uvāca
d kṛṣṇapakṣeṣu dvādaśyāṃ pūjanīyaḥ kathaṃ bhavān
d śṛṇu rājan yathātattvaṃ tat sarvaṃ kathayāmi te
d phalaṃ tu kṛṣṇadvādaśyām arcanāyāṃ phalaṃ mama
d ekādaśyām upoṣyātha dvādaśyām arcayet tu mām
d viprān api yathālābhaṃ bhojayed bhaktimān naraḥ
d sa gacched dakṣiṇāmūrtiṃ māṃ vā nātra vicāraṇā
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d candrasālokyam atha vā grahanakṣatrapūjitaḥ
d keśavenaivam ākhyāte dharmaputraḥ punaḥ prabhum
d papraccha dānakālasya viśeṣaṃ ca vidhiṃ nṛpa
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d deva kiṃ phalam ākhyātaṃ dānasya viṣuveṣu ca
d bhagavān uvāca
d sūryendūpaplave caiva datte dāne ca yat phalam
d śṛṇuṣva rājan viṣuve somārkagrahaṇeṣu ca
d vyatīpāte 'yane caiva dānaṃ syād akṣayaṃ nṛpa
d rājan nayanayor madhye viṣuvaṃ saṃpracakṣate
d samarātraṃ dine tatra saṃdhyāyāṃ viṣuve nṛpa
d brahmāhaṃ śaṃkaraś cāpi tiṣṭhāmaḥ sahitāḥ sakṛt
d kriyākaraṇakāryāṇām ekībhāvatvakāraṇāt
d asmākam ekībhūtānāṃ niṣphalaṃ tat paraṃ padam
d tan muhūrtaṃ paraṃ puṇyaṃ rājan viṣuvasaṃjñitam
d tad evādyākṣaraṃ brahma paraṃ brahmeti kīrtitam
d tasmin muhūrte sarve 'pi cintayantaḥ paraṃ padam
d devāś ca pitaro rudrā vasavaś cāśvinau tathā
d sādhyā viśve ca gandharvāḥ siddhā brahmarṣayas tathā
d sūryādayo grahāś caiva sāgarāḥ saritas tathā
d maruto 'psaraso nāgā yakṣarākṣasaguhyakāḥ
d ete cānye ca rājendra viṣuve saṃyatendriyāḥ
d sopavāsāḥ prayatnena bhavanti dhyānatatparāḥ
d annaṃ gāvas tilān bhūmiṃ kanyādānaṃ tathaiva ca
d gṛham ācchādanaṃ dhānyaṃ vāhanaṃ śayanaṃ tathā
d yac cānyac ca mayā proktaṃ tat prayaccha yudhiṣṭhira
d dīyate viṣuveṣv evaṃ śrotriyebhyo viśeṣataḥ
d tasya dānasya kaunteya kṣayo naivopapadyate
d vardhate 'har ahaḥ puṇyaṃ tad dānaṃ koṭisaṃmitam
d viṣuve snapanaṃ yas tu mama kuryād dharasya vā
d arcanaṃ ca yathānyāyaṃ tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d daśajanmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tasya sadyo vinaśyati
d daśānām aśvamedhānām iṣṭānāṃ labhate phalam
d vimānaṃ divyam ārūḍhaḥ kāmarūpī yathāsukham
d sa yāti māmakaṃ lokaṃ rudralokam athāpi vā
d tatrasthair devagandharvair gīyamāno yathāsukham
d divyavarṣasahasrāṇi koṭim ekaṃ tu modate
d tataś cāpi cyutaḥ kālād iha loke dvijottamaḥ
d caturṇām api vedānāṃ pārago brahmavid bhavet
d candrasūryagrahe vāpi mama vā śaṃkarasya vā
d gāyatrīṃ māmikāṃ vāpi japed yaḥ śaṃkarasya vā
d śaṅkhatūryaninādaiś ca kāṃsyaghaṇṭāsvanair api
d kārayet tu dhvaniṃ bhaktyā tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu
d gāndharvair homajapyaiś ca śabdair utkṛṣṭanādibhiḥ
d durbalo 'pi bhaved rāhuḥ somaś ca balavān bhavet
d sūryendūpaplave caiva śrotriyebhyaḥ pradīyate
d tat sahasrasamaṃ bhūtvā dātāram upatiṣṭhati
d mahāpātakayukto 'pi yady api syān naro nṛpa
d nirlepas tatkṣaṇād eva tena dānena jāyate
d candrasūryaprakāśena vimānena virājatā
d yāti somapuraṃ ramyaṃ sevyamāno 'psarogaṇaiḥ
d yāvad ṛkṣāṇi tiṣṭhanti gagane śaśinā saha
d tāvat kālaṃ sa rājendra somaloke mahīyate
d tataś cāpi cyutaḥ kālād iha loke yudhiṣṭhira
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d vedavedāṅgavid vipraḥ koṭīdhanapatir bhavet
d bhagavaṃs tava gāyatrī budhyate tu kathaṃ nṛbhiḥ
d kiṃ vā tasyāḥ phalaṃ deva mamācakṣva sureśvara
d bhagavān uvāca
d dvādaśyāṃ viṣuve caiva candrasūryagrahe tathā
d ayane śravaṇe caiva vyatīpāte tathaiva ca
d aśvatthadarśane caiva tathā maddarśane 'pi ca
d japtvā tu mama gāyatrīm atha vāṣṭākṣaraṃ nṛpa
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d ārjitaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ tasya nāśayen nātra saṃśayaḥ
d aśvatthadarśanaṃ caiva kiṃ tvaddarśanasaṃmitam
d etat kathaya deveśa paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me
d bhagavān uvāca
d aham aśvattharūpeṇa pālayāmi jagattrayam
d aśvattho na sthito yatra nāhaṃ tatra pratiṣṭhitaḥ
d yatrāhaṃ saṃsthito rājann aśvatthaś cāpi tatra vai
d yas tv enam arcayed bhaktyā sa māṃ sākṣāt samarcati
d yas tv enaṃ praharet kopān mām eva praharet tu saḥ
d tasmāt pradakṣiṇaṃ kuryān na chindyād enam anvaham
d vratasya pāraṇaṃ tīrtham ārjavaṃ tīrtham ucyate
d devaśuśrūṣaṇaṃ tīrthaṃ guruśuśrūṣaṇaṃ tathā
d guruśuśrūṣaṇaṃ tīrthaṃ tīrthajñānasya dhāraṇam
d narāṇāṃ poṣaṇaṃ tīrthaṃ gārhasthyaṃ tīrtham ucyate
d ātitheyaṃ paraṃ tīrtham atithis tīrtham ucyate
d brahmacaryaṃ paraṃ tīrthaṃ tretāgnis tīrtham ucyate
d mūlaṃ dharmaṃ tu vijñāya manas tatrāvadhāryatām
d gaccha tīrthāni kaunteya dharmo dharmeṇa vardhate
d dvividhaṃ tīrtham ity āhuḥ sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ tathā
d sthāvarāj jaṅgamaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tato jñānaparigrahaḥ
d karmaṇāpi viśuddhasya puruṣasyeha bhārata
d hṛdaye sarvatīrthāni tīrthabhūtaḥ sa ucyate
d gurutīrthaṃ paraṃ jñānam atas tīrthaṃ na vidyate
d jñānatīrthaṃ paraṃ tīrthaṃ brahmatīrthaṃ sanātanam
d kṣamā tu paramaṃ tīrthaṃ sarvatīrtheṣu pāṇḍava
d kṣamāvatām ayaṃ lokaḥ paraś caiva kṣamāvatām
d mānito 'mānito vāpi pūjito 'pūjito 'pi vā
d ākṛṣṭas tarjito vāpi kṣamāvāṃs tīrtham ucyate
d kṣamā damaḥ kṣamā dānaṃ kṣamā yajñaḥ kṣamā tapaḥ
d kṣamāhiṃsā kṣamā dharmaḥ kṣamā cendriyanigrahaḥ
d kṣamā dayā kṣamā yajñaḥ kṣamayaitad dhṛtaṃ jagat
d kṣamāvān prāpnuyāt svargaṃ kṣamāvān prāpnuyād yaśaḥ
d kṣamāvān prāpnuyān mokṣaṃ tasmāt sā tīrtham ucyate
d ātmā nadī bhāratapuṇyatīrtham
d ātmā tīrthaṃ sarvatīrthapradhānam
d ātmā tu yajñaḥ satataṃ manyate vai
d svargo mokṣaḥ sarvam ātmany adhīnam
d ācāranairmalyam upāgatena
d satyaprasannakṣamaśītalena
d jñānāmbunā snāti ca yo hi nityaṃ
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d kiṃ tasya bhūyaḥ salilena kṛtyam
d bhagavan sarvapāpaghnaṃ prāyaścittam aduṣkaram
d bhagavān uvāca
d tvadbhaktasya suraśreṣṭha mama tvaṃ vaktum arhasi
d rahasyam idam atyartham aśrāvyaṃ pāpakarmaṇām
d adhārmikāṇām aśrāvyaṃ prāyaścittaṃ bravīmi te
d pāvanaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā madgatenāntarātmanā
d namo brahmaṇyadevāyety abhivādanam ācaret
d pradakṣiṇaṃ ca triḥ kuryāt punar aṣṭākṣareṇa tu
d tena tuṣṭo naraśreṣṭha tat pāpaṃ kṣapayāmy aham
d yatra kṛṣṭāṃ varāhasya mṛttikāṃ śirasā vahan
d prāṇāyāmaśataṃ kṛtvā naraḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyate
d dakṣiṇāvartaśaṅkhād vā kapilāśṛṅgato 'pi vā
d prāksrotasaṃ nadīṃ gatvā mamāyatanasaṃnidhau
d salilena tu yaḥ snāyāt sakṛd eva ravigrahe
d tasya yat saṃcitaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva naśyati
d mastakān niḥsṛtais toyaiḥ kapilāyā yudhiṣṭhira
d gomūtreṇāpi yaḥ snāyād rohiṇyā mama vā dine
d viprapādacyutair vāpi toyaiḥ pāpaṃ praṇaśyati
d namasyed yas tu madbhaktyā śiṃśumāraṃ prajāpatim
d caturdaśāṅgasaṃyuktaṃ tasya pāpaṃ praṇaśyati
d tataś caturdaśāṅgāni śṛṇu tasya narādhipa
d śiro dharmo hanur brahmā pucchāv uttaradakṣiṇau
d hṛdayaṃ tu bhaved viṣṇur hastau syātāṃ tathāśvinau
d agnir madhyaṃ bhaved rājaṃl liṅgaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ bhavet
d mitrāvaruṇakau pādau pucchamūlaṃ hutāśanaḥ
d tataḥ paścād bhaved indras tataḥ paścāt prajāpatiḥ
d abhayaṃ ca tataḥ paścāt sa eva dhruvasaṃjñitaḥ
d etāny aṅgāni sarvāṇi śiṃśumāraprajāpateḥ
d pibet tu pañcagavyaṃ yaḥ paurṇamāsyām upoṣya tu
d tasya naśyati tat sarvaṃ yat pāpaṃ pūrvasaṃcitam
d tathaiva brahmakūrcaṃ tu samantraṃ tu pṛthak pṛthak
d māsi māsi pibed yas tu tasya pāpaṃ praṇaśyati
d pāpaṃ ca brahmakūrcaṃ ca śṛṇu mantraṃ ca bhārata
d pālāśaṃ padmapatraṃ vā tāmraṃ vātha hiraṇmayam
d sādayitvā tu gṛhṇīyāt tat tu pātram udāhṛtam
d gāyatryā gṛhya gomūtraṃ gandhadvāreti gomayam
d āpyāyasveti ca kṣīraṃ dadhikrāvṇeti vai dadhi
d tejo 'si śukram ity ājyaṃ devasyeti kuśodakam
d āpo hi ṣṭheti saṃgṛhya yavacūrṇaṃ yathāvidhi
d brahmaṇe ca yathā hutvā samiddhe ca hutāśane
d āloḍya praṇavenaiva nirmathya praṇavena tu
d uddhṛtya praṇavenaiva pibet tu praṇavena tu
d mahatāpi sa pāpena tvacevāhir vimucyate
d bhadraṃ na iti yaḥ pādaṃ paṭhed ṛksaṃhitāṃ yathā
d antarjale vāthāditye tasya pāpaṃ praṇaśyati
d mama sūktaṃ japed yas tu nityaṃ madgatamānasaḥ
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d na pāpena tu lipyeta padmapatram ivāmbhasā
d kīdṛśā brāhmaṇāḥ puṇyā bhāvaśuddhāḥ sureśvara
d bhagavān uvāca
d yat karma saphalaṃ neti kathayasva mamācyuta
d śṛṇu pāṇḍava tat sarvaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ yathākramam
d saphalaṃ niṣphalaṃ caiva teṣāṃ karma bravīmi te
d tridaṇḍadhāraṇaṃ maunaṃ jaṭādhāraṇamuṇḍanam
d valkalājinasaṃvāso vratacaryābhiṣecanam
d agnihotraṃ vane vāsaḥ svādhyāyaṃ dānasatkriyā
d sarvāṇy etāni vai mithyā yadi bhāvo na nirmalaḥ
d agnihotraṃ vṛthā rājan vṛthā vedās tathaiva ca
d śīlena devās tuṣyanti śrutayas tatra kāraṇam
d kṣāntaṃ dāntaṃ jitakrodhaṃ jitātmānaṃ jitendriyam
d tam agryaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ manye śeṣāḥ śūdrā iti smṛtāḥ
d agnihotravrataparān svādhyāyaniratāñ śucīn
d upavāsaratān dāntāṃs tān devā brāhmaṇān viduḥ
d na jātiḥ pūjyate rājan guṇāḥ kalyāṇakāraṇāḥ
d caṇḍālam api vṛttasthaṃ taṃ devā brāhmaṇaṃ viduḥ
d manaḥśaucaṃ karmaśaucaṃ kulaśaucaṃ ca bhārata
d śarīraśaucaṃ vākśaucaṃ śaucaṃ pañcavidhaṃ smṛtam
d pañcasv eteṣu śauceṣu hṛdi śaucaṃ viśiṣyate
d hṛdayasya tu śaucena svargaṃ gacchanti mānavāḥ
d agnihotraparibhraṣṭaḥ prasaktaḥ krayavikraye
d varṇasaṃkarakartā ca brāhmaṇo vṛṣalaiḥ samaḥ
d yasya vedaśrutir naṣṭā karṣakaś cāpi yo dvijaḥ
d vikarmasevī kaunteya sa vai vṛṣala ucyate
d vṛṣo hi dharmo vijñeyas tasya yaḥ kurute layam
d vṛṣalaṃ taṃ vidur devā nikṛṣṭaṃ śvapacād api
d stutibhir brahmapūtābhir yaḥ śūdraṃ stauti mānavaḥ
d na ca māṃ stauti pāpātmā sa mām ākrośayed bhṛśam
d śvadṛtau tu yathā kṣīraṃ brahma vai vṛṣale tathā
d duṣṭatām eti tat sarvaṃ śunā līḍhaṃ havir yathā
d aṅgāni vedāś catvāro mīmāṃsā nyāyavistaraḥ
d dharmaśāstraṃ purāṇaṃ ca vidyā hy etāś caturdaśa
d yāny uktāni mayā samyag vidyāsthānāni bhārata
d utpannāni pavitrāṇi pāvanārthaṃ tathaiva ca
d tasmāt tāni na śūdrasya spraṣṭavyāni yudhiṣṭhira
d sarvaṃ tac chūdrasaṃspṛṣṭam apavitraṃ na saṃśayaḥ
d loke trīṇy apavitrāṇi pañcāmedhyāni bhārata
d śvā ca śūdraḥ śvapākaś cety apavitrāṇi pāṇḍava
d devalaḥ kukkuṭo yūpa udakyā vṛṣalīpatiḥ
d pañcaite syur amedhyāś ca spraṣṭavyā na kathaṃ cana
d spṛṣṭvaitān aṣṭa vai vipraḥ sacelo jalam āviśet
d madbhaktāñ śūdrasāmānyān avamanyanti ye narāḥ
d narakeṣv eva tiṣṭhanti varṣakoṭiṃ narādhamāḥ
d caṇḍālam api madbhaktaṃ nāvamanyeta buddhimān
d avamatya patanty eva raurave narake narāḥ
d mama bhaktasya bhakteṣu prītir abhyadhikā nṛpa
d tasmān madbhaktabhaktāś ca pūjanīyā viśeṣataḥ
d kīṭapakṣimṛgāṇāṃ ca mayi saṃnyastacetasām
d urdhvām eva gatiṃ viddhi kiṃ punar jñānināṃ nṛṇām
d patraṃ vāpy atha vā puṣpaṃ phalaṃ vā jalam eva vā
d dadāti mama śūdro 'pi śirasā dhārayāmi tat
d viprān evārcayed bhaktyā śūdraḥ prāyeṇa matpriyaḥ
d teṣāṃ tenaiva rūpeṇa pūjāṃ gṛhṇāmi bhārata
d vedoktenaiva mārgeṇa sarvabhūtahṛdi sthitam
d mām arcayanti te viprā matsāyujyaṃ vrajanti te
d madbhaktānāṃ hitāyaiva prādurbhāvaḥ kṛto mayā
d prādurbhāvākṛtiḥ kā cid arcanīyā yudhiṣṭhira
d āsām anyatamāṃ mūrtiṃ yo madbhaktyā samarcati
d tenaiva parituṣṭo 'haṃ bhaviṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ
d mṛdā ca maṇiratnaiś ca tāmreṇa rajatena vā
d kṛtvā pratikṛtiṃ kuryād arcanāṃ kāñcanena vā
d puṇyaṃ daśaguṇaṃ vidyād eteṣām uttarottaram
d jayakāmo 'rcayed rājā vidyākāmo dvijottamaḥ
d vaiśyo vā dhanakāmas tu śūdraḥ puṇyaphalapriyaḥ
d sarvakāmāḥ striyo vāpi sarvān kāmān avāpnuyuḥ
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d kīdṛśānāṃ tu śūdrāṇāṃ nānugṛhṇāsi cārcanam
d bhagavān uvāca
d udvegas tava kasmāt tu tan me brūhi sureśvara
d avratenāpy abhaktena spṛṣṭāṃ śūdreṇa cārcanām
d tāṃ varjayāmi yatnena śvapākavihitām iva
d nanv ahaṃ śaṃkaraś cāpi gāvo viprās tathaiva ca
d aśvattho mama rūpāṇi satyam etad yudhiṣṭhira
d etat trayaṃ hi madbhakto nāvamanyeta karhi cit
d avamānitam etat tu dahaty āsaptamaṃ kulam
d aśvattho brāhmaṇā gāvo manmayās tārayanti ha
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d tasmād etat prayatnena trayaṃ pūjaya pāṇḍava
d brāhmaṇenaiva dehena śūdratvaṃ katham āpnuyāt
d bhagavān uvāca
d brahma vā naśyati kathaṃ vaktuṃ deva tvam arhasi
d kūpasnānaṃ tu yo vipraḥ kuryād dvādaśavārṣikam
d sa tenaiva śarīreṇa śūdratvaṃ yāty asaṃśayam
d yas tu rājāśrayeṇaiva jīved dvīdaśavārṣikam
d sa śūdratvaṃ vrajed vipro vedānāṃ pārago 'pi san
d pattane nagare vāpi yo dvādaśasamā vaset
d sa śūdratvaṃ vased vipro nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
d utpādayati yaḥ putraṃ śūdrāyāṃ kāmato dvijaḥ
d tasya kāyagataṃ brahma sadya eva vinaśyati
d madyapī strīmukhaṃ mohād āsvādayati yo naraḥ
d tasya kāyagataṃ brahma sadya eva vinaśyati
d yaḥ somalatikāṃ vipraḥ kevalaṃ bhakṣayed vṛthā
d tasya kāyagataṃ brahma sadya eva vinaśyati
d maithunaṃ kurute yas tu jihvāyāṃ brāhmaṇo nṛpa
d tasya kāyagataṃ brahma sadya eva vinaśyati
d vipratvaṃ durlabhaṃ prāpya durmārgair evamādibhiḥ
d vināśayanti ye tat tu tāñ śocāmi yudhiṣṭhira
d tasmāt sarvaprayatnena matpriyo yo yudhiṣṭhira
d jātibhraṃśakaraṃ karma na kuryād īdṛśaṃ dvijaḥ
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d deśāntaragate vipre saṃyukte kāladharmaṇā
d bhagavān uvāca
d śarīranāśe saṃprāpte kathaṃ pretavikalpanā
d śrūyatām āhitāgnes tu tathā bhūtasya saṃskriyā
d pālāśavṛntaiḥ pratimā kartavyā kalpacoditā
d trīṇi ṣaṣṭiśatāny āhur asthīny asya narādhipa
d teṣāṃ vikalpanā kāryā yathāśāstraviniścayam
d aśītyardhaṃ śirasi ca grīvāyāṃ daśa eva ca
d bāhvoś cāpi śataṃ dadyād aṅgulīṣu punar daśa
d urasi triṃśataṃ dadyāj jaṭhare cāpi viṃśatim
d vṛṣaṇe dvādaśārdhaṃ tu śiśne cāṣṭārdham eva ca
d dadyāt tu śatam ūrvos tu ṣaṣṭhyardhaṃ jānujaṅghayoḥ
d daśa dadyāc caraṇayor eṣā pretasya niṣkṛtiḥ
d yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
d viśeṣatīrthaṃ sarveṣām aśaktānām anugrahāt
d bhagavān uvāca
d bhaktānāṃ tāraṇārthaṃ vai vaktum arhasi dharmataḥ
d pravaraṃ sarvatīrthānāṃ satyaṃ gāyanti sāmagāḥ
d satyasya vacanaṃ tīrtham ahiṃsā tīrtham ucyate
d tapas tīrthaṃ dayā tīrthaṃ śīlaṃ tīrthaṃ yudhiṣṭhira
d alpasaṃtoṣaṇaṃ tīrthaṃ nārī tīrthaṃ pativratā
d saṃtuṣṭo brāhmaṇas tīrthaṃ jñānaṃ vā tīrtham ucyate
d madbhaktaḥ satataṃ tīrthaṃ śaṃkarasya viśeṣataḥ
d yatayas tīrtham ity eva vidvāṃsas tīrtham ucyate
d śaraṇyaḥ puruṣas tīrtham annadas tīrtham ucyate
d trailokye 'smin nirudvigno na bibhemi kutaś cana
d na divā yadi vā rātrāv udvegaḥ śūdralaṅghanāt
d na bhayaṃ devadaityebhyo rakṣobhyaś caiva me nṛpa
d śūdravaktrāc cyutaṃ brahma bhayaṃ tu mama suvrata
d tasmāt sapraṇavaṃ śūdro mannāmāpi na kīrtayet
d praṇavaṃ hi paraṃ brahma nityaṃ brahmavido viduḥ
d dvijaśuśrūṣaṇaṃ dharmaṃ śūdrāṇāṃ bhaktito mayi
d tena gacchanti te svargaṃ cintayanto hi māṃ sadā
d dvijaśuśrūṣayā śūdraḥ paraṃ śreyo 'dhigacchati
d dvijaśuśrūṣaṇād anyan nāsti śūdrasya niṣkṛtiḥ
d rāgo dveṣaś ca mohaś ca pāruṣyaṃ ca nṛśaṃsatā
d śāṭhyaṃ ca dīrghavairitvam atimānam anārjavam
d anṛtaṃ cāpavādaś ca paiśunyam atilobhatā
d hiṃsā steyaṃ mṛṣāvādo vañcanā roṣalobhatā
d abuddhitā ca nāstikyaṃ bhayam ālasyam eva ca
d aśaucaṃ cākṛtajñatvaṃ ḍambhatā stambha eva ca
d nikṛtiś cāpy avijñānaṃ jātake śūdram āviśet
d dṛṣṭvā pitāmahaḥ śūdram abhibhūtaṃ tu tāmasaiḥ
d dvijaśuśrūṣaṇaṃ dharmaṃ śūdrāṇāṃ tu prayuktavān
d naśyanti tāmasā bhāvāḥ śūdrasya dvijabhaktitaḥ
d patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ toyaṃ yo me bhaktyā prayacchati
d tad ahaṃ bhaktyupahṛtaṃ mūrdhnā gṛhṇāmi śūdrataḥ
d antyajo vāpi yaḥ kaś cit sarvapāpasamanvitaḥ
d yadi māṃ satataṃ dhyāyet sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
d vidyāvinayasaṃpannā brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ
d mayi bhaktiṃ na kurvanti caṇḍālasadṛśā hi te
d vṛthā dattaṃ vṛthā japtaṃ vṛthā ceṣṭaṃ vṛthā hutam
d vṛthātithyaṃ ca tat tasya yo na bhakto mama dvijaḥ
d yat kṛtaṃ ca hutaṃ cāpi yad iṣṭaṃ dattam eva ca
d abhaktimat kṛtaṃ sarvaṃ rākṣasā eva bhuñjate
d sthāvare jaṅgame vāpi sarvabhūteṣu pāṇḍava
d samatvena yadā kuryān madbhakto mitraśatruṣu
d ānṛśaṃsyam ahiṃsā ca dayā satyam athārjavam
d adrohaś caiva bhūtānāṃ madbhaktānāṃ vrataṃ nṛpa
d nama ity eva yo brūyān madbhaktaḥ śraddhayānvitaḥ
d tasyākṣayo bhavel lokaḥ śvapākasyāpi pāṇḍava
d kiṃ punar ye yajante māṃ yājakā vidhipūrvakam
d madbhaktā madgataprāṇāḥ kathayantaś ca māṃ sadā
d bahuvarṣasahasrāṇi tapas tapyati yo naraḥ
d nāsau padam avāpnoti madbhaktair yad avāpyate
d mām eva tasmād rājendra dhyāhi nityam atandritaḥ
d avāpsyasi tataḥ siddhiṃ drakṣyase paramaṃ padam
d apārthakaṃ prabhāṣante śūdrā bhāgavatā iti
d na śūdrā bhagavadbhaktā viprā bhāgavatāḥ smṛtāḥ
d dvādaśākṣaratattvajñaś caturvyūhavibhāgavit
d acchidraḥ pañcakālajñaḥ sa vai bhāgavataḥ smṛtaḥ
d ṛgvedenaiva māṃ hotā yajuṣādhvaryur eva ca
d sāmavedena codgātā puṇyenābhiṣṭuvanti mām
d atharvaśirasā caiva nityam ātharvaṇā dvijāḥ
d stuvanti satataṃ ye māṃ te 'pi bhāgavatāḥ smṛtāḥ
d vedādhīnāḥ sadā yajñā yajñādhīnās tu devatāḥ
d devatā brāhmaṇādhīnās tasmād viprās tu devatāḥ
d anāśrityocchrayaṃ nāsti mukhyam āśrayam āśrayet
d rudraṃ samāśritā devā rudro brāhmaṇam āśritaḥ
d brahmā mām āśrito rājan nāhaṃ kaṃ cid upāśritaḥ
d mamāśrayo na kaś cit tu sarveṣām āśrayo hy aham
d evam etan mayā proktaṃ rahasyam idam uttamam
d dharmapriyasya te rājan nityam evaṃ samācara
d idaṃ pavitram ākhyānaṃ puṇyaṃ vedena saṃmitam
d yaḥ paṭhen māmakaṃ dharmam ahany ahani pāṇḍava
d dharmo vivardhate tasya buddhiś cāpi prasīdati
d pāpakṣayam upaity eva kalyāṇaṃ ca vivardhate
d etat puṇyaṃ pavitraṃ ca pāpanāśanam uttamam
d śrotavyaṃ śraddhayā yuktaiḥ śrotriyaiś ca viśeṣataḥ
d śrāvayed yas tv idaṃ bhaktyā prayato 'tha śṛṇoti vā
d sa gacchen mama sāyujyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
d yaś cedaṃ śrāvayec chrāddhe madbhakto matparāyaṇaḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d pitaras tasya tṛpyanti yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam
d śrutvā bhāgavatān dharmān sākṣād viṣṇor jagadguroḥ
d prahṛṣṭamanaso bhūtvā cintayanto 'dbhutāḥ kathāḥ
d ṛṣayaḥ pāṇḍavāś caiva praṇemus taṃ janārdanam
d pūjayām āsa govindaṃ dharmaputraḥ punaḥ punaḥ
d devā brahmarṣayaḥ siddhā gandharvāpsarasas tathā
d bhūtā yakṣā grahāś caiva guhyakā bhujagās tathā
d vālakhilyā mahātmāno yoginas tattvadarśinaḥ
d tathā bhāgavatāś cāpi pañcakālam upāsakāḥ
d kautūhalasamāyuktā bhagavan bhaktim āgatāḥ
d śrutvā tu paramaṃ puṇyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ dharmaśāsanam
d vimuktapāpāḥ pūtās te saṃvṛttās tatkṣaṇena tu
d praṇamya śirasā viṣṇuṃ pratinandya ca tāṃ kathām
d draṣṭāro dvārakāyāṃ vai vayaṃ sarve jagadgurum
d iti prahṛṣṭamanaso yayur devagaṇaiḥ saha
d sarve ṛṣigaṇā rājan yayuḥ svaṃ svaṃ niveśanam
d gateṣu teṣu sarveṣu keśavaḥ keśihā tadā
d sasmāra dārukaṃ rājan sa ca sātyakinā saha
d samīpastho 'bhavat sūto yāhi deveti cābravīt
d tato viṣaṇṇavadanāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ puruṣottamam
d añjaliṃ mūrdhni saṃdhāya netrair aśrupariplutaiḥ
d pibantaḥ satataṃ kṛṣṇaṃ nocur ārtatarās tadā
d kṛṣṇo 'pi bhagavān devaḥ pṛthām āmantrya cārtavat
d dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ ca gāndhārīṃ viduraṃ draupadīṃ tathā
d kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaṃ vyāsam ṛṣīn anyāṃś ca mantriṇaḥ
d subhadrām ātmajayutām uttarāṃ spṛśya pāṇinā
d nirgatya veśmanas tasmād āruroha mahāratham
d vājibhiḥ sainyasugrīvameghapuṣpabalāhakaiḥ
d yuktaṃ ca dhvajabhūtena patagendreṇa dhīmatā
d anvāruroha cāpy enaṃ premṇā rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d apāsya cāśu yantāraṃ dārukaṃ sūtasattamam
d abhīśūn pratijagrāha svayaṃ kurupatis tadā
d upāruhyārjunaś cāpi cāmaravyajanaṃ śubham
d rukmadaṇḍaṃ bṛhan mūrdhni dudhāvābhipradakṣiṇam
d chattraṃ śataśalākaṃ ca divyamālyopaśobhitam
d vaiḍūryamaṇidaṇḍaṃ ca cāmīkaravibhūṣitam
d dadhāra tarasā bhīmaḥ chattraṃ tac chārṅgadhanvinaḥ
d bhīmasenārjunau cāpi yamau cāpy arisūdanau
d pṛṣṭhato 'nuyayuḥ kṛṣṇaṃ mā śabda iti harṣitāḥ
d triyojane vyatīte tu pariṣvajya ca pāṇḍavān
d visṛjya kṛṣṇas tān sarvān praṇatān dvārakāṃ yayau
d tathā praṇamya govindaṃ tadā prabhṛti pāṇḍavāḥ
d kapilādyāni dānāni dadur dharmaparāyaṇāḥ
d madhusūdanavākyāni smṛtvā smṛtvā punaḥ punaḥ
d manasā pūjayām āsur hṛdayasthāni pāṇḍavāḥ
d yudhiṣṭhiras tu dharmātmā hṛdi kṛtvā janārdanam
d tadbhaktas tanmanā yuktas tadyājī tatparo 'bhavat
d evam etat purāvṛttaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ dharmaśāsanam
d mayā te kathitaṃ rājan pavitraṃ pāpanāśanam
d tac chṛṇuṣva mahārāja viṣṇuproktaṃ kurūdvaha
d tena gacchasi nānyena tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam
